~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~

1.                               Introduction

~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~

Yoshi's Island is the sequel to Super Mario World on the SNES. This game is set 
in the past, when Mario is a baby, and is dropped by a stork onto Yoshi's 
Island. The Yoshis get together and decide to return Mario to his parents, but 
Bowser interferes, and sends a huge range of enemies out into the many levels 
of the game. Unlike previous Mario games, you control Yoshi instead of Mario.

This game has excellent graphics, from the start of the game all the way to the 
end. The screen scrolls left and right very smoothly, and gives quite a zoomed 
out view to allow you to see quite far into the distance before you even get 
there. There is great detail on the foreground as well as the background, and 
though all of the levels are different from one another, they all retain the 
same amount of detail.

In all, there are six worlds in this game, each of which contain eight normal 
levels and one secret level. Add to that one tutorial level, and there are 
fifty-five levels! Quite an incredible statistic for a game, considering the 
size and detail in each and every level, most of which contain new enemies and 
all of which contain new and original backgrounds, items, and tasks to do.

At the end each level, you're given a score depending on how many of the 
required items you picked up on your journey through the level. More often than 
not, these items are hidden high up in difficult to reach places. Finding them 
all in a single level can be difficult, especially when you have an abundance 
of enemies rushing at you from all different directions. But if you do happen 
to get 100% in the eight normal levels on a world, the secret, extra-difficult 
level will be unlocked.

Overall, Yoshi's Island is a superb game. It's one of the few games that I've 
bought for my SNES which I still play occasionally. The originality and size of 
the game are incredible, with 55 huge levels and 127 enemies. Try not to be put 
off by first appearances, as what may first seem to be a simple game will soon 
turn into one of the most complex and difficult platform games on the SNES.

~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~

2.                                  Moves

~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~

Eat
  Upon pressing Y, Yoshi sticks his tongue out. Providing he's close enough to 
  an enemy, Yoshi will usually grab them. From here, you can either spit them 
  out or swallow them.

Hover
  Hold B in the air to hover. This move can be used to travel long distances, 
  and to reach places that you wouldn't be able to with a normal jump.

Jump
  The basic jump.

Run
  Continue to hold left or right, and Yoshi will run fast in that direction.

Shoot
  Providing Yoshi has at least one egg, tapping A to display the egg target, 
  and then releasing A, Yoshi will shoot an egg in the direction he's facing.

Spit
  When Yoshi has an enemy in his mouth, tap Y to spit them out. This is useful 
  for defeating other enemies and opening winged clouds.

Stomp
  While in the air, press down to stomp the ground. This can be used to defeat 
  strong enemies, but as it's quite a slow move, it can be very difficult to 
  hit the faster enemies.

Swallow
  When Yoshi has an enemy in his mouth, tap down to swallow them. Yoshi will 
  receive an egg.

~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~

3.                                Walkthrough

~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~

===============================================================================
                       Intro: Welcome To Yoshi's Island
===============================================================================

This introductory level is here to give new players the chance to get used to 
the controls of the game before the first level. As this is a tutorial level, 
there isn't too much to worry about in the way of enemies and other dangers, so 
I'll use this section of the guide to explain about some of the basic controls 
used in the game. For more specific information, hints and advice on playing 
the game, hit the various message blocks in the game.

At the start of the game, press right on the D-Pad and scroll through the 
messages that pop up on screen. Run past the red arrow on the right to come to 
the first enemy in the game: a Shy Guy. There are various ways to beat enemies 
in this game. As enemies get more difficult later on in the game, some ways may 
work better or worse than others, or may not work at all. Here are all of the 
ways to beat the Shy Guys in this section of the level:

Option 1: Jump
  This is the most basic option for beating most of the easy enemies. Just jump  
  up by pressing X and land on top of the Shy Guy.

Option 2: Pound
  Jump up over the top of the Shy Guy and press down to make Yoshi stamp on the 
  floor. This is more powerful than the jump, but is much slower. For slow 
  enemies such as the Shy Guy in this section of the level, this is fine, but 
  you will need to be accurate.

Option 3: Spit
  Get close to the first Shy Guy and press Y to grab him. Press Y again to spit 
  the enemy out. This is useful for defeating a second enemy, such as the 
  second Shy Guy in this section of the level.

Option 4: Egg
  Get close to the first Shy Guy and press Y to grab him. Press down to create 
  an egg. With the egg, face the second shy guy and press A to bring up a 
  target. Egg throwing is one of the most useful features for defeating enemies 
  in the game, but can look quite confusing at first. When the egg target comes 
  up, wait until it points toward the second Shy Guy, and then press A again to 
  shoot the egg. To pause the egg target, press either the L or R button. To 
  bring up the target and not shoot an egg at all, press down on the D-Pad or 
  press Y to cancel the egg.

With both Shy Guys out of the way, continue right to come to a platform 
consisting of five blocks, with some coins high above. The middle block is 
purple, and increases in size when hit. Hit the purple block, and then jump up 
to the top of it. You can now collect the coins that were too high to reach 
before.

Jump off the right side of the purple block and land on the rock. Jump up to 
the next rock on the right to land near a message block. Hitting the block will 
give information on the Hovering Jump, which can be used to cross large 
distances or gain extra height in jumps. Run right until you come to the edge 
of the path, and then jump high into the gap. Hold up, right and X to hover up 
to the top of the high rock on the other side.

Walk right to come to a small spring ball. Spring balls are used to help Yoshi 
bounce much higher than a normal jump. For a spring ball to work, jump high and 
then jump again as soon as you land on the ball. Launch up to the rock high up 
on the right, and then run right to come to a large spring ball. This is 
similar to the small spring ball, but it launches Yoshi much higher. Use this 
ball to launch up to the rock on the right.

Go right after landing to arrive near two Shy Guys. Use any of the four 
possible attacks shown earlier in this level walkthrough to defeat the Shy 
Guys, and then run right to exit the level.


===============================================================================
                       Level 1-1: Make Eggs, Throw Eggs
===============================================================================

                                 - Flower 1 -

Run right when the level starts, and pass under the message block to come to 
two Shy Guys. Eat both Shy Guys to create two eggs, and continue right until 
you see a platform above with a Shy Guy on it. Jump up to the platform and eat 
the Shy Guy to make a third egg, and then jump off the right side of the 
platform to collect the first flower.

                                 - Flower 2 -

After landing on the blue rock, eat the Shy Guy and jump high off the right 
side of the rock to avoid a Pirahna Plant. Run under the second message block 
to arrive near a platform with a winged cloud above. Jump up to the platform, 
eat the Shy Guy, and shoot an egg at the cloud, which will create some steps 
leading up to the left. Climb the steps to the long platform at the top, and 
collect the middle row of six red coins. Go to the far left side of the 
platform to collect the second flower.

                                 - Flower 3 -

As soon as you collect the second flower, a Fly Guy holding a winged cloud will 
appear up on the left. He doesn't stay for long, so quickly shoot an egg at him 
to burst the cloud, which will make five stars fall down to the platform below. 
Collect the stars, and then jump back up to the platform on the right. Run 
right and go down the steps to the platform at the bottom. Drop down off the 
right edge to activate two Pirahna Plants. Shoot an egg at the bottom plant, 
and go down the pipe on the other side.

After arriving in the cave, go right and drop off the edge to land near an egg 
block. Hit the block to collect eggs, and then go right. Before collecting any 
of the items above, push Chomp Rock all the way to the wall on the right to 
defeat two Shy Guys. Leave the rock near the wall, and run back left to the 
start of the cave. Shoot eggs at the six red coins in the area, and shoot the 
two Fly Guys to make them each drop a red coin.

Shoot an egg at the Baron Von Zeppelin holding the extra life, and push Chomp 
Rock back over to the wall at the right side of the cave. Shoot an egg off the 
ceiling so that it rebounds into the open tulip, which will throw out eight 
stars. Collect all the stars, and run right. Jump on Chomp Rock, hop up to the 
ledge on the right, and then go up the pipe. After emerging from the pipe, jump 
over the wall on the left to collect the third flower.

                                 - Flower 4 -

Walk up the small steep slope on the right, and jump across the gap to land on 
the blue rock. Shoot an egg at the Pirahna Plant that appears, and then jump 
down to any one of the four purple circling platforms. When the platform goes 
low, drop down off the right side of the platform to land on a long platform. 
Collect all four red coins on the platform and run over to the left side to 
collect the fourth flower.

                                 - Flower 5 -

Jump back on one of the circling platforms and jump off to land on the blue 
rock up on the right. Run down the slope to find a pipe which Shy Guys are 
jumping out of. Eat the Shy Guys until Yoshi has six eggs, and then shoot an 
egg up at the winged cloud above, collecting the five stars that fall. Jump 
over the pipe and continue right, eating both Crazee Dayzees along the way.

Shoot an egg at the winged cloud, and climb up the left side of the newly 
created beanstalk. Near the top of the beanstalk, jump off to land on the rock 
on the left, and continue left to find a winged cloud off the edge of a rock. 
Shoot an egg at the winged cloud to reveal the fifth and final flower. Jump off 
the rock to collect the flower, and hover right to land on a rock below.

Although it seems there is nothing on this rock, run right to reveal a hidden 
winged cloud. Shoot an egg at the cloud to reveal five stars, and then drop 
down off the left side of the rock. Go right and climb back up the beanstalk to 
the top, but this time jump up to one of the purple circling platforms above. 
Collect the two red coins when the platform gets to the highest point, and then 
jump over to the blue rock on the right.

Go right to find Chomp Rock. Push it down the hill on the right to defeat two 
Shy Guys and a Pirahna Plant. Jump over Chomp Rock to land on the blue rock on 
the other side. Shoot the neabry winged cloud for five stars. From the rock, 
run right and jump over the five Shy Guys to come to the goal ring. Jump 
through the goal ring to complete the level.

~~ Items ~~

1UP
  Floating under a Baron Von Zeppelin in the cave.

Flower 1
  Above the first blue rock.

Flower 2
  When the steps are created from hitting the first winged cloud, run up the 
  steps to the platform and go left to find this flower.

Flower 3
  After exiting the cave, jump over the wall on the left to find this flower.

Flower 4
  At the bottom-left corner of the first rotating purple platform.

Flower 5
  After climbing the beanstalk, go left and shoot the winged cloud to reveal 
  this flower.

6 Red Coins
  When the steps are created from hitting the first winged cloud, run up the 
  steps to the platform. The middle row of six coins are red coins.

2 Red Coins
  Shoot the two Fly Guys in the cave to make them drop a red coin each.

6 Red Coins
  Shoot eggs at the six red tinted coins in the cave.

4 Red Coins
  On the platform below the first rotating purple platform.

2 Red Coins
  Above the second rotating purple platform.

5 Stars
  When the steps are created from hitting the first winged cloud, run up the 
  steps to the platform and go left past the flower to find a Fly Guy holding a 
  cloud. Shoot an egg at the cloud to reveal five stars.

8 Stars
  In the cave, shoot an egg off the ceiling so that it rebounds into the open 
  tulip, which will throw out eight stars.

5 Stars
  Near the beanstalk, there is a winged cloud above a pipe. Shoot the winged 
  cloud for five stars.

5 Stars
  Near the top of the beanstalk, jump off to the left, and continue left to the 
  edge of the rock. Jump off the rock and hold right to land on the rock below. 
  Run right to reveal a hidden winged cloud which contains five stars.

5 Stars
  Shoot the winged cloud above the Woozy Guys near the end of the level.

===============================================================================
                           Level 1-2: Watch Out Below!
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Run right at the start of the level and jump up the small step. Go up the slope 
and drop down the other side to arrive near two Shy Guys. Eat both Shy Guys and 
continue right. Go up the slope and jump at the top to collect the first 
flower.

                                   - Flower 2 -

From this point in the level to the first middle ring, Chomps will jump from 
the background to make gaps in the floor. The first Chomp will make a gap in 
the floor just after the first flower. Jump the gap and eat the Crazee Dayzee 
on the other side, and then continue up the slope to the top. Jump over the 
small ledge to land near six coins, then quickly hold right and stop under the 
third and fourth coins, which are red coins.

Jump up to collect the red coins, and continue right, jumping over the various 
gaps along the way, to come to a winged cloud. A Chomp will fall down and 
create a gap under the winged cloud, so don't go near it just yet. When the 
Chomp has created the gap, shoot the winged cloud to reveal the second flower, 
and jump over the gap to collect it.

                                   - Flower 3 -

Go right and drop down the step to land near six more coins. The red coins are 
the four middle coins, but be careful as Chomps can create gaps under the first 
and fourth coin. Use a Hover jump to collect the coins, and continue right to 
come to a post. Jump over the first post and eat both Shy Guys, and then shoot 
an egg up at the winged cloud to receive five stars. Collect the stars, then 
jump over the second post and continue right to pass the Middle Ring.

Go right to come to a Shy Guy pipe, and eat Shy Guys until Yoshi has six eggs. 
This will stop the Shy Guys coming out of the pipe, so you can have some time 
to look around. Shoot an egg at the fluffy ceiling above and collect the four 
red coins that are up there, and then shoot an egg through the fluffy wall on 
the right. Shoot a final egg up through the ceiling to make the spring ball 
fall down. Go and collect some more eggs by eating the enemies coming out of 
the Shy Guy pipe, and then bounce up to the next area by using the spring ball.

After landing on the platform, two red arrows will be pointing right. Although 
you can go left, it only leads through a hidden tunnel in the wall to an area 
with an expansion block. So follow the arrows advice and go right through the 
hidden wall. Jump up the two platforms to come to a junction. If you choose to 
go right here, you can follow a path along to a hidden winged cloud which 
contains a 1UP. Apart from the 1UP though, there's nothing else of interest, so 
go left at the junction to come to two more platforms. Jump up the platforms 
and go left at the junction to pass through the second middle ring in the 
level.

After passing the second middle ring, go right and jump over the small gap. On 
the other side of the hidden tunnel, run under the message block and enter the 
hidden tunnel on the right. Bounce off the small spring ball and exit the 
hidden tunnel high up on the right. Go down the slope on the other side to 
arrive near a message block and a Metamorphosis Bubble. Touch the bubble to 
transform into a helicopter. Fly right and go under the first hidden tunnel 
section to collect two red coins. Go up after collecting the final coin to 
collect the third flower.

                                   - Flower 4 -

Continue right after collecting the third flower, and pass through the set of 
coins that lead down and right. After these coins, there will be a section of 
wall which has three hidden entrances, one on the left, one on the right and 
one at the bottom. Go up through the tunnel at the bottom of the wall to find 
the fourth flower.

                                   - Flower 5 -

Exit the tunnel and then fly up and right past the Gusty. When you see the 
floating island over on the right (which has arrows pointing down and right on 
it), go right along the island and then go up and right at the end. When you 
come to the two red arrows on the ceiling that point down, go up close to the 
arrows and then fly through the hidden tunnel on the right. Follow the tunnel 
down and right to collect three red coins, and then fly down and left after 
exiting the tunnel to hit the Yoshi Block, which will return Yoshi to normal. 

Run right to come to a pipe, but don't enter it just yet. Instead, jump up to 
one of the platforms on either side of the pipe, and then jump up into the 
small hidden area just above the platforms to collect two more red coins. Drop 
down to the pipe and go down it.

After arriving in the final area, shoot an egg at the winged cloud to reveal 
the fifth flower. Quickly shoot the Fly Guy holding the 1UP, and then jump up 
to collect the flower. Run right and hover jump over the Pirahna Plant to 
collect the three red coins. On the other side, eat the nearby Shy Guy, and 
shoot an egg at the winged cloud to reveal five stars. Run right, eating the 
Crazee Dayzee and Shy Guy along the way, and watch out for the final Chomp 
which creates a gap just left of the red arrow. Jump over the gap, and jump 
through the goal ring on the other side to complete the level.

~~ Items ~~

1UP
  After passing the first middle ring, use the large spring ball behind the 
  wall on the right to jump up into the area above. Go right at the first 
  junction, and right at the second junction. Continue right and drop down off 
  the edge of the path next to the arrow pointing left. After landing, continue 
  right and run through two hidden walls right to reveal a hidden cloud near a 
  third wall. Shoot an egg at the cloud to receive a 1UP.

1UP
  After arriving in the final area of the level, shoot an egg at the Fly Guy at 
  the right side of the first winged cloud.

Flower 1
  Found at the top of the slope just after the first two Shy Guys in the level.

Flower 2
  Shoot an egg at the first winged cloud in the level to reveal this flower.

Flower 3
  After Yoshi has transformed into a helicopter, fly right and go under the 
  first hidden tunnel section to find this flower.

Flower 4
  About half-way through the journey from the Metamorphosis Bubble to the Yoshi 
  Block, there will be a set of coins leading down and right. After these 
  coins, there will be a section of wall. Go up through the hidden tunnel at 
  the bottom of the wall to find the fourth flower.

Flower 5
  After arriving in the final area of the level, shoot an egg at the first 
  winged cloud to reveal this flower.

2 Red Coins
  About half-way through the first Chomp area, there are six coins in a line. 
  The third and fourth coins are red.

4 Red Coins
  When you come to the second set of six coins in the first Chomp area, collect 
  the four middle red coins.

4 Red Coins
  After passing the first middle ring, shoot an egg up at the ceiling to 
  collect four red coins (first, third, fourth and sixth coins).

2 Red Coins
  After Yoshi has transformed into a helicopter, fly right and go under the 
  first hidden tunnel section to collect these red coins.

3 Red Coins
  After Yoshi has transformed into a helicopter, fly along to the Yoshi Block, 
  but don't touch it. Instead, go straight up to the ceiling with the arrows 
  pointing down, and then fly right to enter a hidden tunnel which contains 
  these coins.

2 Red Coins
  At the end of the area with the helicopter, there is a pipe which leads to 
  the next area. There is a small secret area above the pipe which contains 
  these coins.

3 Red Coins
  After arriving in the final area of the level, run right and hover jump over 
  the Pirahna Plant to collect the three coins.

5 Stars
  Shoot the winged cloud above the two Shy Guys near the end of the first Chomp 
  area.

10 Stars
  Go through the first middle ring.

1 Star
  After passing the first middle ring, run right to find a single star.

10 Stars
  Go through the second middle ring.

5 Stars
  In the final area of the level, shoot an egg at the winged cloud on the right 
  side of the Pirahna Plant.

===============================================================================
                        Level 1-3: The Cave Of Chomp Rock
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

This level starts outside, with a green pipe on the right which leads down to 
the cave. Jump on top of the pipe to activate a Pirahna Plant over on the 
right, and providing you have some eggs left over, shoot an egg at the plant. 
With the plant defeated, jump over to the ledge where it used to be to find a 
hidden winged cloud. Shoot the winged cloud to receive a 1UP, and then go down 
the pipe.

As soon as you arrive in the cave, a Chomp Rock will start rolling down the 
slope up on the left. Let the rock push you down the slope to the post at the 
bottom, then jump over the post and stomp the crate on the other side. Collect 
all six stars, and continue right to find a fluffy wall. Eat the Nipper Plant, 
and then jump up to the top of the wall. Walk over to the middle of the wall, 
and stomp the post two times to receive a single red coin.

Run right and eat the Shy Guy up on top of the mushroom. Jump up to the 
mushroom, and hover jump over the Nipper Plants below to collect the top four 
red coins. On the other side of the Nipper Plant pit, run right up the steep 
slope and drop off the end of the path to land on a mushroom. A Chomp Rock is 
visible over on the right, but don't go there just yet. Instead, drop down to 
the lowest mushroom, and then go down the gap below it to land in a tunnel. 
Follow the tunnel down and along, and collect the first flower and the two red 
coins at the end.

                                   - Flower 2 -

Eat the two Lantern Ghosts if Yoshi needs more eggs, and then run back up the 
tunnel and jump out of the gap under the mushroom. Climb up the steps on the 
right to the Chomp Rock at the top, and push it down the slope. Follow the rock 
down until it collides with a second Chomp Rock, and then continue following 
the first rock down the path on the left. Push the rock along the path to 
defeat two Nipper Plants, and collect the second flower and the two red coins 
at the end.

                                   - Flower 3 -

Head back to the right, noticing the door above with the keyhole along the way, 
and push the Chomp Rock down the slope on the right. Follow the Chomp Rock down 
into the small cave, and jump up to the mushroom. Collect all four red coins, 
and shoot an egg at the winged cloud to reveal five stars. Collect the stars 
and exit the cave on the left. Run up the small slope and jump up to the first 
slope on the right. Run up the slope in the path, and jump over to the mushroom 
on the left. Jump up to the platform on the left and pass through the middle 
ring to receive 10 stars.

Drop down off the right side of the platform and continue right up the path to 
the post, jumping over the rolling Chomp Rock along the way. Wait for the two 
Nipper Plants to bounce down from the mushrooms up on the right. Eat the Nipper 
Plants when they get close, and then jump up to the top of the post. Jump up to 
the first mushroom on the right, and shoot an egg up at the third flower high 
above to collect it.

                                   - Flower 4 -

Jump over to the mushroom on the right, and hold up to look up higher. Shoot an 
egg at the three Baron Von Zeppelins holding the crate up high on the right. 
When the crate falls down, go over and stomp on it to reveal six stars. 
Continue right to find three posts. Jump up to the top of the middle post and 
hold up to see a Baron Von Zeppelin holding a key. Shoot an egg at the Baron 
Von Zeppelin, and run over to collect the key.

With the key, run back to the left and go down the slope to the end of the 
path. Jump across to the middle path on the left and go along to find a door 
with a keyhole. Press up to unlock the door and enter the bonus area. In the 
bonus area, enter the button combinations that are shown to pass the balloon 
between Yoshi and the Bandit. If the balloon pops on the Bandit, you will get a 
1UP.

After exiting the bonus level, run right and jump across the gap to the top 
path. Run up the path and jump over the post. Eat the Lantern Ghost on the 
other side, and continue right to return to the three posts. Stomp the middle 
post twice and the right post three times to collect two red coins, and then 
continue right. Jump up to the high ledge on the right with the three coins on 
each side. The middle coins on each side are red, so collect those, and 
continue right to find another Chomp Rock.

Push Chomp Rock off the edge of the path and follow it as it rolls right to 
defeat a Nipper Plant. Jump up to the path on the left, and jump from the 
mushroom to get up to the next path on the right. Jump up to the next mushroom 
above, and face left. Shoot an egg up to the top-left corner of the fluffy 
ceiling to receive a 1UP, then go right and shoot an egg in the direction of 
the fourth flower to collect it.

                                   - Flower 5 -

Run down the path on the right and jump onto the first post. Pound the post 
twice to reveal a winged cloud, then shoot the winged cloud to reveal a red 
switch. Jump on the red switch and quickly run right to find two posts with a 
Nipper Plant in the middle. Jump between the posts to land on the Nipper Plant, 
and then press down to enter a secret area. In the area, collect as many coins 
as you can on the moving platform, and then use the spring balls at either side 
to exit the area.

After exiting the secret area, jump over the two posts on the right to come to 
a Chomp Rock. Push the rock slowly up the small slope under the gap on the 
right, and then go left just before the top of the slope. Stay under the gap, 
and jump on Chomp Rock as it rolls down. Quickly jump up through the gap and 
hover jump up to the path on the right. Collect the three red coins at the 
right side of the area, and then jump over the gap and collect the fifth and 
final flower at the left side of the area.

Jump down the gap and go right up the steep slope to exit the cave of Chomp 
Rock. Outside, run right and jump over the pipe. Shoot an egg at the Pirahna 
Plant, and go right to the second Pirahna Plant. Quickly shoot the plant, and 
then shoot another egg up at the Fly Guy holding the 1UP. Continue right to 
come to the goal ring, and jump through it to complete the level.

~~ Items ~~

1UP
  Outside the cave at the start of the level, shoot the Pirahna Plant and jump 
  over to the ledge to reveal a winged cloud. Shoot the cloud for the 1UP.

1UP
  Near the end of the cave, there is an area with a fluffy ceiling. Shoot an 
  egg up to the top-left corner of the ceiling to receive this 1UP.

1UP
  A Fly Guy is holding this in the final area of the level.

Flower 1
  Shortly after the second message block in the level, there are six mushrooms 
  in the gap on the right. Drop down the gap below the lowest mushroom and 
  follow the tunnel along to the flower.

Flower 2
  After passing the area in the cave with the six mushrooms, run down the long 
  slope, and take the lowest path left to find this flower between two coins.

Flower 3
  Above the three mushrooms where the Paranipper Plants first appear. Shoot an 
  egg to collect the flower.

Flower 4
  Near the end of the cave, there is an area with a fluffy ceiling. Shoot an 
  egg up to the top-right corner of the ceiling to receive collect the flower.

Flower 5
  Near the end of the cave, push the final Chomp Rock up the first small slope 
  on the right, and use it jump up through the gap. The final flower can be 
  found on the left side of the area.

1 Red Coin
  When you come to the post in a fluffy wall, stomp the post twice to receive 
  this coin.

4 Red Coins
  Before the second message block in the level, there is a pit with four Nipper 
  Plants in it. The four top coins over the pit are red.

2 Red Coins
  Shortly after the second message block in the level, there are six mushrooms 
  in the gap on the right. Drop down the gap below the lowest mushroom and 
  follow the tunnel along to the coins.

2 Red Coins
  After passing the area in the cave with the six mushrooms, run down the long 
  slope, and take the lowest path left to find two coins on either side of a 
  flower.

4 Red Coins
  After passing the area in the cave with the six mushrooms, run down the long 
  slope, and take the lowest path right. Push the Chomp Rock down the slope and 
  follow it to arrive in a cave with the red coins above a blue mushroom.

2 Red Coins
  Near the end of the Paranipper Plant area, there are three coins in a 
  diagonal line on each side of a ledge. The middle coin on each side is red.

2 Red Coins
  Near the end of the Paranipper Plant area, there are three posts at different 
  heights. Stomp the middle post twice for the first coin, and stomp the right 
  post three times for the second coin.

3 Red Coins
  Near the end of the cave, push the final Chomp Rock up the first small slope 
  on the right, and use it jump up through the gap. Three red coins can be 
  found at the right side of the area.

6 Stars
  Near the start of the cave, there is a crate at the right side of a post. 
  Stomp the crate for six stars.

5 Stars
  After passing the area in the cave with the six mushrooms, run down the long 
  slope, and take the lowest path right. Push the Chomp Rock down the slope and 
  follow it to arrive in a cave with a winged cloud, which contains five stars.

10 Stars
  Pass through the middle ring, which is just before the area in the cave where 
  the Paranipper Plants first appear.

1 Star
  Passing through the middle ring will transform a Shy Guy on a blue mushroom 
  on the left into a star.

6 Stars
  Three Baron Von Zeppelins are holding a crate just right of the third flower. 
  Shoot the Baron Von Zeppelins to make them drop the crate, and then pound on 
  it to receive six stars.

Key
  A single Baron Von Zeppelin is holding a key just right of the third flower. 
  Shoot the Baron Von Zeppelin to make him drop the key. The key can be used to 
  open the doors of the locked hut, which is found on the path above the second 
  flower.

Red Switch
  After the fluffy ceiling near the end of the cave, there are three posts. Hit 
  the first post twice to find a winged cloud, and then shoot the winged cloud 
  to reveal a red switch. After jumping on the red switch, you can go down into 
  a secret area shown by the red arrow on the right.

===============================================================================
                        Level 1-4: Burt The Bashful's Fort
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Run right at the start of the level and hit the first egg block to transform it 
into an egg. Hit the remaining five egg blocks on the right, and shoot eggs at 
all three buckets along the way to collect some coins. After the sixth egg 
block, jump over the rotating spikes and continue right to the small spring 
ball. Use the spring ball to bounce up to the ledge on the right, and then run 
right to the edge. Drop off the edge and face left. Shoot both Burts to receive 
some stars, and collect the first flower on the left.

                                   - Flower 2 -

Go right after collecting the first flower and jump onto the platform. When the 
platform goes to the top, jump off at the right side and run along to the 
paddles. After dropping down through the paddles, quickly run left to avoid a 
falling wall and jump up to the ledge to collect the second flower.

                                   - Flower 3 -

Run right to avoid the falling wall again, and use the small spring ball to 
bounce to the ledge high up on the right. Run right and drop off the edge, and 
then shoot the two Burts on the left after landing to collect some more stars. 
Hit the egg block for eggs, and run over to the lava on the right. There are 
two slow horizontally moving platforms over this first section of lava. Jump on 
the first one, hover jump over to the second one, and collect the three red 
coins at the far right side of the lava before landing on the platform with the 
falling wall.

Quickly run right and jump the gap between platforms, collecting the three red 
coins along the way. Hover jump over the next gap on the right and collect the 
coin on the right for the final red coin in the area. On the other side of the 
gap, pass through the middle ring to receive 10 stars, and then go down the 
pipe.

After landing, run right and shoot the winged cloud after the rotating spikes 
to receive five stars. Continue right to find an egg block near a lava pit, 
with another winged cloud on the right. Get some eggs by hitting the egg block, 
and then shoot an egg at the nearby winged cloud to reveal a bridge across the 
lava. Jump on the bridge and run along it to collect three red coins. At the 
end of the bridge, jump up to the wall on the right, and then jump onto the 
see-saw platform. Go to the far right side of the platform to collect the third 
flower, and then jump quickly back to the middle of the platform.

                                   - Flower 4 -

After collecting the third flower, the platform should be tilting up to the 
left. Run up it and hover jump up at the far left side to collect two red coins 
and land on a small platform with the fourth flower.

                                   - Flower 5 -

From the small platform where the fourth flower was found, hover jump over to 
the right and land on the next platform. Jump onto the rotating platform and 
follow it around to collect two red coins, and then jump off at the right side 
to land near a Shy Guy pipe. You can go down this pipe to collect many coins, 
but there are no important items down there. Jump over the pipe and continue 
right past the locked door to arrive at a lava pit.

There are four platforms going over the lava. Jump onto the first platform, and 
then jump quickly back to the left. Shoot the Gargantua Blargg that emerges, 
and then jump across the platforms over the lava, collecting all six of the red 
coins along the way. On the other side of the lava, run right and shoot eggs at 
the flowerpot until it falls off the ledge and smashes on the floor. When it 
does, collect the key that's revealed, and run back to the left. Shoot an egg 
at the eagerly awaiting Gargantua Blargg, and then jump back across the 
platforms above the lava to arrive at the locked door. Press up to go through 
the door.

On the other side of the door, hit the egg block on the left until Yoshi has 
six eggs. Run right under the Burt, and then go through the first door in the 
area to arrive in a room with four Pirahna Plants. Shoot all four Pirahna 
Plants to make a flower appear. Jump up or shoot an egg to collect the fifth 
flower, and then exit the room.

Go right and jump through the middle ring to collect 10 stars. Shoot an egg at 
the nearby winged cloud near the red doors for five more stars. Walk right to 
the red doors, and go through them to enter the first boss fight of the game.

                      - Boss Fight 1: Burt the Bashful -

An easy first boss. Burt the Bashful is a larger version of the Burts seen 
earlier in the level. His only weapon are his large bounces which he uses in an 
attempt to land on you, but these are simple to avoid. There are two gaps at 
either side of the area which can be used for when he gets too close. If you 
press down in either gap, then he can't even reach you. Shoot six eggs at Burt 
the Bashful to defeat him.

~~ Items ~~

Flower 1
  In the first area, just left of the first two Burts in the level.

Flower 2
  In the first area, above the ledge on the left after dropping through the 
  paddles.

Flower 3
  In the second area, at the right side of the see-saw platform.

Flower 4
  In the second area, on a small platform above the left side of the see-saw 
  platform.

Flower 5
  In the third area, go through the first door after the Burt and shoot all 
  four Pirahna Plants to make the fifth flower appear.

3 Red Coins
  In the first area, at the far right side of the first lava pit.

3 Red Coins
  In the first area, at the far left side of the second lava pit.

1 Red Coin
  In the first area, the coin nearest the middle ring.

3 Red Coins
  In the second area, fire an egg at the second winged cloud, and a bridge will 
  form over the lava. There are eight coins on the bridge. The first, second 
  and eighth coins are red.

2 Red Coins
  In the second area, above the left side of the see-saw platform.

2 Red Coins
  In the second area, on the purple rotating platform shortly after the see-saw 
  platform.

6 Red Coins
  In the second area, there are six red coins above the lava pit at the right 
  side of the door with the keyhole.

5 Stars
  In the second area, shoot an egg at the first winged cloud.

10 Stars
  At the end of the first area, go through the middle ring.

10 Stars
  At the end of the third area, go through the middle ring.

5 Stars
  At the end of the third area, shoot an egg at the winged cloud.

Key
  At the far right side of the second area, in a flowerpot. Shoot the flowerpot 
  until it falls off the ledge and reveals the key.

===============================================================================
                        Level 1-5: Hop! Hop! Donut Lifts
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Go left from the start of the level and run down the hill to the blue rock. 
Jump onto the rotating platform and follow it around to collect two red coins. 
Jump over to the vertically moving platform on the left and wait until it goes 
down to collect the first flower.

                                   - Flower 2 -

Jump over to the next rotating platform on the left and follow it around to 
collect two more red coins. Jump off to the blue rock at the top-left corner 
and walk left to come to a manual rotating platform on a wire. To operate this 
platform, jump onto the left platform to start it rotating. When it starts to 
slow down, jump onto the next platform on the left. Repeat this process to keep 
the platform moving. Near the end of the wire, collect the two red coins under 
the platform, and then go all the way to the end of the wire to collect the 
second flower.

                                   - Flower 3 -

At the end of the wire, jump up to the platform above and eat the Fly Guy 
carrying the red coin. Collect the coin, and continue left over the hill to the 
blue rock. Jump onto the donut lifts and cross quickly to the other side, 
eating the Crazee Dayzee along the way. On the blue rock at the other side, 
face right and shoot an egg at the winged cloud to receive five stars. Run 
quickly back onto the donut lifts to collect the stars, and then jump up to the  
next blue rock on the left. Hit the expansion block, and use it to jump up to 
the donut lifts above. Jump from the donut lifts to collect the third flower.

                                   - Flower 4 -

Jump to the horizontally moving platform on the left, and then jump to the 
vertically moving platform above. Jump to the platform at the side of the blue 
rock on the left, jump again to land on a higher platform near an expansion 
block, and then jump up to the two donut lifts on the left to land near the 
middle ring on the blue rock. Go through the middle ring, and then jump up to 
the platform above to find yourself near a manual rotating platform with five 
red coins avove it. Jump on the platform and move it right to collect the five 
red coins and the fourth flower at the end of the wire.

                                   - Flower 5 -

Jump up after collecting the fourth flower to land on a platform, and then jump 
across to the blue rock on the right. Five coins in a '+' formation are above. 
Collect the middle red coin, and then jump up to the highest of the two 
platforms on the left. Quickly shoot the Fly Guy that appears holding the 
cloud, and collect the five stars that fall. Jump to the blue rock on the 
right, and eat the nearby Mufti Guy before jumping up to the vertically moving 
platform above.

Follow the platform up to the top, and collect the middle red coin of the five 
coins on the left. Jump to the blue rock on the right and shoot the winged 
cloud above for five stars. Continue right over the grassy hill, and eat the 
Fly Guy carrying the red coin. Collect the red coin and then jump over to the 
donut lifts. From the first set of three donut lifts, shoot an egg up to 
collect the fifth flower in the fluff up on the right.

Jump onto the set of five donut lifts and wait for each one to drop so that you 
can collect the red coins below. After collecting all five coins, jump over to 
the striped path on the right and run along to the goal ring. Don't jump 
through it yet. Wait until the level finishes scrolling, and then jump up at 
the right side of the goal ring to reveal a hidden winged cloud. Shoot the 
winged cloud for five stars, and then jump through the goal ring to complete 
the level.

~~ Items ~~

Flower 1
  On the first vertically moving platform, left of the first rotating platform.

Flower 2
  Ride the first manually rotating platform to the far left side of the wire.

Flower 3
  Hit the first expansion block in the level, and use it to jump up to the 
  donut lifts above. The third flower is above this set of donut lifts.

Flower 4
  Ride the second manually rotating platform to the far right side of the wire.

Flower 5
  In the fluff above the set of four donut lifts near the end of the level.

2 Red Coins
  On the first rotating platform.

2 Red Coins
  On the second rotating platform, left of the first vertically moving 
  platform.

2 Red Coins
  Ride the first manual rotating platform over to the left side of the wire.

1 Red Coin
  A Fly Guy is holding this, on the platform above the second flower.

5 Red Coins
  When the level starts scrolling right, use the second manually rotating 
  platform to collect the five red coins above.

1 Red Coin
  Shortly after the fourth flower, there are five coins in a '+' formation. 
  Collect the middle coin.

1 Red Coin
  Above and slightly to the left of the first Mufti Guy in the level, there are 
  five coins in a '+' formation. Collect the middle coin.

1 Red Coin
  Shortly before the fifth flower, a Fly Guy is holding this red coin.

5 Red Coins
  Below the final set of five donut lifts in the level, near the fifth flower.

5 Stars
  Hit the first winged cloud in the level to receive these stars.

10 Stars
  Go through the middle ring.

5 Stars
  A Fly Guy holding a cloud appears just left of the first Mufti Guy in the 
  level. Shoot an egg at the Fly Guy to receive five stars.

5 Stars
  Hit the winged cloud above the blue rock just right of the second '+' 
  formation of five coins.

5 Stars
  Hit the hidden winged cloud on the right side of the goal ring.

===============================================================================
                          Level 1-6: Shy-Guys On Stilts
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Run right from the start of the level and jump on the first Shy Guy on Stilts 
to turn him into a normal Shy Guy. Eat him, and then repeat the process on the 
other two Shy Guys on Stilts further on the right. Jump up to the platform with 
the spring ball, and use the spring ball to bounce all the way up to the top of 
the high blue rock on the right.

Walk right to activate a winged cloud which contains a 1UP. Shoot the winged 
cloud, then drop down to the platform below and go through the doors. On the 
other side of the doors, collect all three eggs. Shoot the yellow egg at a Shy 
Guy for a normal coin, the red egg for a two stars, and the flashing egg for a 
red coin. Go through the doors. After arriving back in the main area, drop off 
the right side of the platform and go down the pipe.

In the cave, jump on the two Shy Guys on Stilts and use the small spring ball 
over on the right to bounce up to the ledge on the left. Go left and eat 
Lantern Ghosts until Yoshi has six eggs, and then look up at the Baron Von 
Zeppelin holding the large spring ball.

Wait until the Baron Von Zeppelin starts floating back to the left after 
hitting the platform with the small spring ball on it, and then shoot an egg so 
that it drops the large spring ball. Using the large spring ball, do a small 
jump up to the platform on the right, and then use the small spring ball to 
bounce up to the next ledge on the right. Drop off the right side of the ledge 
to collect the first flower.

                                   - Flower 2 -

Run back to the left and use the large spring ball to bounce up to the high 
path on the right, collecting the three red coins along the way. After landing 
on the path, run down the slope on the right and jump over the two Shy Guys on 
Stilts along the way. At the right side of the path, eat both Lantern Ghosts 
and jump onto the yellow platform to exit the first cave section.

After exiting the cave, follow the platform up to the top of the track and 
collect the three red coins. Drop down to the path and run along to find three 
Shy Guys on Stilts. Eat them all, and then shoot an egg at the winged cloud to 
receive five stars. Continue right and jump through the middle ring at the top 
of the slope, and then run down the slope at the other side. Jump over the gap 
at the end of the slope and jump/stomp on both Shy Guys on Stilts. Go back to 
the left and stomp the post under the tulip three times, then run right to 
collect a red coin and the second flower.

                                   - Flower 3 - 

Jump up to the yellow ledge above and run back to the left until you get under 
the tulip. Hold A to bring up the egg target, and then press either L or R to 
stop the egg target at the lowest point. When the tulip opens, jump up and 
shoot an egg down into the tulip to receive eight stars. Run right and go up 
the hill to come to a message block, which contains some information on 
switches that open secret entrances.

Jump down off the blue rock to land on the platform below, and then turn left 
to face a Pirahna Plant. Shoot an egg at the Pirahna Plant, and drop down into 
the gap on the left to collect a red coin. Jump back up the platform and drop 
down to the gap at the right side to collect another red coin. Jump up to the 
platform again, and stomp the post twice at either side. Run under the platform 
to collect the third flower.

                                   - Flower 4 -

Jump back up to the platform and shoot an egg at the winged cloud to receive a 
red switch. Jump on the switch, and run right to the red arrow pointing down. 
Press down to enter a secret area. Shoot an egg at the winged cloud to reveal a 
Metamorphosis Bubble. Touch the bubble to transform into the Mole Tank. Go 
right and dig through the fluff to find the two red coins: one is the third 
coin from the start and the other is at the top-right corner of the fluff.

After collecting both coins, dig down and hit the Yoshi Block, which will 
return Yoshi to normal. Go right and enter the doors to exit the secret area 
and return to the main level. Jump from the platform up to the blue rock on the 
right, and jump from the blue rock up to the top of the message block. Hover 
jump off the right side of the message block to collect the fourth flower.

                                   - Flower 5 -

Run down the slope on the right and jump onto the post near the bottom. Stomp 
the post three times, and then continue down the slope to enter another cave 
section. After landing in the cave, walk slightly to the right and eat the Fang 
that flutters toward you. Stomp the Shy Guy on Stilts, and eat the two Lantern 
Ghosts shortly after. Run right up the slope and jump across to the mushroom.

Jump over to the next mushroom, and then jump over to the platform on the wire. 
When the platform goes up high and is about to start falling back down, jump up 
and land on the platform. Eat the Lantern Ghosts coming out of the pipe on the 
left if you need to refill the egg supply, and then go to the edge of the 
platform on the right. Shoot an egg that follows the line of coins to collect 
six red coins and the fifth flower.

Drop down off the right side of the platform, and then fall through the paddles 
on the right to land on the blue mushroom below. Fall down to the mushroom on 
the right, and jump over the Shy Guy on Stilts to land on the next red 
mushroom. Shoot an egg at the winged cloud up to reveal a beanstalk.

Climb up to the highest leaf on the left side of the beanstalk, and eat the 
Fang that flies down. There are four coins above, and the two middle ones are 
red. Shoot an egg at the two red coins, and then jump over to the ledge on the 
right. Bounce on the large spring ball to exit the second cave section.

After exiting the cave section, shoot an egg up at the winged cloud to receive 
five stars. Quickly run right under the goal ring and eat the 1UP balloon 
before it gets carried away by a hidden Fly Guy, and then jump through the goal 
ring to complete the level.

~~ Items ~~

1UP
  In the first area, use the large spring ball to bounce up to the top of the 
  high blue rock. There is a hidden winged cloud here, which contains the 1UP.

1UP
  After exiting the second cave section, quickly run under the goal ring and 
  eat the 1UP balloon for this 1UP.

Flower 1
  In the first cave section, shoot an egg at the Baron Von Zeppelin, and use 
  the large spring ball that is dropped to bounce up to the second platform on 
  the right. Drop through the paddles to collect the flower.

Flower 2
  After passing the middle ring, there is a tulip. Stomp the post below the 
  tulip three times, and then run right along the platform to find the flower.

Flower 3
  In the area after the first cave section, pass under the first message block 
  and drop down to the platform below. Stomp the post at either side of the 
  platform, and run under the platform for the flower.

Flower 4
  In the area after the first cave section, jump on the second message block 
  and shoot an egg up and right to hit the flower.

Flower 5
  In the second cave section, jump on the first platform on the wire and jump 
  straight up at the highest point. Shoot an egg in the direction of the coin 
  line to collect the flower.

1 Red Coin
  In the first area, use the large spring ball to bounce up to the platform 
  with the door on it. Enter the door, and shoot the flashing egg at one of the 
  Shy Guys for this red coin.

3 Red Coins
  In the first cave section, shoot an egg at the Baron Von Zeppelin. Bounce on 
  the large spring and follow the line of coins.

3 Red Coins
  After exiting the first cave section, continue to ride the yellow platform up 
  to the top of the wire to find these red coins.

1 Red Coin
  After passing the middle ring, there is a tulip. Stomp the post below the 
  tulip three times, and then run right along the platform to find the red 
  coin, which is the final coin in the line.

2 Red Coins
  In the area after the first cave section, pass under the first message block 
  and drop down to the platform below. There is a red coin at either side of 
  the platform.

2 Red Coins
  In the area after the first cave section, hit the red switch and press down 
  on the red arrow to enter a cave. Using the the mole tank, dig through the 
  fluff on the right to find two coins.

6 Red Coins
  In the second cave section, jump on the first platform on the wire and jump 
  straight up at the highest point. Shoot an egg in the direction of the coin 
  line to collect six red coins.

2 Red Coins
  These coins can be found above the beanstalk in the second cave section.

5 Stars
  In the area after the first cave section, there is a winged cloud above three 
  Shy Guys on stilts. Shoot an egg at the cloud for these stars.

10 Stars
  Pass through the middle ring before the tulip.

8 Stars
  After passing the middle ring, there is a tulip. Shoot an egg into the tulip 
  for these stars.

5 Stars
  After exiting the second cave section, shoot the winged cloud for the stars.

Mole Tank
  In the area after the first cave section, hit the red switch and press down 
  on the red arrow to enter a cave. Hit the winged cloud for the mole tank.

Red Switch
  In the area after the first cave section, pass under the first message block 
  and drop down to the platform below. Shoot the winged cloud above the 
  platform to reveal a red switch.

===============================================================================
                        Level 1-7: Touch Fuzzy, Get Dizzy
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Run up the slope at the start of the level, and eat the Melon Bug at the top. 
Jump over the gap to land on the grassy platform, and then drop down the other 
side to land at the base of another slope. Push the nearby Melon Bug up the 
slope and over the gap at the top. Jump over the gap to land near another Melon 
Bug on the other side. Push this Melon Bug up the slope on the left, and he'll 
fall down the gap to collect the first flower.

                                   - Flower 2 -

Continue right to come the bottom of a large step. Shoot an egg at the Pirahna 
Plant if it hasn't already been hit by a Melon Bug, and keep moving right to 
reveal a hidden winged cloud. Shoot an egg at this winged cloud to receive five 
stars, and then jump both steps on the right. At the top, push one of the two 
Melon Bugs down the grassy slope on the right to defeat five Tap-Taps. Run down 
the slope and jump up the small step at the bottom to land near a locked hut.

Jump up to the wooden platform with the hut on it, and walk right until you see 
three Tap-Taps on a platform over on the right. Wait until the two red Tap-Taps 
have walked off the edge of the platform, and then jump over the small gap to 
the platform on the right. When the remaining Tap-Tap has walked right, jump up 
to the platform above and go over to the left side. Jump left and hover jump up 
to the platform at the bottom-right corner of the fluff. Go to the left side of 
this small platform, and shoot an egg up and left to collect the second flower.

                                   - Flower 3 -

Collect both flashing eggs, and then jump up to the middle of the platform on 
the left after collecting the second flower. Shoot an egg straight up to hit a 
winged cloud. A key will drop. Collect the key, and then jump up and over the 
fluff on the left to drop back down to the grassy floor. Jump up the small step 
on the right again, and jump back up to the platform with the hut. Press up to 
enter it. In the bonus area, gather more coins than the Bandit before the 30 
seconds are up and you will win a bonus item.

After exiting the bonus level, go right to the end of the platform, and wait 
again for the two Tap-Taps to to walk off to the left. This time, shoot the 
Tap-Taps with both flashing eggs, and two red coins will appear. Collect the 
red coins, and then look up to find a watermelon. Shoot an egg to make it drop, 
and then eat it. You will now have 30 watermelon seed bullets to shoot.

Jump over the small gap to the platform on the right, and when the remaining 
Tap-Tap on the platform above walks left, jump up on the right side of the 
platform. Quickly turn left and fire a seed to shoot the Tap-Tap off the 
platform. Go right and jump on top of the block of fluff.

Stomp it to collect the red coin, and then jump out of the fluff to land on the 
platform down on the right. Shoot an egg/seed up to the block of fluff above to 
collect another red coin. Jump from the platform over to the grass slope on the 
right, and run down it to find the middle ring. Pass through the middle ring, 
and then jump over the high ledge on the right to collect the third flower.

                                   - Flower 4 -

After landing on the grass floor on the other side of the high ledge, the Fuzzy 
section will begin. If you still have the watermelon seeds left over from 
earlier in the level, this would be the best place to use them. Go right and 
jump up the first big step. Collect the three red coins above, and then 
continue right along the path.

Shoot eggs/seeds at the Fuzzys that hover around this section, and then jump 
over the gap to land on a higher section of path. Shoot an egg/seed at the 
Pirahna Plant that emerges soon after you land, and collect the two red coins 
above. Continue right quickly and drop down the two steps before the Fuzzys get 
too close. Hit the egg block at the bottom if you need to refill the egg 
supply. Go right and jump over the ledge to land in a gap where the fourth 
flower is found.

                                   - Flower 5 -

Jump up the two steps on the right, and shoot eggs/seeds at the numerous Fuzzys 
at the top. Jump over the small gap to land on a small section of floor, and 
shoot an egg up at the winged cloud to receive five stars. Go right and drop 
down the two steps to land on a section of floor with lots of coins above. Run 
right until you see the flower above, and shoot an egg/seed up to collect the 
fifth flower.

Run right and jump up the two steps. At the top of the steps, quickly shoot an 
egg/seed at the Fly Guy that appears holding a 1UP. Jump over the big gap on 
the right, and jump on one of the two Mildes to fire the other one off the 
platform. Collect the two red coins above, and jump over the next gap to land 
on the path up on the right. Shoot the winged cloud near the start of the path 
to receive five stars, and then run right to enter the final area of the level.

Go right and jump over the two blocks to land on a bendy platform. You can 
break these platforms by stomping on them, but there's no need to stomp this 
one. Just walk on it to collect the red coin below, and continue right to find 
another bendy platform. Stomp this platform to break it, and then jump through 
the shallow water to collect three red coins. Jump up through the third bendy 
bridge at the right side of the water, and go left to come to a slope. Go to 
the top of the slope, and jump straight up to reveal a small spring ball. Jump 
on the spring ball to enter a secret area.

After arriving in the secret area, jump up to the ledge on the left and 
continue to find a Chomp Rock. Jump on top of the Chomp Rock and walk slowly to 
the right to roll Chomp Rock away from the wall. When there's quite a big gap, 
jump over to the left side of Chomp Rock and push it right to reveal a winged 
cloud. Shoot an egg at the winged cloud and a beanstalk will grow.

Jump up the beanstalk to the top and then jump off at the right side to land on 
a long cloud. Run along the cloud to the right, jumping up to collect all four 
red coins along the way, and shoot an egg at the winged cloud at the end of the 
cloud to receive five stars. Run back to the left and drop down the gap in the 
clouds. Go right after landing, and eat the two Mufti Guys on the way to
the pipe. Go down the pipe to return to the main part of the level.

Go right after landing to come to the fourth bendy bridge in the area. Walk on 
the bridge to collect the final red coin in the level. Continue right and jump 
through the goal ring to complete the level.

~~ Items ~~

1UP
  After passing the Fuzzy section, a Fly Guy appears holding this 1UP just 
  before the two Mildes.

Flower 1
  In a gap between slopes at the start of the level. Roll a Melon Bug down the 
  gap from the right side to collect the flower.

Flower 2
  In the fluff above the hut.

Flower 3
  On the right side of the ledge after the middle ring.

Flower 4
  In the Fuzzy section, this flower is found in the gap after the egg block.

Flower 5
  Near the end of the Fuzzy section, this flower is found above the middle of 
  the long line of coins.

2 Red Coins
  There are two flashing eggs in the fluff near the second flower. You will get 
  one red coin for each flashing egg that you hit an enemy with.

1 Red Coin
  In the lower fluff block shortly after the hut.

1 Red Coin
  In the higher fluff block shortly after the hut.

3 Red Coins
  At the start of the Fuzzy section, these coins are found at the top of the 
  first step.

2 Red Coins
  In the Fuzzy section, these two coins are above the Pirahna Plant.

2 Red Coins
  Above the two Mildes after the Fuzzy section.

1 Red Coin
  Below the first bendy bridge in the second area.

3 Red Coins
  Break the second bridge in the second area, and run through the shallow water 
  to collect these coins.

1 Red Coin
  Below the fourth and final bendy bridge in the second area.

4 Red Coins
  After passing the second bendy bridge in the second area, jump up to the top 
  of the slope and then jump straight up to find a spring ball. Jump on this to 
  enter a secret area. Roll Chomp Rock right to reveal a winged cloud. Shoot 
  the winged cloud and climb the beanstalk. There are four red coins above the 
  long cloud on the right.

5 Stars
  Shortly after the first flower there is a Pirahna Plant. Roll a Melon Bug 
  into the Pirahna Plant and continue right to reveal a winged cloud, which 
  contains these stars.

10 Stars
  Pass through the middle ring, which is just before the third flower.

5 Stars
  In the Fuzzy section, shoot the first winged cloud for these stars.

5 Stars
  Shoot the final winged cloud in the first area to receive these stars.

5 Stars
  After passing the second bendy bridge in the second area, jump up to the top 
  of the slope and then jump straight up to find a spring ball. Jump on this to 
  enter a secret area. Roll Chomp Rock right to reveal a winged cloud. Shoot 
  the winged cloud and climb the beanstalk. Run right along the long cloud and 
  shoot the winged cloud at the right side for these stars. 

Key
  This key is found in the fluff above the second flower. Shoot the winged 
  cloud to receive it.

Watermelon
  At the right side of the fluff there is a platform. This watermelon can be 
  found off the right side of the platform.

===============================================================================
                       Level 1-8: Salvo The Slime's Castle
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Run right at the start of the level and jump onto the sloped platform. Run up 
to the top of the slope, and jump over to the rolling platform. From the 
rolling platform, quickly jump up to collect both red coins and hover jump over 
to the ledge on the right. Walk over to the right side of the ledge and jump 
onto the green rotating platform.

Wait on the platform until it stops rotating, and then jump back over to a 
green platform on the left. Collect both red coins, and then jump back over to 
a green platform on the right. When the platform has moved close enough to the 
rolling platform, jump up to the top of the rolling platform and quickly hover 
jump to collect both red coins above it. Continue hovering right, and land on 
the purple rotating platform.

Move the platform right and jump down to the platform on the other side. 
Continue right to come to another rolling platform. Jump onto the left side of 
the rolling platform and then quickly hover jump up and left to collect the 
three red coins. Jump back onto the rolling platform, but this time hover jump 
up and right to collect three more red coins and land on the small platform 
above. Go to the right side of this platform, and use the thin platforms to 
jump up through the gap. At the top of the gap, run left to collect a red coin, 
and then drop down the wide gap to collect the first flower.

                                   - Flower 2 -

After collecting the first flower, you will land on the rolling platform, so 
quickly run right to avoid falling into the lava. After passing the rolling 
platform, enter the pipe on the right.

After arriving in the second area, you should notice a Spray Fish in the water 
over on the right. Wait for the Spray Fish to stop shooting water, and then 
quickly jump onto the green platform that the ghost is holding. The platform 
will go slowly up and right, and then it will quickly move left and down. When 
it starts to move left and down, hover jump to land on a small ledge at the 
entrance to a tunnel. Go left through the tunnel, and then walk left to collect 
the second flower. 

                                   - Flower 3 -

Go through the pipe on the right to enter the second area again. Run and hover 
jump twice to land on the platform at the top-right corner of the area, 
collecting the third flower on the way.

                                   - Flower 4 -

Go through the tunnel on the right to enter a small secret room. Collect both 
red coins, pass through the middle ring to receive ten stars, and shoot the 
winged cloud for a further five stars. Exit the room by going through the pipe 
on the left. Drop off the platform and hold right to land on a platform below. 
Go through the tunnel on the right. After arriving in the third area, run under 
the message block and hit the green block to switch the green platforms over. 
Continue right and jump onto the log platform near the Bandit to collect the 
fourth flower.

                                   - Flower 5 -

Run back to the left and jump onto the green platform. Jump up to the platform 
up on the left and shoot an egg at the winged cloud to receive five stars. Jump 
over to the small platform on the right, and then jump to the slope up on the 
right. Go about half-way up the slope and jump to the green platform on the 
left. Jump over to the purple rotating platform, and wait for the platform to 
go around about three-quarters of the way before jumping up to the log platform 
above.

Go right along the platform and shoot an egg at the red block to switch the red 
platforms over. Go right and drop down onto the first red platform. Continue 
right and fall down the gap under the second red platform. Run left down the 
slope and drop onto the small log platform at the bottom. Walk right and drop 
onto the green platform below, and then jump over to the log platform on the 
right. Jump over to the red platform on the right and walk right to collect 
three red coins.

Go to the right side of the red platform and jump up to the purple rotating 
platform above. Wait for the platform to go three-quarters of the way around, 
and then jump up to either the right or left log platform above. Jump up to the 
higher log platform, and push the flowerpot right or left so that it crashes 
down to the platform below.

Collect the key that is revealed, and jump back up to the log platform where 
the flowerpot used to be. Run left and jump onto the tiny log platform next to 
the wall, and then jump up through the log platform. Run right and hover jump 
over the big gap to land on a path. Run right along the path to collect the 
fifth flower.

Go left along the path and drop down the small step near the end. Drop off the 
edge of the path to land on a sloped log platform below, and then jump to the 
red platform up on the right. Jump over the small gap to the second red 
platform and run right to collect two red coins and arrive near the locked 
door. Press up to enter the door.

After arriving in the fourth area, walk right and stop under the spinning arrow 
platform. Jump onto the platform when the arrow is pointing up and ride the 
platform up until you see the ledge over on the right. Jump over to the ledge, 
and run right to find the middle ring. Jump through the middle ring, and then 
jump onto the arrow platform on the left when the arrow is pointing straight 
up. Jump to the log platform when the arrow platform gets high enough, and 
press up to enter the red doors.

                      - Boss Fight 2: Salvo the Slime -

Run right and jump up the steps to enter the boss arena. Kamek appears and 
transports a Lemon Drop into a huge monster one named Salvo. A slightly more 
difficult boss fight than the first, Salvo the Slime will bounce around trying 
to push you into the lava at the right side of the area. Shoot one egg at Salvo 
the Slime to make some Lemon Drops appear. Eat the Lemon Drops to refill the 
egg supply, and shoot eight eggs at Salvo the Slime to defeat him.

~~ Items ~~

Flower 1
  Above the third rolling platform in the first area.

Flower 2
  Jump on the Support Ghost's platform in the second area, and jump off to the 
  platform at the top-left corner of the room when the platform quickly moves 
  left. Go left through the tunnel to arrive next to the flower.

Flower 3
  Jump on the Support Ghost's platform in the second area, and jump straight up 
  when the platform moves quickly to the left to collect the flower, which is 
  at the top of the room.

Flower 4
  At the bottom-right corner of the third area, near the Bandit.

Flower 5
  At the top-right corner of the third area, on the log platform above the door 
  with the keyhole.

2 Red Coins
  Above the first rolling platform in the first area.

2 Red Coins
  At the start of the green rotating platform in the first area.

2 Red Coins
  Above the second rolling platform in the first area.

3 Red Coins
  Above the top-left section of the third rolling platform in the first area.

3 Red Coins
  Above the top-right section of the third rolling platform in the first area.

1 Red Coin
  In the first area, jump from the top-right section of the third rolling 
  platform to land on a log platform. Jump up to the top of the gap on the 
  right and go left to find this red coin.

2 Red Coins
  Jump on the Support Ghost's platform in the second area, and jump off at the 
  top-right corner to land on a log platform. Go through the tunnel to arrive 
  in a room with the two red coins.

3 Red Coins
  At the bottom of the third area, above the red platform near the purple 
  rotating platform.

2 Red Coins
  In the third area, at the left side of the door with the keyhole.

5 Stars
  Jump on the Support Ghost's platform in the second area, and jump off at the 
  top-right corner to land on a log platform. Go through the tunnel to arrive 
  in a room with a winged cloud, which contains these stars.

10 Stars
  Jump on the Support Ghost's platform in the second area, and jump off at the 
  top-right corner to land on a log platform. Go through the tunnel and pass 
  through the middle ring to receive 10 stars.

10 Stars
  In the fourth area, pass through the middle ring under the red door.

5 Stars
  At the top-left corner of the third area, near the purple rotating platform, 
  hit the winged cloud for these stars.

Key
  Push the flowerpot off the log platform in the third area to find this key.

===============================================================================
                          Extra 1: Poochy Ain't Stupid
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Walk left at the start of the level and stand under the winged cloud. Eat six 
of the Fangs that fly toward you, and shoot an egg up at the winged cloud to 
receive five stars. Eat one more Fang, and then run right. Jump up the small 
step to land on top of a ledge near some lava. At this point, Poochy will make 
his appearance. Quickly jump on Poochy and face right to make him run in that 
direction. Tap left and right to control Poochy as he runs through the lava, 
and continue right to jump up the big step on the other side.

After landing on the slope, jump off Poochy and shoot the winged cloud for five 
stars. Jump back on Poochy and run into the lava on the right. When you come to 
the platform in the lava with the small gap below, jump from Poochy and land on 
top of the platform. Shoot the winged cloud above the platform for five more 
stars, and then hover jump down from the platform to collect the first flower 
and land back on Poochy.

                                   - Flower 2 -

Continue right through the lava and jump up both steps at the other side. Shoot 
an egg at the winged cloud at the top of the second step for five stars, and 
then drop down into the lava on the right. Go through the lava and jump up both 
steps on the other side. Tap left and right to control Poochy from going too 
fast at the top of the second step. Walk slowly off the right side of the slope 
to drop down into a gap with the second flower.

                                   - Flower 3 -

Wait until the Bullet Bill has passed above, and then quickly jump out the 
right side of the gap. Hover jump from Poochy and hold up to float to the top 
of the platform high up on the right, following the trail of coins along the 
way to collect three red coins. Shoot the winged cloud above the platform to 
receive five stars, and then hover jump off the right side of the platform to 
collect three red coins. After collecting the third red coin on the right side 
of the platform, drop down to collect the third flower and land on Poochy.

                                   - Flower 4 -

After landing back on Poochy, run right through the lava. At the other side of 
the lava, jump up the small step to land at the bottom of a big slope. Run up 
the slope, eating Fangs along the way to refill the egg supply. At the top of 
the slope, shoot an egg at the winged cloud for five stars, and then jump up 
the large step on the right.

Run down the big slope on the right while eating any of the Fangs that get too 
close. There are four Tap-Taps on the way down the slope, which cause no 
problem as long as you have Poochy. At the bottom of the slope, drop into the 
small gap to collect two red coins, and jump out on the other side. Run up the 
small slope, and Poochy will automatically jump to collect the fourth flower at 
the top.

                                   - Flower 5 -

Drop down into the lava section on the right. Run quickly to the right and jump 
from Poochy to collect the three red coins. Quickly land back on Poochy and run 
back to the left before the Ball and Chain gets too close. When the Ball and 
Chain is horizontal, quickly run right to pass under the Ball and Chain. Shoot 
the first winged cloud on the other side of the Ball and Chain to receive five 
stars and then continue right to collect two red coins.

Shoot the second winged cloud for a further five stars, and go right for two 
more red coins. After collecting the second set of two red coins, jump up to 
collect the fifth flower and hover jump over to the platform on the right. Drop 
off the right side of the platform and hover near the lava to collect five red 
coins and land near the goal ring. Jump through the goal ring to complete the 
level.

~~ Items ~~

Flower 1
  After passing the first winged cloud, ride Poochy through the second lava 
  section and jump up to the platform about half-way. Drop down off the right 
  side of the platform to collect the flower.

Flower 2
  Drop down into the fourth lava pit, which is shortly after the third winged 
  cloud, and land on Poochy to collect the flower.

Flower 3
  After passing the second flower, there will be a cannon which shoots Bullet 
  Bills. Jump on the Bullet Bill and hover up to the top of the platform. Drop
