  down off the right side of the platform to collect the flower.

Flower 4
  At the top of the long slope shortly after the third flower, jump up the big 
  step and go down the slope on the other side to arrive at a lava pit. Jump 
  over the lava pit and continue up the small slope on the other side to find 
  the flower at the top.

Flower 5
  After passing the second winged cloud after the Ball and Chain, jump up to 
  collect this flower

6 Red Coins
  After passing the second flower, there will be a cannon which shoots Bullet 
  Bills. Jump on the Bullet Bill and hover up and over the platform, collecting 
  the red coins along the way.

2 Red Coins
  At the top of the slope shortly after the third flower, jump up the big step 
  and go down the slope on the other side to arrive at a lava pit with two red 
  coins in it. Jump on Poochy and ride through the lava to collect the coins.

3 Red Coins
  Near the Ball and Chain shortly after the fourth flower.

2 Red Coins
  Under the first winged cloud after the Ball and Chain.

2 Red Coins
  Under the second winged cloud after the Ball and Chain.

5 Red Coins
  Above the final lava pit in the level.

7 Stars
  Shoot an egg at the winged cloud just left of the starting point.

5 Stars
  After crossing the first lava section with Poochy, shoot an egg at the winged 
  cloud on the other side.

5 Stars
  After passing the first winged cloud, ride Poochy through the second lava 
  section and jump up to the platform about half-way. Shoot the winged cloud 
  above the platform.

5 Stars
  Shoot the third winged cloud in the level, which is above the third lava pit.

5 Stars
  After passing the second flower, there will be a cannon which shoots Bullet 
  Bills. Jump on the Bullet Bill and hover up to the top of the platform. Shoot 
  the winged cloud above the platform.

5 Stars
  Shoot the winged cloud at the top of the slope after the third flower.

5 Stars
  Shoot the second winged cloud after the Ball and Chain.

===============================================================================
                      Level 2-1: Visit Koopa And Para-Koopa
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Go right over the small rock at the start of the level and run up to the top of 
the big rock. Jump over to the block on the right and eat the Koopa. Jump up 
both small steps on the right and shoot the Koopa shell at the next Koopa. Wait 
until the Paratroopa has floated low, and then jump over the gap to land on the 
big rock on the other side. Run right to the edge of the path and drop down to 
the pipe. Go down the pipe.

After arriving in the secret area, jump up to the platform on the right and 
continue right under the message block to encounter a Super Star. Collect the 
first Star to transform into Mario. Run up the curved wall on the right and 
continue over the red blocks to arrive in another area with a Super Star.

Collect the second Star and run up the next curved wall on the right to come to 
another Super Star. Collect the third Star and run along the ceiling until you 
hit the wall and land on the floor. After landing, quickly run left along the 
blocks and down the sloped wall on the other side to collect the first flower.

                                   - Flower 2 -

After landing back on the platform, go up the pipe to return to the main 
section of the level. Jump up to the grass slope up on the left and then hover 
jump over to the block on the right. Jump up the step to the thin block on the 
right and quickly jump up to collect the second flower before the block drops.

                                   - Flower 3 -

After collecting the second flower, hover over to the block on the right. Face 
left and stomp the Koopa on the block below. Walk to the middle of the block 
and face right. Shoot an egg down and right at the winged cloud to receive a 
1UP, and then jump up to the block on the right. Jump over the gap to the next 
block and quickly collect the two red coins above before the block falls.

Jump over to the thin block on the right, and then jump up to the big block on 
the right. Collect the two red coins above the block, and then quickly run to 
the left side of the block as it starts to fall. Run right to collect the two 
red coins when the block gets low enough, and then hover jump over the 
Paratroopa to land on the final block in the area. Jump off the right side of 
the block and go down the pipe.

After arriving in the second area, drop off the platform and run right to find 
Poochy. Hit the egg block to refill the egg supply, and then jump on Poochy. 
Face right to make Poochy run in that direction. After Poochy defeats the seven 
Tap-Taps and passes the third spike gap, he'll jump up and enter a tunnel. When 
Poochy jumps, jump up and right to land on a ledge. Run right and drop down off 
the other side of the ledge to land near a crate. Collect the four red coins 
around the crate and then stomp the crate to receive a key.

Collect the key, then jump back on Poochy and face left. Jump up and left when 
Poochy jumps to land on top of the ledge. Hover jump from the left side of the 
ledge to float over all three pits, and then run all the way back to the pipe 
at the start of the area. Go up the pipe. After emerging from the pipe, run 
right and pass through the middle ring. Go over to the large spring ball and 
use it to bounce up to the third area.

After arriving in the third area, the screen will start to slowly scroll up, 
and blocks will fall from above. Wait for the first block to drop down on the 
right side and jump onto it. Two more blocks will drop. Run left and jump up to 
the far left block. Two more blocks will drop. As soon as the second block 
lands, quickly jump up to the top of it. When the next two blocks have dropped, 
run right and jump to the top of the far right block.

Three blocks will drop. Run left and jump up to the far left block. Three more 
blocks will drop. Jump up to the closest block on the right, and then quickly 
jump onto the far right block to avoid the block above. Don't collect the 
flower just yet. Instead, jump to the grass path on the right and wait for the 
final two blocks to fall. Jump onto the blocks and run left to collect the 
third flower.

                                   - Flower 4 -

Continue left after collecting the fourth flower and jump near the wall to 
reveal a winged cloud. Shoot an egg at the winged cloud to receive five stars. 
Go right to the grass path and jump up the three platforms to the small ledge 
at the top. Drop down off the right side of the ledge and go left onto the thin 
platform, which will start to drop. Face right as the platform drops, and eat 
the four Shy Guys on the way to collect the red coins that they hold.

Go right and use the small spring ball to bounce up to the platform above. Jump 
up to the grass path on the right and run off the right edge of the path to 
land near a pipe. Run right to the post, and then quickly stomp to make the 
Eggo-Dil hide. Jump over the tall post and the short post, and then run to the 
edge of the path and jump over the gap.

On the other side of the gap, quickly run right under the three Baron Von 
Zeppelins and jump the next gap. Jump back to the left side of the gap, and 
then shoot the three Barron Von Zeppelins holding the crate. Stomp the crate to 
receive six stars. Jump over the gap on the right and shoot the Baron Von 
Zeppelins holding the second crate. Stomp this crate for six more stars, and 
then jump over the gap on the right.

After landing on the other side of the gap, go up to the left side of the small 
slope and face right. Shoot the Fly Guy that appears holding the 1UP, and then 
quickly run under the Baron Von Zeppelin and jump the gap at the right side of 
the path. Stomp when you land on the other side of the gap to make the Eggo-Dil 
hide, and then continue right to find some more falling blocks. Quickly run 
right into the gap and jump out the other side to collect the fourth flower.

                                   - Flower 5 -

As soon as you collect the fourth flower, run back to the left through the gap 
to avoid the blocks dropping above. Back on the left side of the gap, face 
right and jump up the blocks to the small ledge at the top. Drop down off the 
right side of the ledge and continue right. Jump over the gap to land on the 
other side, where two blocks will be falling. Quickly jump onto the first 
block, then the second block, then jump up to the ledge on the right. Run right 
to reveal a winged cloud and collect the fifth flower.

Shoot an egg at the winged cloud to receive five stars, and then drop down 
through the paddles on the right. Run up the slope on the right and drop down 
to the blocks on the other side. Run along the first block and hover jump over 
to the second block, collect the two red coins as you hover. Hover from the 
second block and land on the third block, collecting two more red coins.

The third block will start to drop, but stay on it and wait for the fourth 
block to get lower. When the third block starts to drop quickly, jump up to the 
fourth block and then jump to the fifth block. Hover jump from the fifth to 
collect the two red coins and land on the striped platform. Press up next to 
the hut to enter it and play a bonus game. After exiting the hut, run right and 
jump through the goal ring to complete the level.

~~ Items ~~

  collect the flower.

  Above the fifth of the final set of blocks in the third area.

  Pass through the middle ring, which is just right of the pipe after the 
  second area.

6 Stars
  Shoot the three Baron Von Zeppelins holding the first crate in the third 
  area, and stomp the crate for the stars.

6 Stars
  Shoot the three Baron Von Zeppelins holding the second crate in the third 
  area, and stomp the crate for the stars.

Key
  At the far right side of the second area. Use Poochy to jump over the tall 
  platform, and then stomp the crate to reveal the key.

===============================================================================
                          Level 2-2: The Baseball Boys
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Run right under the message block at the start of the level and hit the right 
side of the egg block to refill the egg supply. If you hit the left side of the 
egg block, the Green Glove on the right will throw an egg at you. Shoot an egg 
up at the arrow cloud above the message block to collect some coins, and then 
continue right. Stomp on the two Green Gloves and the Slugger, and shoot an egg 
at the winged cloud to lower the platform on the right. Jump over the platform 
and land on the other side to collect the first flower.

                                   - Flower 2 -

Continue right and jump over the two Shy Guys on the way up the slope. At the 
top of the slope, hover jump over the Blow Hard to land at the top of another 
slope. Hover jump from the top of the second slope to jump over another Blow 
Hard, and land on the first Milde on the other side. Jump over the other two 
Mildes and go right to come to three platforms.

Jump to the top platform and eat the Shy Guy, and then jump straight up over 
the Needlenose that the Blow Hard shoots. After landing back on the platform, 
shoot an egg at the winged cloud above the Blow Hard for a 1UP, and then 
quickly jump over the Blow Hard and land on the platform on the other side.

Drop down off the right side of the platform and continue right to come to a 
pipe. Eat the Shy Guys coming out of the pipe until Yoshi has six eggs, and 
then jump on top of the pipe and face left. Shoot an egg at the winged cloud to 
create a beanstalk. Climb the beanstalk to the top and jump into the tunnel at 
the left side.

Run left along the tunnel and jump onto the platform when the tunnel curves up. 
Jump over to the path on the right and jump up the four platforms at the right 
side of the Blow Hard. From the fourth platform, jump up to the path on the 
right. Jump up the next four platforms, and then jump to the left path from the 
fourth platform.

Run left up the small curved path, and look up to see two Fly Guys holding red 
coins. Shoot both Fly Guys to collect the red coins and then run right along 
the platform and jump up to the grass path. Go right and drop down the gap with 
the red arrow pointing down to land on a platform near a message block.

Go right along the platform and drop down through the outline blocks to land on 
some steps. Run down the long steps all the way to the bottom, and continue 
right after landing to drop down another gap. After dropping down the second 
gap, shoot an egg up at the arrow cloud to make the Super Star fall down from 
the gap up on the left.

Collect the Super Star to transform into Mario, and then quickly run through 
the paddles on the left to find the second Star. Continue left up the steep 
slope and along the red blocks to find the third Star. Keep going left to find 
the fourth Star just after the red blocks. Run up the steep slope to find the 
fifth Star, and run up the wall to collect the sixth Star.

Shortly after collecting the sixth Star, Mario will be outside. Quickly jump up 
to the platform and run right, jumping up about half-way along the platform to 
collect the seventh star. Jump onto the grass path at the right side of the 
platform and jump into the gap at the right side of the path to collect the 
eighth and final star.

After landing, quickly run right and jump over the blocks to land on some 
spikes. Run along the spikes and jump through the middle ring on the other 
side. Shortly after this, Mario will return to normal and you will be able to 
continue playing as Yoshi. Jump over the small gap on the right and hit the egg 
block to refill the egg supply.

Continue right down the tiny slope and walk near the right edge. A Slugger will 
be walking about on a small platform down on the right. Wait until the Slugger 
is facing right and then shoot an egg at the winged cloud to reveal the second 
flower. Wait for the Slugger to face right again, and shoot an egg at the 
second flower to collect it.

                                   - Flower 3 -

After collecting the second flower, jump up to the platform on the right and 
run along to the gap. Jump over the first gap and hover jump over the second 
gap. Hover over to the horizontally moving red and yellow platform, and then 
stomp the Green Glove on the platform down on the right. Jump up to the red and 
yellow platform on the right, and shoot an egg down and right along the spikes 
to collect the three red coins and a 1UP for hitting the winged cloud. Jump up 
to the ledge on the right, and then jump up to the grass path. Drop down both 
big steps on the right and continue right to enter the second area.

After arriving in the second area, run right and eat the blue watermelon on the 
second tree. Continue right up the steps and shoot ice at the Pirahna Plant and 
the four Shy Guys. Run right and use the large spring ball to bounce up to the 
platform above. Run left along the platform and jump up the big step to land on 
the grass path. Go left along the grass path and enter the hidden tunnel at the 
end to find a middle ring. Pass through the middle ring, and then run back to 
the far right side of the grass path. Jump into the first small hidden tunnel 
up on the right.

Jump from the hidden tunnel to the platform on the right, and walk to the far 
left side of the platform. Jump up and tap right to land in a hidden tunnel 
above. Shoot an egg at the winged cloud to receive five stars, and then jump 
over to the platform on the left. Jump over to the next platform on the left. 
From this platform, jump up and right to land in a hidden tunnel which contains 
a red coin.

Collect the red coin, and then drop back down to the platform on the left. Jump 
over to the grass path and hit the egg block at the left side of the path to 
refill the egg supply. Use the large spring ball to bounce up to the top of the 
high platform on the right. Jump down to the platform on the right, and then 
jump into the hidden tunnel of the next platform on the right to find a winged 
cloud. Shoot an egg at the winged cloud to reveal the third flower.

                                   - Flower 4 -

After collecting the third flower, jump back to the platform on the left and 
then jump up to the platform on the right. From this platform, jump over the 
gap and enter the long hidden tunnel on the right. After entering the hidden 
tunnel, run down the slope on the right.

Stop near the bottom of the slope and quickly fire an egg at the Blow Hard on 
the ceiling. Continue right to come to the first junction in the path. Take the 
high path and eat the Little Mouser on the way up the slope to come to a small 
area with three coins. Shoot an egg at the Pirahna Plant, then jump over the 
small gap on the right and collect the middle red coin.

Run back to the left, jump over the gap and go down the slope to come to the 
junction again. The Blow Hard have reappeared, so quickly drop off the 
platform, turn right and take the low path. Walk down the path until you get 
near the edge. Slowly walk off the edge of the path and hold left to avoid the 
Pirahna Plant.

After landing, eat the Little Mouser that runs up the slope and then go down 
the slope to come to another junction. Go left at the junction and eat the 
Little Mouser that rushes toward you. Fire an egg at the Pirahna Plant, jump up 
to eat the blue watermelon near the ceiling, and go left to collect the fourth 
flower.

                                   - Flower 5 -

Go right to the junction and continue right. Shoot ice at the Little Mouser 
that runs toward you, and run under the Pirahna Plant that appears on the 
ceiling. Jump over the small gap and continue right to enter the third area.

After arriving in the third area, run right and enter the hidden tunnel. Shoot 
an egg at the winged cloud to reveal a Metamorphosis Bubble. Touch the bubble 
to transform into a Mole Tank, and then start digging through the fluff on the 
right. Collect the second coin, the fourteenth coin and the eighteenth coin for 
all three red coins, and then dig out of the fluff on the right side to hit the 
Yoshi Block, which will return Yoshi to normal.

Run down the small slope on the right and drop down onto the first of many 
junctions in this area. Go right at the junction and jump the gap further on 
the right. On the other side of the gap, walk close to the Slugger on the 
platform. Wait until the Slugger walks to the right side of the platform, and 
then shoot an egg up and right over the top of him so that it collects the two 
red coins in the room. With both red coins collected, run back to the left and 
jump over the gap to arrive back at the first junction.

Go left at the first junction and jump the gap. Eat the Little Skull Mouser on 
the other side of the gap and continue left to come to a crate. Stomp the crate 
for six stars, and then run right and drop down the gap. After landing on the 
path, face right and eat the Little Mouser that rushes toward you. Go right and 
jump over the gap. Continue right after landing on the other side of the gap to 
come to a small room with three coins. Eat the Little Skull Mouser and then 
collect the middle red coin. Run back to the left and drop down the gap.

After landing on the path at the bottom of the gap, run right and eat the 
Little Skull Mouser. Continue right and hover jump over the Tap-Tap to arrive 
near a winged cloud. Shoot the winged cloud for a 1UP and then run back to the 
left. Jump over the small gap with a Tap-Tap in it and collect the middle red 
coin on the other side. Jump over the second gap with a Tap-Tap in it and 
continue left. When you come to the slope that goes down, jump over to the 
other side of the gap and fire an egg at the Tap-Tap to move him out of the 
way. Collect the middle red coin and eat the blue watermelon, and then go right 
to the gap.

Drop into the gap and run down the slope on the left. Wait at the bottom of the 
slope for the Tap-Tap to appear on the other side of the gap. When he walks 
back to the left, jump over the gap. Run left on the other side of the gap and 
shoot the winged cloud for three stars.

Run back to the right and drop down the gap. Go down the slope and eat the 
Little Mouser that emerges from the hole. Continue right down the slope to 
enter a large circular area. Jump onto the platform in the middle of the long 
circular area and then jump on top of the message block. When the tulip opens, 
bounce an egg off of the ceiling so that it lands in the tulip, which will 
throw out eight stars.

After collecting the stars, drop down off the left side of the platform and run 
right to drop down to a log platform. Drop down off the right side of the log 
platform to land on a grass path. Run over to the far right side of the grass 
path, and shoot an egg down and right to collect the only red coin in this 
room. Run back to the left side of the room and jump up both log platforms. 
From the top log platform, jump up to the right yellow platform.

Jump up the small step and then run along the path on the right. Eat the Little 
Skull Mouser at the top of the first slope under the Pirahna Plant, and 
continue down the slope on the other side to come to a small gap. Drop down the 
small gap to land on a small spring ball. Shoot an egg down and right under the 
blocks to collect the fifth flower.

Bounce on the small spring ball and jump out the right side of the gap. Run up 
the slope on the right and eat the two Little Mousers that come out of the 
holes. Go up to the top of the slope and shoot an egg at the Pirahna Plant. 
Exit the hidden tunnel and continue right to the goal ring. Jump through the 
goal ring to complete this huge level!

~~ Items ~~

1UP
  Shoot the winged cloud above the third Blow Hard in the first area.

1UP
  Above the spikes, just right of the final Green Gloves in the first area. 
  Jump onto the horizontally moving red and yellow platform and shoot an egg 
  right to hit the winged cloud.

1UP
  In the tunnel maze located in the third area, go right at the first junction 
  and drop down the gap. Go left after landing and drop down the next gap. Go 
  right after landing and jump over the Tap-Tap to come to a winged cloud. 
  Shoot the winged cloud for the 1UP.

Flower 1
  On the other side of the platform in the first area. Shoot the winged cloud 
  to lower the platform.

Flower 2
  Shoot the winged cloud above the Slugger after the middle ring in the first 
  area.

Flower 3
  Jump into the top-right hidden tunnel near the start of the second area and 
  shoot the winged cloud to find the flower.

Flower 4
  In the tunnel maze located in the second area, go left at the second junction 
  and jump over the Pirahna Plant to collect the flower on the other side.

Flower 5
  Near the end of the tunnel maze located in the third area, drop down the gap 
  under the Pirahna Plant to land on a small spring ball. Fire an egg down and 
  right for the flower.

2 Red Coins
  Above the first Blow Hard in the first area.

2 Red Coins
  Above the second Blow Hard in the first area.

2 Red Coins
  After climbing up to the top of the beanstalk in the first area, run left and 
  jump up the small platforms to the long platform at the top. Two Fly Guys 
  holding red coins are floating above this platform.

2 Red Coins
  After climbing up to the top of the beanstalk in the first area, run left and 
  jump up the small platforms to the long platform at the top. Jump up to the 
  grass path and drop down the gap on the right. Run down the steps on the 
  right to find the red coins.

3 Red Coins
  In the tunnel maze in the third area, shoot the first winged cloud and touch 
  the Metamorphosis Bubble to transform into a Mole Tank. Dig through the fluff 
  on the right and collect the second, fourteenth and eighteenth coins.

1 Red Coin
  Above the second Green Glove after the middle ring in the first area.

1 Red Coin
  Above the spikes, just right of the final Green Glove in the first area. Jump 
  onto the horizontally moving red and yellow platform and shoot an egg right 
  to collect the red coin.

1 Red Coin
  Jump into the hidden tunnel up and right from the grass path with the second 
  large spring ball in the second area.

1 Red Coin
  In the tunnel maze located in the second area, go up at the first junction 
  and collect the red coin near the Pirahna Plant.

1 Red Coin
  In the tunnel maze in the third area, go right at the first junction and jump 
  over the gap. Shoot an egg above the Slugger to collect the red coin.

1 Red Coin
  In the tunnel maze located in the third area, go right at the first junction 
  and drop down the gap. Continue right after landing to find the red coin 
  after the Little Skull Mouser.

1 Red Coin
  In the tunnel maze located in the third area, go right at the first junction 
  and drop down the gap. Go left after landing and drop down the next gap. Go 
  left after landing and jump over the Tap-Tap in the small gap to come to 
  three coins. The red coin is in the middle.

1 Red Coin
  In the tunnel maze located in the third area, go right at the first junction 
  and drop down the gap. Go left after landing and drop down the next gap. Go 
  left after landing and jump over both Tap-Taps in the small gaps. Jump over 
  the next big gap and shoot the Tap-Tap on the other side. Run left to find 
  the red coin.

1 Red Coin
  Near the end of the tunnel maze located in the third area, drop down the gap 
  in the platforms under the tulip to land on the grass path. Shoot an egg off 
  the spikes to collect this red coin near the Green Glove.

10 Stars
  Pass through the middle ring, which is after the spikes in the first area.

10 Stars
  Pass through the middle ring, which is near the start of the second area. Use 
  the large spring ball to bounce up to the platform above and then run left to 
  find the middle ring.

5 Stars
  Jump into the bottom-right hidden tunnel near the start of the second area 
  and shoot the winged cloud.

3 Stars
  In the tunnel maze located in the third area, go left at the first junction 
  and jump over the gap. Stomp the crate for the stars.

3 Stars
  In the tunnel maze located in the third area, go right at the first junction 
  and drop down the gap. Go left after landing and drop down the next gap. Go 
  left after landing and jump over both Tap-Taps in the small gaps. Go down the 
  slope in the next big gap and jump over the gap at the bottom of the slope. 
  Shoot an egg at the winged cloud on the left for the stars.

8 Stars
  Near the end of the tunnel maze located in the third area, shoot an egg into 
  the tulip to receive these stars.

===============================================================================
                       Level 2-3: What's Gusty Taste Like?
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Run up and over the slope at the start of the level, and eat any of the Gustys 
that fly toward you. Jump up the yellow fluff platforms to the third platform, 
and stomp down through the middle of the platform to reveal a winged cloud. 
Shoot an egg at the winged cloud to reveal a red switch. Stomp on the red 
switch and run right up the slope. Hover jump over the gap and collect as many 
of the coins as you can before landing on the other side.

On the other side of the gap, run down the slope and eat the Shy Guy. Run up 
the small grass slope on the right to come to another slope leading up to the 
left. Walk to the bottom of this slope and jump straight up to collect the 
single red coin above. Continue right to come to a gap with a winged cloud 
floating above it. Shoot the winged cloud to reveal a flower, and then jump 
over the gap to collect the first flower.

                                   - Flower 2 -

On the other side of the gap, run right up the small slope and jump up to the 
ledge at the top. Quickly jump over the gap to the ledge on the right and shoot 
an egg at the Fly Guy holding the 1UP. Face left and shoot an egg up at the 
winged cloud above to receive five stars.

Drop off the right side of the ledge and continue right to come to a gap. Jump 
over the three gaps on the right and run up the big slope after the third gap. 
Jump over the fourth gap at the top of the slope, and then face left. Walk left 
to the top of the slope, and shoot an egg at the winged cloud in the gap to 
reveal the second flower. Shoot another egg into the gap to collect the second 
flower.

                                   - Flower 3 -

Run down the slope on the right and duck under the first low-flying Gusty. 
Continue right to find a Shy Guy. Eat the Shy Guy, and then hold down to duck 
under the second low-flying Gusty. Run up the big slope on the right and drop 
down onto the pipe. Go down the pipe.

After arriving in the second area, face right and eat the Lantern Ghosts coming 
out of the pipe until Yoshi has six eggs. Drop down to the pipe and then jump 
through the middle ring up on the right. Continue right under the message block 
after landing and jump up to the small ledge on the right. Shoot an egg down 
and right so that it bounces through both fluff walls and collects the two red 
coins along the way. Drop down the step on the right and continue right to the 
next big step. Jump up the step and shoot an egg through the wall on the right. 
Go right and jump over the gap.

On the other side of the gap, run right to come to a series of fluff walls. 
Shoot an egg right so that it goes through all of the walls and collects the 
two red coins. Run right through the gaps in the wall, collecting the two eggs 
along the way, and drop down the small step. Walk right and shoot an egg up 
near the top-right corner of the fluff ceiling to receive three stars from a 
hidden winged cloud. Shoot an egg up and right, and then jump up the big step 
on the right.

Go down the small slope on the right, and jump up at the bottom of the slope to 
collect the top-right red coin. After landing, shoot an egg up at the Fly Guy 
to make him drop the red coin. Collect the red coin and continue right. Eat the 
two Mildes on the way along the path and continue right to come to a tunnel 
with three winged clouds and lots of Fangs. Shoot the first winged cloud for 
five stars, the second cloud for a single coin and the third cloud for the 
third flower. Avoiding the Fangs, run right and jump up to the platform to 
collect the third flower.

                                   - Flower 4 -

Drop down off either side of the platform and fall through the paddles below to 
collect a Super Star. As Mario, run left down the slope and defeat the various 
enemies along the way. When you come to the junction in the path, continue left  
arrive in a room with a huge fluff ceiling. Stand on top of the pipe and jump 
over to the platform on the left. Walk over to the left side of the small 
platform and shoot an egg up and left to create some steps in the fluff. Climb 
up the fluff steps to the top, and then jump over the block on the right to 
collect the fourth flower on the other side.

                                   - Flower 5 -

Jump over the high section of the platform on the right and stomp the fluff on 
the other side to land back near the pipe. Eat the Lantern Ghosts coming out of 
the pipe until Yoshi has six eggs, and then walk left. Look up to see a block 
in the middle of the fluff. Fire an egg up in the fluff at the right side of 
the block to receive three stars. Walk left and fire an egg up near the left 
side of the block to reveal a red switch. Stomp on the red switch, jump up the 
big step on the left and press down on the red arrow to enter a secret area.

After arriving in the secret area, hit the three egg blocks on the right and 
collect the eggs. Go left and drop onto the bridge, and then quickly run left 
and jump onto the platform at the left side of the bridge to collect the two 
red coins. Walk over to the right side of the platform and wait for the Nep-
Enut to appear on the right. Shoot an egg at the Nep-Enut and then quickly run 
right over to the next set of platforms.

Jump up to the left platform and hover jump over to the right platform to 
collect the six red coins. Face left and walk over to the left edge of the 
right platform. Shoot an egg at the Nep-Enut, drop down the gap between 
platforms and quickly run right to the next set of coins. Jump up to collect 
the top two red coins, and then quickly run right. Exit the area by going up 
the pipe.

After arriving back in the main section of the level, go right and stomp 
through the fluff to land on the path. Run right and jump over the pipe to land 
on the slope on the other side. Go up the slope and continue right through the 
small tunnel. Eat the Fang on the other side, then drop down the step and eat 
the green watermelon on top of the small tree.

Continue right and jump up to the fluff. Run along the fluff floor and shoot an 
egg up at the winged cloud to receive five stars. Continue right and drop down 
the big fluff step to land back on the path. Jump over the big gap on the right 
and shoot the winged cloud above to reveal a Metamorphosis Bubble.

Touch the bubble to transform into a Mole Tank, and then start digging through 
the fluff on the right. Dig right, down, up, left, down, left and go up the 
small gap to hit the Yoshi Block at the top. After transforming into Yoshi, 
jump up the small gap and go left to collect the key. Jump up to the yellow 
platform above and then jump over to the red bridge on the left.

Run along the red bridge and jump up the two platforms at the end of the path. 
Go up the small slope on the left and wait for the Chomp Rock to roll slowly up 
the slope. Quickly jump on Chomp Rock before it rolls back down the slope and 
jump up to the tiny ledge high up on the left. Jump from the ledge up to the 
platform on the left, and enter the hut to play a bonus game.

After exiting the hut, drop down off the platform and land on the path below. 
Run right past the two Fangs, then turn around and head back to the left. When 
the Chomp Rock starts roll down the slope, run after it and follow it all the 
way down to the room with the huge fluff ceiling. Push the Chomp Rock over the 
pipe and continue pushing it left to reveal a winged cloud near the wall.

Shoot the winged cloud to receive five stars, and then run back to the right. 
Jump over the green pipe, run up the slope and go through the tunnel on the 
right. Drop down the big step on the other side of the tunnel and jump up to 
the fluff on the right. Go right and drop down from the fluff to land on the 
path.

Jump over the gap on the right and shoot the winged cloud to reveal the 
Metamorphosis Bubble for the second time in this level. Touch the bubble to 
transform into the mole tank, and instead of digging through the fluff on the 
right, move left. Move left and go down the pit. Continue moving to come to a 
small secret area with a Baron Von Zeppelin holding a 1UP. Touch the Baron Von 
Zeppelin to collect the 1UP, and then wait to be transformed to Yoshi.

After transforming into Yoshi, jump up the four steps on the right and drop 
down to the path on the other side. Jump over the pipe on the right and 
continue along the platform to drop down to the next section of path. Go right 
and shoot an egg up through the fluff to knock the large spring ball down. Jump 
on the large spring ball and bounce up to the high path on the right.

Run right along the path and drop down into the small gap to land on some 
fluff. Stomp the fluff and then jump over to the left side of the Chomp Rock on 
the left. Hold right to push Chomp Rock down the path, defeating the various 
enemies along the way. When you get to the gap, stop pushing Chomp Rock and 
jump over to the other side. Run down the small slope and jump through the goal 
ring to complete the level.

~~ Items ~~

  area. Touch the bubble and dig left into the gap to come to a room with a 
  Baron Von Zeppelin holding the 1UP.

Flower 5

Red Switch

Red Switch
  After collecting the Super Star in the second area, run left to come to a 
  room with a huge ceiling. Shoot an egg up near the left side of the block in 
  the fluff to reveal the red switch.

===============================================================================
                          Level 2-4: Bigger Boo's Fort
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Go right at the start of the level and jump onto the log platform above the 
lava. Run over to the right side of the log platform to encounter the first Boo 
in the level. Like all Boos in the level, when you face toward them they will 
hide, but if you turn away from them they will float toward you. Run under the 
Boo and drop down into the gap to land on the red switch. Quickly jump out of 
the gap and run over the red blocks on the right. Run under the first gap with 
the Big Boo and jump up into the second gap to collect the first flower.

                                   - Flower 2 -

After landing back on the red blocks, continue right to come to a slightly 
curved log platform above some lava. Jump over the small gap to the second 
platform and collect the two red coins along the way, and then face left so 
that the Big Boo floats toward you. When the Big Boo gets close, face right and 
hover jump over him to collect the two red coins and land on the next log 
platform. Continue right and go through the blue doors.

After arriving in the second area, run right and enter the blue doors near the 
paddles. There are two Big Boos inside this room. Face away from them so that 
they float toward you, and then shoot an egg so that it bounces off the wall 
and hits the Big Boo. Defeat both Big Boos to make a flower appear at the left 
side of the room. Jump up to the platform and collect the second flower, and 
then go through the blue doors to exit the room.

                                   - Flower 3 -

After returning to the second area, walk left and then face right. Shoot an egg 
up and right at the diagonal line of three red coins to collect them. Face left 
and shoot an egg at the winged cloud to create some steps. Jump onto the steps 
and climb them up to the top. Jump onto the path at the top of the steps and 
continue right to come to a winged cloud. Shoot the winged cloud to receive 
five stars, and then drop down the gap on the right to land on a log platform 
near a red switch.

Jump up to the platform on the right and land on the red switch to make the red 
blocks appear. Drop down off the platform to the left and then run right onto 
the red blocks above the lava. Shoot an egg so that it follows the coin trail 
and hits the winged cloud to reveal a key. Collect the key and run quickly to 
the left. Eat the five Boo Guys as you run left and run through the paddles at 
the end of the tunnel to land near a blue door. Go left and jump up to the 
bottom of the steps.

Jump left from the steps to land on the path above. Go left to collect three 
eggs, and then jump onto the sloped log platform on the right. Jump up to the 
log platform above, and then jump over to the yellow platform on the left. Stay 
on the middle of the platform as it moves along the platform to collect both 
red coins. After collecting the second red coin, jump over to the platform on 
the left and open the door with the keyhole.

After arriving in the third area, face toward the wall on the right and fire 
eggs to defeat both Boos floating toward you. With the Boos defeated, walk left 
and fire an egg to collect the two red coins above the blue doors. Continue 
left and jump onto the log platform near the wall. Jump up to the platform 
above and then jump up to the sloped platform.

Jump right from the platform to collect the two red coins and land on the big 
sloped platform. Jump over to the small sloped platform on the right and then 
jump up to the log platform next to the wall. Jump up to the small log platform 
above, and jump left to collect the third flower. Jump left along the platforms 
and go down the pipe at the left side of the area.

                                   - Flower 4 -

After returning to the second area, push the crate off the ledge to the right 
and drop down to the path below. Stomp the crate to receive six stars. Run 
through the three eggs on the right to come to a winged cloud. Don't shoot the 
winged cloud, as this will create steps which block the entrance to the middle 
ring. Instead, jump up the two log platforms above and then jump over to the 
yellow platform on the left. Ride the platform up and over the wire to the 
other side to land at the start of a tunnel. Go right to pass through the 
middle ring. Run right to the second small dip in the path and jump up to 
collect the fourth flower.

                                   - Flower 5 -

Continue right after collecting the fourth flower and drop down the small step 
to land near some Boo Blahs. The Boo Blahs will grow large, and will then 
return to normal size. Wait for the Boo Blah on the floor to return to normal 
and then jump over him and continue right to come to a red switch.

Drop into the gap to land on the red switch, and quickly jump out of the right 
side of the gap. Run right along the red blocks while avoiding the two Boo 
Blahs on the ceiling. Jump up to the path at the right side of the red blocks 
and continue right. Jump over the Boo Blah on the floor, run under the Boo Blah 
on the ceiling and go through the pipe on the right.

After arriving in the fourth area, jump on top of the pipe on the left and jump 
up to the block on the left to reveal a winged cloud. Shoot the winged cloud 
for a 1UP and then run right to come to a vertically moving block. Walk onto 
the moving block and look at the rotating flame down on the right. When the 
flame is pointing up, go right and jump over it.

Quickly run onto the second vertically moving block and hover jump over the 
second rotating flame when it is pointing diagonally up and right. Run right 
after passing the second flame and jump over the step to land on the log in the 
lava on the other side. Walk over to the right side of the log and it will 
start floating across the lava. Jump up to the path at the other side of the 
lava and go through the pipe on the right.

After arriving in the fifth area, jump up to the first platform on the right 
and face right so that the Boo hides. Hover jump over the Boo to collect the 
two red coins on the other side. After landing back on the path, continue right 
under the first Big Boo and jump up under the second Big Boo to collect the two 
red coins.

Continue right and jump onto the platform on the other side of the third Big 
Boo. Face left and jump up to the platform above. Shoot an egg straight up at 
the cracked block above to create a gap. Jump up through the gap and run left 
to drop down next to some blue doors. Go through the doors.

After arriving in the secret area, go left and shoot a Boo Balloon three times 
to receive a red switch. Quickly run left and jump up the red blocks to collect 
the fifth flower at the top-left corner of the area. Drop down off the right 
side of the red blocks. Eat the Boo Guys coming out of the pipe to refill the 
egg supply, and then run right and go through the blue doors.

After returning to the fifth area, run through the paddles and continue running 
right under the three big boos to arrive near some blue doors at the far right 
side of the area. Go through the blue doors.

After arriving in the sixth area, pass through the middle ring and then jump 
onto the middle of the first rotating platform up on the right. Run over to the 
right side of the platform and jump up to the log platform on the right. Jump 
to the second rotating platform and run across to the log platform on the left. 
Jump to the log platform and then jump up to the final rotating platform in the 
area. Run across to the right side and jump up to the log platform near the red 
doors. Enter the red doors.

                         - Boss Fight 3: Bigger Boo -

Run right at the start of the area and Kamek will transform a ordinary Big Boo 
into Bigger Boo. Hit Bigger Boo by looking away from him and then firing an egg 
so that it hits him as he floats toward you. After every successful hit with an 
egg, he will grow even bigger. Eat the Fangs that fly about and shoot five eggs 
at Bigger Boo to defeat him.

~~ Items ~~

1UP
  At the start of the fourth area, jump up to the pipe on the left and then 
  jump up to the block to reveal a winged cloud. Shoot the winged cloud for 
  this 1UP.

Flower 1
  In the second gap after the first Big Boo near the start of the level.

Flower 2
  Enter the blue doors near the start of the second area and defeat both Big 
  Boos to reveal the flower.

Flower 3
  At the top-right corner of the third area.

Flower 4
  Found just after the middle ring.

Flower 5
  In the fifth area, jump up to the platform just after the third Big Boo and 
  shoot an egg at the cracked block. Jump up through the gap and run left to 
  drop down near some doors. Go through the doors and run left to find the 
  flower at the top-left corner of the secret area.

4 Red Coins
  Just left of the second Big Boo near the end of the first area.

3 Red Coins
  Going up in a diagonal line just right of the first winged cloud in the 
  second area.

2 Red Coins
  Above the door with the keyhole in the second area. Ride the yellow platform 
  to collect the coins.

2 Red Coins
  Above the blue doors at the start of the third area.

2 Red Coins
  On a sloped platform at the left side of the third area.

3 Red Coins
  Near the top-left corner of the third area.

2 Red Coins
  In the fifth area, these red coins are found just after the first platform.

2 Red Coins
  In the fifth area, these red coins are found above the platform just before 
  the second Big Boo.

5 Stars
  Shoot the winged cloud after the Gustys in the second area.

6 Stars
  After exiting the third area, stomp on the crate for the stars.

10 Stars
  Pass through the first middle ring which can be found by riding the yellow 
  platform after exiting from the third area.

10 Stars
  Pass through the second middle ring at the start of the sixth area.

Key
  Jump on the red switch under the Boo Blahs in the second area, drop down to 
  the red blocks above the lava and shoot the winged cloud.

Red Switch
  In the gap below the five coins near the start of the level.

Red Switch
  Under the Boo Blahs in the second area.

Red Switch
  After passing the middle ring, run right and drop into the gap after the two 
  Boo Blahs to find this red switch.

Red Switch
  In the fifth area, jump up to the platform just after the third Big Boo and 
  shoot an egg at the cracked block. Jump up through the gap and run left to 
  drop down near some doors. Go through the doors and shoot a Balloon Boo three 
  times to find this red switch.

===============================================================================
                         Level 2-5: Watch Out For Lakitu
===============================================================================

                           - Map of the train section -

                  S T A R T

~~ Legend ~~

C = Coin
F = Flower
M = Metamorphosis Bubble
Y = Yoshi Block

                                   - Flower 1 -

Jump up the small step at the start of the level and stomp the post two times 
to collect a red coin. Jump onto the see-saw platform on the right and run over 
to the right side to collect the red coin. Jump over to the fluff and wait for 
the Woozy Guy to bounce up from the lower section of fluff on the right. Eat 
the Woozy Guy and then drop down to the fluff on the right.

Eat the eggs coming out of the Egg Plant until Yoshi has six eggs. Jump up the 
two steps in the fluff on the right and jump over to the see-saw platform. 
Quickly jump off to the right side of the platform to land on the block of 
fluff. At this point, Lakitu will appear.

Jump to the next see-saw platform and then jump to the small fluff path on the 
right. Eat the Shy Guy on the path and continue moving right before Lakitu 
starts throwing enemies at you. Jump to the next see-saw platform and run over 
to the right side to collect a single red coin. Jump over the fluff wall on the 
right and land on the fluff path on the other side.

Eat the Woozy Guy that bounces toward you and then run down the two small 
steps. Eat the Shy Guy at the bottom of the steps and then shoot of Lakitu. 
With Lakitu gone, shoot an egg at the Fly Guy to make him drop the coin, and 
shoot an egg at the winged cloud to reveal the first flower. Collect the red 
coin and shoot an egg up at the first flower to collect it.

                                   - Flower 2 -

Continue right and jump over the red shell on the fluff wall. On the other side 
of the red shell, shoot another egg up at Lakitu if he's appeared, and then eat 
the green shell. Wait for the tulip to open, and then shoot the green shell 
into the tulip to make it throw out eight stars. Collect the stars and continue 
right. Jump over the small wall at the end of the fluff path and land on the 
see-saw platform on the other side. Run to the right side of the see-saw 
platform and jump onto the small platform outside of the tunnel on the right.

Go right to enter the tunnel and jump up to eat the red shell on the ledge. 
Drop back down to the left and shoot the red shell out of the tunnel. Shoot an 
egg up the first gap in the tunnel to reveal a winged cloud. Shoot the winged 
cloud for five stars and then jump up to the ledge on the right. Drop down the 
other side and eat the Shy Guy. Shoot an egg straight up into the gap after 
landing to reveal another winged cloud. Shoot this winged cloud to receive a 
red switch, and then stomp the red switch to make the red blocks appear over on 
the right.

Quickly jump up to the ledge on the right and knock the green shell right. Drop 
down onto the fluff and follow the green shell right as it hits into the Shy 
Guy. Jump up the small step in the fluff and jump over the green shell before 
the step down. Drop down the step and continue right to come to some tiny fluff 
platforms leading over a crate. Eat the Woozy Guy and then jump up to the 
highest fluff platform. Stomp down through the fluff and land on the crate to 
receive a key. Quickly collect the key and jump out of the left side of the gap 
to land back on the fluff.

Continue left back to the winged cloud near the exit of the tunnel. Shoot an 
egg at the winged cloud to receive five stars, and then walk right. Eat the 
eggs coming out of the Egg Plant until Yoshi has six eggs, and then shoot an 
egg up at the red coin at the left side of the egg plant. Go right and jump up 
the small step. Shoot an egg up at the winged cloud for five stars.

Shoot an egg up at the red coin just left of the green shell, and then run 
right to the tiny fluff platforms. Jump up and over the platforms and eat the 
Woozy Guy that bounces up from the other side. On the other side of the tiny 
fluff platform, collect the second and sixth red coins in the line and then 
shoot an egg through the fluff steps to collect the second flower.

                                   - Flower 3 -

Jump over the gap in the steps and climb up to the top. Pick up the green shell 
at the top and walk over to the right side of the top step. Jump straight up 
and shoot the green shell at the winged cloud to receive five stars. Run down 
the steps to come to a Pokey throwing a Needlenose. Collect the red coin at the 
left side of Pokey and then eat the Needlenose to defeat the Pokey. Jump over 
to the other side of the Pokey and eat the Woozy Guy. Walk right and open the 
blue doors with the key.

In this train area, there is a large train track which leads to the flower. 
I've created a map, found at the top of this level walkthrough, which lists the 
locations of the Metamorphosis Bubbles as well as the coins. Read the next 
paragraph for the text walkthrough to this area:

Hit the first Metamorphosis Bubble to transform into a train and follow these 
directions to the flower and the Yoshi Block: 2nd Right, Up, 2nd Right, Up, 
Right, 2nd Up, Right (to collect the third flower), Down, Right, Up, Right, 2nd 
Down (to land on the path near the Yoshi Block). Go left after landing on the 
grass path to hit the Yoshi Block. Walk left and go through the blue doors.

                                   - Flower 4 -

After returning to the first area, jump up to the platform above. Jump up to 
the grass path on the left and run left. Drop down the two platforms at the 
edge of the grass path and drop out of the tunnel to land near a Chomp Rock. 
Push the Chomp Rock slowly to the right until it is under the tunnel leading 
up. Jump onto the Chomp Rock and then jump up to the ledge on the right. Go 
through the blue doors.

After arriving in the second area, run right and pass through the middle ring. 
Shoot an egg at the winged cloud near the post on the right and collect the 
five stars. Jump up and collect the red coin above the post. On the other side 
of the post, jump over the Crazee Dayzee and then quickly shoot an egg up at 
the second Fly Guy on the right holding the red coin before he flies away.

Walk back to the left and shoot the remaining Fly Guy to receive another red 
coin. Jump up to collect the red coin above the red side of the yellow flowers, 
and then jump up to the ledge on the right. Eat the Shy Guys coming out of the 
pipe until Yoshi has six eggs, and then drop down to the grass path on the 
right. Eat the Crazee Dayzee and continue right to come to a small spring ball.

Around this point in the level, Lakitu will reappear. Bounce on the spring ball 
and Eat the Fly Guy that flies down holding the red coin. Collect the red coin 
and then jump on the spring ball. Bounce up to land on Lakitu so that he leaves 
his cloud, and then jump up to land on the cloud. On the cloud, fly left under 
the three blocks of fluff and then fly up and left to land on a high ledge 
above the entrance to this area.

Run left on the ledge to reveal a winged cloud. Shoot the winged cloud to 
receive five stars, and then walk right off the edge of the path to drop onto a 
post. Stomp the post two times and run into the cave on the left to reveal 
another hidden winged cloud. Shoot this winged cloud to find a red switch. Jump 
on the red switch and then jump onto the small post on the right. Jump up to 
the ledge on the left and press down on the red arrow.

After arriving in the secret area, there will be a long drop down to the path. 
On the path, run right along the tunnel to come to a high room with fifteen 
rotating platforms. Jump up all the platforms to the top and then go up the 
pipe to exit the area.

After returning to the second area, run right to the small spring ball and jump 
up to the ledge on the right. Eat Lakitu and then fire an egg over at the 
Bubble Dayzee on the right. Jump over to the small fluff ledge on the right and 
eat the Fly Guy holding the red coin on the other side. Jump straight up and 
tap down. Yoshi will stomp through the fluff but will stop shortly after 
revealing a winged cloud.

Jump over to the path on the right and collect the red coin, then face left and 
shoot an egg at the winged cloud for five stars. Jump over the pipe on the 
right and eat the Bubble Dayzee on the other side. Jump over the gap to the 
ledge on the right and shoot an egg straight up to reveal the flower. Shoot an 
egg up to collect the fourth flower.

                                   - Flower 5 -

Jump over the gap to the path on the right and shoot the winged cloud at the 
left side of the three posts for five stars. Shoot an egg at the Cactus Jack 
and then shoot an egg at Lakitu. Go right and jump onto the posts. Stomp the 
middle post three times to reveal a winged cloud, and stomp the right post 
twice for a red coin. Shoot the winged cloud for a 1UP, then run right and jump 
over the gap. On the other side of the gap, continue right and eat the Bubble 
Dayzee. Shoot an egg up at the first winged cloud to reveal the fifth flower 
and then shoot another egg to collect it.

Continue right and jump onto the first post. Stomp the post twice to collect a 
red coin, and then shoot an egg up at the winged cloud above to receive five 
stars. Jump up to collect the middle red coin at the left side of the Bubble 
Dayzee up on the ledge, and then run right through the small tunnel. On the 
other side of the tunnel, shoot an egg up at the Fly Guy to make him drop the 
red coin. Run right and jump over the purple bush (where a Bandit is hiding) to 
come to the goal ring. Jump through the goal ring to complete the level.

~~ Items ~~

1UP
  Near the end of the second area, a Cactus Jack will be standing on the 
  highest of three posts. Shoot the Cactus Jack off the post and stomp the 
  middle post three times.

Flower 1
  Shoot the winged cloud after the fourth see-saw platform in the first area.

Flower 2
  In the first area, under the fluff steps at the left side of the Pokey near 
  the door with the keyhole.

Flower 3
  In the secret train section of the level.

Flower 4
  Shoot the winged cloud above the Bubble Dazyee standing on the ledge about 
  half-way through the second area.

Flower 5
  Shoot the winged cloud after the Cactus Jack near the end of the second area.

1 Red Coin
  In the first area, stomp the first post twice for the red coin.

1 Red Coin
  At the right side of the first see-saw platform in the first area.

1 Red Coin
  At the right side of the fourth see-saw platform in the first area.

1 Red Coin
  A Fly Guy is holding this red coin shortly after the fourth see-saw platform 
  in the first area.

1 Red Coin
  After exiting the tunnel section about half-way through the first area, go 
  right and shoot an egg up at the left side of the egg plant.

1 Red Coin
  After exiting the tunnel section about half-way through the first area, shoot 
  an egg at the red coin near the right side of the egg plant (just left of the 
  green shell).

2 Red Coins

  Collect the second and the fifth coins.

1 Red Coin
  The fifth coin in the line at the left side of the Pokey near the door with 
  the keyhole.

1 Red Coin
  Above the first post near the start of the second area.

1 Red Coin

  middle coin.

2 Red Coins
  Shortly after the first post in the second area, two Fly Guys appear holding

1 Red Coin
  A Fly Guy appears holding this red coin shortly after the small spring ball 
  in the second area.

1 Red Coin
  A Fly Guy appears holding this red coin at the right side of the tunnel after 
  the spring ball in the second area.

1 Red Coin
  A Fly Guy appears holding this red coin just after the Bubble Dayzee standing

1 Red Coin
  Near the end of the second area, a Cactus Jack will be standing on the

1 Red Coin

1 Red Coin
  Under the right side of the second winged cloud after the Cactus Jack near 
  the end of the second area.

1 Red Coin

8 Stars
  Shoot an egg or a shell into the tulip after the first flower.

5 Stars
  After entering the tunnel section about half-way through the first area, 
  shoot an egg up into the first gap to reveal a winged cloud. Shoot the winged 
  cloud for the stars.

5 Stars
  After exiting the tunnel section about half-way through the first area, shoot 
  an egg at the first winged cloud.

5 Stars
  After exiting the tunnel section about half-way through the first area, shoot 
  an egg at the winged cloud after the egg plant.

5 Stars
  In the first area, above the left side of the Pokey near the door with the 
  keyhole.
