5 Stars
  Shoot the first winged cloud at the start of the second area.

5 Stars
  Shoot the winged cloud above the left side of the Cactus Jack in the second 
  area.

5 Stars
  Shoot the second winged cloud after the Cactus Jack near the end of the 
  second area.

Key
  After entering the tunnel section about half-way through the first area, 
  shoot an egg up into the second gap to reveal a winged cloud. Shoot the 
  winged cloud for the red switch. Jump on the switch and stomp the crate 
  further on in the level to find the key.

Red Switch
  After entering the tunnel section about half-way through the first area, 
  shoot an egg up into the second gap to reveal a winged cloud. Shoot the 
  winged cloud for the red switch.

===============================================================================
                     Level 2-6: The Cave Of The Mystery Maze
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Run right along the grass path at the start of the level and jump onto the two 
yellow egg blocks at the end. Quickly shoot an egg at the Fly Guy that floats 
down to receive five stars, and then drop off either side of the egg blocks. 
Hit both egg blocks and collect the yellow eggs, and then walk over to the far 
left side of the fluff. Stomp through the fluff and hold left to enter the 
first tunnel on the left.

Eat the two Mufti Guys and collect the two red coins above. Run back to the 
fluff on the right and stomp down through the left side of the fluff again. 
Enter the next tunnel on the left. Run left and drop off the slope to land near 
three Mufti Guys below a flower. Eat all three of the Mufti Guys, and then jump 
up to collect the first flower and the two red coins on either side.

                                   - Flower 2 -

Continue along the tunnel and follow it around to the paddles at the end. Pass 
through the paddles and stomp through the fluff on the right. Hold right to 
enter the tunnel. Shoot an egg at the arrow cloud to collect a 1UP, and then 
pass through the gap in the fluff on the right. Stomp through the fluff and use 
the large spring ball to bounce up to the ledge high on the left. Collect the 
three red coins and then shoot an egg at the winged cloud to receive five 
stars. Go through the paddles on the left and stomp down through the fluff on 
the right until you land on the large spring ball.

Drop down to the fluff on the left and stomp all the way down to the room at 
the bottom of the area. Collect the three red coins in the line, shoot an egg 
at the right winged cloud for five stars and then shoot an egg at the left 
winged cloud to receive a key. Jump on the left large spring ball and bounce up 
to the tunnel high up on the right. Eat the two Lantern Ghosts in the tunnel 
and then shoot an egg at the winged cloud to reveal some blue doors. Enter the 
doors.

After arriving in the second area, run right to find some grey blocks. Eat the 
Lantern Ghost and walk onto the middle grey block. Shoot an egg straight up to 
make a large spring ball drop down. Jump on the spring ball and bounce up to 
the second large spring ball high above. Bounce from the second spring ball to 
collect the second flower and land on the yellow platform high above.

                                   - Flower 3 -

From the yellow platform, bounce from the third spring ball and land on the 
ledge up on the left. Drop down off the left side of the ledge and follow the 
coin trail down to land near a hut. Enter the hut to play a bonus game. After 
exiting the hut, drop down to the left and walk right to find an arrow cloud 
above. Shoot an egg at the arrow cloud to collect the third flower.

                                   - Flower 4 -

After collecting the third flower, walk left and drop down the gap to land on a 
small ledge. Eat the Lantern Ghost and then drop off the right side of the 
ledge to land at the start of the area. Run right past the grey blocks and stop 
at the top of the slope just before the Lantern Ghost pipe. Shoot an egg up at 
the left side of the fluff above to reveal some blue doors.

Enter the doors to arrive in a small room with four Lantern Ghosts and a winged 
cloud. Eat all four of the Lantern Ghosts to receive four red coins. This will 
also make the flower appear at the top-right corner of the room. Shoot the 
winged cloud to receive five stars, collect the fifth flower and exit the room.

                                   - Flower 5 -

After returning to the second area, run right and jump over the Lantern Ghost 
pipe. Run to the top of the slope on the other side and then jump left to land 
on a platform. Jump through the middle ring on the left and land on the next 
platform. Jump across the small gap on the left and collect the three red coins 
on the other side.

Run back to the right and return to the top of the slope. Wait for the Ball and 
Chain on the right to become horizontal, then quickly run under it and jump up 
to the yellow platform on the right. Jump over to the large spring ball on the 
left and bounce up to the second yellow platform above.

Jump up the five yellow platforms and go left at the top to collect three red 
coins and reveal a winged cloud. Shoot the winged cloud to receive a 1UP. Go 
back to the right and drop down the five yellow platforms. Drop off the left 
side of the lowest platform to land on a small path near two Lantern Ghosts. 
Eat the Lantern Ghosts and jump over the gap to the next path on the left. 
Continue left along the path. Jump over the Kaboomba about half-way up the 
path, and continue on to the second gap in the path.

Drop down the gap and tap right after landing on the ledge to arrive once again 
at the start of the area. Run right to the three grey blocks and shoot an egg 
straight up from the middle block to reveal the large spring ball. Jump up to 
the third spring ball, but this time, go right at the top.

Walk right and shoot the winged cloud near the start of the path to receive 
five stars. Continue right to the end of the path, and jump over the two 
Kaboombas before entering the blue doors. Go through the middle ring on the 
other side of the blue doors and continue right to enter the third area.

After arriving in the third area, run right and jump over the first gap with 
the vertically moving Gusty in it. Shoot the Cactus Jack that appears over the 
second gap and then jump across the next two gaps to land on the half-way 
platform of the area. Jump over the next two Gusty gaps. Jump the normal gap 
and then jump over the second Cactus Jack in the area. Finally, jump down to 
the platform at the far right side and use the large spring ball to exit the 
area.

After arriving in the fourth area, jump out of the water to land on the grass 
path on the right. Hit the egg block to refill the egg supply, and then run 
right to the top of the slope. Wait for the Spray Fish to stop spraying water, 
and then quickly jump across the number platforms to the far right platform. 
Jump up to the yellow fluff on the right and stomp down. Shoot an egg through 
the remaining fluff and run right to find the flower.

Run left after collecting the fifth flower and drop down to the grass path 
below. Run right along the grass path and jump up the small step near the end. 
Run across the number platforms and jump over the Chomp Rock at the other side. 
Drop down off the right side of the grass path to land on a small grass slope, 
and then jump over the gap. On the other side of the gap, run right and stomp 
near the Eggo-Dil to make it hide. Run right to reveal a winged cloud, and 
shoot it to receive a 1UP. Continue right and jump through the goal ring to 
complete the level.

~~ Items ~~

1UP
  Stomp through the fluff in the first area and enter the second tunnel on the 
  right. Shoot an egg at the arrow cloud for the 1UP.

1UP
  There is a hidden winged cloud behind the Eggo-Dil in the fifth area. Shoot 
  the winged cloud for the 1UP.

Flower 1
  Stomp through the fluff in the first area and enter the second tunnel on the 
  left to find the flower above three Mufti Guys.

Flower 2
  Run onto the grey blocks near the start of the second area and shoot an egg 
  straight up to make a spring ball drop down. Use the spring ball to bounce up 
  to the flower.

Flower 3
  Run onto the grey blocks near the start of the second area and shoot an egg 
  straight up to make a spring ball drop down. Use the spring ball to bounce up 
  to the yellow platform. Jump up to the ledge on the left and shoot an egg at 
  the arrow cloud to collect the flower.

Flower 4
  Run right at the start of the second area and stop at the top of the slope 
  before the Lantern Ghost pipe. Shoot an egg at the fluff above to reveal a 
  door. Go through the door and eat the four Lantern Ghosts in the room to 
  reveal the flower.

Flower 5
  After arriving outside in the fourth area, jump across the number platforms 
  and jump up to the yellow fluff. Stomp through the fluff and run right to 
  find the flower.

5 Stars
  Shoot the Fly Guy above the yellow egg blocks at the start of the first area.

5 Stars
  Stomp through the fluff in the first area and enter the second tunnel on the 
  right. Stomp the fluff and use the spring ball to bounce up to the high ledge 
  on the left. Shoot the winged cloud for the stars.

5 Stars
  Stomp through the fluff in the first area and go all the way through to the 
  room at the bottom with the two winged clouds. Shoot the right winged cloud 
  for the stars.

5 Stars
  Run right at the start of the second area and stop at the top of the slope 
  before the Lantern Ghost pipe. Shoot an egg at the fluff above to reveal a 
  door. Go through the door and shoot the winged cloud for the stars.

10 Stars
  Pass through the middle ring up on the ledge before the Ball and Chain.

5 Stars
  Shoot the winged cloud near the end of the second area.

10 Stars
  Pass through the second middle ring in the room before the third area.

2 Red Coins
  Stomp through the fluff in the first area and enter the first tunnel on the 
  left to find the red coins above two Mufti Guys.

2 Red Coins
  Stomp through the fluff in the first area and enter the second tunnel on the 
  left to find the red coins above three Mufti Guys.

3 Red Coins
  Stomp through the fluff in the first area and enter the second tunnel on the 
  right. Stomp the fluff and use the spring ball to bounce up to the high ledge 
  on the left. The three red coins are at the right side of the winged cloud.

3 Red Coins
  Stomp through the fluff in the first area and go all the way through to the 
  room at the bottom with the two winged clouds. The coins can be found in the 
  middle of this room.

3 Red Coins
  When you come to the top of the hill just before the Ball and Chain in the 
  second area, jump left and continue left to find the red coins.

3 Red Coins
  Use the large spring ball near the Ball and Chain in the second area to 
  bounce up to the yellow platform. Jump up the yellow platforms to the top and 
  go left to find the red coins.

4 Red Coins
  Run right at the start of the second area and stop at the top of the slope 
  before the Lantern Ghost pipe. Shoot an egg at the fluff above to reveal a 
  door. Go through the door and eat the four Lantern Ghosts in the room to find 
  the red coins.

Key
  Stomp through the fluff in the first area and go all the way through to the 
  room at the bottom with the two winged clouds. Shoot the left winged cloud 
  for the key.

===============================================================================
                             Level 2-7: Lakitu's Wall
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Run left at the start of the level and jump up the small step to land near a 
Fat Guy. Eat the Fat Guy to create a large egg, which can be used to defeat all 
the enemies in a screen. As an example of this, walk over to the left side of 
the ledge and throw the big egg to defeat all six Mildes. As another advantage, 
all the defeated enemies transform into stars.

Drop down off the left side of the ledge and collect the six stars. Eat some of 
the Wall Lakitus on the left, then go right and jump up to red egg block. From 
the red egg block, jump up to the small tunnel high up on the right. Walk out 
of the right side of the tunnel and jump up to the platform above. Jump to the 
grass path and jump up to the left log platform to collect the first flower.

                                   - Flower 2 -

Walk to the left side of the log platform and hover jump over to the two posts 
on the left. Shoot an egg at the winged cloud to create a bridge. Stomp the 
right post twice to collect a red coin, and then run left across the bridge to 
the other side. Quickly eat the three Fly Guys that appear holding red coins at 
the left side of the bridge. Collect the red coins and then shoot the winged 
cloud just left of the bridge to receive five stars.

Continue left past the hut and eat the Fly Guy above the Fat Guy on the grey 
block platform. Collect the red coin that is dropped, then eat the Fat Guy and 
continue left under the Wall Lakitus to enter a small tunnel. Jump up to the 
platform in the cave to collect the red coin, and then continue left to enter 
another tunnel at the left side of the path. Jump up to the second platform and 
hit the egg block to refill the egg supply.

Shoot an egg through the yellow fluff on the right and eat the four Shy Guys on 
the purple rotating platform. Jump onto the rotating platform and shoot the 
winged cloud at the top to receive five stars. Walk into the tunnel at the 
right side of the rotating platform. Walk out of the left side of the tunnel 
and stomp the post twice. Run right and jump onto the second set of grey blocks 
to arrive near the hut. Enter the hut to play a bonus game.

After exiting the hut, run right and stomp the post at the left side of the 
bridge three times. Drop off the edge of the grass path and run left through 
the two paddles. Eat the Wall Lakitu after the paddles and then jump onto the 
first section of yellow fluff. Jump from the fluff over to the platform on the 
right, and continue right to find the second flower after two posts.

                                   - Flower 3 -

After collecting the second flower, stomp the right post three times and then 
jump over to the yellow fluff on the left. There is a red switch under the 
small spring ball in the first yellow fluff section. As it only reveals some 
coins over on the left, it's not necessary to find. Jump over the top of the 
first fluff section and jummp up to the middle step of the second fluff 
section. Shoot an egg up at the top of the fluff to reveal a winged cloud, and 
shoot another egg to receive the five stars. Jump over the top of the fluff and  
jump over to the grass path on the other side.

Two cannons shooting Bullet Bills will be down on the left. Wait for the Bullet 
Bills to appear, then jump on the top Bullet Bill and bounce up to the ledge on 
the right. Shoot the nearby winged cloud for a 1UP and then walk off the left 
side of the ledge to land on the two posts near the Bullet Bills. Duck under 
the Bullet Bills that are shot from the cannons, and then stomp the posts four 
times to receive two red coins. Run right and jump through the middle ring. Go 
through the blue doors.

After arriving in the Fat Guy area, run left and jump over the first gap. 
Continue left and jump onto the ledge after the second gap. Wait for the Fat 
Guy to run near the third gap and then start running back to the left. Quickly 
jump left and eat the fast Fat Guy on the path. Continue left and drop down the 
step to find six Mildes.

Shoot the Fat Guy egg to transform the Mildes into six stars, and then continue 
left to come to a bridge. Run left over the bridge and jump up to the ledge at 
the left side of the blue doors. Shoot an egg at the Tap-Tap and jump up to the 
platform on the left to collect the third flower. Run back to the right and go 
through the blue doors. Back in the first area, jump up to the ledge on the 
left and go down the pipe. 

                                   - Flower 4 -

After arriving in the second area, jump onto the first block and walk to the 
left side so that you can see the third block falling over on the left. When 
the first block starts to fall, jump across to the third block and then jump 
down to the fourth block.

Jump quickly across the fifth, seventh and ninth blocks, and then jump over to 
the tenth block in the top-left corner of the area to collect two red coins. 
Drop down off the right side of the tenth block and land on the platform at the 
right side of the grass path. Jump up to the grass path on the left and go up 
the pipe.

After arriving in the third area, walk left off the pipe and stomp the third 
post twice for a red coin. Jump up to the fifth post and jump over the Eggo-
Dil. On the left side of the Eggo-Dil, continue left to the third post and 
stomp it twice for another red coin.

Jump over the fifth post to land near a large spring ball. Use the spring ball 
to bounce up to the grass path on the left. Drop down to the post at the right 
side of the post and stomp it twelve times to reveal a winged cloud. Shoot the 
winged cloud to receive a 1UP and then jump back on the large spring ball.

Bounce back up to the grass path on the left. Go to the left side of the path 
and jump over the post to land on the steps. Walk left on the steps and shoot 
the winged cloud for five stars. Continue left to the top of the steps and then 
hover jump left to land on a platform at the side of a high grass path. Jump up 
to the grass path to reveal a winged cloud.

Shoot the winged cloud and jump on the red switch to reveal a red arrow over on 
the left. Walk over to the red arrow and press down to enter a secret area. In 
the secret area, walk left and stomp down the second line of fluff to collect 
the fourth flower. After landing at the bottom of the area, go down the pipe 
over on the right.

                                   - Flower 5 -

After returning to the third area, jump over the gap to the platform on the 
right and collect the two red coins. Jump up to the grass path on the right and 
eat the Fat Guy that's running about. Shoot the Fly Guy above when he is 
floating above the grass path to make him drop the red coin.

Collect the red coin and then jump up to the top of the steps on the right. 
Stomp the post two times at the top of the steps to collect a red coin, and 
then slowly walk off the left side of the grass path to land on a tall post. 
Stomp the post ten times to collect a red coin, and then walk right into the 
cave.

Jump over the Tap-Tap and collect the red coin on either side of the platform. 
Jump up to the platforms at the top of the cave and shoot an egg into the tulip 
to receive eight stars. Drop off the platform and go left to exit the cave. 
Jump over the small step and run left along the grass path to drop down to a 
platform at the end. Walk off the right side of the first platform, then drop 
off the left side of the second platform and hover right to land on a small 
platform near some winged clouds.

Drop off the right side of the platform to land on a small platform at the 
entrance to a small room at the right side of the cave. Walk right and shoot 
the winged cloud in the small room to receive five stars. Drop down the gap at 
the bottom of the room and then walk right until you come to the expansion 
block near the end of the area. Hit the block and then jump on top of it. Jump 
up to the platform on the right and shoot an egg straight up into the fluff to 
collect the fifth flower. Drop off the right side of the platform and continue 
right to enter the fourth area.

After arriving in the fourth area, pass through the second middle ring and then 
continue right to find a Metamorphosis Bubble. Touch the bubble to transform 
into a car. Drive right and jump to avoid the three sets of Tap-Taps on the way 
to the purple rotating platform. Jump and ride onto the rotating platform, and 
then drive right at the top to hit the second Metamorphosis Bubble.

Continue right to come to a platform with a red arrow pointing right on it. 
Drop off the platform and then drive left onto the yellow platform. After 
riding the yellow platform down, drive right and hit the message block to 
transform into Yoshi. Continue right and drop down off the platform to come to 
a large spring ball.

Jump on the spring ball and bounce straight up to hit a helicopter 
Metamorphosis Bubble. After transforming into the helicopter, fly right and 
follow the coin trail along to hit three Baron Von Zeppelins holding 1UPs. 
Continue following the coin trail as it leads down to hit a final Baron Von 
Zeppelin holding a 1UP. Fly down through the paddles to transform into Yoshi 
for the second time in this level. Run right and jump through the goal ring to 
complete the level.

~~ Items ~~

1UP
  When you come to the two cannons shooting Bullet Bills shortly before the 
  middle ring, jump on the top Bullet Bill and bounce up to the ledge on the 
  right. Shoot the winged cloud.

1UP
  In the third area, jump on the large spring ball after the Eggo-Dil and

  twelve times. Shoot the winged cloud.

1UP * 4
  After transforming into a helicopter, hit the four Baron Von Zeppelins in the 
  fourth area.

Flower 1

Flower 3

  left side of the area to find the flower.

Flower 4

  the switch. Press down on the red arrow and Stomp the second line of fluff.

Flower 5

  the bridge.

  A Fly Guy is holding this red coin above the left side of the hut.

  three times.

2 Red Coins

  After arriving in the third area, stomp the third post from the left side of

  In the third area, jump on the spring ball after the Eggo-Dil and bounce up

1 Red Coin
  In the third area, jump on the spring ball after the Eggo-Dil and bounce up

  drop down to the post below and stomp it ten times for the red coin.

2 Red Coins
  Under the tulip in the third area.

1 Red Coin
  A Fly Guy has the red coin at the bottom of the steps in the third area.

2 Red Coins

5 Stars
  Shoot the winged cloud above the right side of the hut.

5 Stars
  Run left past the Lakitus at the left side of the hut and jump up the 
  platforms at the far left side of the path to find a rotating purple 
  platform. Shoot the winged cloud above the platform.

5 Stars
  After passing the first set of paddles in the level, jump over the first

  section on the other side.

10 Stars
  Pass through the middle ring after the two cannons shooting Bullet Bills.

5 Stars

5 Stars
  Shoot the winged cloud at the far right side of the cave near the end of the 
  third area.

10 Stars
  Pass through the second middle ring at the start of the fourth area.

Key
  Run left past the Lakitus at the left side of the hut and jump up the 
  platforms at the far left side of the path to find a rotating purple 
  platform. The key is in the tunnel at the right side of the platform.

Red Switch
  After passing the first set of paddles in the level, shoot an egg under the 
  spring ball in the yellow fluff to find the red switch.

===============================================================================
                       Level 2-8: The Potted Ghost's Castle
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Run right at the start of the level and go down the pipe. After arriving in the 
first area, run right along the path and jump onto the first vertically moving 
purple platform above the lava. Jump down to the first post in the lava to 
collect a red coin. Jump over to the second post to collect another red coin, 
and then quickly shoot an egg at the Fly Guy that appears up on the right to 
receive a 1UP. Jump over to the second purple platform and from there jump over 
to the green platform on the small wire. When the green platform reaches the 
far right side of the wire, jump over to the path on the right.

Walk over to the right side of the path and drop down to the first post in the 
lava to collect a red coin. When the Lava Bubble jumps out of the lava and geos 
back in, do a small jump and then hover over to the next post on the right to 
collect two more red coins. Jump over to the green platform on the vertical 
wire and then jump over to the next green platform on the long wire. Ride this 
platform all the way along the wire to collect the first flower.

                                   - Flower 2 -

Jump onto the path on the right when the platform reaches the end of the wire. 
Continue right and jump across the two green platforms to land on the yellow 
platform. Collect the red coin at the left side of the yellow platform and then 
jump right to land on the final green platform in the area. When the platform 
gets near the end of the wire and starts going down, jump right and pass 
through the first middle ring. Run right along the path and go up the pipe.

After arriving in the second area, run left down the two steps and wait near 
the rotating arrow platform. Jump on when the platform points up and left and 
ride up to the cloud at the top-left corner of the area. Go up the pipe. In the 
secret area, jump up to the ledge on the right and shoot the winged cloud to 
reveal a train Metamorphosis Bubble. Touch the bubble and then ride along the 
track to the junction. At the junction, take the top track and continue along 
to collect the second flower. Touch the Yoshi block at the end of the track and 
run left back to the start of the area. Go down the pipe.

                                   - Flower 3 -

After returning to the second area, wait for the arrow platform below to point 
right and then jump onto it. Follow the coin trail to collect three red coins 
and then jump onto the platform at the end of the trail. Go through the pipe to 
enter the third area. After arriving in the third area, go right and drop down 
to the tunnel below. Go right and then go left at the junction. Continue left 
to enter the fourth area.

After arriving in the fourth area, walk left and eat Shy Guys coming out of the 
pipe until Yoshi has six eggs. Jump on top of the pipe and shoot the winged 
cloud for three stars. Run left and jump over the small gap to land near the 
first Dizzy Dandy in the game. Jump over the Dizzy Dandy and then run under the 
yellow fluff. Go to the left side of the platform and jump over the two gaps to 
land near another Dizzy Dandy.

Quickly jump over the Dizzy Dandy and then jump over the next gap on the left 
to land near a normal flower under a platform of fluff. Walk to the left side 
of the small fluff platform and wait for one of the Boo Guys above to drop a 
missile down onto the fluff, which will create a gap. Drop down into the fluff 
gap and collect the third flower.

                                   - Flower 4 -

Jump out of the fluff gap and run left to come to a fluff platform in a gap. 
Quickly jump onto the middle of the platform to collect the red coin, and then 
jump over to the path at the left side of the gap. Shoot the winged cloud for 
five stars and then continue left to find a vase. Jump over to the left side of 
the vase and push it right along the log platform. Push it off the edge of the 
log platform to reveal a key. Run right all the way back to the start of the 
area. Shoot the winged cloud above the Shy Guy pipe for three more stars, and 
then go through the pipe at the far right side of the area.

After returning to the third area, run up the slope on the right and drop down 
the first gap. Walk left and then right to drop down the two ledges, and run 
right along the tunnel to enter a room with five coins. Collect the middle red 
coin, then go left and jump up the two platforms. Go right at the top of the 
gap and continue right to enter the fifth area.

After arriving in the fifth area, eat the Shy Guys coming out of the first pipe 
until Yoshi has six eggs. Jump over the pipe and continue right under the 
message block to come to a spiked log with a wheel at the top. Shoot the wheel 
twice to raise the log, an then quickly run under it. On the other side of the 
log, eat two more Shy Guys coming out of the pipe and then go through the pipe 
at the far right side of the area. Run right along the tunnel and enter the 
door with the keyhole.

After arriving in the sixth area, walk right and jump up the three platforms. 
From the third platform, go left at the junction and jump up the two platforms 
to come to a small room with the second middle ring. Pass through the middle 
ring and then drop down the gap on the right. Jump over the small gap to come 
to another junction. Take the low path and go through the blue doors at the 
bottom of the slope. Defeat both Burts in the room to reveal the flower. 
Collect the fourth flower and then go through the blue doors.

                                   - Flower 5 -

After returning to the sixth area, jump up the small step and then run left up 
the slope. Jump up the platform at the top of the slope and then jump up to the 
path on the right. Of the six coins, collect the second and fifth coin, and 
then continue right to enter the seventh area.

After arriving in the seventh area, eat the Shy Guys coming out of the first 
pipe until Yoshi has six eggs. Run right and jump onto the small platform near 
the first spiked log. Shoot the wheel twice and then quickly jump over to the 
vertically moving purple platform on the other side. Jump across to the path 
and hit the egg block to refill the egg supply. Continue right and jump onto 
the next purple moving platform. Shoot the wheel above the second spiked log 
twice to raise it. Jump right to drop down into the gap under the spiked log 
and run right to collect the fifth flower.

Walk right after collecting the fifth flower and jump up through the log 
platform. Drop down off the edge of the path on the right, and continue right 
to come to an arrow platform. Jump on the platform when it points up and 
slightly right, and then ride it to collect the first red coin. At this point, 
hover jump straight up and land back on the platform when it points up and 
left.

After the second red coin, hover jump and ride the platform up to collect the 
third red coin. Jump off to the ledge on the right after collecting the third 
red coin, and then jump up to the log platform above. Shoot an egg up at the 
small section of blue thorns to reveal some doors. Go through the blue doors.

After arriving in the eighth area, run into the hidden tunnel on the left and 
jump up to the lowest platform. Jump out of the tunnel and land on the lowest 
log platform on the right. Jump up the log platforms to the top to collect two 
red coins, avoiding the Bandits along the way. On the top log platform, walk 
left to land on a vase. Get on the left side of the vase and push it right to 
reveal a key.

Collect the key and then jump back to the log platforms on the left. From the 
top log platform, jump over to the grass path on the right and pass through the 
third middle ring in the level. Walk onto the log platform at the right side of 
the path and drop down the platforms to collect the final two red coins. Jump 
over to the hidden tunnel on the right and go through the blue door with the 
keyhole.

After arriving in the ninth area, run right and hit the three yellow egg 
blocks. Jump through the fourth middle ring in the level, and then jump up to 
the high ledge on the right. Push the vase off the ledge on the right for six 
coins, and then continue right to the far right side of the area. Go through 
the red doors.

                        - Boss Fight 4: The Potted Ghost -

This is by far the easiest boss fight in the game! When the fight starts, run 
right and push the Potted Ghost right. If he pushes you away, just run back and 
keep pushing him right. When he spits blue flames, wait until they disappear 
and then continue to push him right until he falls off the platform.

~~ Items ~~

===============================================================================
                            Extra 2: Hit That Switch!!
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Run left at the start of the level and go down the green pipe to arrive in a 
secret area. Stomp the two crates for twelve stars, and shoot the two winged 
clouds for a further ten stars. Walk left and go up the pipe to exit the area. 
After returning to the main level, run right to come to the first red switch in 
the level. From this point on, the level gets very difficult... especially if 
you're going for a 100 point score.

Jump on the first red switch and quickly jump up the three red block steps on 
the right. Jump over to the red and yellow platform at the top of the steps and 
wait as it travels up to a long flat wire. On the flat wire, immediately jump 
to land on the second red switch in the level on three red blocks. Wait until 
the platform returns, and then walk off the right side of the red blocks to 
land back on the platform.

After landing back on the platform, wait as it travels along the wire and up 
the ramp at the other end. When it goes off the ramp, wait to collect four red 
coins, and then quickly jump over to the first of four red block platforms on 
the right. Jump over to the third red block platform, and then jump over to the 
large spring ball on the fourth red block platform. Bounce up through the gap 
in the red blocks to collect the first flower, and hold left to land on the 
blocks at the left side of the gap.

                                   - Flower 2 -

After landing at the left side of the gap, quickly run left to collect two red 
coins and then jump over the gap to land on the third red switch. Quickly go 
right and jump over the two gaps to land near another red and yellow platform. 
Jump onto the platform. The platform will go down and right along a wire. When 
the platform goes right, hold down to pass under a first set of red blocks. 
Jump over the Pirahna Plant on the other side to collect three red coins and 
the second flower.

                                   - Flower 3 -

After collecting the second flower, land on the next platform on the right and 
hold down to pass under a second set of red blocks. Jump over the Pirahna Plant 
on the other side to collect three more red coins and the third flower.

                                   - Flower 4 -

Land on the next platform on the right and hold down to pass under the third 
and final set of red blocks. The platform will go off a small ramp at the end 
of the wire. Collect the two red coins in the trail, and then jump over to the 
red switch on the red block platform on the right. Use the large spring ball to 
bounce over the high red block platform to collect the fourth flower.

                                   - Flower 5 -

After collecting the fourth flower, hold right to fall down the long gap and 
land at the right side of a red and yellow platform. The platform will go along 
a small wire, and will then start to fall. When the platform starts to fall, 
jump to the red block platform on the left. Jump on the large spring ball and 
bounce over the high red block platform to collect the fifth flower.

Wait for the red block timer to run out, and then drop down to the red and 
yellow platform on the right. The platform will go up and along a wire. When 
the platform starts to drop at the end of the wire, jump right and pas through 
the goal ring to complete the level.

~~ Items ~~

Flower 1
  After jumping off the first red and yellow platform, jump across to the  
  fourth red block platform and use the large spring ball to bounce up through 
  the gap to find the flower.

Flower 2
  Above the first Pirahna Plant in the level.

Flower 3
  Above the second Pirahna Plant in the level.

Flower 4
  After hitting the red switch near the end of the level, use the large spring 
  ball to bounce up to the flower above the first high red block platform on 
  the right.

Flower 5
  Use the final spring ball in the level to jump up to the high red block 
  platform on the right.

4 Red Coins

  wire to find these coins.

4 Red Coins

  fourth red block platform and use the large spring ball to bounce up through 
  the gap. There are four red coins on the red blocks.

3 Red Coins

3 Red Coins
  Above the second Pirahna Plant in the level.

2 Red Coins
  After passing the second Pirahna Plant in the level, the platform will go off 
  a ramp at the end of the wire. Ride the platform to collect the coins.

  In the first winged cloud in the secret area.

===============================================================================
                       Level 3-1: Welcome To Monkey World!
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Run right at the start of the level and jump on top of the yellow fluff. Walk 
to the middle of the fluff platform and stomp the post three times to reveal a 
winged cloud. Shoot the winged cloud to receive five stars, and then jump right 
to land on top of the remaining fluff. Collect the red coin level with the 
fluff, and continue right up the slope. Shoot an egg at the winged cloud at the 
top of the slope to reveal a flower. Walk slowly onto the edge of the slope to 
collect the first flower, and then jump over the large gap on the right to land 
on the next slope.

                                   - Flower 2 -

On the other side of the gap, quickly eat the Grinder before he bounces away. 
Run under the Seedy Sally up in the trees and go up the slope. Drop down on the 
other side of the path, and walk right to collect a red coin. Shoot an egg up 
at the winged cloud above to receive five stars, and then stomp the post on the 
right twice to collect a red coin. Go up to the top of the slope on the right 
to see the flower. Jump off to collect the second flower, then quickly hold 
left to collect the red coin below.

                                   - Flower 3 -

After landing on the grass path, run right and jump over the gap below the 
Seedy Sally in the tree. Walk right and eat both Grinders on the red bridge, 
then collect the red coin, which is the fourth coin in the line of coins on the 
bridge. Run right to the end of the bridge to exit the first area.

After arriving in the second area, jump off the bridge to the grass path on the 
right. Drop down the small slope and collect the middle red coin in the set of 
three coins above. Go right and jump up the big slope to the path at the top. 
Jump over the post and continue down the slope on the other side. Jump up the 
small slope to the path above, and run right all the way along to the end of 
the long path.

Jump through the middle ring and slide down the mud slope to the bottom. Drop 
down the five big mud steps and slide down the next mud slope to land in the 
water. Hold left in the water to get close to the mud slope, then jump and hold 
left to swim under the mud to a gap at the other side. Jump up the six 
platforms in the gap and use the large spring ball on the sixth platform to 
bounce up to a secret area. In the secret area, walk left to the big donut 
lifts and fire eggs at the Fly Guys which appear holding 1UPs. On the cloud 
platform at the bottom of the area, run right and go down the green pipe.

After returning to the second area, go right and drop down the five mud steps. 
Go down the slope at the bottom of the steps and drop back into the water. Jump 
onto the orange floating platform in the water and then jump up to the small 
green platform on the right. Collect the red coin above the right side of the 
platform and jump onto the first floating platform in the water on the right. 
Collect the red coin at the right side of the platform, and then jump over to 
the next floating platform on the right. Collect the red coin at the left side 
of the platform and then shoot an egg up to collect the third flower.

                                   - Flower 4 -

Jump over to the green platform on the right and then jump over to the mud 
slope on the right. Jump up to the top of the post and eat the Grinder on the 
next post on the right. Collect the middle red coin between the posts, and then 
continue right up the small mud slope to the third post. Stomp the post twice 
to collect a red coin, and continue right to come to an egg block. Hit the egg 
block to refill the egg supply, and then shoot the winged cloud above the egg 
block to receive six stars.

Jump over the next post on the right and run up to the top of the mud slope. 
Jump to the log platform at the top of the slope, ignoring the Pirahna Plant 
over on the left. Jump up the three log platforms above, eating any Grinders 
that get in the way. On the fourth log platform, jump left over to the fifth 
log platform, eating the Grinders there if you need more eggs, and then jump 
right to the sixth log platform.

Jump up two platforms to the eighth platform, and eat the green watermelon at 
the right side of the platform. Jump up and shoot a single watermelon seed at 
the Grinder on the ninth platform, and then jump over to the platform. Jump 
right to the tenth platform and shoot two watermelon seeds in the same 
direction: One to hit the winged cloud and one to collect the fourth flower.

                                   - Flower 5 -

Jump up to the platform above and shoot a watermelon seed at the Pirahna Plant 
up on the left. Jump left over to the platform, and then jump up to the tiny 
platform above. Jump up to collect the red coin above the left side of the 
platform, and then jump over to the long platform on the right. Go right along 
the platform and jump over to the grass path. Run quickly right along the path 
to avoid the three Grinders up in the trees. Jump over the post about half-way 
along the path, and stop before the gap at the end of the path.

Jump over the two gaps, collecting the red coin above each gap, and then jump 
over the next three gaps. After passing the fifth gap, face left and shoot a 
watermelon seed to collect the red coin in the gap. Face right and quickly 
shoot the Grinder holding the watermelon. Eat the watermelon and shoot the 
watermelon seeds at the various Grinders as you run right right along the path. 
Jump over the two gaps at the end of the path and continue right to exit the 
second area.

After arriving in the third area, run right and jump up to the top of the post. 
Quickly eat the Grinder on the right, and then stomp the post three times to 
collect a red coin. Eat the watermelon that the Grinder dropped, and go right 
to the pit with the swinging Grinders. Jump up and shoot a watermelon seed 
above the pit to collect a red coin, and continue right to the pit. Quickly 
jump over the pit when the Grinders swing up to the left, and jump over the 
next gap on the other side.

On the other side of the gap, jump up to collect the red coin at the right side 
of the Grinder with the watermelon, and continue right to come to a see-saw 
platform. Jump onto the right side of the platform and wait for it to drop 
enough so that you can collect the red coin. After collecting the red coin, 
quickly jump over to the pink platform on the right. Ride the platform up as 
high as it can go, and then jump up to collect the fifth flower.

After collecting the fifth flower, jump over to the see-saw platform on the 
right, and then quickly jump right to the grass path on the other side. Jump up 
to the small bump in the path and wait for the swinging Grinders to appear on 
the right. When they swing left, run right off the bump, do a small jump to 
collect the red coin, and jump over the next bump on the right. Continue right 
and jump through the goal ring to complete the level.

  left to swim under a ledge to a gap. Jump up the platforms in the gap and use 
  the spring ball to bounce up to a hidden area, where six Fly Guys holding

===============================================================================
                           Level 3-2: Jungle Rhythm...
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Run right at the start of the level and jump up to the top of the first block. 
Jump over the small gap and eat the Milde, and then jump over the large gap on 
the right with the two Spear Guys in it. Land on the two Mildes on the block so 
that they don't knock you over the side, and then jump over the next gap and 
eat the two Mildes on the high block. Walk right and shoot an egg at the 
Pirahna Plant.

Jump over the small gap on the right and drop down onto the blocks below when 
the Spear Guy is facing right. Quickly eat the Spear Guy before he turns back 
to the left, and continue right along the blocks to see two more Spear Guys on 
the path below. Drop down to the path and eat both Spear Guys as they walk 
right, and continue right to collect three red coins and the first flower.

                                   - Flower 2 -

Go back to the left and jump up to the small block. Jump over the gap on the 
right to land on the high block, and eat the four Mildes that are walking 
about. Jump up the small step on the right and continue right to come to a 
platform block. Run under the block and shoot an egg up at the winged block to 
reveal a key. Drop down off the block and eat the four Dancing Spear Guys. A 
Fly Guy holding a red coin will appear above the fourth Spear Guy, so quickly 
shoot an egg at him and collect the red coin.

Walk left and jump up at the right side of the egg plant to collect another red 
coin. Go right and jump up the mud slope to the grass path at the top. Shoot 
the winged cloud to receive five stars, then continue right and walk slowly off 
the right edge of the path to reveal a winged cloud on the block below. Shoot 
the winged cloud and jump on the red switch. Quickly jump up to the grass path 
on the left and press down above the red arrow to land on Poochy in a secret 
area. Face right after landing on Poochy, and he'll run through the water to 
the other side. After he jumps up under the log platform above the water, go up 
the pipe to return to the main level.

After exiting the pipe, jump over to the high horizontally moving platform on 
the left. Jump down to the block on the left and shoot an egg at the Tap-Tap in 
the gap. Jump through the gap on the left and drop down to the first vertically 
moving platform on the other side. Shoot an egg into the tulip to receive eight 
stars, and then jump up to collect the second flower.

                                   - Flower 3 -

Jump back through the gap on the right and jump onto the highest of the two 
horizontally moving platforms. Wait for the green rotating platform to get 
near, then jump on it and stay on it to pass through the middle ring. Wait for 
the platform to point up and left, and then jump left onto the vertically 
moving platform. Hit the pink platform block above and jump onto the new 
vertically moving platform above. Jump up to the tiny log platform on the 
right, and then jump left to collect the four red coins.

Drop back down to the platform below, and then walk slowly off the edge to land 
on the big vertically moving platform. Wait for the platform to go down low, 
then shoot an egg up at the blue platform block. Wait for the green rotating 
platform to appear, and then quickly drop down onto it. When the platform 
points up and right, jump up to the blue platform that you created by hitting 
the blue platform block earlier, and then jump up to the pink vertically moving 
platform above. Wait for the platform to go up, and then jump through the gap 
to land on the right log platform, collecting the third flower along the way.

                                   - Flower 4 -

Hit the egg block to refill the egg supply, and then jump onto the pink 
vertically moving platform on the left. Jump up to the block on the left and 
eat the two Spear Guys as they face left. Jump up to the tiny pink rotating 
platform above. When the platform goes half-way around, shoot the low platform 
to reveal the steps on the right, and shoot the high winged cloud to reveal the 
fourth flower. Jump up to collect the fourth flower and hold right to land on 
the steps below.

                                   - Flower 5 -

Run up to the top of the steps on the right and jump onto the block at the top. 
Jump over the gap on the left to land on another block, and jump up the three 
big steps on the left to land near a Spear Guy. Eat the Spear Guy when he faces 
left, and then use the spring ball to bounce up to the high block on the left. 
Jump over the block on the left to land near an egg plant. Continue left and 
drop down the small step to collect two red coins.

Jump up the step on the right and run past the egg plant. Jump up the small 
step on the right, and then jump straight up to the pink rotating platform. 
Stay on the platform until it points up and left, then jump left to enter a 
secret area in the trees. In the secret area, hover jump from the pipe to 
collect the four red coins hidden in the trees. Press up next to the hut to 
play a bonus game. After exiting the hut, run left and go down the pipe.

After returning to the main level, jump up the small step on the right and jump 
straight up to the pink rotating platform. Jump off the platform when it points 
up and right, and collect the two red coins nearby. Continue right and jump up 
the small step on the right. Eat the three Dancing Spear Guys, and then jump up 
to collect the fifth flower.

Continue right to come to a gap with a Pirahna Plant on the other side. Quickly 
shoot the Fly Guy that appears above the Pirahna Plant to make him drop a red 
coin. Shoot an egg at the Pirahna Plant, and then jump over to the other side 
of the gap to land on a tall block. Wait for the Dancing Spear Guys down on the 
block on the right to move over to the right side, and then jump down to the 
left side of the block. Quickly eat the three Dancing Spear Guys and go  right 
along the block to collect two red coins. Jump over the Tap-Tap on the block on 
the right and land on the block on the other side. Continue right and jump 
through the goal ring to complete the level.

~~ Items ~~

Flower 1    - Down the two steps after the first Pirahna Plant in the level.

Flower 2    - At the left side of the tulip, shortly after the first Tap-Tap in
              the level.

Flower 3    - Above a pink platform about half-way up the first vertically 
              scrolling section of the level.

Flower 4    - Shoot the highest of the two winged cloud above the tiny pink
              rotating platform in the first vertically scrolling section of
              the level.

Flower 5    - Above the three Spear Guys just after the pink rotating platform
              at the top of the vertically scrolling section of the level.

3 Red Coins - Down the two steps after the first Pirahna Plant in the level.

              Collect the middle coin.

              platform blocks, shortly before the second flower.

4 Red Coins - Jump onto the green rotating platform at the end of the first 
              horizontally scrolling section, and then jump up the platforms at 
              the top-left corner to find the coins.

2 Red Coins - Jump on the small spring ball near the end of the vertically
              scrolling section, and bounce up to the left. Run left past the
              egg plant to find the coins.

4 Red Coins - Jump on the pink rotating platform at the top of the vertically
              scrolling section, and jump off at the top-left corner to enter
              a secret area. The four coins can be found in the trees in this
              area.

2 Red Coins - At the right side of the pink rotating platform at the top of the 
              vertically scrolling section of the level.

1 Red Coin  - A Fly Guy holding this red coin appears above the final Pirahna 
              Plant in the level.

2 Red Coins - Near the final three Spear Guys in the level.

5 Stars     - Shoot the winged cloud after the two blue platform blocks.

10 Stars    - Pass through the middle ring above the pipe at the end of the
              first horizontally scrolling section of the level.

Key         - Hit the winged cloud after the first blue platform block.

Red Switch  - In the first area, run under the winged cloud shortly after the 
              two blue platform blocks and drop down off the edge of the path
              to reveal a winged cloud. Shoot the winged cloud for the stars.

===============================================================================
                           Level 3-3: Nep-Enuts' Domain
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Jump over the post at the start of the level and run down the steep mud slope 
on the other side. Run across the two trees at the bottom of the slope 
(stopping at the egg plant if you need some more eggs), and jump up to the 
grass path to land near a Grinder. Quickly eat the Grinder before he bounces 
away, and continue right to approach the first Nep-Enut lake. Jump on top of 
the post before the lake and shoot an egg at the winged cloud inside Nep-Enut's 
mouth to reveal the flower. Shoot an egg at Nep-Enut, and then jump over the 
lake to collect the first flower.

                                   - Flower 2 -

After landing on the big post at the other side of the lake, jump up to the 
grass path and eat the Grinder that bounces toward you. Shoot the winged cloud 
up on the right and collect the five stars that drop down. Go along to the far 
right side of the path to come to the second lake. Shoot the Nep-Enut that 
emerges, and then jump down to the tree over at the right side of the lake. 
Collect the red coin above the left side of the tree, and jump the small gap 
over to the big post on the right.

Jump up and slightly to the left to collect the red coin high above the post, 
and then hold right to land back on the post without touching the Nep-Enut. 
Jump up to the mud slope on the right and run up to the top. Quickly eat the 
Grinder at the top of the slope before he bounces away. Start sliding down the 
mud slope on the right, and drop off the end to land on one of the three posts 
near the third lake.

Shoot an egg at the Nep-Enut that appears. When the Nep-Enut sinks back into 
the lake, jump over to the low tree on the right, and do a small hover jump 
right to collect the red coin above the post at the right side of the lake. 
Jump up to the trees above, and run up to the top of the mud slope on the 
right. After arriving on the small grass path on top of the slope, face left 
and shoot an egg up at the winged cloud to reveal the flower. Jump off the left 
side of the path to collect the second flower, and then hover right to land 
back on the path.

                                   - Flower 3 -

Jump over the post and run down the mud slope to the post at the bottom. A Nep-
Enut will emerge from the lake, so quickly shoot an egg at it. When the Nep-
Enut goes back into the lake, jump over to the fourth tree on the right and 
quickly shoot an egg up at the winged cloud to receive five stars. Drop down 
off the right side of the tree to land in the water. Swim right and jump up 
under the fifth tree to collect a red coin. Jump up to the sixth tree and eat 
the Grinder.

Jump up to the seventh tree, jump left to collect the red coin, and then hover 
right to land back on the seventh tree. Jump over to the ninth tree and collect 
the red coin under the right side of it. Swim right and jump up under the right 
side of the eleventh tree to collect another red coin. Swim right and jump up 
to collect the final coin above the lake. Jump out of the lake to land on the 
grass path.

Jump up to the second tree on the grass path and shoot an egg up at the winged 
cloud to reveal five stars. Walk right along the path until you get near to the 
tree with the Seedy Sally in it. A Grinder will bounce along from the right, so 
quickly eat him and then jump up to eat the Seedy Sally in the tree. Jump from 
the right side of the path to land on a set of six poles. Jump over to the 
fifth pole and eat the Grinder that bounces toward you. Shoot the Nep-Enut that 
emerges from the lake, and then jump over the trees in the lake to the other 
side. Jump through the middle ring and continue right to exit the first area.

After arriving in the second area, go down the mud slope on the right and eat 
the Grinder. Jump over the post at the bottom of the slope and jump over the 
Huffin Puffin on the other side. Run up the first slope on the right and eat 
the Short Fuse up in the tree. Run up the next slope on the right and eat the 
Seedy Sally on the vine at the top. Eat the watermelon that the Seedy Sally 
dropped, and then cross over the tiny gap on the right.

Shoot the winged cloud in the trees above on the other side of the gap to 
receive five stars. Continue right up and over the hill. Eat the Grinder on the 
other side of the hill, and then head down the big slope on the right. Eat the 
Stretch and the two Shy Guys on the bridge, and quickly eat the Seedy Sally on 
the right.

Eat the watermelon, and shoot the winged cloud up on the right to reveal a 
bridge going along above the water. Jump down to the bridge and run right along 
to the other side. Jump over the gap at the end of the bridge, eat the Grinder 
on the vine, and shoot an egg up at the winged cloud to reveal some doors. Go 
through the blue doors to enter a secret area. In the secret area, wait for the 
three Spear Guys to face right, then quickly drop down and eat them to reveal 
the third flower. Collect the third flower and then go through the blue doors.

                                   - Flower 4 -

After returning to the second area, drop down through the gap on the left and 
run right to collect a red coin above the water. Run back to the left and jump 
back up through the gap to land on the tall post on the left side. Drop down 
off the post to hit the metamorphosis bubble, which will transform Yoshi into a 
helicopter. Fly left and go up slightly to fly over the post. Continue left 
under the bridge, and go through the small tunnel on the other side of the tall 
post. Fly down on the other side of the tunnel to hit the Yoshi block, and then 
go through the blue doors on the left.

After arriving in the third area, jump through the middle ring up on the right 
and drop down into the water to hit the metamorphosis bubble, which will 
transform Yoshi into a submarine. Follow the coin trail down and right, and 
continue right past the various fish, tapping Y to fire a missile if any get 
too close.

After touching the second metamorphosis bubble, continue right to come to a 
ball and chain. Collect the red coin at the left side of the ball and chain 
block, and then swim over to the other side of the ball and chain to touch the 
third metamorphosis bubble.

Continue right and follow the coin trail to a small ball and chain. Wait for 
the ball and chain to point left, and then quickly swim right under it. Go 
through the small tunnel and go up on the other side to touch the Yoshi block, 
which will return Yoshi to normal. After landing on the log platform above the 
water, jump up the step on the right and go through the blue doors.

After arriving in the fourth area, jump up to the log platform on the right and 
pass through the middle ring. Quickly shoot the two Fly Guys that appear 
holding the 1UPs, and then drop down to the mud hill on the right. Walk down 
the right side of the hill and eat the Flopsy Fish that flies over the first 
post. Jump up to collect the red coin, and then jump over to the top of the 
first post. Jump over to the second post, eating the next Flopsy Fish after 
landing, and jump over to the next mud hill on the right.

Hit the red egg block above the slope and collect the egg. There are two 
bridges over on the right. Jump over to land on the lowest bridge, and then 
quickly run right to collect a red coin. Jump quickly up to the higher level of 
the bridge before the Clawdaddy gets to you, and shoot the winged cloud for 
five stars. Run to the far right side of the bridge and jump over to land on 
the small grass path at the top of a mud slope.

Hit the egg block to refill the egg supply, and then jump over the big gap on 
the right to land on the bridge at the other side. Eat the Frog Pirate and go 
right to drop down to the lower level of the bridge. Run left and shoot the 
winged cloud to reveal the fourth flower. Collect the fourth flower, and then 
jump up to the lowest of the pink vertically moving platforms up on the right.

                                   - Flower 5 -

When the platform goes up about half-way, jump left to collect the red coin and 
then hover back to the platform on the right. Jump up to land on the higher 
platform, and then jump over to the high mud ledge on the right. Go right to 
drop down onto the first small red platform. Run right and left to drop down 
the remaining four platforms. On the lowest platform, bounce three eggs off the 
wall so that they hit the Clawdaddy.

After the Clawdaddy has been defeated, hold right to land in the water. Run 
right to collect the red coin at the end of the trail of coins, and then run 
back to the left. Jump up to the post where the Clawdaddy used to be, and 
collect the red coin before jumping up to the low red platform above. Jump up 
the six red platforms, and jump from the highest platform onto the mud slope on 
the right.

Go down the slope to come to the top of some steps. Eat the Woozy Guy that 
bounces down the slope on the right, and then run down the steps, collecting 
the red coin along the way. After dropping down onto the platform at the bottom 
of the steps, go through the blue doors.

After arriving in the fifth area, jump to the second post on the right and use 
the left egg block to refill the egg supply. Run up the steps on the right and 
quickly eat the Frog Pirate. Collect the fourth and eighth coins above the 
bridge, and then continue right, watching out for the Flopsy Fish that jump out 
of the water. Shoot the first winged cloud above the right side of the bridge, 
and jump up to collect the fifth flower.

Shoot the next winged cloud on the right to receive five stars. Run down the 
steps at the right side of the bridge, and jump over to the steps on the right. 
Run up the long set of steps and quickly eat the Grinder on the post at the 
top. Jump onto the post and stomp it seven times. Go right to drop down to the 
lowest of the three bridges. Run right to land on the steps on the right, 
collecting a red coin along the way. Eat the Whirly Fly Guy, and then continue 
right. Jump through the goal ring to compete the level.
