===============================================================================
                         Level 3-4: Prince Froggy's Fort
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Go right at the start of the level and jump over the gap to land on the block. 
Eat the Shy Guy, and jump over the next gap on the right. Hover jump over the 
three Spear Guys on the bridge, and continue right to the end of the bridge. 
Shoot an egg up at the winged cloud on the right to reveal the small red bridge 
below. Run to the right side of the red bridge and eat the Flopsy Fish that 
jumps out of the water. Shoot an egg down at the bottom-right blue thorn to 
reveal a winged cloud. Shoot the winged cloud and go through the blue doors 
that are revealed.

In the secret area, touch the metamorphosis bubble to transform into a 
submarine. Swim down and left in the water to come to a ball and chain. Follow 
the trail of coins as the ball and chain rotates to collect two red coins. 
Continue left in the water and touch the Yoshi block at the other side.

After returning to the first area, jump up to the block on the right and hover 
jump over the three Spear Guys on the bridge again. Face left and eat the three 
Spear Guys, and then continue right. Shoot the winged cloud to reveal the red 
bridge. Run to the right side of the bridge and jump up to the wall on the 
right. Run down the red steps, and then continue right to trigger a Dizzy 
Dandy. Jump over the Dizzy Dandy and eat the Grinder that bounces toward you on 
the other side. Jump over the second Dizzy Dandy, eat the next Grinder, and go 
through the blue doors.

After arriving in the second area, run right and jump over the first big gap. 
Wait for the Flopsy Fish over on the right to jump right. When it does, jump 
over the second gap to collect a red coin above the water, and then quickly 
jump the third gap before the Flopsy Fish jumps back to the left. After 
landing, go through the first set of blue doors.

On the other side of the first set of blue doors, eat the Grinder that jumps 
down from the gap up on the left, and then face right. Jump over the two gaps 
with the Flopsy Fish in them to collect three red coins. Go through the blue 
doors on the other side of the two gaps to enter a room with two Clawdaddy's. 
Shoot both Clawdaddy's to reveal the flower. Collect the first flower, and then 
exit the room.

                                   - Flower 2 -

Face left and jump over both gaps. Hit the egg block to refill the egg supply, 
and then jump back over both gaops on the right. Jump up through the red steps 
and shoot the winged cloud up on the right to receive five stars. Run up the 
steps on the left and jump on the path at the top. Run left along the path, 
eating the Grinder about half-way, and drop down off end of the path. Go 
through the blue doors.

After returning to the second area, walk right to the gap, and watch the ball 
and chain on the other side. When the ball and chain goes under the path, 
quickly jump over the gap, shoot an egg up and right into the fluff to collect 
the red coin, and then quickly jump right through the gap in the fluff. On the 
other side of the fluff, hover jump right to land on the platform above the 
water. Jump down to the left side of the path on the right, and stay still to 
avoid the ball and chain. When the ball and chain has passed, go right and jump 
up in the gap to collect the second flower.

                                   - Flower 3 -

Quickly continue right and jump up to the platform above the water. Stay on the 
platform until the ball and chain on the right has gone under the path, and 
then jump down to the path on the right. Shoot an egg up into the gap to 
collect the two red coins, and then jump across the gap on the right to land 
near the second set of blue doors in the area. Go through the blue doors.

On the other side of the second set of blue doors, hit the egg block on the 
right to refill the egg supply. Shoot an egg up at the bucket on the left, and 
it will drop into the water. Jump onto the bucket and hold left to float across 
the water, eating the Flopsy Fish along the way. Jump up to collect the second, 
fourth and six coins in the trail, and jump up through the red steps at the 
other side of the water. Shoot the winged cloud up up on the left for a 1UP, 
and then run up the steps on the right to the path at the top. Run along the 
path and drop down the gap at the end. Go through the blue doors.

After returning to the second area, go right and jump onto the tiny pink 
rotating platform. Continue right, and slow down when you get near the Boo 
Guys. Collect the red coins below the second and fourth Boo Guys. After passing 
the first Boo Guy section, jump up to the right platform above and shoot the 
winged cloud to receive five stars. Collect the stars, and then jump over the 
gap to the platform on the left. Shoot the winged cloud to reveal the flower. 
Collect the third flower, and then drop down to the rotating platform.

                                   - Flower 4 -

Continue moving the rotating platform right under the second set of Boo Guys. 
Jump up to collect the red coins below the sixth and ninth Boo Guys. After 
passing the second set of Boo Guys, continue right and jump up to the path at 
the other side of the water. Pass through the middle ring, and continue right 
to the third set of blue doors in the area. Go through the blue doors.

After arriving in the third area, jump up the step on the left and run along 
until you see the red arrows above. Stop under the right red arrow, and wait 
for the Clawdaddy to scuttle in from the left. When the Clawdaddy gets close, 
quickly jump over him and run left to the wall. Jump up the two small platforms 
at the end of the first tunnel, and then jump up to the tunnel on the right.

Collect the top row of red coins as you run right, and then jump up the two 
small platforms at the end of the second tunnel. Jump up to the tunnel on the 
left, and run left until you see the Clawdaddy. Shoot three eggs to defeat the 
Clawdaddy, and then run left to the blue doors at the end of the tunnel. Hit 
the egg block above to refill the egg supply, and then go through the blue 
doors.

After arriving in the fourth area, jump up the big step on the left, and walk 
left to the edge. Shoot an egg at the winged cloud on the left, and cross over 
to the other side of the new bridge. Shoot the next winged cloud, and run over 
the second new bridge. At the other side of the second bridge, shoot an egg 
down and left to collect the fourth flower.

                                   - Flower 5 -

Shoot an egg up at the winged cloud on the left, and run over to the other side 
of the third new bridge. At the other side of the third bridge, shoot an egg up 
at the winged cloud to receive five stars, and then continue left to come to a 
pink rotating platform. Jump onto the pink rotating platform and ride it left 
along the wire to collect the fifth flower. At the end of the wire, jump off to 
the left and go through the blue doors.

After arriving in the fifth area, pass through the middle ring on the right. 
Jump up the first step and eat the Frog Pirate at the top. Jump up the next two 
steps, and quickly eat the Frog Pirate nearby at the top of the third step. On 
the fifth step, jump over the Dizzy Dandy that immediately rolls toward you, 
and then jump up the next three small steps to the red doors at the top. Enter 
the red doors.

                         - Boss Fight 5: Prince Froggy -

Run right at the start of the area and Kamek will shrink Yoshi. A Frog Pirate 
will then eat Yoshi. In the stomach, avoid the acid drops, and eat the huge Shy 
Guys that drop down. When Yoshi has an egg, shoot it up at the uvula, and the 
stomach will shrink. Shoot the uvula six times to defeat Prince Froggy.

~~ Items ~~

1UP
  In the second area, go through the second blue door. Shoot the bucket up on 
  the left and it will fall into the water. Jump on the bucket and hold left to 
  travel across the water to the other side. Hover jump up through the steps at 
  the other side and shoot the winged cloud for the 1UP.

Flower 1
  In the second area, go through the first blue door. On the other side, jump 
  over the gaps on the right and go through the blue door to arrive in a room 
  with two Claw Daddys. Defeat both Claw Daddys to reveal the flower.

Flower 2
  Below the second Ball and Chain in the second area.

Flower 3
  Run past the second blue door in the second area and jump on the tiny pink 
  rotating platform on the other side. Ride the platform right and shoot the 
  first winged cloud to reveal the flower.

Flower 4
  In the fourth area, don't shoot the third winged cloud. Instead, get close to 
  the edge where the bridge would normally be built and shoot an egg down and 
  left to collect the flower.

Flower 5
  In the fourth area, ride the pink rotating platform left over the thorns to 
  collect the flower.

2 Red Coins
  In the first area, run right and shoot the bottom-right blue thorn to reveal 
  a winged cloud. Shoot the winged cloud and go through the blue doors that are 
  revealed. Hit the metamorphosis bubble to transform into a submarine, and 
  swim down and left to the ball and chain. There are two red coins around the 
  ball and chain: One at the right side and one at the top.

1 Red Coin
  Above the second gap in the second area.

1 Red Coin
  Above the third gap in the second area.

1 Red Coin
  Above the fluff at the right side of the first blue door in the second area.

2 Red Coins
  Above the third Ball and Chain in the second area.

3 Red Coins
  In the second area, go through the first blue door. On the other side, go 
  right to find these three red coins above the water.

3 Red Coins
  In the second area, go through the second blue door. On the other side, go 
  left to find these three red coins above the water.

4 Red Coins
  Run past the second blue door in the second area and jump on the tiny pink 
  rotating platform on the other side. Ride the platform to find the red coins.

3 Red Coins
  In the third area, these coins can be found after the first Claw Daddy. 
  Collect the top row of coins.

5 Stars
  Run past the second blue door in the second area and jump on the tiny pink 
  rotating platform on the other side. Ride the platform right and shoot the 
  second winged cloud for the stars.

5 Stars
  In the second area, go through the first blue door. On the other side, jump 
  over the gaps on the right and jump up through the red steps. Shoot the 
  winged cloud up on the right for the stars.

10 Stars
  In the second area, pass through the middle ring before the third blue door.

5 Stars
  Shoot the winged cloud at the right side of the pink rotating platform in the 
  fourth area.

10 Stars
  Pass through the middle ring at the start of the fifth area.

===============================================================================
                       Level 3-5: Jammin' Through The Trees
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Hit the egg block at the start of the level to refill the egg supply, and jump 
the gap on the right to land on the yellow fluff. Quickly eat the Grinder that 
starts to bounce away, and continue right to come to a fluff wall. Don't go 
near it just yet, as there's a Short Fuse up above. When the Short Fuse creates 
the gap under the wall, run through the gap and jump out the other side.

Stand on the blue block, and wait for the second Short Fuse to create a gap 
under the next wall. Run through the next gap and jump out the other side to 
land near an egg block. Stand under the egg block and shoot an egg through the 
fluff wall on the right to hit the Grinder. Run through the gap in the wall 
created by the egg to arrive near a tulip. Shoot an egg up at the Grinder on 
the left, the Seedy Sally up on the right, and then face toward the tulip.

Jump up, and shoot an egg down into the tulip to receive eight stars. Shoot an 
egg through the wall on the right and pass through the gap. On the other side, 
shoot an egg at the Grinder with the watermelon, and then eat the Potted Spiked 
Fun Guy that bounces toward you. Shoot an egg up at the winged cloud above, and 
shoot another egg in the same direction to collect the first flower.

                                   - Flower 2 -

Jump up to collect the two red coins, and then jump over to land near the fluff 
wall on the right. Shoot an egg straight through the wall so that it hits the 
next fluff wall on the right as well. Pass through the first gap and eat the 
Grinder that hops toward you. Hit the egg block to refill the egg supply, and 
then go through the next gap on the right. Jump up the two fluff steps, and 
shoot an egg up and right to collect the second flower.

                                   - Flower 3 -

Shoot an egg up and right to collect the red coin in the trail and hit a winged 
cloud for five stars. Jump up through the gap in the fluff and collect the five 
stars. Jump down to the right and face left. Eat the Grinder, and then shoot an 
egg down and left to collect the red coin below. Run right along the fluff, 
eating any of the Gustys that get too near, and jump the gap to land on a path 
at the start of a tunnel. Run right through the tunnel to exit the first area.

After arriving in the second area, run right under the Short Fuse in the tree, 
and eat the Grinder near the post. Jump over the post, and then jump onto the 
pink rotating platform. Shoot an egg up at the Short Fuse up on the right, and 
then hover jump off when the platform is at the top-right corner. Hover over 
the next rotating platform with the Shy Guys on it, and land on the red and 
yellow horizontally moving platform on the other side.

When the platform moves over to the right, shoot an egg up at the Short Fuse in 
the tree, and then jump over to the next pink rotating platform. Jump off at 
the top-right corner and pass through the middle ring above the egg plant. Drop 
down to the grass ledge on the right, and then jump over to the pink rotating 
platform at the bottom of the mud slope.

Eat the Short Fuse when the platform goes to the highest point, and then stay 
on the platform to collect a red coin. Hover jump off to the right when the 
platform goes to the lowest point, and collect the two red coins before landing 
on the tiny pink rotating platform. Stay on the rotating platform to collect a 
red coin, and then jump off at the right side to land on some blocks.

Run right along the blocks and jump up the three steps. Jump over the gap, and 
then jump over the high block. On the other side of the high block, eat the 
Grinder in the vines. Jump over the post and hit the Grinder on the other side 
of the gap. Eat the watermelon that the Grinder was carrying, and jump back 
over the gap to the top of the post on the left. Stomp the post four times, and 
then shoot a watermelon seed left to collect the third flower.

                                   - Flower 4 -

Run right down the step and fall into the gap to collect four red coins. Jump 
over the gap on the left, and then jump up to the block on the left. Jump right 
over the gap, and jump over the next block to see the flower. Jump up the small 
step and walk near the edge of the block. Bounce an egg off the wall to collect 
the fourth flower. Jump over the gap on the right and go through the tunnel at 
the top of the steps.

                                   - Flower 5 -

After arriving in the third area, walk right and drop off the edge of the block 
to land on a lower block. Hit the egg block to refill the egg supply, and then 
go right to drop off the edge of this block. Hover left to land on a path at 
the start of a tunnel. Run left through the tunnel to enter a secret area.

After arriving in the secret area, collect the two eggs on the left, and then 
face right. Shoot an egg up in the direction of the red arrow to reveal a 
winged cloud. Shoot the winged cloud, and jump on the red switch that is 
revealed. Quickly jump up the three red block platforms, and jump left from the 
third red block platform to land on the green platform.

Stay on the platform as it goes along the wire, and shoot eggs at the six Fly 
Guys that appear holding 1UPs. Near the end of the wire, shoot eggs at the two 
Fly Guys holding winged clouds to receive ten stars. At the end of the wire, 
the platform will drop you back down to the start of the area. Go right through 
the tunnel to exit the secret area.

After returning to the third area, jump over the gap to the block with the 
small spring ball, and use the spring ball to bounce up to the block on the 
left. Hit the egg block to refill the egg supply, and then jump up the two 
trees on the right. Jump over the gap under the high tree to the next tree on 
the right, and jump over the next two gaps to land on two trees at the left 
side of a Wild Ptooie Pirahna.

Shoot three eggs at the Wild Ptooie Pirahna, and jump over the post to collect 
the two red coins. After landing on the two trees on the other side of the 
post, quickly shoot the Fly Guy holding the 1UP that appears above the second 
Wild Ptooie Pirahna. Walk right to the second tree and shoot three eggs down 
and right to defeat the second Wild Ptooie Pirahna.

Jump down to the tree on the right, and then jump over the post on the right to 
collect two red coins. After landing on the tree on the other side of the 
second Wild Ptooie Pirahna post, jump left and land on the tree below the post. 
Hover jump right over the gap to collect the two red coins, and then jump up to 
the high tree on the right. Jump right to land on the block with the red arrow 
pointing right.

Run right along the block and drop down onto the path. Eat the Shy Guys at the 
left side of the pipe, and then eat the Seedy Sally in the left tree. Jump on 
top of the pipe, and quickly eat the Seedy Sally in the tree above before the 
Needlenose gets thrown down. From the pipe, jump up to the tree on the right, 
and shoot the nearby winged cloud to receive five stars. Collect the stars, and 
then jump back onto the tree at the right side of the pipe.

Jump up to the tree on the left, and then jump two trees on the right. On the 
highest tree, jump over to the block on the right. Jump up the next two blocks 
on the right, eating the Shy Guy on each one. From the third block, jump to the 
top of the tree with the two Short Fuses below. Jump over to the taller tree on 
the right, and then jump over the gap to land on the thin block. Walk off the 
left side of the thin block to fall through a gap onto a small block below. 
Face left on the small block, and shoot an egg down and left to collect the 
fifth flower.

Jump up to the block on the left, and shoot an egg at the Short Fuses in the 
tree above. Shoot an egg at the Short Fuses in the tree above the block on the 
left, and jump over the gap to land on the block. Jump over to the small block 
on the left, and then jump right to land on top of the tree. Jump onto the next 
tree on the right, and then jump over the thin block to land on top of a tree 
with a Shy Guy. Eat the Shy Guy, and drop down the trees on the right to land 
near the goal ring. Jump through the goal ring to compete the level.

~~ Items ~~

1UP * 6
  At the start of the third area, walk right and drop off the edge of both 
  blocks. Hover left off the second block, and walk left through the tunnel to 
  enter a secret area. Shoot an egg up and right in the direction of the red 
  arrow to reveal a winged cloud. Shoot the winged cloud and jump on the red 
  switch. Jump up the red block platforms to the green platform, and ride the 
  green platform to find the Fly Guys that carry the 1UPs.

1UP
  In the third area, shoot the Fly Guy that appears above the second Wild 
  Ptooie Pirahna.

Flower 1
  In the first area, shoot the first winged cloud.

Flower 2
  In some fluff near the end of the first area.

Flower 3
  Near the end of the second area, stomp the post four times, face left and 
  shoot a watermelon seed through the gap to collect the flower.

Flower 4
  Near the end of the second area, under a block. Bounce an egg off the block 
  on the right to collect the flower.

Flower 5
  Near the end of the third area. The flower is under the tall tree with the 
  Short Fuses on it, after the three small blocks.

2 Red Coins
  In the first area, there is a red coin at either side of the first winged 
  cloud.

2 Red Coins
  In the first area, there are two sets of three coins shortly after the second 
  flower: One set is near the bottom of the screen and one set is at the top. 
  Collect the middle coins.

2 Red Coins
  Near the start of the second area, the top two coins between the two pink 
  rotating platforms.

4 Red Coins
  In the second area, there are four red coins between the first two pink 
  rotating platforms after the middle ring.

4 Red Coins
  In the second area, drop down the gap in the blocks shortly after the third 
  flower to find these coins.

2 Red Coins
  In the third area, at the left side of the first Wild Ptooie Pirahna.

2 Red Coins
  In the third area, above the second Wild Ptooie Pirahna.

2 Red Coins
  In the third area, above the trees below the second Wild Ptooie Pirahna.

8 Stars
  Shoot an egg into the red tulip near the start of the first area.

5 Stars
  In the first area, there is an egg block shortly before the second flower. 
  Shoot the highest part of the fluff near the right side of the egg block to 
  reveal a winged cloud, which contains the stars.

10 Stars
  Pass through the middle ring above the egg plant in the second area.

10 Stars
  At the start of the third area, walk right and drop off the edge of both 
  blocks. Hover left off the second block, and walk left through the tunnel to 
  enter a secret area. Shoot an egg up and right in the direction of the red 
  arrow to reveal a winged cloud. Shoot the winged cloud and jump on the red 
  switch. Jump up the red block platforms to the green platform, and ride the 
  green platform. Near the end of the ride, two Fly Guys appear holding clouds. 
  Shoot the Fly Guys to receive the stars.

5 Stars
  Near the end of the third area, shoot the winged cloud before the red switch.

===============================================================================
                      Level 3-6: The Cave Of Harry Hedgehog
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Go right along the grass path at the start of the level, and jump on top of the 
first tree on the mud slope. Jump up to the higher tree on the left, and then 
hover jump right to the tree at the right side of the area. Jump up to the 
higher tree on the right, and collect the four red coins above the log platform 
before going through the tunnel on the right. In the cave, jump up to collect 
the first flower.

                                   - Flower 2 -

After collecting the first flower, walk right and drop off the ledge to land 
near a large spring ball below. Jump up to collect the key on top of the 
mushroom on the right, and then use the large spring ball to bounce up to the 
high path on the right. Shoot an egg into the tulip above the left side of the 
path for eight stars, and then drop off the right edge of the path.

Hit the nearby egg block to refill the egg supply, and then use the platform on 
the right to jump up to the next path. The first Harry Hedgehog in the game 
appears on this path, so watch out for a fast moving tiny blue object. Quickly 
eat Harry Hedgehog before he becomes large, and then continue along the path to 
come to three mushrooms.

Jump up to the highest mushroom, and then shoot an egg up at the winged cloud 
above to reveal some red steps. Run left up the steps and jump on to the path 
at the top. Jump up to the first mushroom on the path and collect the two red 
coins, and then jump over to the next mushroom on the left. Shoot the winged 
cloud above the mushroom to receive five stars, and then continue left along 
the path. At the left side of the path, jump up to collect the two red coins 
and the second flower.

                                   - Flower 3 -

Run right along the path and descend the red steps to arrive near Chomp Rock. 
Walk up to Chomp Rock and push it down the series of sloped tunnels to the path 
at the bottom. Push Chomp Rock right along the final path until it comes to the 
wall at the end. Jump on Chomp Rock and then hop up to the yellow platform. 
Jump up the next five yellow platforms above, and then go left from the highest 
platform. Shoot an egg up at the winged cloud, and climb the beanstalk that is 
revealed.

At the top of the beanstalk, jump up the four yellow platforms, and then jump 
over the block on the left to land on the tiny yellow platform on the other 
side. Don't hit the metamorphosis bubble just yet. Instead, collect the red 
coin under the highest tiny yellow platform on both sides of the bubble. To do 
this, walk off the edge of the platform and then hover toward the coin. When 
both red coins have been collected, jump over to the metamorphosis bubble.

After transforming into the Mole Tank, hold right to enter the maze. Go down at 
the first junction in the maze, and dig right along the tunnel to collect four 
red coins. Go up at the end of the tunnel to collect the third flower. Continue 
following the tunnels in the maze (ignoring the tunnel which has the three 
normal coins in it), to hit the Yoshi Block.

                                   - Flower 4 -

After Yoshi has returned to normal, walk right and jump onto the large spring 
ball. Bounce once to remove the yellow block above, and then bounce again to 
land on the high yellow platform above. Hit the yellow block above the 
platform, and jump up to collect the yellow egg. Shoot an egg up at the Lantern 
Ghost on the mushroom, and then jump over to the first mushroom. Jump down the 
next two mushrooms, and jump right from the third mushroom to land on the path.

Walk slightly up the slope of the path and hit the egg block to refill the egg 
supply. Continue up the slope to the top, and shoot an egg at the winged cloud 
above the receive five stars. Collect the stars, and then jump through the 
middle ring over on the right. Drop down the two steps at the right side of the 
path, and then jump right to collect the fourth flower. Immediately after 
collecting the fourth flower, hover up to the mushroom on the right, collecting 
the three red coins along the way.

                                   - Flower 5 -

Jump up to the higher mushroom on the right, and then jump right and follow the 
line of coins to collect the final three red coins. After landing on the 
mushroom with the locked door, ignore the door and jump off the right side of 
the mushroom to land near a green pipe below. Jump on top of the green pipe and 
go down it to arrive in a secret area.

In the secret area, shoot the winged cloud and jump on the red switch that is 
revealed. Run right, jumping up to collect the many coins along the way, and 
jump on the next red switch at the far right side of the area. Jump up onto the 
platform made of three red blocks, and then jump left up the next long red 
block platform. Run left along the red blocks, and jump over the blocks at the 
end to collect the fifth flower.

After collecting the fifth flower, jump over the blocks on the right and go up 
the pipe at the far left side of the area. After returning to the cave, hover 
jump left from the top of the pipe to land on a tall mushroom. Go through the 
door with the keyhole in it. Outside the cave, run right along the blocks and 
jump through the goal ring to complete the level.

~~ Items ~~

Flower 1
  In the first area, run right and jump up to the fourth treetop. Hover jump 
  right over to the next treetop, and then jump up to the platform on the 
  right. Run right along the platform and go through the tunnel to arrive in a 
  high entrance to the cave. Go right to collect the flower.

Flower 2
  Near the start of the cave section, there is a winged cloud above three 
  mushrooms. Shoot the winged cloud and climb the steps. Run left at the top of 
  the steps to find the flower.

Flower 3
  After jumping up the five yellow platforms about half-way through the cave 
  section, jump up to the high yellow platform on the left. Shoot the winged 
  cloud and climb the beanstalk that is revealed. Climb the yellow platforms 
  above the beanstalk and touch the metamorphosis bubble to transform into the 
  mole tank. After dropping down to the path below, dig right through the fluff 
  maze to collect the flower.

Flower 4
  After passing the middle ring, run down the two small steps on the right and 
  jump off the edge of the path to collect the flower.

Flower 5
  After jumping up the five yellow platforms about half-way through the cave 
  section, jump over the pipe on the right and run down the slope to drop down 
  to a path. Run right all the way along to the end of the path and go down the 
  Lantern Ghost pipe. In the secret area, shoot the winged cloud. Jump on the 
  red switch and follow the red block platforms up and along to the flower.

4 Red Coins
  In the first area, run right and jump up to the fourth treetop. Hover jump 
  right over to the next treetop, and then jump up to the platform on the 
  right, where the four red coins can be found.

4 Red Coins
  Near the start of the cave section, there is a winged cloud above three 
  mushrooms. Shoot the winged cloud and climb the steps. At the top of the 
  steps, run left to find these red coins above the mushrooms.

4 Red Coins
  There are four red coins under the third flower in the fluff maze.

2 Red Coins
  On the way to the third flower, there is one red coin on either side of the 
  metamorphosis bubble.

3 Red Coins
  After collecting the fourth flower, hover to collect the red coins.

3 Red Coins
  After collecting the fourth flower, hover right to land on the lowest of the 
  two mushrooms. Jump up to the high mushroom and then jump right. Follow the 
  trail of coins to collect the red coins.

8 Stars
  In the cave section. Below the first flower, there is a large spring ball. 
  Use the spring ball to bounce up to a high ledge on the right, where a tulip 
  can be found. Shoot an egg into the tulip to receive the stars.

5 Stars
  Near the start of the cave section, there is a winged cloud above three 
  mushrooms. Shoot the winged cloud and climb the steps. At the top of the 
  steps, go left and shoot the winged cloud above the second set of mushrooms 
  to receive the stars.

5 Stars
  After jumping up the five yellow platforms about half-way through the cave 
  section, jump over the pipe on the right and run down the slope to land on a 
  mushroom near a winged cloud. Shoot the winged cloud for the stars.

5 Stars
  Shoot the winged cloud shortly before the middle ring. The location of the 
  middle ring is shown below.

10 Stars
  Dig through the fluff maze where the third flower is located and touch the 
  Yoshi block at the other side. Use the large spring ball to bounce up through 
  the yellow egg block to the yellow platform above. Jump across the mushrooms 
  and run right along the path to pass through the middle ring.

Key
  In the first area, run right and jump up to the fourth treetop. Hover jump 
  right over to the next treetop, and then jump up to the platform on the 
  right. Run right along the platform and go through the tunnel to arrive in 
  the cave. Go right and drop down to the path below. The key will be above a 
  mushroom up on the right.

Red Switch
  There are two red switches in the secret area with the fourth flower.

===============================================================================
                        Level 3-7: Monkeys' Favorite Lake
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Run right through the water at the start of the level, and jump up to the mud 
platform. Go right along the platform and jump over the water to the next mud 
platform. Jump over the Shy Guy on Stilts on the right, and paddle through the 
water to the mud slope. Jump onto the mud slope, and then jump up to the grass 
path on the right. Drop down off the right side of the path and eat the 
Grinder, and then shoot an egg up at the winged cloud on the right to receive 
five stars.

Walk down into the water on the right, and jump up to the green rotating 
platform nearby. Move the platform right through the water, and stop after 
passing the second Flopsy Fish. Move the platform slowly right, and watch the 
swinging Grinders above. When the Grinders swing left or right, jump off of the 
platform, collect the first flower, and land back on the green platform before 
the Swingers get too near.

                                   - Flower 2 -

Continue moving the rotating platform all the way over to the right side of the 
water. Jump over to the block on the right, and then jump up the steps to the 
block at the top. Drop down into the gap between the blocks to reveal a winged 
cloud. Shoot the winged cloud, and jump on the red switch that is revealed. 
Quickly run back to the left and drop down two steps to stand above the red 
arrow pointing down. Press down on the red arrow to enter the secret area.

After arriving in the secret area, touch the metamorphosis bubble to transform 
into the submarine. Swim down and shoot missiles at the two Preying Mantas. Go 
right near the bottom of the area, and swim up after the block to collect two 
red coins. Swim right and swim up the next gap to find a red coin in a group of 
four coins. Continue right and collect the final two red coins in the area 
before swimming up to the Yoshi Block. After transforming into Yoshi, use the 
large spring ball on the left to exit the secret area. After returning to the 
first area, run right and go through the tunnel.

After arriving in the second area, run right and drop into the water. Shoot the 
winged cloud above the right side of the water to receive five stars, and then 
jump up the mud slope to the small grass path at the top. On the grass path, 
eat the nearby Shy Guy and quickly shoot an egg at the Fly Guy holding the red 
coin up on the right before he flies away.

Drop down onto the first post in the water to collect the red coin. From the 
first post, shoot three eggs at the Clawdaddy on the second post to defeat him. 
Jump over to the second post and shoot an egg up at the winged cloud to reveal 
a beanstalk. Jump up to the highest leaf of the beanstalk, and jump right onto 
the blocks to collect the second flower.

                                   - Flower 3 -

After collecting the third flower, hit the nearby egg block to refill the egg 
supply, and then walk left to drop down onto the second leaf of the beanstalk. 
Walk right to drop onto the post below, and shoot an egg diagonally up and 
right to hit the two Short Fuses in the vines. Drop into the water and run 
right to arrive on a small platform. Shoot an egg up at the winged cloud on the 
right to reveal five stars, and then continue right under the Short Fuse to the 
second platform in the water.

From the second platform, run right under the two Short Fuses in the vines 
above, and jump up to the post at the right side of the water. Jump from the 
post over to the trees on the right, and run along to the far right tree to 
arrive near the Claw Daddy. Although you could shoot eggs to defeat the Claw 
Daddy, there is an easier way. When the Claw Daddy shuffles over to the left 
side of the platform he stands on, jump on top of the Claw Daddy, and then 
quickly hover jump right to land on the nearby trees.

After passing the Claw Daddy, run right to the third tree. There will be a 
Seedy Sally up in the first vine on the right. Move close to the edge of the 
tree, and shoot an egg up and right at the Seedy Sally. The egg should hit the 
winged cloud on the other side of the Seedy Sally, which will cause a beanstalk 
to be revealed. Climb up the beanstalk to the highest leaf, and jump straight 
up to enter a secret area.

After arriving in the secret area, run right along the trees and ignore the two 
green watermelons surrounded by the four coins. Near the end of the flat path 
of trees, a Grinder will bounce toward you. Eat the Grinder, and then drop down 
slightly to the lower tree. Jump up the three tree steps on the right and 
collect the red coin at the top. Run down the next two tree steps and collect 
the red coin on the right. At the end of the path of trees, jump the large gap 
and collect the red coin after landing. Jump right to collect the third flower.

                                   - Flower 4 -

Walk right slightly onto the third of the high trees, and jump up to collect 
the red coin above. Hover jump right to find a large coin arrow. After dropping 
down from the first jump, hover again to collect the red coin at the right tip 
of the arrow. Jump up to the high trees and walk right to find an egg block and 
two winged clouds. Shoot the first winged cloud for five stars, and the second 
winged cloud for a 1UP. Hit the egg block to refill the egg supply, and then 
drop off the end of the tree on the right to exit the secret area.

After returning to the second area, walk slowly right until the Dizzy Dandy 
rolls toward you. Don't drop down to the lower tree, and the Dizzy Dandy will 
roll through the gap into the water. When the first Dizzy Dandy has gone, drop 
down to the lower tree and hop up to the higher one on the right to see a 
second Dizzy Dandy. Walk to the far right edge of this tree, and the Dizzy 
Dandy will roll into the water.

When the Spear Guy up on the tree on the right faces right, quickly jump up to 
the tree and eat him. Two lines of coins will be just above. Jump right to 
collect the two red coins in the middle of the top line. After landing on the 
tree below, walk right and jump over to the next tree on the right, avoiding 
the Dizzy Dandy as it rolls under you. Jump up to eat the Spear Guy as he faces 
right, and land on the higher tree with the six coins above. Jump over the gap 
to the trees down on the right.

Shoot the winged cloud at the right side of the two trees to receive five 
stars, and then drop down to the low trees below. Use the large spring ball 
partially hidden in the far right tree to bounce up to the blocks on the right. 
Walk right along the blocks and jump onto the post. Face left on the post and 
watch the Spear Guy down on the left.

When the Spear Guy below walks into the post and faces left, quickly stomp the 
post four times and eat the Spear Guy before he turns around. Go left and 
collect the two red coins. Return to the post and stomp it two times. Watch the 
two Spear Guys on the left. When they face left, stomp the post a third time 
and then quickly eat both Spear Guys. Run left to collect the fourth flower.

                                   - Flower 5 -

Go back to the post on the right and watch the two Spear Guys down on the left. 
When they Spear Guys walk left, quickly stomp the post four times and walk 
right to drop down to the lowest red bridge. Nearby on the right, the Barney 
Bubble will make his first appearance in the game. This strange creature shoots 
bubbles when jumped on, which can be used in defeating other enemies. Shoot an 
egg at this Barney Bubble, and continue right to the trees under the bridge.

Jump up to the far right tree, and watch the Barney Bubble above. When the 
Barney Bubble walks over to the left, jump up to the first bridge above, and 
then quickly jump up two bridges to the third bridge. Go left on the third 
bridge to pass through the middle ring, and then run right along the bridge to 
exit the second area.

After arriving in the third area, run right and slide down the mud slope to the 
water at the bottom. Jump onto the floating orange platform in the water, and 
collect the two red coins above. Jump over to the small grass path on the 
right, and eat the Shy Guy that is shuffling about. Go over to the right side 
of the path to discover the Lunge Fish in the nearby water. Hover jump over the 
Lunge Fish and land on the small section of mud path.

Jump from the mud path over to the first floating platform in the water, and 
the second Lunge Fish will disappear under the water. Quickly jump from the 
floating platform and hover over to the block at the right side of the water. 
After landing on the block, face left and drop back into the water. As soon as 
Yoshi lands in the water, hold right to swim under the block. On the other side 
of the block, swim right through the red coin to arrive near the flower. Jump 
out of the water to collect the fifth flower.

After collecting the fifth flower, shoot an egg at the winged cloud on the 
right and collect the key that is revealed. Jump up the tiny step on the right 
and press up to enter the hut for a bonus game. After exiting the hut, hit the 
egg block on the left to refill the egg supply. Jump on top of the egg block, 
and jump up to the trees above. Run right along the trees and jump up to the 
block. Continue right along the block to arrive on some trees.

Jump over the Dizzy Dandy that rolls toward you from the far right tree, and 
then jump down to the grass path on the right. Jump up to the large post on the 
path, and shoot an egg down at the Lunge Fish in the water on the right. When 
the Lunge Fish has been hit, quickly drop down into the water between the two 
floating platforms, and jump straight up. In the air, shoot an egg straight up 
at the winged cloud between the two blocks above to receive a 1UP.

Swim right through the water and jump up to the post on the small mud platform 
at the other side. Shoot the winged cloud up on the right to receive five 
stars, and then jump to land at the far right side of the water. Collect the 
red coin, and then quickly jump out onto the post on the next mud platform 
before the Lunge Fish gets too near.

Hover jump over the next section of water to land on a tall post at the next 
mud platform. Shoot the Lunge Fish in the water, and then jump from the post to  
the middle of the water to collect the final red coin. Jump out of the water to 
the mud path on the right. Eat the Shy Guy walking on the grass path nearby, 
and then run right to find the goal ring. Jump through the goal ring to 
complete the level.

~~ Items ~~

  In the second area, shoot the winged cloud before the first Dizzy Dandy, and

  winged cloud at the right side of this area to receive the 1UP.

  jump on the red switch. Run left and press down on the red arrow to arrive in 
  a room with a metamorphosis bubble. Touch the bubble to transform into a 
  submarine and then swim through the water to find the coins.

  In the second area, jump up to the grass platform after the first lake, and

5 Stars
  In the first area, shoot the winged cloud above the start of the second lake.

3 Stars
  In the second area, shoot the winged cloud above the first lake.

  In the second area, shoot the winged cloud shortly after the second flower.

5 Stars
  In the second area, shoot the winged cloud shortly before the first Dizzy 
  Dandy, and climb to the top of the beanstalk to arrive in a secret area. 
  Shoot the left winged cloud at the right side of this area for the stars.

5 Stars
  In the second area, shoot the winged cloud near the large spring ball shortly 
  before the middle ring.

10 Stars
  Pass through the middle ring at the end of the second area.

5 Stars
  In the third area, shoot the winged cloud above the fifth Lunge Fish.

  Shoot the winged cloud shortly after the fifth flower.

===============================================================================
                        Level 3-8: Naval Pirahnas' Castle
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Run right along the blocks at the start of the level and go down the pipe. 
After arriving in the first area of the castle, run right to find a Caged Ghost 
which shoots out Shy Guys. Eat the Shy Guys until Yoshi has six eggs, and then 
shoot the Caged Ghost, following it as it backs down the tunnel. After the 
ghost has been reduced to a small blob, jump over it and pass through the 
paddles on the right.

On the other side of the paddles, wait for the Hootie the Blue Fish to go down 
through the log platform nearby. When the fish has passed by, run right and 
jump over the gap to the top white platform. Continue right to arrive in a room 
with two Hootie the Blue Fish. Eat the two Ravens that scurry toward you, and 
then run right under the block that the fish are orbiting. Jump up the two 
white platforms at the right side of the block, and collect the red coin, which 
is the middle coin of the three.

Drop off the left side of the block, and run left to the edge of the white 
platform. Drop down to the white platform below, and then run to the edge of 
the next white platform to see a waterfall over on the right. Drop down to the 
white platform below, and then go left at the junction to drop down to another 
white platform. Drop down off the various white platforms below, and go left to 
arrive in a room with four coins in it. Collect the two left red coins in this 
room, and then exit the room.

Jump up the five white platforms above to return to the waterfall. This time, 
go right at the waterfall to slide down a steep slope. At the bottom of the 
slope, ignore the first Pirahna Plant on the ceiling, jump over the second 
Pirahna Plant, and then just run under the third Pirahna Plant. After passing 
the three Pirahna Plants, continue right to exit the first area.

After arriving in the second area of the castle, hit the egg block to refill 
the egg supply, and then walk to the edge of the block on the right. Shoot an 
egg down toward the red arrow on the wall so that it bounces off toward the 
four red coins under the pipe. Jump over to the single pipe on the right, and 
then jump over the next gap to the two pipes. Jump up to the block on the right 
and pass under the message block to find a gap.

Shoot an egg at the thin wall on the right to collect the three red coins under 
the left pipe. Jump over the gap and face left. Shoot an egg at the wall so 
that the egg bounces under the right pipe to collect two red coins and reveal 
the flower. Drop down into the water and swim right to collect the first 
flower.

                                   - Flower 2 -

Swim back to the left and jump out of the gap to land on the right path. Run 
right and hit the egg block after the step to refill the egg supply. Jump up 
the big step on the right, and continue right to the edge of the path. Shoot an 
egg at the wall on the right so that the egg hits the left Pirahna Plant. Jump 
over the gap and face left.

Shoot another egg at the wall on the left so that the egg hits the right 
Pirahna Plant. Drop into the water and swim right to collect three red coins, 
then swim right to collect the second flower. Swim right and jump out of the 
gap to land on the right path, and then go through the pipe on the right to 
exit the second castle area.

                                   - Flower 3 -

After arriving in the third castle area, run right along the first tunnel and 
drop down into the sloped water tunnel at the end. At the bottom of the water 
tunnel, immediately run right to avoid the Hootie the Blue Fish that is lurking 
on the left. Continue to run right to drop down into a wider tunnel. Jump up 
the two white platforms on the right, and then jump right into the gap to 
collect the third flower.

                                   - Flower 4 -

Walk left to exit the gap, and run right after landing on the floor below. Jump 
over the neabry Hootie the Blue Fish, and continue right to the end of the 
tunnel. A Wild Ptooie Pirahna will be over on the right, so don't exit the 
tunnel just yet. Instead, wait for the second plant to shoot a Needlenose 
toward you, and then eat the Needlenose to get an egg.

When Yoshi has six eggs, shoot three eggs to defeat the first Wild Ptooie 
Pirahna. Eat three more Needlenoses, and then defeat the second Wild Ptooie 
Pirahna in the same way. After the second Wild Ptooie Pirahna has been 
defeated, jump over to the platform on the right and pass through the middle 
ring.

After passing through the middle ring, walk off the right side of the white 
platform and drop into the water below. Swim left in the water to the other 
side, and jump up to the white platform to land at the start of a secret path. 
Run down the slope on the left, and stop at the bottom. Eat the Nipper Plant 
and the Aqua Lakitu on the left, and then run under the first Pirahna Plant.

Eat the next Nipper Plant and the second Aqua Lakitu when he appears from the 
water, and continue left under the second Pirahna Plant. Go down the slope in 
the tunnel to find a Hootie the Blue Fish orbiting a block. Wait for the fish 
to move to the left side of the block, and then run left to find a Caged Ghost. 
Shoot six eggs at the Caged Ghost, and jump over the small blob that remains. 
On the other side, face right toward the Caged Ghost. Eat six Shy Guys that the 
ghost spits out, and then continue left along the tunnel.

In the room with the three Hootie the Blue Fish, jump up to the first platform 
when the first fish is at the left side of the block. Jump up to the platform 
above when the second fish is above the block. Jump up to the block on the left 
when the third fish is below the block. From the block, jump up to the start of 
the path on the right, and shoot an egg at the Pirahna Plant. Shoot the winged 
up on the right to receive five stars, and then jump up to the white platform 
on the left to collect the three red coins.

Watch the Hootie the Blue Fish below. When the fish moves to the bottom of the 
block, drop down to the platform at the right side of the block. Jump onto the 
long block, and run off the right edge to drop down to the tunnel below. Run 
right along the tunnel, and stop just before the Caged Ghost, which will start 
spitting out Shy Guys. Eat the Shy Guys until Yoshi has six eggs, and then 
shoot the Caged Ghost six times. Jump over the blob, and face left.

When the Caged Ghost appears, eat six more Shy Guys, and then run right along 
the tunnel. Go up the tunnel and run under the two Pirahna Plants, and then go 
up the next tunnel and drop into the water. Swim right under the two large 
blocks, and jump up to the white platform at the right side of the second 
block. Jump over to the white platform near the tunnel entrance on the right, 
and then jump up two white platforms. Shoot an egg at the Pirahna Plant above, 
and then jump into the tunnel on the right.

Wait at the start of the tunnel for the three Paranipper Plants to drop down 
and transform into Nipper Plants. Eat the three Nipper Plants, and then enter 
the tunnel. Jump up the three white platforms, and jump into the the next 
tunnel leading right. Run along the tunnel, and stop after entering the small 
room. Shoot three eggs at the Wild Ptooie Pirahna over on the right side of the 
room, and then drop down into the room. In the room, eat the Nipper Plants, and 
then run over to the far right side of the room to collect the fourth flower.

                                   - Flower 5 -

Run left to exit the room after collecting the fourth flower, and run left 
through the tunnel. Drop down at the end of the first tunnel, and then run left 
off the white platform at the end of the second tunnel to drop down to a 
slightly longer platform below. Run right from this white platform to land at 
the start of another tunnel.

Run right through this tunnel and jump over the Hootie the Blue Fish near the 
Caged Ghost. Eat the Shy Guys that the Caged Ghost spits out until Yoshi has 
six eggs, and then return to the tunnel on the left. Face right, and wait for 
the Hootie the Blue Fish to pass by. When it does, go back to the right and 
shoot six eggs at the Caged Ghost to defeat it. Jump over the remaining blob, 
and face left on the other side. Eat six more Shy Guys when the Caged Ghost 
appears, and then run along the tunnel on the right.

When the tunnel dips drops down slightly, shoot an egg at the Pirahna Plant, 
and then continue right to the end of the tunnel to arrive near a small room. 
Eat the two Nipper Plants that bounce toward you from the white platform, and 
shoot an egg down and right into the water to defeat the Pirahna Plant. Drop 
into the water and swim right onto the block. Drop into the next small section 
of water and jump up to the higher block on the right.

A Wild Ptooie Pirahna will be down on the right, but the Needlenoses it spits 
can't hit you from the platform. Walk to the middle of the block, and shoot 
three eggs down into the water on the right to defeat the Wild Ptooie Pirahna. 
Drop down into the water on the right and jump over the block to the next 
section of water. Jump up to the white platform, and jump up again to collect 
two red coins and the fifth flower.

After collecting the fifth flower, run down the slope in the tunnel on the 
right, and wait for the three Paranipper Plants to land. Eat the three Nipper 
Plants, and then shoot an egg of the right wall so that it bounces off the 
ceiling into the red tulip. Collect the eight stars from the tulip, and then 
continue right along the tunnel to the red doors. Enter the red doors.

                       - Boss Fight 6: Naval Pirahna -

After sliding down the tunnels and landing in the water, swim right in the 
water and jump up to the far left edge of the white platform. Before Kamek 
appears, shoot the small Pirahna Plant to win the boss fight. To win the boss 
fight fairly, read below:

When Naval Pirahna puts his head down, he will start to charge toward you. Jump 
over him as he charges from right to left, and then face left. He will then 
spit out three Paranipper Plants. Wait for the plants to land, and quickly eat 
the three Nipper Plants to get three eggs.

Jump over Naval Pirahna as he charges from right to left, and then move over to 
the left side of the platform. Shoot an egg so that it bounces off the wall 
into the water, and hits the bump on the pirahna which has the 'X' on it. 
Repeat this process of jumping over Naval Pirahna when he charges and then 
hitting the bump with an egg. Hit the bump three times to defeat Naval Pirahna.

~~ Items ~~

Flower 1
  Shortly after the second message block in the second castle section, jump 
  over the gap, face left and bounce an egg off the left wall to hit the winged 
  cloud, which will reveal the flower. 

Flower 2
  At the end of the second castle section, stay at the left side of the gap and 
  bounce an egg off the wall on the right to hit the Pirahna Plant. Shoot 
  another egg to collect the flower.

Flower 3
  Near the start of the third castle section, run along the tunnel and jump 
  onto the white platform before the two Hootie the Blue Fish. The flower can 
  be found up on the right.

Flower 4
  After passing the middle ring in the third castle section, jump up the 
  platforms on the right and enter the top-right tunnel. Follow the tunnel to 
  the end to find the flower hidden behind a Wild Ptooie Pirahna.

Flower 5
  Near the end of the third castle section. Shortly after the Wild Ptooie 
  Pirahna before the red tulip.

1 Red Coin
  At the top-right corner of the first castle section, near the two Hootie the 
  Blue Fish.

2 Red Coins
  At the bottom-left corner of the first castle section, above some water with 
  an Aqua Lakitu in it.

4 Red Coins
  At the start of the second castle section, under the horizontal green pipe.

3 Red Coins
  Shortly after the second message block in the second castle section, bounce 
  an egg off the right wall to collect the red coins in the water below.

2 Red Coins
  Shortly after the second message block in the second castle section, jump 
  over the gap, face left and bounce an egg off the left wall to collect the 
  red coins in the water below.

3 Red Coins
  At the end of the second castle section, jump over the gap and face left. 
  Bounce an egg off the wall on the left to hit the Pirahna Plant, and shoot 
  another egg to collect the coins.

2 Red Coins
  There is one red coin at either side of the fifth flower.

3 Red Coins
  After passing the middle ring in the third castle section, walk right and 
  drop into the water under the second Wild Ptooie Pirahna. Swim left in the 
  water and jump out at the far left side to land on a platform. Continue left 
  past the various enemies to find the red coins.

10 Stars
  Pass through the middle ring half-way through the third castle section.

5 Stars
  After passing the middle ring in the third castle section, walk right and 
  drop into the water under the second Wild Ptooie Pirahna. Swim left in the 
  water and jump out at the far left side to land on a platform. Continue left 
  past the various enemies to and shoot the winged cloud for the stars.

8 Stars
  In the third castle section, shoot an egg into the red tulip shortly before 
  the red doors to receive these stars.

===============================================================================
                           Extra 3: More Monkey Madness
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Stay still at the start of the level, and eat the Fly Guy to collect a red 
coin. Shoot the two winged clouds above and collect the ten stars, and then 
walk right to the arch of coins. Collect the left and right red coins in the 
arch, and jump up to the post on the right. There are two Grinders on the 
right, happily spitting watermelon seeds at you. Ignore the second Grinder, as 
the seeds will hit the post. Jump up and eat the watermelon that the first 
Gridner holds, and drop down off the right side of the post.

Jump up and shoot a seed at the Grinder on the right, and then jump up to the 
second post. Stomp it once to reveal a red coin. Continue right along the grass 
path and jump up to the red and yellow platform, which will move right to a 
tiny pink rotating platform. Jump onto the rotating platform, and walk as close 
to the right edge as you can. When the platform points down and right, jump up 
to the bigger rotating platform on the right collect the two red coins in the 
line along the way.

Stay on the rotating platform to the top, and the wall will knock you down to a 
lower platform. As soon as this happens, do three small jumps right over to the 
next platforms, staying on the same rotating platform. You should aim to jump 
so quickly so that you land on one of the platform while it's at the right side 
of the wall. After landing, quickly jump up and shoot the Grinder on the vine, 
and then jump up near the right side of the wall to collect the first flower.

                                   - Flower 2 -

After collecting the first flower, jump straight up from the platform to enter 
a secret area. Stomp both crates in the area, and collect the twelve coins. 
Shoot the winged cloud for another five coins, and then drop down the gap at 
the right side of the area to return to the main level. After landing on the 
rotating platform, shoot an egg down and left to collect the second flower.

                                   - Flower 3 -

Jump back over to the manually rotating platform on the right, and immediately 
jump up to collect the Grinder in the vines. Move the platform right, and jump 
up to collect the two red coins before the second Grinder. Wait for the second 
Grinder to spit watermelon seeds, and then quickly jump up and eat him. 
Continue moving the platform right to find a third Grinder down below. Just 
above this Grinder, there is a vertical line of seven coins. Jump up to collect 
the red coin before this line, and then push the Tap-Tap off the post on the 
right. Jump onto the post and stomp it three times to collect the third flower.

                                   - Flower 4 -

Shoot an egg at the Tap-Tap on the right, and then jump over to the rotating 
platform. Stay on the platform to see a Fly Guy carrying a red coin at the top-
right corner. Jump on top of the Fly Guy, and he will drop the red coin. Drop 
straight down to collect the red coin as it falls, and then hover left to land 
back on the rotating platform. Stay on the platform and jump near the wall at 
the top to collect the fourth flower.

                                   - Flower 5 -

Jump down to the red and yellow platform, and stay still as it moves right. 
Jump off to the pink vertically moving platform with the egg plant on it, and 
face left. When the platform goes down as far as it can, shoot an egg left to 
collect the two red coins in the line. Face right, and shoot an egg up the 
Grinder. Jump over to the rotating platform on the right, and jump up to the 
horizontally moving platform on the left to collect the red coin in the line.

Hover jump down to the green and white floor near the goal ring, and two Fly 
Guys will appear holding a red coin. Eat both Fly Guys, and collect the two red 
coins. Run right to the goal ring, but don't jump through it. Instead, run past 
the goal ring, and shoot an egg up to collect the fifth and final flower. Run 
back to the left, and jump through the goal ring to complete the level.

~~ Items ~~

Flower 1
  On the right side of the wall above the second rotating platform.

Flower 2
  This flower is down in the gap between the two posts after the first Tap-Tap 
  in the level.

Flower 3
  There is a manually rotating platform about half-way through the level. The 
  third flower is just left at the left side of the post that the Tap-Tap is 
  standing on.

Flower 4
  Jump onto the rotating platform after the third flower, and ride it around to 
  collect the fourth flower at the right side of the wall at the top.

Flower 5
  On the right side of the goal ring.

1 Red Coin
  A Fly Guy appears holding this red coin betwee the two winged clouds at the 
  start of the level.

2 Red Coins
  Walk right from the start of the level to see an arch of coins. The left and 
  right coins in this arch are red coins.

1 Red Coin
  Pound the post just before the second Grinder in the level.

1 Red Coin
  Above the second Grinder in the level, shortly before the first horizontally 
  moving platform.

1 Red Coin
  There are three coins above the first horizontally moving platform. The red 
  coin is the left coin in the line.

2 Red Coins
  At the right side of the first rotating platform in the level, there are four 
  coins leading up and right in a diagonal line. The first and third coins in 
  this line are red coins.

1 Red Coin
  There are three coins on the right side of the wall above the second rotating 
  platform. The left coin, nearest the first flower, is a red coin.

3 Red Coins
  There is a manually rotating platform about half-way through the level. There 
  are red coins above the second, third and fourth Grinders along the platform 
  track.

1 Red Coin
  Jump onto the rotating platform after the third flower, and ride it around to 
  collect the red coin.

1 Red Coin
  Jump onto the rotating platform after the third flower, and ride it around to 
  see a Fly Guy appear holding a red coin. Jump on the Fly Guy and fall down to 
  collect the coin.

2 Red Coins
  Under the first horizontally moving platform after the fourth flower. To 
  collect the red coins, stand on the vertically moving platform further on the 
  right and shoot an egg left.

2 Red Coins
  In the line of coins above the right side of the final horizontally moving 
  platform with the egg plant on it.

2 Red Coins
  Two Fly Guys appear holding red coins on the path to the goal ring.

10 Stars
  Shoot the first and second winged clouds near the start of the level.

12 Stars
  Stomp both crates in the secret area above the first flower.

5 Stars
  Shoot the winged cloud in the secret area above the first flower.

===============================================================================
                            Level 4-1: Go! Go! Mario!!
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Run right at the start of the level and eat the Green Koopa Troopa that is 
standing near the three pipes. Jump up to the second pipe, and shoot the shell 
at the Pirahna Plant on the third pipe. Jump over the gap to the pipe on the 
right, and run down the slope on the other side. About half-way down the slope, 
jump right to land on a platform with two Goombas. Eat both Goombas, and then 
jump off the right side of the platform to collect the first flower.

                                   - Flower 2 -

Drop down to the path after collecting the first flower, and run over the slope 
on the right. Eat the Green Koopa Paratroopa at the top of the slope, and shoot 
the shell down at the nearby Pirahna Plant. Run up the next two slopes on the 
right to find a coin trail at the start of the third slope. Collect the first 
and tenth coins in the coin trail for two red coins, and jump over the Shy Guy 
Pipe at the top of the slope.

On the right side of the Shy Guy pipe, eat the Red Koopa Troopa, and shoot the 
shell at one of the Pirahna Plants on the right. Turn left and eat the Shy Guys 
until Yoshi has six eggs, and then shoot an egg at the remaining Pirahna Plant 
on the right. Jump over the pipe on the right and eat the Goomba on the other 
side.

Continue right to find a winged cloud above two pipes with Red Koopa Troopas on 
top. Eat the nearby Green Koopa Paratroopa, and shoot the shell up at the 
winged cloud to receive five stars. Continue right to find a Wild Ptooie 
Pirahna on the other side of a pipe. When the Wild Ptooie Pirahna shoots a 
Needlenose, quickly jump up to the top of the pipe and go down it.

In the cave, run right and jump over the first two gaps to land near some 
crystals. Eat the Shy Guy hidden in the first crystal, and then jump over the 
next five gaps to collect a red coin above each gap. After landing on the other 
side of the fifth gap, jump up the yellow platforms to the top-right corner of 
the cave.

Run left and jump over the first gap to collect three normal coins, and then 
jump the second gap to collect a red coin. Eat the Shy Guy hidden in the second 
crystal on the path, and jump over the next two gaps to land near the pipe at 
the exit of the cave. Run left under the pipe, and stomp the crate at the top-
left corner of the cave for six stars. Run right and go up the pipe.

After returning to the first area, eat the first Red Koopa Paratroopa on the 
right, and shoot the shell into the tulip on the left for eight stars. Jump 
over the pipe on the right, and run under the remaining Red Koopa Paratroopa. 
Continue right down the two steps on the right, and jump over the first Bullet 
Bill cannon on the path. Drop off the platform at the end of the path, and drop 
down to the next platform on the left to collect a red roin.

Drop off either side of the platform, and run left to find two more platforms, 
each with a red coin on top. Collect the red coins, and then shoot the winged 
cloud above the gap between the platforms to reveal a blue watermelon. Eat the 
watermelon, and run left to find a Beach Koopa walking toward a shell. When he 
jumps into the shell, shoot ice at the Green Koopa Troopa, and then jump left 
to collect the second flower.

                                   - Flower 3 -

Run right after collecting the second flower, jump onto the yellow platform at 
the far right side of the path, and then jump over to the next yellow platform 
on the left. Run left and jump over the first Bullet Bill to land on a yellow 
platform. Shoot ice at the Bullet Bill Cannon on the left, and eat the Fly Guy 
holding the red coin above.

Collect the red coin, and jump up to the next yellow platform on the right. 
Hover jump off the left side of this platform to land on a small section of red 
path. Run to the left side of this path to reveal a winged cloud, and then 
shoot the winged cloud for the stars. After collecting the stars, hover jump 
right to land on the next section of red path.

Eat the Green Koopa Paratroopa on the right, and shoot the shell left. Run 
right and jump to the path above the first Bullet Bill cannon. Drop down off 
the path to land at the right side of the cannon, and collect the red coin in 
the middle of the set of three coins on the right. Jump above the second Bullet 
Bill cannon, and drop down to the path on the right to collect the next red 
coin. Jump over the third Bullet Bill cannon and continue right to exit the 
first area.

After arriving in the second area, jump to the log platform on the right and 
pass through the middle ring. Jump along the platforms near the start of the 
area, and then jump to the red path at the right side of the second see-saw 
platform. Wait for the Red Koopa Paratroopa on the right to fly down, and then 
jump over the gap. Jump up the step, and continue right along the path to the 
end. Drop off the end of the path, and jump left to collect the third flower.

                                   - Flower 4 -

Jump up the big step on the right, and hover jump right over the two Red Koopa 
Paratroopas. Jump up the next two steps, and run right to collect a single egg. 
Eat the Green Koopa Paratroopa, and drop down the next step. Jump over the gap 
to the log platform on the right, and eat the Fly Guy holding the 1UP above. At 
this point, there will be a large number of Fuzzys floating about. Try and 
avoid the various Fuzzys while jumping over the log platforms on the right. 
From the seventh log platform, jump over the two gaps on the right, and 
continue right along the path to exit the second area.

After arriving in the third area, run right along the short path, and jump up 
to the yellow platform at the end. Run down the slope and continue right to 
come to the middle ring. Jump through the middle ring, and then follow the path 
down below the message block. Go left to see a section of yellow fluff above, 
with a Super Star behind it. Shoot an egg off the wall on the left so that it 
bounces through the fluff. Collect the Super Star as it drops down to transform 
into Powerful Mario.

After collecting the first Super Star, run up the slope on the left to collect 
a single red coin. Continue holding left after collecting the second Super Star 
to arrive in an area with the flower. Quickly jump up to collect the fourth 
flower, and then run up the slope to collect the third Super Star.

                                   - Flower 5 -

After collecting the third Super Star, run down the yellow platforms and drop 
down to the path under the Red Koopa Troopas. Jump up to collect the fourth 
Super Star above the red arrows, and then run up the slope on the right to 
collect two red coins. On the path at the top of the slope, jump right to 
collect the fifth Super Star and the fifth flower. Hover right after collecting 
the fifth flower to collect the three red coins, and then drop down to the path 
below. Run right and jump through the goal ring to complete the level.

~~ Items ~~

  In the second area, a Fly Guy appears holding this 1UP above a log platform, 
  about half-way through the Fuzzy section.

  ledge with a large spring ball. Walk to the left side of this ledge, and jump 
  up to reveal a winged cloud. Shoot the winged cloud for the 1UP.

6 Red Coins
  In the first area, go down the pipe just before the Wild Ptooie Pirahna to 
  arrive in a cave. There are five red coins at the bottom level the cave, and 
  one red coin above the second gap at the top level of the cave.

1 Red Coin
  In the first area, a Fly Guy is holding this red coin above the Bullet Bill 
  section.

  Bullet Bill, and drop down to the path on the right. Run left along the path 
  to find the red coins.

2 Red Coins
  Near the end of the first area, there are three coins in each gap between the 
  Bullet Bills. The middle coin in each gap is a red coin.
