  After collecting the first Super Star in the third area, run up the wall on 
  the left to find this red coin.

2 Red Coins
  On the slope shortly before the fifth Super Star in the third area.

3 Red Coins
  After collecting the fifth Super Star in the third area, parachute right 
  along the trail of coins to collect the three red coins.

5 Stars
  In the first area, shoot the winged cloud in the gap between the two pipes, 
  shortly before the Wild Ptooie Pirahna.

6 Stars
  In the first area, go down the pipe just before the Wild Ptooie Pirahna to 
  arrive in a cave. Stomp the crate at the top-left corner of the cave.

8 Stars
  In the first area, shoot an egg into the tulip after the Wild Ptooie Pirahna.

5 Stars
  In the Bullet Bill section of the first area, jump up to the platform at the 
  right side of the top bullet bill, and then hover jump left to land on a 
  small path. Run along the path to reveal a winged cloud, and shoot the winged 
  cloud for the stars.

10 Stars
  Pass through the middle ring near the start of the second area.

10 Stars
  Pass through the middle ring near the start of the third area.

===============================================================================
                        Level 4-2: The Cave Of The Lakitus
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Turn left at the start of the level, and eat the Shy Guys coming out of the 
second pipe until Yoshi has six eggs. Shoot an egg at the Pirahna Plant on the 
far left pipe, and then go down the pipe. After arriving in the first cave 
area, run right under the yellow egg block to find an arrow cloud, with eight 
Koopa Troopa nearby. Shoot an egg at the arrow cloud when it points right to 
collect a 1UP. Go right and pass through the paddles.

On the other side of the paddles, run right and jump over the first gap to 
collect a red coin. Eat the Green Koopa Troopa on the other side of the gap, 
and jump up the big step on the right. Jump over the second gap to collect 
another red coin, and shoot the shell at the nearby Red Koopa Troopa. Jump up 
the next big step, and run down the three sections of red steps to collect 
three red coins.

At the bottom of the steps, run right under the Wall Lakitus and hit the POW 
block just before the Tap-Tap. Shoot the winged cloud above the POW block for 
five stars, and then continue right to find another Tap-Tap shortly before two 
spring balls. Jump up and use Yoshi's tongue to push the Tap-Tap off the right 
side of the ledge. With the Tap-Tap gone, jump over the ledge to land near the 
two spring balls.

Jump on the large spring ball, and bounce very lightly up to the first tunnel 
on the left. Run along the tunnel, and push the crate left to the room at the 
end of the tunnel. In the room, stomp the crate for six stars, and then shoot 
the winged cloud to reveal the first flower. Collect the flower, and then run 
back through the tunnel and drop down to the two spring balls.

                                   - Flower 2 -

After returning to the two spring balls, jump on the right spring ball and 
bounce up to the high path on the left. Run left and jump up on the small 
spring ball on the platform to defeat the Wall Lakitus. Run left and jump up to 
the left pipe. Hover jump right to collect two red coins, then run right and 
drop off the end of the path to land near the two spring balls.

Jump on the right spring ball and follow the coin trail to avoid two Pirahna 
Plants. On the other side of the Pirahna Plants, shoot an egg up at the fluff 
above, and the red switch will drop. Jump on the red switch, and press down on 
the red arrow to enter a secret area.

In the secret area, run right along the path and stop near the end. Use a 
magnifying glass if you have it in your inventory, as it makes it much easier 
to find the red coins in this area. Jump off the right side of the path, and 
follow the coin trail down to find the five red coins. Run right at the bottom 
of the area and go up the pipe.

After returning to the first area, jump up to the path on the left, and hover 
jump left over the Pirahna Plant to land on the small blue fluff platform with 
the red switch. Jump on the red switch, and then bounce right. Hover over the 
top of the post to land in a small area with a Red Koopa Troopa. Shoot the 
winged cloud at the left side of the area to receive a 1UP, and then jump up to 
the yellow platform on the right. Eat the Red Koopa Troopa and shoot the shell 
right to collect the second flower.

                                   - Flower 3 -

Stomp the post once at the right side of the yellow platform, and run left to 
land on the path below. Collect the single egg, and jump up the big step on the 
right. Continue right along the path to find three Pirahna Plants. Run under 
the first Pirahna Plant, shoot an egg at the second Pirahna Plant, and run 
under the third Pirahna Plant. Run through the tunnel on the right to exit the 
first area.

After arriving in the second area, eat the red shell on the right, and spit it 
out. Follow the shell as it moves right, and it will hit a Green Koopa Troopa. 
Follow the green shell right to come to a set of red steps. The green shell 
will enter a room on the right to collect the third flower.

                                   - Flower 4 -

Run down to the bottom of the red steps after collecting the third flower, and 
do a small jump right. Quickly hover jump left to land on the pipe below the 
red steps. Collect the red coin at the right side of the pipe, and then go down 
the pipe to arrive in a secret area with a Fly Guy and a Baron Von Zeppelin.

In the secret area, jump to the platform on the left and collect both eggs. 
Shoot an egg straight up at the Baron Von Zeppelin to collect the key, and 
shoot an egg at the Fly Guy to collect the red coin. Jump to the ledge on the 
right and go up the pipe.

After returning to the second area, jump up to the red steps above, and then 
jump over to the path on the right. Run along the path and enter the hut if you 
want to play a bonus game. Run right after the hut and pass through the middle 
ring shortly after the drop.

Continue right after passing through the middle ring to arrive in a big cave 
section. Collect the first red coin at the start of the cave, and then collect 
the second red coin just before the first red and yellow platform. Jump on the 
platform, and hover jump right to collect the third red coin above the second 
red and yellow platform.

Drop off the right side of the second platform to land on a slope, and then run 
left onto the third red and yellow platform. Drop off the right side of the 
platform to collect the fourth red coin below, and run down the steep slope on 
the left.

After dropping off the slope, hover right to collect the fifth red coin in the 
cave. Run left after landing on the path, and drop on the red and yellow 
platform. When the platform moves left, drop off the right side of the platform 
and hover over the spikes on the right. On the other side of the spikes, shoot 
an egg up into the gap to collect the fourth flower.

                                   - Flower 5 -

Go through the first set of paddles on the right after the fourth flower, and 
run to the middle of the red bridge. Hit the left yellow egg block, and look at 
the arrow cloud on the left. When the arrow cloud points up and left, shoot an 
egg at the arrow cloud above to collect the red coin. Hit the right yellow egg 
block and look at the arrow cloud on the right. When the arrow cloud points up 
and left, shoot an egg at the arrow cloud above to collect the fifth flower. 
Run right through the second set of paddles and jump through the goal ring to 
complete the level.

~~ Items ~~

1UP
  Near the end of the first cave section, a Red Koopa Troopa is walking about 
  on a high yellow platform. Shoot an egg at the right side of the Koopa so 
  that his shell hits the winged cloud on the left.

Flower 1
  There are two spring balls shortly after the POW block in the cave. Use the 
  large spring ball to bounce up to the first tunnel on the left. Run along the 
  tunnel and push the crate down into the larger area. In the room, shoot the 
  winged cloud to reveal the flower.

Flower 2
  Near the end of the first cave section, a Red Koopa Troopa is walking about 
  on a high yellow platform. Shoot an egg at the left side of the Koopa so that 
  his shell collects the flower on the right.

Flower 3
  Near the start of the second area, under the hut. To get this flower, stand 
  on the middle of the pipe under the small set of red steps, and shoot an egg 
  through the gap on the right to collect the flower.

Flower 4
  After the middle ring in the second area, run right to enter a huge room. 
  Hover jump under the horizontally moving platform at the bottom-right corner 
  of the room, and float to the other side of the spikes. The fourth flower is 
  in the gap just before the paddles.

Flower 5
  Near the end of the level, shoot the right arrow cloud to collect the flower.

2 Red Coins
  One red coin is above each of the first two gaps in the first cave section.

3 Red Coins
  Above the red steps that lead down after the first two gaps in the first cave 
  section.

2 Red Coin
  There are two spring balls shortly after the POW block in the first cave 
  section. Use the large spring ball to bounce up to the high path on the left. 
  Run along the path under the Wall Lakitus to find a line of six coins. The 
  left and right coins in the line are red coins.

5 Red Coins
  In the first cave section, shoot the red switch out of the fluff after the 
  two Pirahna Plants, and stomp it to reveal a red arrow. Press down on the red 
  arrow to enter a secret area. Follow the coin trail down to collect the five 
  red coins.

1 Red Coin
  Near the start of the second area, above the pipe under the set of red steps.

1 Red Coin
  Near the start of the second area, go down the pipe under the small set of 
  red steps to arrive in a room with a Fly Guy that holds the red coin.

5 Red Coins
  After the middle ring in the second area, run right to enter a huge room. 
  Follow the red arrows in this room to collect the red coins.

1 Red Coin
  Near the end of the level, shoot the left arrow cloud to collect the flower.

5 Stars
  Above the POW block in the first cave section.

6 Stars
  There are two spring balls after the POW block in the cave. Use the spring 
  ball to bounce up to the first tunnel on the left. Run along the tunnel and 
  push the crate down into the room. Jump on the crate for the stars.

10 Stars
  Pass through the middle ring after the hut in the second area.

5 Stars
  After the middle ring in the second area, run right to enter a huge room. 
  Shoot the winged at the bottom-left corner of the room for the stars.

Key
  Near the start of the second area, go down the pipe under the small set of 
  red steps to arrive in a room with a Baron Von Zeppelin that holds the key.

===============================================================================
                           Level 4-3: Don't Look Back!
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Go right at the start of the level and run under the message block. Jump on the 
single number platform, and jump again to hit the yellow fluff for an egg. Drop 
down to the path below, and jump over to the number platforms on the right. Run 
all the way along the platforms to the post at the end, and wait for a balloon 
to appear. Jump on the balloon, and ride it to collect the first flower.

                                   - Flower 2 -

Continue riding the balloon until you pass the platform. Drop down to the log 
platform, and jump onto the first see-saw log platform on the right. Hover jump 
at the left side of the platform to collect a red coin, and then jump up to the 
second see-saw platform on the right. Jump up to collect two red coins above 
the middle of the platform, and then jump from the third see-saw platform to 
the log platform on the right. Go up the pipe above the middle of the platform.

After arriving in the secret area, drop off the left side of the pipe, and 
shoot the winged cloud to reveal a metamorphosis bubble. Touch the bubble to 
transform into a helicopter, and then fly up. Fly right from the top-left 
corner of the area, and pass through the middle ring to defeat the Wild Ptooie 
Pirahna. Hover up to collect three red coins, and then fly down to the bottom-
right corner of the area to touch the Yoshi block. Go down the pipe on the left 
to exit the area.

After returning to the first area, run right along the log platform and jump 
onto the first number platform. Walk over to the right side of the platform and 
wait for the Bullet Bill to pass by, and then quickly jump right to the second 
platform, and left to the third platform. Jump left to the fourth platform, and 
shoot an egg left to collect the red coin. Wait for the Lava Drop to move 
right, and then jump up to the fifth platform on the right, and the sixth 
platform on the left. Jump up to the number platform above, and jump right to 
collect the second flower.

                                   - Flower 3 -

Hover right after collecting the second flower, and collect the three eggs on 
the platform. Drop off the right side of the platform to land on an enlarge 
block, and then jump right to land on another log platform. Watch the 
vertically moving Red Koopa Paratroopa on the right. When it is at the same 
height as the green shell, quickly shoot an egg at the green shell. To receive 
a 1UP, follow the green shell as it defeats the Red Koopa Paratroopa and the 
seven Red Koopa Troopas.

Jump over the post on the right, and then jump up to the blue platform above. 
Run to the far right side of the platform to avoid being hit by the Needlenose. 
Shoot three eggs at the Wild Ptooie Pirahna, and then jump up to the platform 
on the right. Quickly jump up and eat the Fly Guy to collect the red coin 
before he flies away. Jump up the next two blue platforms, and eat the Red 
Koopa Paratroopa on the right. Jump up to the next blue platform, and walk 
right to find another Wild Ptooie Pirahna.

Walk right, and shoot the red shell at the Red Koopa Paratroopa on the right. 
As there is another platform above, the Needlenoses that the Wild Ptooie 
Pirahna shoots can't reach Yoshi on the left side of the lower platform. One 
out of three Needlenoses will land on the right side of the platform. Walk to 
the right side of the lower platform and eat the Needlenoses that drop down 
until Yoshi has six eggs, and then shoot three eggs up and right to defeat the 
Wild Ptooie Pirahna.

With the Wild Ptooie Pirahna defeated, jump up the next two blue platforms on 
the right, and jump onto the red switch to reveal four red block platforms on 
the left. Jump up to the fourth platform, and hit the egg block to refill the 
egg supply. When Yoshi has six eggs, quickly jump on top of the egg block 
before the red block platforms disappear. Shoot the winged cloud up on the 
left, and then jump left to collect the third flower.

                                   - Flower 4 -

Hover right after collecting the third flower, and land on top of the egg 
block. Jump right to collect the red coin in the middle of the set of three 
coins, and land on the blue platform near the tulip. Drop down to the next 
platform on the right and eat the Red Koopa Troopa, and then jump back up to 
the platform on the left. Stand at the far right side of the platform and face 
left. When the tulip opens, jump up and spit the red shell into the tulip for 
eight stars.

Drop down to the platform on the right, and jump right to the next platform. 
Walk to the far right side of the platform to see the final Wild Ptooie Pirahna 
in this area. Two out of three Needlenoses will drop near enough for Yoshi to 
eat. Eat the Needlenoses until Yoshi has six eggs, and then shoot three eggs 
right to defeat the Wild Ptooie Pirahna. Jump across the two vertically moving 
platforms to land on a grass path. Shoot an egg up to collect the fourth 
flower, and then continue right to exit the first area.

                                   - Flower 5 -

After arriving in the second area, jump through the middle ring, and shoot an 
egg up at the yellow fluff on the right to reveal a large spring ball. Jump on 
the large spring ball to bounce up to the third area.

After arriving in the third area, jump on the large spring ball to land near a 
pump. Jump on top of the pump, and stomp it four times to inflate the balloon. 
Jump on top of the balloon, and ride it as it floats right. As the balloon 
decreases in size, it becomes more difficult to stay on. Try and stay on the 
middle of the ballon to avoid sliding off. Jump up to collect the fifth flower 
about half-way along the balloon journey.

Land back on the balloon after collecting the fifth flower, and eat the Baron 
Von Zeppelin to receive a 1UP. Continue riding the balloon to the end, and 
collect the five red coins shortly before the goal path. Run along the path and 
eat the three Fly Guys holding 1UPs. Continue right and jump through the goal 
ring to complete the level.

~~ Items ~~

1UP * 3
  Shoot an egg up at the yellow fluff at the start of the second area, and use 
  the large spring ball to bounce up to the area above. Jump on the pump five 
  times, and the ride the huge balloon right to the goal path. Run along the 
  path, and three Fly Guys will appear holding 1UPs.

1UP * 3
  After passing through the middle ring at the start of the second area, 
  continue running right to find three Mock Ups. Quickly eat the Mock Ups 
  before they explode to get the 1UPs.

Flower 1
  At the top-right corner of the balloon section near the start of the level.

Flower 2
  Above the top-left platform of the Bullet Bill section in the first area. 
  Find the platform with the '3' on it, and jump up two platforms to find the 
  flower.

Flower 3
  After hitting the red switch in the first area, quickly jump up the red 
  platforms on the left and shoot the winged cloud above the egg block.

Flower 4
  After the final Wild Ptooie Pirahna in the first area.

Flower 5
  Shoot an egg up at the yellow fluff at the start of the second area, and use 
  the large spring ball to bounce up to the area above. Jump on the pump five 
  times, and ride the huge balloon right to find the flower.

1 Red Coin
  Ride the balloons up near the path at the start of the level, and a Fly Guy 
  will appear holding this coin.

4 Red Coins
  There are two sets of two red coins at the top of the balloon section near 
  the start of the level. 
              
1 Red Coin
  In the first area, above the left side of the first see-saw log platform.

2 Red Coin
  In the first area, above the middle of the second see-saw log platform.

3 Red Coins
  After passing the three see-saw platforms, go up the pipe to arrive in a 
  secret area. Shoot the winged cloud over on the left, and touch the 
  metamorphosis bubble to transform into a helicopter. Fly up to the top of the 
  area to find the coins above the Wild Ptooie Pirahna.

1 Red Coin
  At the start of the Bullet Bill section in the first area, jump left up the 
  platforms to find three coins. The left coin in the line is a red coin.

1 Red Coin
  There is a platform at the right side of the second flower. Jump onto the 
  platform and eat the Fly Guy that appears holding the red coin.

1 Red Coin
  A Fly Guy appears holding this red coin after the Wild Ptooie Pirahna shortly 
  after the Bullet Bill section in the first area.

1 Red Coin
  In the first area, above the third red block platform after the red switch.

5 Red Coins
  Shoot an egg up at the yellow fluff at the start of the second area, and use 
  the large spring ball to bounce up to the area above. Jump on the pump five 
  times, and the ride the huge balloon right to find the red coins.

10 Stars
  After passing the three see-saw platforms in the first area, go up the pipe 
  to arrive in a secret area. Shoot the winged cloud over on the left, and 
  touch the metamorphosis bubble to transform into a helicopter. Fly through 
  the middle ring at the top of the area to receive the ten stars.

8 Stars
  Shoot an egg into the tulip near the third flower.

10 Stars
  Pass through the middle ring at the start of the second area.

6 Stars
  Run right at the start of the second area, and shoot the two Baron Von 
  Zeppelins holding the crate after the Boo Balloons. Stomp the crate.

Red Switch
  Run right at the start of the second area, and defeat all three Boo Balloons 
  to reveal the red switch. 

===============================================================================
                         Level 4-4: Marching Milde's Fort
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Run right along the grass path at the start of the level, and eat the three 
Mildes shortly before the yellow fluff. Jump onto the fluff and run right to 
start the Shark Chomp chase. Jump over the first Milde on the fluff to land on 
a small raised section near four coins. Jump over to the second raised section, 
and jump up to collect the red coin, which is the right coin in the set.

Continue right and jump over the dip in the fluff to collect the next red coin 
at the right side of the set of four coins. Jump over the gap in the fluff, and 
then jump onto the pink vertically moving platforms. Jump from the first, third 
and fifth platforms, and then jump from the fifth platform onto the grey fluff. 
Collect the red coin above the middle of the first block of fluff, and then 
continue right over the gaps in the fluff to collect the first flower.

                                   - Flower 2 -

There are three coins shortly before the three Mildes near the end of the grey 
fluff section. Collect the red coin at the right side of the set, and then jump 
over the three Mildes to the final section of grey fluff. Jump right and land 
near the egg block to end the Shark Chomp chase. Hit the egg block to refill 
the egg supply, and then shoot the winged cloud to reveal some steps. Run up 
the steps on the left, and shoot an egg up at the winged cloud on the right. 
Run up the next set of red steps, and then go down the pipe on the right.

After arriving in the first castle section, pass through the middle ring on the 
right, and then jump up to the path on the left. Run up the path and go through 
the blue doors at the top-left corner of the area. Go right and eat the Spiked 
Fun Guy on the way to the arrow platform. Jump onto the arrow platform when it 
points up and slightly left. Shoot an egg at the Pirahna Plant, and then jump 
left to land in the tunnel. Collect the two red coins (the first and sixth 
coins in the set) above the crate, and then stomp the crate for six stars.

Run back to the right and hover jump over to the next tunnel on the right. 
Stand in front of the arrow platform, and shoot an egg straight up to create 
gaps in the fluff. Jump on the arrow platform when it points up, and ride 
straight up through the gaps in the fluff. After passing through the third gap, 
jump right to land near a winged cloud under four coins. Jump up to collect the 
red coin (the fourth coin in the set), and then shoot an egg at the winged 
cloud for five stars.

Walk left along the blocks, and hover jump over the fluff to the blocks on the 
other side. Hit the egg block to refill the egg supply, and then jump up to the 
fluff on the left. Shoot an egg left to collect a red coin and defeat a Spiked 
Fun Guy. Run left through the gap created by the egg, and shoot an egg down and 
left through the fluff to defeat the Potted Spiked Fun Guy. Run left and shoot 
three eggs to defeat the Wild Ptooie Pirahna near the blue doors. Jump up to 
the gap on the left to collect the second flower. Drop off the ledge and go 
left to collect the first key, and then go through the blue doors.

                                   - Flower 3 -

After returning to the first castle section, run down the path on the left and 
go through the blue doors at the bottom-left corner of the area. Go right and 
drop down to land near an egg block. Hit the egg block to refill the egg 
supply, and then use the log platforms on the left to jump back up to the blue 
doors. Continue left and drop down the step to land near a lava pit. Shoot an 
egg at the bucket up on the left, and then jump on the bucket. Hold left to 
move the bucket over to the left side of the lava. Jump up to collect the red 
coin, and then jump over to the wall on the left.

Jump left to land on the green rotating platform in the second section of lava, 
and ride it left by jumping up to the next platform just before the first 
platform touches the lava. At the left side of the lava, jump up to collect the 
red coin, and then jump over to the wall on the left. Jump to the horizontally 
moving red and yellow platform in the third section of lava, and ride it left. 
At the left side of the lava, jump to the arrow platform when it points up, and 
jump to the wall at the top-left corner of the area.

Jump across the log platforms above the lava. On the third log platform, shoot 
an egg down and right to collect the third flower, and then continue jumping 
over the platforms. Jump onto the pink vertically moving platform at the far 
right side of the lava, and shoot an egg up and left to collect the red coin. 
Jump down to the wall on the right, and go through the gap to land near the 
blue doors. Shoot the winged cloud up on the right to reveal the second key. 
Collect the key, and then go through the blue doors.

                                   - Flower 4 -

After returning to the first castle section, jump up to the path on the right. 
Run up the path and go through the blue doors at the top-right corner of the 
area. Drop off the right side of the log platform and jump up the two steps. 
Jump up the three log platforms above, and hit the egg block to refill the egg 
supply. Jump on top of the egg block and shoot an egg right to destroy the 
cracked blocks. Run through the gap on the right and jump up to the top cracked 
block. Shoot an egg at the winged cloud on the right to receive five stars.

Drop down to the green block on the right, to see two sets of coins in the 
green blocks up on the right. Shoot eggs to destroy the green blocks, and jump 
up to collect the red coin at the bottom of each set of coins. Shoot at the 
fluff, and quickly stomp the Bandit that rushes out. Shoot an egg at the bottom 
of the fluff to receive five stars from a hidden winged cloud. Shoot one more 
egg up to the middle of the fluff for another five stars, and then run left 
back to the egg block near the start of the area. Hit the egg block to refill 
the egg supply, and then return to the fluff.

Jump through the gap in the fluff, and jump up to the platform at the top-right 
corner of the area. Shoot the winged cloud for five stars, and then drop down 
the right side of the block to the path below. Shoot an egg at the Snifit down 
on the left, and drop down through the gaps in the log platforms to the path 
below. Jump up the two steps on the left, and jump up the next five log 
platforms to land near a Bullet Bill. Jump over the cannon, and then quickly 
drop into the first gap on the left and duck to avoid two Bullet Bills. When 
the Bullet Bills have passed, quickly run left and jump over the second Bullet 
Bill cannon to drop down to the path below.

Eat the Snifit on the path, and then drop down the two log platforms on the 
right. Wait for the Bullet Bill to pass by, and then drop down to the very 
steep log platform on the left. Drop left down to the platform below, and then 
eat the Snifit on the left. Run up the steep log platform on the left, and 
shoot the winged cloud above to reveal the flower. Jump up to collect the 
fourth flower, and then run back down the log platform on the right.

                                   - Flower 5 -

Walk right and stomp the first Bandit that runs toward you. Run down the steep 
log platform, and stomp the second Bandit. Drop off the edge of the platform on 
the right to land near some blue thorns. Shoot two eggs at the two lowest 
thorns, and run through the gap. On the right side of the thorns, stomp the 
Coin Bandit and collect the red coin. Shoot the left winged cloud for five 
stars, and shoot the right winged cloud for the third key. Run left and pass 
through the gap in the thorns.

On the left side of the thorns, run left and eat the Bullet Bill that is fired 
out of the cannon. Stomp the first Bandit, and then jump over the cannon. Stomp 
the second Bandit, and hit both yellow egg blocks on the left. Collect both 
yellow eggs, and then jump up to the path on the right. Jump up to the log 
platform on the left, and then hop up to the path on the left. Shoot an egg 
through the lowest crack block, and run left to the log platforms. Jump up two 
log platforms, and run right to collect a red coin. Jump up the next two log 
platforms, and go through the blue doors.

After returning to the first castle section, run down the path on the left and 
go through the blue doors at the bottom-right corner of the area. Run right and 
jump up the two steps. Eat the Grunt at the top, and then jump over to the 
rotating platforms on the right. Jump up to the seventh rotating platform, and 
then jump into the tunnel on the right. Drop down through the gaps in the log 
platforms to land on the pink vertically moving platform above the blue thorns. 
Shoot an egg through the gap on the left to collect the fifth flower.

After collecting the fifth flower, shoot an egg at the coins above the blue 
thorns on the right to collect two red coins. Ride the platform up, and then 
jump onto the platform. Eat the Grunt, and walk right to find an arrow 
platform. When the arrow platform points up, jump on the platform and ride it 
up to the top of the tunnel. Jump off the right side of the platform at the top 
of the tunnel and drop down through the gap to land near four coins. Eat the 
Grunt, and run right to collect two red coins.

Jump out of the gap and drop down to the vertically moving platform on the 
right, and drop off either side of the platform. Drop down the gap to land on a 
rotating platform, and then jump up to the tunnel on the left. Go through the 
blue doors to arrive in a room with a rotating platform. Shoot an egg at the 
winged cloud above the platform, and the key will drop down to the bottom of 
the room. Drop down to the bottom of the room to collect the fourth key, and 
then go through the blue doors on the left.

Jump over to the log platform on the right, and hit the egg block to refill the 
egg supply. Jump onto the rotating platform on the left, and ride it up to the 
top. Jump up to the tunnel on the left, and go through the blue doors to return 
to the room with the rotating platform. Jump onto the pink vertically moving 
platform, and jump up to the log platform at the top of the room. Go through 
the blue doors.

After returning to the first castle section, run up the path on the left and go 
through the first keyhole door in the middle of the room. Jump through the 
middle ring and shoot the winged cloud for five stars, and then go through the 
second keyhole door on the right. Run right and go through the third keyhole 
door. Run right over the loose platform, and go through the fourth keyhole 
door. Drop down the step, and eat the six Mildes on the right. Jump through the 
middle ring, and then go through the red doors.

                       - Boss Fight 7: Marching Milde -

Jump onto the log platform on the left at the start of the boss fight, and 
stomp Marching Milde to create two big Mildes. Stomp the big Milde to create 
two small Mildes. Stomp the small Milde to create four normal Mildes. Eat the 
normal Mildes.

This isn't a hard boss fight, but it's easy to make it difficult by stomping 
the two big Mildes and having lots of Mildes all running around at once. Make 
sure that you defeat one Milde first of all, and then move onto the next Milde. 
Defeat all sixteen normal Mildes to win this boss fight.

===============================================================================
                            Level 4-5: Chomp Rock Zone
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Go right at the start of the level, and run up the slope to find a Chomp Rock 
after a message block. Push the Chomp Rock right until it drops off the ledge 
and hits the Red Koopa Troopa, and then jump over to the other side of the rock 
and push it left. When the Chomp Rock starts rolling down the slope toward the 
two Tap-Taps, jump left to collect the first flower above the yellow platform.

                                   - Flower 2 -

Drop down from the yellow platform and push Chomp Rock right along the path to 
defeat the four Tap-Taps. Continue pushing the Chomp Rock right to defeat a Shy 
Guy and a Red Koopa Troopa. When the Chomp Rock falls onto the yellow platform 
after the four logs, stand on top of the Chomp Rock and shoot an egg up at the 
winged cloud above to receive three stars. Eat the three Shy Guys on the path 
on the right, and then continue right to find a red arrow pointing left.

Drop down the gap at the left side of the red arrow to land on a large spring 
ball. Jump over the yellow fluff and eat the green shell nearby. Walk left 
until the yellow fluff is just visible on the right, and then face right. Shoot 
the green shell right so that it hits the bottom of the yellow fluff, and then 
eat the shell when it returns. Shoot the shell again, and follow it left as it 
hits the six Koopa Troopas to collect a 1UP.

Collect the two red coins at the right side of the Tap-Tap, and then run back 
to the entrance of the cave. Jump on the large spring ball, and bounce up to 
the high path on the left. Continue left along the path to return to the Chomp 
Rock at the right side of the four logs. Stomp the two right logs once, and the 
two left logs twice. Jump on top of the left side of the Chomp Rock, and roll 
it over the logs to the slope on the other side.

After the Chomp Rock lands on the slope, jump over to the right side, and 
follow the Chomp Rock as it rolls left. When the Chomp Rock lands between the 
posts at the bottom of the slope, jump up to the post on the right and stomp it 
four times. Shoot the winged cloud on the right to create a bridge over the 
gap, and then jump on top of the right side of the Chomp Rock to roll it over 
the bridge.

After dropping off the end of the bridge, jump up to collect the red coin in 
the middle of the first set of three coins, and then push Chomp Rock to the 
right. Stop Chomp Rock shortly before the short tunnel with the yellow fluff. 
Jump on top of Chomp Rock, and then jump up to the path above the tunnel to 
collect the second flower.

                                   - Flower 3 -

Drop off the left side of the path, and push Chomp Rock slowly to the yellow 
fluff on the right. Chomp Rock should land on the left side of the fluff, and 
fall down to the path below. Jump over the gap, and run right to find a Shy Guy 
pipe. Stand on the red bridge at the left side of the pipe, and eat the Shy 
Guys until Yoshi has six eggs. Run back to the left and drop down the gap to 
land at the left side of the Chomp Rock. Push Chomp Rock right along the tunnel 
and over the bridge with the two Red Koopa Paratroopas.

After exiting the tunnel, push Chomp Rock quickly along the red path with the 
yellow fluff above, and stop before the middle ring. Run back to the left, and 
eat the Fly Guy holding the red coin. Collect the red coin, and then jump 
through the middle ring on the right. Push Chomp Rock down the slope on the 
right to defeat the four Koopa Troopas, and shoot the winged cloud above the 
red arrow at the top of the next small slope to receive five stars.

Continue right to find Chomp Rock at the left side of a post. Eat the Red Koopa 
Paratroopa above, and shoot the shell down at the Green Koopa Paratroopa on the 
right. Stomp the post twice, and then push Chomp Rock down the two steps to the 
steep slope leading down to the left. Jump over to the right side of Chomp 
Rock, and follow it down the slope to avoid two Shy Guys.

When it lands on the next slope, jump over to the left side, and push Chomp 
Rock right along the path. After passing the red arrow, jump over to the right 
side of Chomp Rock and hold left to slow it down. Stop Chomp Rock under the 
gap, and then jump on top of Chomp Rock. Jump up to the ledge on the left, and 
then jump to the path on the right. Run right to collect three red coins, and 
drop off the right side of the path to collect the third flower.

                                   - Flower 4 -

After landing on the path below the paddles, run left and jump over to the left 
side of Chomp Rock. Push Chomp Rock right along the path until it bumps into 
the post near the red switch. Jump on top of the post and stomp it twice. 
Continue right to the outline blocks to find three more posts. Stomp the first 
post once, the second post twice, and the third post once.

Hover jump back to the left, and then jump up to the platform with the red 
switch. Jump on the red switch, and then quickly jump over to the left side of 
Chomp Rock. Push Chomp Rock right over the red switch, and collect the two red 
coins at the right side of the coin trail. Jump on Chomp Rock, and jump up to 
the yellow platform above. Jump up to the next yellow platform, and go through 
the blue doors.

After arriving in the second area, stomp to defeat the Eggo-Dil up on the 
right, and then push Chomp Rock right to the yellow fluff. About half-way down 
the left side of the fluff, the Chomp Rock will reveal a winged cloud. Stomp 
down through the right side of the fluff, and shoot an egg at the winged cloud 
to reveal the flower. Collect the fourth flower, and then push Chomp Rock 
through the paddles on the right.

                                   - Flower 5 -

Push Chomp Rock over to the right side of the blue doors, and then jump on top 
of Chomp Rock. Jump up to collect the red coin on the platform above, and then 
drop down to the left side of Chomp Rock. Push Chomp Rock right along the path, 
and jump up to collect the red coins in the middle of the first and third set 
of three coins.

After passing the Shy Guy pipe on the platform, push Chomp Rock up the steep 
slope and jump at the top to collect the two red coins. Push Chomp Rock down 
the other side of the slope, and continue right to the wall. Push Chomp Rock 
near the wall, and then jump on top of Chomp Rock. Jump up to the gap on the 
right, and drop down to the red bridge on the other side.

Walk onto the large jelly block on the right, and stomp it until it spreads out 
along the spikes. Run right off the edge of the block and shoot an egg at the 
winged cloud on the right to collect a 1UP. Run back to the left, and push the 
jelly block. Jump onto the block and run left to collect five red coins. Run 
right, and go down the pipe to enter a secret area.

Run right to collect the four eggs, and then shoot an egg up at the piece of 
yellow fluff to make the small spring ball drop down. Shoot an egg at the Green 
Glove on the right, and wait for him to start aiming the egg. Just before he 
throws the egg, jump on the spring ball and bounce up and right. The Green 
Glove will throw an egg which should hit the fifth flower. Go up the pipe.

After returning to the second area, run right up the small slope, and eat the 
Green Koopa Paratroopa flying above the platform. Jump up to the platform, and 
then jump up to the red platform on the right. Face right, and shoot the shell 
at the two Green Koopa Paratroopas down on the right. Drop off the right side 
of the platform, and continue right to the goal ring. Jump through the goal 
ring to complete the level.

~~ Items ~~

1UP
  In the second area, push Chomp Rock right all the way to the wall near the 
  outline steps. Jump on Chomp Rock, and jump up through the gap on the right. 
  Walk onto the large jelly block on the right, and stomp it until it spreads 
  out along the spikes. Shoot the winged block on the right for the 1UP.

Flower 1
  Push the first Chomp Rock into the tunnel with the Tap-Taps, and jump up to 
  the platform on the left to find the flower.

Flower 2
  After pushing the Chomp Rock down to the bottom of the second slope, stomp 
  the post and run right to find this flower on a path above the yellow fluff.

Flower 3
  After pushing the Chomp Rock down to the bottom of the second slope, stomp 
  the post and shoot the winged cloud on the right to reveal a bridge across 
  the gap. Continue rolling Chomp Rock all the way to the gap before the red 
  switch near the end of the first area. Jump on Chomp Rock and use it to jump 
  up into the gap. Run right through the gap to collect the third flower.

Flower 4
  Push Chomp Rock across the red block platform revealed by the red switch, and 
  jump up the platform at the other side. Go through the blue doors, and push 
  Chomp Rock through the yellow fluff on the right to reveal a winged cloud. 
  Shoot the winged cloud for the flower.

Flower 5
  In the second area, push Chomp Rock right all the way to the wall near the 
  outline steps. Jump on Chomp Rock, and jump up through the gap on the right. 
  Walk onto the large jelly block on the right, and stomp it until it spreads 
  out along the spikes. Run right off the edge of the block and face left. Push 
  the block left and go down the pipe to arrive in an area with the flower.

2 Red Coins
  After pushing the Chomp Rock down to the bottom of the first slope, continue 
  past the Chomp Rock and go down the gap at the left side of the red arrow. 
  Run left to find the two red coins.

1 Red Coin
  After pushing the Chomp Rock down to the bottom of the second slope, stomp 
  the post and run right to find this red coin in the first set of three coins.

1 Red Coin
  After pushing the Chomp Rock down to the bottom of the second slope, stomp 
  the post and run right to find some yellow fluff. Stomp the fluff to collect 
  the red coin below.

1 Red Coin
  Shortly before the middle ring in the first area, a Fly Guy holding the red 
  coin is floating over the yellow fluff.

3 Red Coins
  At the left side of the third flower.

2 Red Coins
  At the end of the red switch bridge near the end of the first area.

3 Red Coins
  The first, fifth and eleventh coins at the start of the second area.

2 Red Coins
  In the second area, there are six coins in a line at the top of the slope 
  after the Shy Guy pipe. The middle two coins are the red coins.

5 Red Coins
  In the second area, push Chomp Rock right all the way to the wall near the 
  outline steps. Jump on Chomp Rock, and jump up through the gap on the right. 
  Walk onto the large jelly block on the right, and stomp it until it spreads 
  out along the spikes. Shoot an egg left to collect the coins.

3 Stars
  Shoot the winged cloud above the Chomp Rock at the end of the first slope.

10 Stars
  Pass through the middle ring about half-way through the first area.

5 Stars
  When Chomp Rock comes to a stop at the end of the first slope, stomp the post 
  on the left and roll Chomp Rock down to the path below. Push Chomp Rock right 
  to reveal a hidden winged cloud.

5 Stars
  Shoot the winged cloud shortly after the middle ring in the first area.

===============================================================================
                          Level 4-6: Lake Shore Paradise
=============================================================================== 

                                   - Flower 1 -

Run right at the start of the level, and eat the Green Koopa Paratroopa flying 
above the steps. Run down the three sets of steps, and stand near the bottom of 
the third set. Wait for the Flopsy Fish to hit into Yoshi, and then drop into 
the water and swim left. Swim under the steps and jump up near the wall. When 
Yoshi lands in the water, hold left to swim under the wall. Jump up to the path 
on the left, and run left to exit the first area.

In the secret area, drop off the left side of the platform and eat the green 
shell. Wait for the tulip to open, and then jump up and shoot the shell into 
the tulip for eight stars. Collect the stars, jump up to the platform on the 
right, and run right to exit the secret area.

After returning to the first area, run along the tunnel and jump up to the 
curved path on the right. Jump up to collect the red coin at the right side of 
the set of three coins. Drop down to the path on the left, and then drop down 
to the water on the right. Swim right, jump near the wall, and hold right to 
swim under the wall. Jump up to the yellow platform at the right side of the 
steps, and then jump up to the red path on the right.

Run right along the path and eat the Red Koopa Paratroopa flying near the 
coins. Shoot the shell right, and follow it as it defeats two Red Koopa Troopas 
and a Shy Guy. Wait near the Shy Guy pipe, and eat Shy Guys until Yoshi has six 
eggs. Stand on top of the pipe, and shoot an egg at the winged cloud on the 
right to collect a red coin and create a bridge.

Cross over the bridge, and stand on top of the next pipe. When the Fly Guy 
floats left, shoot an egg at the winged cloud to create a second bridge. Jump 
up to collect the red coin in the middle of the set of three coins, and then 
jump up and eat the Fly Guy to collect another red coin. Run right along the 
bridge and drop into the water at the end. Swim right under the wall, and then 
jump up to hit the yellow fluff on the other side. Jump up through the gap in 
the yellow fluff to collect the first flower.

                                   - Flower 2 -

Drop down through the gap in the yellow fluff to land in the water, and swim 
right. Jump and swim under the next wall at the right side of the yellow fluff, 
and eat the Flopsy Fish on the other side. Swim right and jump up to the small 
platform when the Red Koopa Paratroopa flies to the right. Eat the Red Koopa 
Paratroopa, and shoot the shell over at the next Paratroopa on the right.

Jump right to the second platform, and walk to the far right side. When the Red 
Koopa Paratroopa flies low, hover jump right and land on the Red Koopa Troopa 
on the third platform. Eat the Red Koopa Paratroopa at the right side of the 
third platform, and jump down to the small spring ball on the right. Bounce 
right to the second spring ball, and bounce up to collect two red coins. Jump 
right to the third spring ball, and bounce up to collect the second flower.

                                   - Flower 3 -

Ignore the winged cloud up on the right, and bounce right to the fourth spring 
ball. Shoot an egg at the winged cloud on the right to create a bridge leading 
back to the left. Shoot an egg at the Fly Guy above, and collect the red coin 
that is dropped. Shoot an egg at the winged cloud on the left to receive five 
stars, and then drop down to the bridge on the right.

Jump up to the path at the end of the bridge, and jump right from the platform 
to land on the red path. Eat the Red Koopa Troopa, and shoot the shell right to 
destroy the yellow fluff. When the red shell has gone, drop down through the 
gaps in the platforms, and push the crate to the right side of the log 
platform. Stomp the crate and collect the key.

Run back to the left, and jump up the two log platforms. Jump up to the red 
path on the left, and drop off the left side of the path to land in the water. 
Face left, and eat both Flopsy Fish. Jump out of the left side of the water to 
land on a platform, and jump up to collect the two red coins in the line of 
five coins.

Jump on the large spring ball and bounce up to the platform high above. Run 
right and press up next to the hut to enter it and play a bonus game. After 
exiting the hut, drop off the left side of the log platform and hover right to 
land on the red path. Run along the tunnel and go through the blue doors.

After arriving in the second area, run right and drop down to the second 
platform. Run left to drop down to the yellow platform with the three coins 
below, and then run right to drop down to the lower yellow platform. Face left, 
and jump off the left side of the platform to collect the middle red coin in 
the set of three coins. Jump back onto the platform, and run over to the right 
side of the path.

Jump up to the ledge on the left, and pass through the middle ring. Drop down 
to the lower yellow platform on the right, and drop into the water. Jump to 
collect the two red coins near the Needlenose Plant, and then continue right 
under the long yellow platform to find a second Needlenose Plant. Jump over the 
top of the Needlenose Plant to collect the third flower. Jump onto the yellow 
platform at the right side of the egg plant, and run right. Go through the blue 
doors. Run right and go through the next doors.

                                   - Flower 4 -

After arriving in the third area, drop off the step and run right along the 
yellow platform to find a Claw Daddy. Wait for the Claw Daddy to move to the 
right side of the platform, and then jump up to the next yellow platform. Eat 
the two Woozy Guys, and run to the far right side of the platform. Shoot three 
eggs to defeat the Claw Daddy below, and then drop down to the yellow platform 
on the right. Run left to collect the fourth flower.

                                   - Flower 5 -

Run right along the yellow platform and stop near the end. Eat the two Woozy 
Guys bouncing down the steps, and then jump from the platform to the top of the 
steps. Jump to the platform above, and jump over to the platform on the right 
to land near the egg plant. Stand near the egg plant until Yoshi has six eggs, 
and then drop down into the water on the right. Swim close to the wall on the 
right, jump, and swim under the wall. Continue right to exit the third area.

After arriving in the fourth area, run right along the path and eat the first 
vertically moving platform. Run back to the left, and jump up to the platform 
with the egg plant on it. Face right, and spit out the platform. Jump on the 
vertically moving platform, and ride it up to the coins at the top-left corner 
of the area. Collect the top-left red coin, and then hover right to the path at 
the left side of the spikes.

Hover right and collect the third coin in the line before landing on the 
platform in the middle of the spikes. Jump left and collect the seventh coin in 
the line, and then hover down to the platform at the right side of the spikes. 
Hover jump right over to the platform on the other side of the spikes. Jump 
over the next spikes to land near an egg plant at the top-right corner of the 
area. Jump up to collect the red coin at the right side of the set of coins, 
and then hover left to the path at the left side of the spikes.

Drop off the left side of the path, and hover right to land on the path below. 
Run right along the path to find two sets of twelve coins. Jump up to collect 
the red coin between the two sets of coins, and then run back to the left side 
of the path. Jump on the vertically moving platform, and ride it up to the top. 
Jump left over the spikes, and hover down to the path on the left. Run left 
along the path and go through the tunnel to exit the fourth area.

After returning to the third area, jump into the water and swim under the wall. 
Jump up to the platform on the left, and then jump up to the yellow platform 
above. Go to the far right side of the platform, and jump up to the next yellow 
platform. Jump up the two steps on the left, and shoot three eggs up to defeat 
the Claw Daddy on the platform above. Jump up to the platform and shoot an egg 
to the top-left corner of the fluff to receive five stars. Shoot an egg up and 
right through the fluff, and jump through the gaps. Go through the blue doors.

After arriving in the fifth area, run down the slope and drop down to the path. 
Run down the slope on the left, and jump over the platform with the two Koopa 
Troopas on it. After landing on the second platform, drop down to the platform 
on the right and hit the Koopa Troopa. Hit the shell off the platform, and then 
shoot an egg right to collect the middle red coin in the set of three coins. 
Jump back up to the top yellow platform, and run up the slope on the right.

Eat the Green Koopa Paratroopa on the right, and shoot the green shell down the 
slope on the right to defeat two of the Woozy Guys. Eat the remaining Woozy 
Guy, and shoot an egg up at the Fly Guy holding the red coin. Collect the red 
coin, and then run down the slope on the right. Jump to the log platform at the 
bottom of the slope, and shoot an egg at the first winged cloud on the right to 
create a bridge.

Shoot an egg at the second winged cloud for five stars, and shoot an egg at the 
third winged cloud to create a long bridge leading back to the left. Drop down 
to the bridge, and run left. Shoot the Fly Guy above the left side of the 
bridge and collect the red coin that is dropped. Jump into the gap on the left 
and collect the fifth flower.

Drop back down to the bridge, and run right. Go down the steps at the end of 
the bridge, and jump over the Shy Guy on Stilts to land on the path. Jump over 
the water and land on the next path. Defeat the Shy Guy on Stilts near the 
start of the path, and face right. Wait for the Wild Ptooie Pirahna to stop 
shooting the Needlenoses, and then quickly run to the middle of the path and 
shoot three eggs to defeat the Wild Ptooie Pirahna.

Continue right along the path, jumping over the various Shy Guys on Stilts 
along the way. At the right side of the red path, a Shy Guy on Stilts will be 
walking in a tunnel on the right. When the Shy Guy on Stilts starts walking to 
the right, jump into the tunnel and follow him to the right. Near the right 
side of the tunnel, push the Shy Guy on Stilts out of the tunnel. Jump over to 
the platform on the right, and when the Red Koopa Paratroopa flies down, hover 
right to the path near the Wild Ptooie Pirahna.

At the left side of the path, the Needlenoses won't reach Yoshi. Eat the Green 
Koopa Troopa floating above the path, and shoot the shell left. Face right, and 
eat the Needlenoses until Yoshi has six eggs. After the Wild Ptooie Pirahna has 
shot three Needlenoses, quickly run to the top of the path and shoot three eggs 
right to defeat the final Wild Ptooie Pirhana in the area. Jump over to the 
ledge on the right, and run down the steps. Continue right over the bridge, and 
jump through the goal ring to complete the level.

  the level.

Flower 2
  Above the third small arrow ball near the end of the first area.

Flower 3
