Flower 4
  At the left side of the second Clawdaddy in the third area.

Flower 5
  When you come to the three winged clouds near the start of the fifth area, 
  shoot the left and right winged clouds to create a bridge leading back to the 
  left. Run left along the bridge to find the flower.

1 Red Coin
  Go down the steps to the water at the start of the level, and swim under the 
  steps on the left. Jump up to the path on the right to land under three 
  coins. The right coin in the line is a red coin.

1 Red Coin
  Near the start of the level, above the first outline bridge shortly after the 
  Shy Guy pipe.

1 Red Coin
  Above the second outline bridge shortly after the Shy Guy pipe.

1 Red Coin
  A Fly Guy is holding this red coin above the second outline bridge shortly 
  after the Shy Guy pipe.

2 Red Coins
  Above the second small spring ball near the end of the first area.

1 Red Coin
  A Fly Guy is holding this red coin above the fourth small spring ball near 
  the end of the first area.

2 Red Coins
  Near the end of the first area, drop down to the platform at the right side 
  of the fourth small spring ball. Run right to find the red coins.

1 Red Coin
  There are three coins near the start of the second area. The middle coin in 
  the line is a red coin.

2 Red Coins
  There is one coin at either side of the Needlenose Plant in the second area.

1 Red Coin
  At the top-left corner of the fourth area. To get to the fourth area, stomp 
  into the water at the bottom-right corner of the third area, and swim under 
  the wall to the fourth area. Yoshi can move the vertically moving platforms 
  about by eating them and spitting them out at different places.

2 Red Coins
  Above the spikes near the top-left corner of the fourth area.

1 Red Coin
  Above the egg plant at the top-right corner of the fourth area.

1 Red Coin
  Near the egg plant at the bottom-right corner of the fourth area.

1 Red Coin
  In the water below the entrance to the fifth area.

1 Red Coin
  A Fly Guy holds this red coin near the start of the fifth area, above some 
  Woozy Guys that bounce up the slope.

1 Red Coin
  A Fly Guy holds this red coin at the right side of the fifth flower.

8 Stars
  Go down the steps to the water at the start of the level, and swim under the 
  steps on the left. Go through the tunnel on the left, and shoot an egg or 
  shell into the tulip.

5 Stars
  Shoot the winged cloud shortly after third small arrow ball near the end of 
  the first area.

10 Stars
  Pass through the middle ring near the start of the second area.

5 Stars
  When you come to the three winged clouds near the start of the second area, 
  shoot the middle winged cloud for the stars.

Key
  In the crate at the bottom-right corner of the first area, below the doors.

===============================================================================
                          Level 4-7: Ride Like The Wind
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Eat the Green Koopa Troopa on the right at the start of the level, and shoot 
the shell right. Follow the shell right as it defeats another Green Koopa 
Troopa, and run up to the top of the slope. Jump over the gap to the next 
section of yellow path, and drop off the right side of the path to land on a 
small platform. Eat the first Red Koopa Paratroopa, and jump up to the yellow 
path on the right. Face left, and shoot the shell down the gap to collect the 
first flower.

                                   - Flower 2 -

Run down the slope on the right, and jump right to land on the red and yellow 
platform. Ride the platform up to the top, and then jump right to land on the 
path after the two Red Koopa Paratroopas. Run down the slope in the path, and 
drop down to the large spring ball in the gap. Jump on the large spring ball 
and bounce up to the right.

Land in the tunnel leading up and right after the Pirahna Plant. Follow the 
tunnel right, and then jump left to land on the yellow path at the end of the 
tunnel. Jump to collect the two red coins at the left side of the trail of 
coins, and run down the steep slope to the red and yellow platform. Ride the 
platform along the track, and shortly after the Pirahna Plant, jump into the 
tunnel.

Run right to the platform at the end of the tunnel, and jump onto the red and 
yellow platform. Ride the platform up to the top, and jump off at the left 
side. Run up the tunnel, and shoot an egg at the winged cloud to receive five 
stars. Run right to the end of the tunnel, and jump over the gap to the yellow 
path on the other side. Continue right to the next tunnel, and run down to the 
bottom of the slope.

Jump over the Huffin Puffin, and eat the Red Koopa Troopa on the yellow 
platform. Jump up to the platform, and shoot the shell at the Red Koopa Troopa 
on the left. Jump over to the platform on the left, and run up the slope to the 
second Huffin Puffin in the area. Shoot the winged cloud above the Huffin 
Puffin for five stars, and then jump up to the highest yellow platform on the 
left with the three coins above.

Eat the Gustys until Yoshi has six eggs, and then shoot an egg straight up in 
line with the coins to reveal a large spring ball. Jump on the large spring 
ball and bounce up to the platform above. Jump on the next large spring ball 
and bounce up to the secret area.

After arriving in the secret area, jump up to the top platform, and then jump 
over the path on the right to land near the pump. Jump on the pump five times, 
and then jump on the balloon to move right. Stand on the middle of the balloon, 
and eat the Fly Guy holding the 1UP that appears near the start of the ride. At 
the end of the balloon ride, drop down through the gap in the clouds at the 
right side of the area.

After returning to the first area, run right along the yellow path and collect 
the five red coins in the first dip. Shoot an egg at the Fly Guy holding the 
1Up above the first dip, and then continue right up the slope. Run down the 
next slope to collect the second flower, and run up and over the next hill. 
Continue right, and go through the blue doors.

                                   - Flower 3 -

After arriving in the second area, run right and drop down to the green 
vertically moving platform. Jump down to the hidden tunnel on the left, and 
pass through the middle ring. Drop out of the tunnel, and hover left to the 
hidden tunnel below. Shoot the winged cloud for five stars, and stomp the crate 
for the key. Collect the key, and then jump over to the next hidden tunnel on 
the right.

Jump onto the green vertically moving platform, and jump up to the hidden 
tunnel on the left. Face right, and wait for the cannon to fire a Bullet Bill. 
When it does, jump on Bullet Bill and bounce up to the platform above to 
collect the third flower. Jump right and press up next to the hut to enter it 
and play a bonus game. 

                                   - Flower 4 -

After exiting the hut, walk right and drop off the edge of the path onto the 
green rotating platform below. Move the platform right, and jump up to collect 
the four red coins above the wire. After collecting the fourth red coin, ride 
the platform down the slope in the wire to collect the four red coins below the 
wire. At the end of the wire, jump to the first red and yellow platform on the 
right. Jump up to the yellow platform at the end of the track, and then jump 
into the hidden tunnel on the left to collect the fourth flower.

                                   - Flower 5 -

Jump over to the hidden tunnel on the right, and drop down the gap with the red 
arrow pointing down to land on the second red and yellow platform. Ride the 
platform off the end of the track to collect three red coins. As the second 
platform begins to go down, jump up and land on the third red and yellow 
platform.

Ride the third platform off the end of the track, and jump before the three 
normal coins to land on the fourth platform. Stay on the fourth platform to 
land on a circular wire. Jump at the top of the wire to collect two red coins 
and the fifth flower. Jump right off the platform to land on the path. Run 
right along the path, and jump through the goal ring to complete the level.

~~ Items ~~

1UP
  At the start of the Gusty section, shoot an egg straight up from the platform 
  near the wall to reveal a large spring ball. Bounce up both large spring 
  balls above to enter a secret area. Jump on the pump five times, and then 
  jump on the balloon to move right. The Fly Guy holding the 1UP will appear 
  near the start of the balloon ride.

1UP
  A Fly Guy appears holding this 1UP above the first dip in the path in the 
  Gusty section.

Flower 1
  In the second gap from the start of the level, with the two Red Koopa 
  Paratroopas.

Flower 2
  In the second dip in the path in the Gusty section.

Flower 3
  In the second area, drop down to the green platform on the right, and go 
  right again to the hidden tunnel. Jump on the Bullet Bill, and hover up to 
  the platform with the flower on the right.

Flower 4
  Ride the first red and yellow platform in the second area, and jump off near 
  the end of the wire onto the horizontally moving yellow platform. Jump to the 
  hidden tunnel up on the left to find this flower.

Flower 5
  In the second area, ride the final red and yellow platform onto the circular 
  wire. The flower is above the wire.

2 Red Coins
  Use the spring ball near the start of the level to jump into the tunnel above 
  the right side of the Pirahna Plant. Follow the tunnel to the red coins.

5 Red Coins
  In the first dip in the path in the Gusty section.

8 Red Coins
  In the second area, ride the green rotating platform near the first fast red 
  and yellow platform along the wire to find the eight red coins.

3 Red Coins
  In the second area, ride the second red and yellow platform to the end of the 
  wire to collect these coins.

2 Red Coins
  In the second area, ride the final red and yellow platform onto the circular 
  wire. The final two red coins are above the wire.

5 Stars
  Before the Huffin Puffin in the first area, ride the vertically moving 
  platform up and jump into the left tunnel to find a winged cloud. Shoot the 
  cloud for the stars.

5 Stars
  Shoot an egg at the winged cloud above the second Huffin Puffin.

5 Stars
  There is a winged cloud above the paddles at the end of the first area. You 
  can either ride the balloon to get above the paddles, or hover jump from the 
  top of the final hill in the Gusty section.

10 Stars
  In the second area, in the hidden tunnel below the entrance.

5 Stars
  In the second area, in the lowest hidden tunnel below the entrance. Shoot the 
  winged cloud for the stars.

Key
  In the second area, in the lowest hidden tunnel below the entrance. Stomp the 
  crate for the key.

===============================================================================
                      Level 4-8: Hookbill The Koopa's Castle
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Run right along the tunnel at the start of the level and eat the first Boo Guy. 
Shoot the Boo Guy right, and follow him as he defeats three more Boo Guys and a 
Green Koopa Troopa. When the shell moves right, stay on the top level of the 
platform. The shell will hit into another Green Koopa Troopa, which will cause 
another shell to move left to collect the first flower.

                                   - Flower 2 -

Drop off the right side of the platform to the path below, and then jump right 
to the bridge. Stay at the left side of the bridge, and duck to avoid the 
spiked ball and chain. When it has passed, run right and jump to the platform 
above the second spiked ball and chain. Jump down to the bridge on the right, 
and run right. Drop down to the lower section of the bridge, and eat the first 
Green Koopa Troopa. Shoot the shell left to collect the second flower.

                                   - Flower 3 -

Jump over the remaining Green Koopa Troopa, and run right along the bridge to 
the Boo Guy pipe. Eat Boo Guys until Yoshi has six eggs, and then continue over 
to the right side of the bridge. Jump over the small gap to the path on the 
other side. Run right along the path to find a spiked ball and chain with a 
crumbling block below. Shoot an egg at the block, and then run under the spiked 
ball and chain.

Continue right to the second spiked ball and chain. Shoot an egg at the block, 
and continue right. Hover jump over the lava to land near a third spiked ball 
and chain. When the spiked ball and chain rises, shoot the crumbling block and 
drop down through the gap. Run right to collect two red coins, and drop down to 
the lowest platform. Run left and go through the blue doors.

After arriving in the second area, jump up to the platform on the right, and 
run to the middle to find two egg blocks. Hit either egg block to refill the 
egg supply, and then shoot an egg at the winged cloud to create steps leading 
up to the right. Run up the steps, and shoot the next winged cloud to create 
another set of steps.

Run left up the steps, and jump onto the block at the top. When the spiked ball 
and chain rises, drop into the gap and collect the two middle red coins. Jump 
right to land on the steps, run left to the top. Jump right onto the block, and 
shoot the winged cloud to create another set of steps leading up to the right. 
Run up this set of steps, and run right along the path. Drop off the right side 
of the path to collect the third flower, and then run through the paddles on 
the left. Jump up the platforms on the left, and go through the blue doors.

                                   - Flower 4 -

After returning to the first area, eat the Red Koopa Troopa on the left, and 
run right along the path. Drop down the gap with the red arrows pointing down, 
and run right down the platforms to the path at the bottom. Shoot the shell 
right, and follow it as it goes through the gap on the right. The shell will 
hit a winged cloud, which will create steps leading up to the right. Climb up 
the steps to the top, and go through the blue doors.

After returning to the second area, jump left to collect the two red coins in 
the line. Stomp the crate to receive a key, and pass through the middle ring. 
Run left through the paddles, and hit the two yellow egg blocks. Collect the 
two eggs, and run left along the path. Jump up the platforms on the left, and 
go through the blue doors.

After returning to the first area, run up the small slope on the right, and 
jump up to the platform above. Shoot an egg up at the crumbling block above the 
arrow platform, and ride the arrow platform up to the gap. Jump up through the 
gap to exit the first area. In the secret area, defeat the Mildes and then 
collect the red coin. Go down the pipe.

After returning to the first area, jump on the arrow platform when it points 
right. Ride the platform under the block to collect the four red coins, and 
jump off the platform to the path at the right side of the thorns. Drop down to 
the log platform, and shoot an egg down and left to collect the two red coins. 
Jump up to the path on the right, and go through the door with the keyhole.

After arriving in the third area, jump to the steps on the left and run up to 
the top. Jump to the second set of steps and run left to the top. Collect the 
four eggs on the path at the top of the steps, and collect the red coin under 
the curved path. Run right and jump onto the curved path above the steps. Run 
up to the top of the path, and jump up to the next path on the right to collect 
three red coins.

Jump up to the platform above, and run left. Drop down to the platform on the 
left, and shoot an egg up and left to collect the three red coins. Jump back up 
to the path on the right, and run along to the far right side of the path. Go 
up the pipe to exit the third area. After arriving in the fourth area, shoot an 
egg through the blocks on either side of the pipe to collect the fourth flower.

                                   - Flower 5 -

Shoot an egg through the blocks at the other side of the pipe to collect the 
fifth flower. Shoot an egg straight up through the blocks to make the large 
spring ball fall down. Jump on the large spring ball, and bounce up to the high 
platform above. Go through the red doors.

                     - Boss Fight 8: Hookbill the Koopa -

At the start of the area, run right along the blocks and jump up the two log 
platforms. Jump left up the steps, and jump right from the top step to land on 
the blocks. Jump up to the red steps, and run left up to the top. Jump to the 
block on the left, and then jump to the block on the right. Jump to the log 
platform, and then jump to the blocks on the right. Run right and jump through 
the middle ring, and then jump over the two gaps on the right. Run right along 
the blocks, and the boss fight will start.

At the start of the boss fight, stomp Hookbill's shell, and he will spit out 
eggs. Collect the eggs and face toward Hookbill. Shoot four eggs at Hookbill, 
and he will fall over. When he falls, quickly stomp his shell. Stomp his shell 
three times to defeat Hookbill the Koopa.

~~ Items ~~

1UP
  Eat one of the Koopa Troopas from the group at the right side of the first 
  area, and jump over the gap which has the red arrows pointing down. Run down 
  the small log slope, and shoot an egg through the gap to hit the winged cloud 
  on the other side.

Flower 1
  At the right side of the first Hot Lips in the first area.

Flower 2
  At the right side of the second Hot Lips in the first area.

Flower 3
  At the right side of the paddles near the top of the second area.

Flower 4
  At the start of the fourth area, in the blocks on the left.

Flower 5
  At the start of the fourth area, in the blocks on the right.

2 Red Coins
  Below the third set of Boo Guys that drop the spiked ball and chain.

1 Red Coin
  When you come to the arrow platform at the right side of the first area, 
  shoot an egg at the cracked block above, and ride the platform up into the 
  gap. In the secret room, defeat the Mildes to reveal the red coin.

4 Red Coins
  When you come to the arrow platform at the right side of the first area, ride 
  it over the thorns on the right to find the red coins.

2 Red Coins
  Run down the log platform near the keyhole door at the far right side of the 
  first area.

2 Red Coins
  Near the crate at the top-right corner of the second area.

2 Red Coins
  Below the spiked ball and chain near the top-left corner of the second area.

1 Red Coin
  At the bottom-left corner of the third area where the Fishing Lakitu appears.

3 Red Coins
  At the top-left corner of the third area.

3 Red Coins
  Below the platform at the top-right corner of the third area.

5 Stars
  Shoot the winged cloud at the bottom-right corner of the second area.

5 Stars
  Shoot the winged cloud at the left side of the paddles near the top-right 
  corner of the second area.

10 Stars
  Pass through the middle ring at the top-right corner of the second area.

5 Stars
  Shoot the winged cloud at the left side of the third area.

Key
  Stomp the crate at the top-right corner of the second area.

===============================================================================
                          Extra 4: The Impossible? Maze
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Go through the first tunnel on the right. Drop off either side of the platform, 
and take the right junction at the waterfall. Go through the second tunnel on 
the right. Jump up the platforms and collect the two red coins and the first 
flower.

                                   - Flower 2 -

Drop off the left side of the platform to land near the water. Jump on the 
platforms above the water on the left, and use the large spring ball to bounce 
up to the four red coins. Continue jumping up the white platforms, and use the 
small spring balls to jump up to the large spring ball above. Jump from the 
large spring ball and collect the second flower, and then go through the tunnel 
on the right.
              
                                   - Flower 3 -

After returning to the maze, drop down the waterfall below the platform, and 
jump at the end of the slope to collect the third flower.

                                   - Flower 4 -

Jump over to the waterfall on the left with the red arrow pointing down it, and 
slide down the waterfall to the platform near the arrow door. Go down the 
waterfall under the platform, and go through the tunnel with the red blocks 
above. In this area, shoot the winged cloud to receive five stars, and then 
bounce on the spring balls to get to the top of the area. Run right and go 
through the tunnel.

After returning to the maze, push the crate right, left, right, left, and then 
follow it down the right junction of the waterfall. At the bottom of the 
waterfall, push the crate right, and use it to jump up the high white platforms 
to the room with the flower. Bounce an egg off the wall on the left to collect 
two red coins and the fourth flower.

                                   - Flower 5 -

Go through the tunnel on the right. In this area, touch the metamorphosis 
bubble on the left to transform into the mole tank. Dig up the tunnel on the 
right, and go into the left and right tunnels on the way to collect two red 
coins. Go left at the top of the tunnel, and hit the Yoshi block, which will 
return Yoshi to normal. Shoot the winged cloud on the left to receive five 
stars, and then go through the tunnel.

After returning to the maze, jump up to the platform on the left, and push the 
crate off the left edge of the platform. Follow the crate down the waterfall on 
the right. Push the crate down the waterfall on the left. After landing on the 
platform at the bottom of the waterfall, push the crate along the platform 
toward the tunnel on the right. Jump on the crate and go through the tunnel.

In this area, touch the metamorphosis bubble to transform into a helicopter, 
and fly up the tunnel. Fly right shortly before the top of the tunnel to 
collect the four red coins, and then continue up to the Yoshi block at the top 
of the tunnel. Hit the Yoshi block to transform to Yoshi, jump over the Pirahna 
Plant on the right, and then go through the tunnel.

After returning to the maze. Walk left until the Pirahna Plant and crate fall 
down from the waterfall, and then follow the crate down to the arrow door. Push 
the crate in front of the tunnel. Jump on top of the crate and go through the 
tunnel. Run right to collect the fifth flower, and then hold down to avoid the 
blocks. After passing the blocks, jump up to the platform on the right, and run 
through the tunnel to the goal ring. Jump through the goal ring to complete the 
level.

===============================================================================
                              Level 5-1: BLIZZARD!!!
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Run right along the path from the start point of the level, and hit the egg 
block to refill the egg supply. Continue right, and Thunder Lakitu will soon 
appear. Quickly jump up and eat his cloud before he throws the flame, and jump 
up to the post on the right. Stomp the post twice, and run through the tunnel 
to the other side. Hit the expansion block, and jump up to the top of it. Eat 
the cloud of Thunder Lakitu if he gets too near, and then jump up to the path 
on the left. Run left along the path to collect the first flower.

                                   - Flower 2 -

Run right and drop off the end of the path to land on the path below. Run right 
over the two small slopes, and jump up to eat the Fly Guy holding the red coin 
at the top of the second slope. Collect the red coin, and run right under the 
two expansion blocks to find a Mace Guy. Quickly jump over the top of the Mace 
Guy before he starts swinging the mace, and continue right to the second Mace 
Guy near some yellow platforms. Eat the Mace Guy, and then jump up to the 
highest platform.

Jump right from the highest platform to land on the grass path. Eat the two Shy 
Guys on the right, and then drop off the right side of the path to land on a 
platform above a gap. Drop off the right side of the platform, and hover down 
to the lowest platform on the left. Drop off the right side of the platform, 
and hover left to the grass path. Run left and stomp the crate to collect a 
key, then run back to the right and jump up to the top platform.

Jump right from the top platform to land on the grass path, and run under the 
egg block on the right. Jump up to the second platform above, and stay at the 
right side of the platform to see two Wild Ptooie Pirahnas above. Run to the 
left side of the platform, and eat the Needlenoses that drop down onto the 
platforms above. When Yoshi has six eggs, face right and shoot three eggs up 
and right to defeat the first Wild Ptooie Pirahna.

After the second Wild Ptooie Pirahna has shot a Needlenose, quickly jump up to 
the platform above, and then jump up to the grass path on the right. Shoot 
three eggs down and right to defeat the second Wild Ptooie Pirahna, and then 
drop down to the platform on the left. Run left to collect the red coin at the 
left side of the platform, and then jump back up to the path on the right. Jump 
up to the platform on the right, and jump up the two clouds on the left.

From the second cloud, jump to the platform on the right, and then jump up to 
the grass path. Shoot the winged cloud up on the right to receive five stars, 
and then run right along the path to find a gap. Jump over the first gap, and 
wait at the left side of the path. A second Chomp Rock up on the right will 
roll into the first Chomp Rock. Jump over the first Chomp Rock as it rolls 
toward you, and then jump over the second gap to collect the red coin and land 
on a steep path.

Walk up to the top of the path, and ignore the first Chomp Rock that rolls left 
into the gap. Jump over the second Chomp Rock that rolls down onto the path, 
and then jump over the third gap to collect a red coin. Run right up the slope 
in the path, and jump the fourth gap at the top. Jump into the tunnel on the 
right, and ignore the Chomp Rock that drops down from the tunnel above. Jump up 
to the ledge on the left, jump to the ledge on the right, and then jump up to 
the grass path on the right. Eat the Shy Guy, run to the right side of the 
grass path, and shoot an egg up and right to collect the second flower.

                                   - Flower 3 -

Run back to the left side of the grass path, and jump over to the highest ledge 
on the left. Jump up to the high ledge on the right, and jump up the steps on 
the right to the grass path at the top. Run up the slope in the grass path, and 
then jump over to the grass path on the left. Run down the slope in the path, 
and jump left to the platform with the hut. Press up next to the hut to enter 
it and play a bonus game.

After exiting the hut, jump over to the cloud on the left, and then jump up to 
the high cloud on the right. Jump from the top cloud and go up the pipe above. 
After arriving in the secret area, run right to collect four eggs, and then 
shoot the winged cloud up on the right to reveal a metamorphosis bubble. Touch 
the bubble to transform into a helicopter, and then fly around the area to 
collect the five red coins. Exit the secret area. After returning to the first 
area, jump over to the grass path on the right, and enter the tunnel. Run to 
the end of the tunnel and go through the blue doors.

After arriving in the second area, eat the blue watermelon, and walk onto the 
ice on the right. Shoot ice at the Lantern Ghost, and then shoot the winged 
cloud above the platform after the first ice section to receive five stars. Run 
across the second ice section and shoot ice at the Lantern Ghost. Eat the next 
Lantern Ghost up on the first step, and then jump up to the top of the steps on 
the right. Eat the two Lantern Ghost, and then run across the ice to the pipe 
at the other side.

Jump on top of the pipe, and then jump over to the step on the left. Eat the 
blue watermelon above the first step, and then bounce up the next two steps to 
the platform at the top. Jump over to the step on the right, and jump right to 
the top step. Walk to the far right side of the step, and a Bumpty will slide 
across the ledge on the right and drop down the gap. Jump over the gap to land 
on the ledge, and then shoot the winged cloud above the left side of the ledge 
to create steps leading up to the left. Run up to the top of the steps and jump 
through the middle ring.

Jump right from the top of the steps to collect the middle red coin in the set 
of three coins, and then drop down to the ledge at the bottom of the steps. 
Jump up the two big steps on the right, and shoot ice at the Bumpty that slides 
toward you at the top. Continue right, and jump up to collect the middle red 
coin above the first ice section. Run to the right side of the ice, and shoot 
ice at the Bumpty. Shoot an egg up at the spike above the gap on the right, and 
then jump over the gap.

On the other side of the gap, quickly run right down the slope and under the 
spikes. Jump up the two steps at the other side of the ice, and shoot an egg at 
the spike above the gap. Jump over the gap, and drop down the two steps on the 
other side. Jump over the next gap and eat the Bumpty on the small platform. 
Jump up and eat the blue watermelon, and then drop down off the right side of 
the platform to land near the final section of ice in the area.

Walk slowly across the ice, shooting ice at the Bumptys along the way. Jump up 
to collect the red coin at the right side of the first set of seven coins. 
Shoot an egg at the first winged cloud, and jump up to collect the third 
flower. Continue walking slowly across the ice, and shoot the second winged 
cloud to receive five stars. Run to the platform at the far right side of the 
ice, and go up the pipe.

                                   - Flower 4 -

After arriving in the third area, jump up to the path on the right, and run 
right to find two Bumptys. Eat the first Bumpty, and shoot it right to defeat 
the second Bumpty. Shoot an egg up at the Fly Guy that appears holding the red 
coin above the winged cloud, and collect the red coin. Shoot an egg at the 
winged cloud to receive five stars, and then continue right along the path. 
Shoot an egg at the Fly Guy that appears at the left side of the fourth flower, 
and collect the red coin that is dropped. Jump on top of the post on the right, 
and then jump left to collect the fourth flower.

                                   - Flower 5 -

Jump back to the post on the right, and stomp it twice for a red coin. Eat the 
Needlenose that the Cactus Jack is holding on the right, and then shoot three 
eggs up and right to defeat the Wild Ptooie Pirahna on the ledge. Jump over the 
Cactus Jack, and jump up the two steps on the right. When the Thunder Lakitu 
appears, eat his cloud, and then jump over the second Cactus Jack to the path 
on the other side. Shoot an egg at the Fly Guy that appears above the platform 
on the right, and then jump up to the platform to collect the red coin.

Shoot an egg at the winged cloud on the left to receive five stars, and then 
jump over to the next platform on the right. Eat the cloud of the Thunder 
Lakitu when he gets near, and then shoot an egg at the winged cloud on the 
right to receive five stars. Hover right from the platform to collect the fifth 
flower, and land on the next platform. Face left, and wait for Thunder Lakitu 
to fly down. When he does, jump on him and land on his cloud. Float up, and 
jump to the cloud under the pipe. Go up the pipe.

After arriving in the secret area, drop down to the big cloud on the right and 
eat the green shell. Jump back up to the pipe on the left, and shoot an egg 
into the first tulip on the right to receive eight stars. Jump to the small 
cloud in the middle of the area, and eat the red shell. When the right tulip 
opens, jump up and shoot the red shell into the tulip for eight more stars. 
Drop off the right side of the small cloud to collect the red coin, and then 
jump up to the pipe at the left side of the area. Go down the pipe.

After returning to the third area, drop down off the right side of the cloud 
and shoot an egg up and right to hit the Fly Guy holding the red coin. Run 
right down the slope to collect the red coin, and eat the Bumpty that slides 
left. Continue right along the path, and jump over the Dizzy Dandy that rolls 
left. Run to the top of the small slope after the Dizzy Dandy, and shoot the 
Bumpty right to defeat the Pirahna Plant. Run down to the bottom of the small 
slope, and use the small spring ball to bounce up to the fluff above. Jump on 
the red switch that drops down to reveal the red blocks on the right.

Run right and jump over the first gap. Drop into the second gap to collect the 
red coin, and then jump back up to the path on the left. Jump right over the 
second gap, and drop into the third gap to collect the red coin. Jump up to the 
path on the right, and jump over the fourth gap. Jump over the next gap to land 
near the red arrow, and then run down the slope on the right. At the bottom of 
the slope, jump through the goal ring to complete the level.

  the expansion block to get up to the path.

  find the flower.

  Rock section.

  area. Shoot the winged cloud to reveal the metamorphosis bubble, and 
  transform into a helicopter to find the five red coins.

  platform. Jump on the platform, and go up the pipe to arrive in a secret area 
  with two tulips. Shoot a shell or egg into the tulips for the stars.

Key
  In the first area, drop down the gap in the path shortly before the Wild 
  Ptooie Pirahnas, and hover down to the grass path on the left. Stomp the 
  crate for the key.

Red Switch
  In the third area, wait for the Thunder Lakitu to appear near the fifth 
  flower. Jump on Thunder Lakitu when he appears, and ride his cloud up and 
  right. Keep moving right to a grey fluff platform with the red switch.

===============================================================================
                          Level 5-2: Ride The Ski Lifts
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Run right up the first slope at the start of the level, and jump over the 
snowball that rolls left down the second slope. Push the snowball left to the 
red arrow at the start of the level to reveal a winged cloud. Shoot the winged 
cloud and touch the bubble to receive a 1UP, and then push the snowball right 
along the path. On the small slope with the Tap-Tap, jump on top of the 
snowball, and then jump up to collect the four red coins above. Drop down to 
the path below, and continue pushing the snowball right.

When the snowball hits the wall at the right side of the area, jump on top of 
the snowball, and then jump up to the ledge on the right to collect two red 
coins. Jump up to the next ledge, and run down the small slope. Jump up to the 
ledge on the right, and drop down to the platform. Drop off the right side of 
the platform and pass through the middle ring, and then jump up the platforms 
above to exit the first area. After arriving in the second area, hover jump up 
to collect the second flower.

                                   - Flower 2 -

At the start of the second area, jump up to the path on the right and eat the 
Bumpty. Jump left to reveal a winged cloud near the wall, and then spit the 
Bumpty at the winged cloud to reveal a red switch. Jump on the red switch, and 
then quickly run up the slope on the right. Drop down both steps, and then jump 
over to the red blocks under the first ski lift. Run right and shoot the winged 
cloud above the first section of the ski lift to receive five stars, and then 
continue right along the first red block platform.

Eat the Bumpty above the platform, and then jump right from the end of the 
platform to land on the cloud. Shoot the Bumpty up to collect the red coin 
above the post, and then jump to the second red block platform on the right. 
Shoot an egg up at the Fly Guy that appears holding the 1UP above the right 
side of the winged cloud, and then shoot an egg up at the winged cloud to 
reveal the flower. Jump up to collect the second flower, and then jump over to 
the cloud on the right.

                                   - Flower 3 -

Shoot an egg up to collect the red coin above the post, and then collect eggs 
from the egg plant. Hover jump over the gap on the right and land on the snow 
path under the red switch. Jump up to hit the fluff, and then jump on the red 
switch to reveal the red blocks. Run right and jump to the red block platform. 
Shoot the winged cloud and collect the three stars, and then jump over the 
first cloud to land on the next red block platform.

Shoot the winged cloud for a 1UP, and then drop off the right side of the 
platform to land on the cloud. When the red blocks disappear, shoot an egg left 
to collect the two red coins in the line of six coins. Jump up and eat Lakitu's 
cloud, and then hover jump right. Eat the Bumpty and land on the ski lift 
platform, and then hover jump down to the platform on the right. Jump to the 
snow path up on the right, and pass through the middle ring. Continue right 
along the path to exit the second area.

After arriving in the third area, jump to the red steps on the right, and then 
jump up to the snow path at the top of the steps. Run down to the bottom of the 
slope on the right, and jump up to collect the top two red coins in the set of 
four coins. Jump over the Doctor Freezegood as he slides toward you, and run up 
and the next slope. Run down to the bottom of the next slope, and jump over the 
gap to collect the two red coins and the third flower.

                                   - Flower 4 -

On the other side of the gap, run up the slope on the right and drop down to 
the platform near the first ski lift. When the ski lift platform moves near, 
jump onto the platform to collect the two red coins. Hit the expansion block at 
the right side of the ski lift, and then jump left to land on top of the block. 
Hover jump right to land on the snow path near the red arrow. Run right under 
the second ski lift to pass through the middle ring, and then jump left to land 
on the ski lift platform.

Ride the ski lift platform along the track, and eat the Fly Guy holding the 1UP 
that appears at the start of the steep downward slope. Eat the other Fly Guy at 
the bottom of the steep slope, and then quickly jump to avoid the Doctor 
Freezegood on the platform. Land back on the platform, and jump up to collect 
the two red coins above the track. Ride to the end of the second ski lift to 
collect the fourth flower.

                                   - Flower 5 -

Drop down to the platform on the right, and then drop off the left side of the 
platform to land on the third ski lift. Ride down the long slope of the ski 
lift, and eat the Bumpty about half-way down. Shoot the first Bumpty left to 
defeat the second Bumpty, and then jump left to collect the fifth flower above 
the third Bumpty. Ride down to the corner of the track, and shoot the winged 
cloud to receive five stars.

Continue riding the ski lift right, and jump right at the end of the track to 
land on the platform of the fourth ski lift. Ride down the track and jump up to 
collect the middle red coin. Jump right at the end of the track and land on the 
fifth ski lift platform. Ride the ski lift to the end of the track, and drop 
down to the path below. Move to the right side of the path, and jump to the 
sixth ski lift when the Doctor Freezegood drops off the platform.

Collect the red coin above the middle of the track, and then stay on the 
platform to drop down to the seventh ski lift. Jump up to eat the first Bumpty 
on the way up the steep slope, and shoot the Bumpty up to defeat the second 
Bumpty. Stay on the seventh ski lift platform to pass through the goal ring and 
complete the level.

===============================================================================
                     Level 5-3: Danger - Icy Conditions Ahead
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Run right under the message block at the start of the level, and jump over the 
gap to land on the ice. Eat the red watermelon, and shoot fire right to hit the 
Bumpty. Run to the right side of the ice, and jump over the gap to land near 
the ice blocks. Run to the ice block on the right to stop moving, and wait 
above the egg plant until Yoshi has six eggs. Shoot fire at the ice on the 
right to melt the ice block, and run right to collect the first flower.

                                   - Flower 2 -

When the Spray Fish stops shooting water, do a low hover jump right, and shoot 
fire up at the winged cloud between the ice blocks to create a bridge over the 
water. Jump out of the water to land on the bridge, and run right to the tulip 
above the middle of the bridge. Shoot an egg of either of the blocks above so 
that it bounces into the tulip, and collect the eight stars. Run to the right 
side of the bridge and jump up to the ice blocks. Jump over the Bumpty on the 
right, and then drop down the two ice block steps to land on the ice path.

Jump over the gap on the right, and eat the Bumpty on the path. Jump over the 
gap on the right, and shoot the Bumpty to defeat the Pirahna Plant at the right 
side of the ice path. Walk to the far right side of the path, and shoot an egg 
right to defeat the next Pirahna Plant. Jump over the next two gaps on the 
right, and run right along the path to the Bumpty near the water. Eat the 
Bumpty, and spit him up at the bucket to knock the bucket into the water.

Drop down from the path to land on the bucket, and hold right to float across 
the water. Jump up to the left to land on the ice block at the side of the 
first gap, and then jump right to collect the top two red coins. Drop back down 
to the bucket in the water, and continue moving right. Jump up into the second 
gap and collect the top two red coins, and then drop down to the bucket. Float 
across to the right side of the water, and jump right to land on the ice path.

Face right on the path, and a Bumpty will slide left. Eat the first Bumpty, and 
shoot it right to defeat the second Bumpty. Eat the red watermelon, and then 
jump off the right side of the path to land on the pink rotating platform. Move 
the platform right, and shoot fire at the two ice blocks. Continue moving 
right, and shoot fire up at the ice block below the two red coins. Jump up to 
collect the two red coins, and then jump to the snow path on the right. Run 
right along the snow path to exit the first area.

After arriving in the second area, walk right and stand near the egg plant 
until Yoshi has six eggs. Drop down to the ice on the right, and run along to 
the right. Jump onto the small spring ball at the right side of the ice, and 
bounce up to the blocks on the right. Drop down off the right side of the 
blocks, and shoot the winged cloud up on the right to reveal a red watermelon. 
Eat the watermelon, and shoot fire at the ice block on the left. Run through 
the gap and pass through the middle ring.

Run through the gap on the right, and continue right along the ice to the 
platforms near the blocks. Jump up to the platform at the left side of the 
blocks and collect the red coin at the middle of the line of the three coins. 
Jump over the blocks to the platform on the right, and collect the middle red 
coin in the line. Drop down off the right side of the platform, and shoot fire 
left to melt the ice block. Run left to collect the second flower and the first 
super star.

                                   - Flower 3 -

Run right after collecting the first super star, and jump over the first two 
gaps. Quickly jump over the ice blocks after the second gap, and collect the 
second super star on the other side. Jump over the next set of ice blocks, and 
jump up the three steps. Collect the middle red coin at the top of the steps, 
and then run down the next three steps on the other side. Jump up to the snow 
path near the red arrow, and jump up to collect the third super star above the 
blue doors.

Run right over the blocks, and jump up to collect the red coin in the fourth 
ice block gap. Jump up to the snow path on the right, and drop down off the 
step to land near the egg plant. After transforming to Yoshi, Stand near the 
egg plant until Yoshi has six eggs, and then shoot an egg up at the three Baron 
Von Zeppelins holding the crate. Stomp the crate to receive six stars, and then 
run along to the right side of the path. Go up the pipe.

After arriving in the secret area, drop down off the right side of the pipe, 
and jump off the right side of the path. Touch the metamorphosis bubble to 
transform into a helicopter, and fly right to collect the coins. Stay near the 
top of the coins to avoid the first three Bumptys, fly low to avoid the fourth 
Bumpty, fly high to avoid the fifth Bumpty, and then fly low to avoid the sixth 
Bumpty. Fly down and touch the metamorphosis bubble to transform to Yoshi. Jump 
up to the path on the right, and go down the pipe.

After arriving in the third area, run right to the top of the steep slope. Jump 
up to collect the red coin above the tree, and then run down the slope on the 
right to arrive near the first ski lift. Wait for the Doctor Freezegood to drop 
off the ski lift platform, and then jump right to land on the platform. Ride 
the ski lift up to the top of the slope, and jump up to collect the middle red 
coin in the line of five coins.

Jump right at the end of the first ski lift, land on a Doctor Freezegood, and 
then drop down to the platform of the second ski lift. Ride the ski lift to the 
top of the steep slope, and then jump down to the snow path on the right. Eat 
the Bumpty on the path, and spit it right. Walk to the right side of the path, 
and the Doctor Freezegood will drop off the third ski lift. Jump over to the 
platform of the third ski lift, and the Doctor Freezegood will drop off the 
platform on the right.

Jump right to the fourth ski lift, and jump up to the third red coin in the 
line of four coins. Hover right from the fourth ski lift, and land at the right 
side of the Bumpty on the ice blocks. Eat the Bumpty, and then spit it over the 
gap on the right to defeat the Bumpty on the other side. Jump over the next 
three ice block gaps, and eat the Bumpty that slides left under the egg block. 
Hit the egg block to refill the egg supply, and then walk right along the ice 
blocks to the blue thorns.

Wait at the left side of the blue thorns, and spit the Bumpty right to defeat 
the Bumpty that slides under the blue thorns. Shoot the two lowest blue thorns, 
and then right along the ice blocks to the gap. Jump over the first gap to land 
on the tall ice block, and jump over the small gap on the right to collect the 
red coin. Land on the next tall ice block, and then drop down to the ledge at 
the left side of the ice block on the right.

Jump up to the ice block on the right, and hover jump right to land on the snow 
path. Run right along the path and jump over the Doctor Freezegood. Run up the 
slope and jump over the gap at the end of the path. Run right down the next 
small slope, and jump over the gap to collect the third flower. Jump over the 
Bumpty on the other side of the gap, and continue right along the path to exit 
the third area.

                                   - Flower 4 -

After arriving in the fourth area, run right to pass through the middle ring, 
and then jump up to the platform with the hut. Press up to enter the hut and 
put on the skis. Ski down the first big slope on the right, and jump the rock 
at the bottom of the slope to collect the red coin. Ride up the next small 
slope and jump the second rock to collect the red coin and land on the other 
side of the gap. Ride down the next slope and jump the two rocks at the bottom 
of the slope to collect the red coin. Jump the next gap and collect the fourth 
flower on the other side.

                                   - Flower 5 -

Ride down to the bottom of the next slope and jump the big gap to collect two 
red coins. Jump the rock, and then quickly jump again to clear the next gap. 
Ride down to the bottom of the slope and jump the gap to collect the fifth 
flower. Ski down to the bottom of the path to exit the fourth area. After 
arriving in the fifth area, ski down the slope and jump the huge gap. Continue 
skiing along the path to exit the fifth area.

After arriving in the sixth area, ski right along the path and go down the 
steep slope below the Baron Von Zeppelins. Jump the small rock at the bottom of 
the slope, and ride up the small slope. Ride down to the bottom of the next 
small slope, and jump the rock and the gap. On the other side of the gap, ride 
down the next small slope and jump the rock shortly after the Skeleton Goonie.

Drop off the end of the path to clear the gap, and ride down to the bottom of 
the slope. Jump over the next gap, jump the rock at the bottom of the next 
slope, and continue right along the path to exit the sixth ara. After arriving 
in the seventh area, run right along the path and jump through the goal ring to 
complete the level.

===============================================================================
                      Level 5-4: Sluggy The Unshaven's Fort
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Jump right to the platform at the start of the level, and run under the first 
Dangling Ghost. Run up the small slope on the other side, and then drop down 
off the platform to land near a Shy Guy pipe. Eat the Shy Guys until Yoshi has 
six eggs, and then continue right to the outline steps. Shoot an egg up at the 
winged cloud to create steps leading up to the right, and run right up to the 
top of the steps.

Jump up the three big steps on the right, and then face left. Hover jump left 
over to the bottom step with the red arrow, and jump up the three big steps on 
the left. Jump up to the yellow block at the top of the steps, and then jump 
left over the blue thorns to land on the next yellow block. Run left under the 
blue thorns, and jump to the yellow block at the left side of the area. Shoot 
an egg up through the blue thorns to collect the first flower.

                                   - Flower 2 -

Jump back to the yellow block on the right, and run under the blue thorns. Jump 
over to the right yellow block, and then jump right from the right side of the 
block to collect the middle red coin in the set of three coins. Land down on 
the red steps, and run right up to the top. Jump up the next three big steps to 
land on the path, and run right. Jump over both Georgette Jellys, and continue 
right to the second Dangling Ghost in the area.

Quickly run right under the Dangling Ghost to avoid the four Sluggys that drop 
down. Face left after passing the Sluggys, and shoot to collect the two red 
coins near the top of the Dangling Ghost. Continue right along the path, and go 
down the pipe. After arriving in the secret area, defeat the three Sluggys to 
reveal the flower. Shoot an egg up to collect the second flower, and then go up 
the pipe at the left side of the area.

                                   - Flower 3 -

After returning to the first area, shoot an egg up at the winged cloud on the 
right to create a bridge over the blue thorns. Jump right from the pipe, and 
run along to the other side of the bridge. Jump up the two big steps at the end 
of the bridge, and drop down the next two steps to land near the third Dangling 
Ghost. Jump over the two Georgette Jellys, and run right under the Dangling 
Ghost. Jump up the two small steps, and then drop down the big step to land 
near the Shy Guy.

Eat the Shy Guy, and shoot an egg off the wall on the right to hit the block. 
Shoot another egg up and right to collect the red coin in the gap, and then 
jump up to the yellow platform on the right. Ride the yellow platform to the 
end of the wire, and shoot the winged cloud to create steps leading up to the 
right. Drop off the right side of the platform to land on the steps, and then 
jump left and land on the blue spiral platform. Ride the blue spiral platform 
left along the wire to collect the red coin.

Hover jump right from the blue spiral platform and land on the path at the 
bottom of the steps. Run right to the top of the steps, and jump onto the path 
near the egg plant. Shoot an egg up at the winged cloud to receive five stars, 
and then jump left over the gap to the path on the other side. Jump up the step 
on the left, and jump left over the crumbling block to land near the fourth 
Dangling Ghost in the area. Run under the Dangling Ghost, and shoot an egg at 
the crumbling blocks on the other side. Run left, and go down the pipe.

After arriving in the second area, eat the two Fly Guys and collect the two red 
coins that are dropped. Run left along the path and drop down through the 
paddles to the egg block. Drop down to the crumbling block below the egg block, 
and hit the egg block to refill the egg supply. Shoot an egg at the crumbling 
block, and drop down through the gap to land on top of the pipe below. Go 
through the pipe.

After returning to the first area, drop down off the right side of the pipe to 
land on the blue block, and shoot an egg at the winged cloud on the right to 
create a bridge over the blue thorns. Run to the right side of the bridge, and 
jump up to the next bridge above. Jump through the middle ring, and then jump 
up the step to the path on the left. Quickly run left along the path to avoid 
four Sluggys and a Whirly Fly Guy. Shoot an egg up at the Dangling Ghost, and 
then shoot another egg up to collect the middle red coin in the line of seven 
coins.

Continue left under the Dangling Ghost, and run left to the top of the red 
steps. Jump onto the platform at the top of the first set of red steps, and 
drop off the left side of the platform. Hover right to collect two red coins, 
and land back on the red steps. Run left to the top of the steps, jump onto the 
platform, and run up the next set of steps on the right. Jump up to the ledge 
at the top of the steps, and shoot an egg up at the winged cloud above to 
receive five stars.

Jump up the two big steps on the right, and drop down to the ledge on the right 
near the sixth Dangling Ghost in the area. Drop off the right side of the ledge 
and hover to the ledge down on the right. Jump up the three big steps on the 
right, and continue right to the seventh Dangling Ghost. Drop down off the 
step, and hover right. Follow the line of coins, and collect the red coin at 
the right side of the line. Jump up the three steps on the right, and go 
through the blue doors.

After arriving in the third area, run right and pass through the middle ring. 
Jump up the two steps on the right, and drop down to the see-saw platform. Stay 
on the left side of the platform to collect the red coin, and then run up to 
the right side of the platform. When the platform tilts down, drop off the 
right side of the platform and hover right to pass through the paddles.

Run right along the tunnel, and jump right from the top of the small block to 
collect the second flower. Run right and push the jelly block to the wall on 
the right. Jump on top of the block, and jump up the two red platforms above. 
Run through the pipe on the right.

                                   - Flower 4 -

After arriving in the fourth area, drop off the right side of the pipe and run 
right along the path. Drop off the edge of the path and land on the Support 
Ghost below. The Support Ghost moves right and stops at various locations in 
the area. When the Support Ghost stops for the second time, shoot an egg up at 
the winged cloud on the right to receive five stars. When the Support Ghost 
stops for the third time, jump right to collect the fourth flower.

                                   - Flower 5 -

Drop back down to the platform on the left, and continue riding the Support 
Ghost right. When the Support Ghost stops for the fourth time, stay at the far 
left side of the platform to avoid the Sluggys that drop down. When the Support 
Ghost stops for the sixth time, jump left to collect the red coin in the gap, 
and then drop back down to the Support Ghost platform. When the Support Ghost 
stops for the seventh time, stay at the left side of the platform to avoid the 
blue thorns.

When the Support Ghost starts moving for the seventh time, hold down to duck 
under the block. Shoot an egg at the winged cloud on the left to receive five 
stars, and then hold down to duck under the blue thorns when the Support Ghost 
starts moving for the eighth time. When the Support Ghost stops for the eighth 
time, shoot an egg right to collect the two red coins near the blue thorns. 
Drop down the two steps on the right, and drop down off the right side of the 
bottom step to land on the Support Ghost when it starts moving.

When the Support Ghost stops moving for the ninth time, jump up and eat the two 
Fly Guys holding the red coins. Collect the two red coins, and then drop off 
the right side of the platform to land on the Support Ghost platform when it 
stops for the tenth time. When the Support Ghost stop for the eleventh time, 
shoot an egg left to collect the red coin at the left side of the line of four 
coins, and then shoot an egg through the fluff on the right to collect the 
fifth flower.

When the Dangling Ghost stops for the thirteenth time, shoot an egg up at the 
cracked block, and then shoot an egg up at the winged cloud for a 1UP. When the 
Support Ghost starts moving for the thirteenth time, jump over the block on the 
right and land back on the platform. When the Support Ghost starts moving for 
the fourteenth time, hold down to duck under the block, and then jump over the 
blue thorns to collect the two red coins. When the Support Ghost stops moving 
for the seventeenth time, drop off the right side of the platform and run right 
along the path. Go through the blue doors.

After arriving in the fifth area, run right under the Sluggys to the middle 
ring at the other side of the area. Jump through the middle ring, collect the 
three eggs on the platform, and then go through the red doors.

                     - Boss Fight 9: Sluggy the Unshaven -

After arriving in the area, stand near the egg plant on the left until Yoshi 
has six eggs. Run right along the path to find Sluggy the Unshaven. At the 
start of the boss fight, shoot eggs toward the heart of the slug. Shoot the 
heart of the slug five times to win the boss fight.

===============================================================================
                            Level 5-5: Goonie Rides!
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Run right at the start of the level and run up the small slope to the gap. Jump 
over the gap, and eat the Bubble Dayzee on the other side. Jump over the gap, 
and then run down the small slope to the next gap. Jump the gap to collect the 
six coins, and wait at the left side of the path for the Goonie to pass by. Run 
up the small slope, and go down the steep slope on the other side. Jump over 
the Crazee Dayzee at the bottom of the slope to avoid being hit by the Shy Guy 
dropped from the Goonie.

Run to the end of the path on the right, and jump over the gap to the path on 
the other side. Run down the steep slope on the right, and eat the Mufti Guy in 
the flowers at the bottom of the slope. Run under the Hefty Goonie when it 
drops down onto the flowers, and then run to the right side of the path. When 
the Goonie drops the Shy Guy, jump over the gap on the right and eat the Shy 
Guy. Run down the slope in the path and jump over the Mufti Guy in the yellow 
flowers.

Continue right along the path, and wait on the slope before the purple bush to 
defeat the three Flightless Goonies. Shoot an egg at the Fly Guy holding the 
winged cloud up on the right to receive five stars, and then jump over the 
Bowling Goonie as it rolls left. Run right to the edge of the path, and jump 
over the gap to collect the five coins. Quickly run right along the path to 
avoid the Shy Guy dropped by the Goonie, and jump over the gap at the right 
side of the path.

Jump right over the gap from the small section of sloped path, and continue 
right over the bumpy path to the red arrow. Jump over the Bowling Goonie that 
rolls from the ledge on the right, and then jump right to land on the ledge. 
Jump over to the platform on the right, and then jump to the path on the right. 
Wait at the left side of the path until a Goonie flies down from the right. 
Jump on the Goonie, and face left.

Ride the Goonie up and left, and drop left onto the green path after passing 
the pipe. Run left along the path to collect the red coin, and then jump up to 
the ledge at the right side of the path. When a Goonie passes by flying right, 
drop off the right side of the ledge to land on the Goonie, and then go up the 
pipe on the right. After arriving in the secret area, jump right to avoid the 
Bumptys that slide left. Defeat the remaining four Bumptys to reveal the 
flower. Hover jump up to collect the first flower, and then go down the pipe.

                                   - Flower 2 -

After returning to the first area, jump down to the platform on the right, and 
then jump up to the path on the right. Run along to the right side of the path, 
and shoot an egg down and right to collect the two red coins at the left side 
of the set of three coins. Hover jump right under the Pirahna Plant and land on 
the platform on the other side. Jump up to the third platform, and then jump up 
to the path at the top of the slope. Shoot the winged cloud above the left side 
of the path to receive five stars, and then run right to exit the first area.

After arriving in the second area, run right along the path and pass through 
the middle ring. Continue right up the slope in the path, and jump up at the 
top of the slope to touch the metamorphosis bubble. After transforming into the 
helicopter, fly right to the first set of twelve coins. Collect the two red 
coins at the bottom-right corner of the set of coins, and then continue right 
to hit the second metamorphosis bubble. Fly right along to the end of the path, 
and then fly up and right to collect the two red coins.

Fly right at the set of eight coins to collect two red coins. Fly up after 
collecting the red coin, and fly right along the path to collect the two red 
coins before the third metamorphosis bubble. Hit the metamorphosis bubble, and 
continue right to collect the next two red coins. At the end of the path, fly 
right to the set of sixteen coins. Fly up and right after passing the set of 
coins to collect three red coins in the line of five coins. Fly right after 
collecting the fifth coin in the line, and collect the second flower below the 
fourth metamorphosis bubble.

                                   - Flower 3 -

Fly up and right after collecting the second flower, and fly right over the top 
of the Wild Ptooie Pirahna. Continue flying right, and collect the third flower 
in the top-right corner of the area. Fly left toward the Wild Ptooie Pirahna, 
and then fly down to the right to hit the Yoshi block. After transforming to 
Yoshi, shoot the winged cloud at the right side of the platform to receive five 
stars. Drop off the right side of the platform, and run right to exit the 
second area.

                                   - Flower 4 -

After arriving in the third area, run right down the small slope in the path, 
and continue right to pass through the middle ring. Run to the right side of 
the path, and jump the gap. On the other side of the gap, eat the Goonie that 
flies left, and then jump up to eat the Fly Guy holding the winged cloud for 
five stars. Run right to the top of the slope in the path, and jump over the 
gap. Wait at the left side of the path, and eat the Needlenoses that the Wild 
Ptooie Pirahna spits until Yoshi has six eggs.

After the Wild Ptooie Pirahna spits the third Needlenose in the set, run right 
to the top of the slope and shoot three eggs down and right to defeat the Wild 
Ptooie Pirahna. Drop down into the gap on the right to reveal a winged cloud, 
and shoot the winged cloud to receive five stars. Jump out of the gap to land 
on the path on the right, and run right down to the path at the bottom of the 
slope. Jump down to the platform on the right, and then shoot an egg down at 
the Pirahna Plant on the left. Drop down to the platform on the left, and run 
up the slope on the left to collect two red coins and the fourth flower.

                                   - Flower 5 -

Run right down the slope to the platform, and jump over the small gap to the 
next platform up on the right. Jump up to the path on the right, and jump over 
the gap at the right side of the path to land near a red arrow. Run right along 
the path and hit the two egg blocks to collect two eggs, and then continue 
right to the first red switch. Jump on the red switch, and hover jump over to 
the lowest vertically moving platform on the right. When the platform moves up, 
jump right to land on the slope under the Wild Ptooie Pirahna, and then quickly 
jump left to land on the second vertically moving platform.

Jump left to land on the red block platform, and jump off the left side of the 
platform to land on the vertically moving platform. Jump left from the platform 
to land on the red block, and jump right up to the next vertically moving 
platform. Jump right to the red block platform, and then jump right to the 
final vertically moving platform in the area. Jump up to the platform on the 
right and land on the second red switch. Jump left to land on the red block 
platform, and jump up to the final red block platform on the left. From the 
platform, jump onto one of the Goonies that flies to the right.

Face right, and stay on the Goonie to collect the two red coins at the start of 
the line of four coins. Continue riding the Goonie up to the high path above 
the normal path. Jump up to the high path, and then jump over the small gap on 
the right to land near the flower. Jump up to collect the fifth flower above 
the path, and then drop off the right side of the path to land on the path 
below. Shoot an egg up at the winged cloud on the right to receive five stars, 
and then continue right along the path to the goal ring. Jump through the goal 
ring to complete the level.

===============================================================================
                        Level 5-6: Welcome To Cloud World
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Run right along the platforms at the start of the level, and drop down onto the 
pipes. Eat the Shy Guys coming out of the fifth pipe, and then shoot a Shy Guy 
into the tulip above for eight stars. Jump to the far right pipe, and then jump 
right to the big cloud. Run right up the first slope in the cloud, and eat the 
Gusty that flies left before the Pirahna Plant. Eat the Lakitu that floats 
above on his cloud, and then jump up to collect the first flower.

                                   - Flower 2 -

Shoot an egg up at the winged cloud on the right to receive three stars, and 
run down the slope in the cloud. Eat the Woozy Guy at the bottom of the slope, 
and jump up to collect the two red coins in the set of five coins. Run to the 
far right side of the first cloud, and jump over the gap to land on the second 
cloud. Eat the Lakitu when he floats near, and then hover jump left to collect 
the red coin in the middle of the diagonal line of three coins. Land back on 
the second cloud, and shoot the winged cloud up on the right for five stars.

Run up the slope in the second cloud and eat the Woozy Guy at the top. Jump up 
to the small cloud above the right side of the second cloud, and stomp the 
Green Glove down on the small cloud on the right. Jump up to the top of the 
green pipe, and then drop down off the right side of the pipe to land on a 
cloud with the Huffin Puffin. Jump over to the right side of the Huffin Puffin, 
and jump to the next cloud on the right to collect the red coin. Drop down to 
the cloud on the right to collect the next red coin, and then shoot an egg up 
at the right side of the Slugger to collect the second flower.

                                   - Flower 3 -

Shoot an egg at the Green Glove on the right, and then jump up to the first 
green pipe on the right. Jump straight up from the pipe to collect the red coin 
at the left side of the set of coins, and then jump up to the cloud on the 
right. Collect the red coin at the right side of the set of coins, and then 
hover jump right toward the two Sluggers on the clouds. Stomp both Sluggers, 
and shoot the winged cloud above the right cloud. Jump up from the right cloud 
to collect the third flower.

                                   - Flower 4 -

Jump over to the next cloud on the right, and jump up to the cloud above the 
left side of the Green Glove. Drop down off the right side of the cloud and 
stomp the first Green Glove. Jump up to the highest cloud on the right, and 
then jump down off the right side of the cloud to land on the second platform. 
Jump up to the big cloud on the right, and jump the gap at the right side of 
the cloud to land on the next cloud.

Jump up and eat both Lakitus, and then run right along the cloud. Eat the Woozy 
Guy near the middle of the cloud, and shoot the Pirahna Plant above the right 
side of the cloud. Jump up to the small cloud, and jump to collect the two red 
coins. Drop down to the next big cloud on the right. Run right to avoid the two 
Baron Von Zeppelins which drop Needlenoses, and jump up to collect the fourth 
flower near the start of the big cloud.

                                   - Flower 5 -

Run to the far right side of the big cloud, and shoot an egg up at the winged 
cloud under the Huffin Puffin to receive five stars. Jump the gap over to the 
next big cloud on the right, and eat the two Lakitus that appear. Run under the 
two Baron Von Zeppelins above the middle of the cloud, and jump off the right 
side of the cloud to land on the logs. Eat both Woozy Guys at the left side of 
the logs, run under the Baron Von Zeppelin, and jump onto the small cloud at 
the right side of the logs. Run right along the cloud to exit the first area.

After arriving in the second area, jump off the right side of the small cloud 
and pass through the middle ring. Run right along the logs and jump over the 
three Flightless Goonies near the right side. Jump off the right side of the 
logs to land on the big cloud, and then jump off the right side of the cloud to 
collect the red coin. Hover over to the small cloud on the right, and stomp the 
Green Glove. Face left, and a balloon will appear. Jump onto the balloon, and 
stay on it as it floats up.

Jump right from the balloon to land on the see-saw platform, and jump off the 
right side of the platform to collect two red coins and land on the green 
pipes. Go down the second pipe. After arriving in the secret area, jump up at 
the right side of the fifth pipe to reveal a winged cloud. Shoot the winged 
cloud to reveal the red switch, and then jump on the switch to reveal a red 
arrow. Stand above the arrow and press down to arrive in a secret area with 114 
coins. Go up the pipe at the bottom-left corner of the area.

After returning to the second area, wait for the three Flightless Goonies to 
drop off the left side of the cloud, and then jump up to the big cloud on the 
right. Jump off the right side of the cloud, collect the two red coins, and 
land on the platform at the left side of the green pipe. When the Green Glove 
at the right side of the pipe hits the green switch, jump up to the green 
switch platform on the left. Jump up the two small clouds above, and then jump 
left to land on the big cloud.

Shoot the winged cloud above the big cloud to receive five stars, and then jump 
up to the small cloud on the right. Jump to the next cloud on the right, and 
then jump up to the tiny cloud above. Jump up to the red switch platform on the 
left, jump up to the next red switch platform on the right, and then jump up to 
collect the red coin. Jump from the platform to the small cloud on the left, 
and then jump up the next two clouds. Jump right to land on top of the green 
pipe, and then jump over to the small cloud on the right.

Jump up to the big cloud on the right, and drop off the right side of the big 
cloud to land on the small cloud. Drop off the right side of the small cloud, 
and hover right to collect the red coin in the middle of the set of three 
coins. Land on the pipe, and run along the small clouds to find two Pirahna 
Plants. Wait near the start of the second cloud, and a Green Glove will shoot 
an egg up to defeat the first Pirahna Plant. Run under the second Pirahna 
Plant, and shoot an egg to defeat the third Pirahna Plant. Jump up to the pipe 
at the right side of the small clouds, and jump off the right side of the pipe.

Hover right to collect the red coin under the pipe, and land on the cloud. Jump 
to the big cloud on the right, and shoot an egg up at the winged cloud to 
receive five stars. Jump to the platform on the right, and hover under the pipe 
on the right to collect two red coins. Jump up to the small platform on the 
right, and shoot an egg at the Pirahna Plant. Hover under the pipe to collect 
the fifth flower, and jump down the small clouds on the other side of the pipe 
to find the goal ring. Jump through the goal ring to complete the level.
