===============================================================================
                       Level 5-7: Shifting Platforms Ahead
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Run left along the path at the start of the level, and jump left from the top 
of the first rock to land on the yellow platform. Ride the platform over the 
bump in the track, and then jump over to the next yellow platform on the left. 
Jump left down to the green platform on the circular track, and then jump up to 
the next green platform on the left. Jump up to the yellow platform, and ride 
it along the track. Jump over the block at the bottom of the track, and land 
back on the platform. Ride the platform to the end of the track, jump left to 
land on the block, and then run left to the path with the red arrow.

Eat the Bumpty, and drop down off the platform at the left side of the path to 
land on the yellow platform. Ride the platform over and under the first three 
spheres, and then face right. Shoot the Bumpty from the path at the Raven on 
the fourth sphere, and then continue to ride the platform to the end of the 
track. Jump up at the end of the track, and land on the green platform above. 
Ride the platform to the top of the circular track, and then jump up to the 
platform on the left to collect four coins. Jump up from the platform to land 
on the log platform.

Jump up to the log platform on the right, and jump up to the green platform on 
the horizontal track. Jump up to the next log platform, and then jump up to the 
green platform on the sloped track. Ride the platform up the slope at the right 
side of the track, and jump up to the yellow platform above. Stand on the 
middle of the platform to avoid the Tap-Taps, and jump right at the end of the 
track to land on the platform near the green rotating platform. Jump onto a 
Goonie, and fly up and left to the pipe at the top-left corner of the area. Go 
up the pipe.

After arriving in the secret area, jump up to the fourth cloud on the right, 
and jump across the six falling blocks to the platform with the flower. Jump up 
to collect the first flower, and jump right to land on the red switch on the 
next platform. Drop off the left side of the platform to land on the first red 
block step. Drop off the right side of the first step, and then run left down 
the next three steps. Shoot the winged cloud at the left side of the bottom 
step to receive five stars, and then run left to the pipe at the bottom-left 
corner of the area. Go down the pipe.

                                   - Flower 2 -

After returning to the first area, jump over the gap on the right, and then 
jump up to the green rotating platform. Ride the platform to the end of the 
first track, and continue to ride the platform along the second track. Jump 
right at the end of the second track and land on the yellow platform. When the 
platform starts to go down the wire, jump right to land on a red and yellow 
platform. Stay on the platform to collect two red coins and the second flower.

                                   - Flower 3 -

Jump right to land on the platform, and ride down the track. Hit the Raven on 
the second sphere, and jump right at the end of the track to land on the green 
platform. Jump across the next two platforms, and drop down to the yellow 
platform on the horizontal track. Jump up to the green platform on the track 
above, and jump right from the platform to land on the blocks at the right side 
of the Tap-Tap. Drop down off the right block to land on the yellow platform, 
and stay on the platform as it drops down to the next section of track.

Ride down the track to find three Tap-Taps. Move to the right side of the 
platform after the first Tap-Tap to collect two red coins, and move to the left 
side of the platform after the second Tap-Tap to collect the next two red 
coins. Jump off the right side of the platform to land on the cloud, and jump 
up to the next cloud on the right. Run right along the cloud to avoid the first 
Shy Guy, and jump up to hit the three Baron Von Zeppelins holding the crate.

Stomp the crate for four stars, and run to the right side of the cloud. Jump 
onto the red and yellow platform, and stay on the track to collect eleven 
coins. After collecting the final coin in the line, jump right to land on the 
block. When the Raven moves to the right side of the sphere, jump right to land 
on the sphere, and jump up to the path on the right. Shoot the winged cloud up 
on the right to receive five stars, and then go down the pipe on the right to 
exit the first area.

After arriving in the second area, ride the green platform down to the circular 
track at the left side of the Wild Ptooie Pirahna. Stand at the left side of 
the platform, and eat the Needlenoses until Yoshi has six eggs. Shoot three 
eggs right to defeat the Wild Ptooie Pirahna, and then jump to the tunnel on 
the right. Jump over the pipe, and shoot an egg down and right to create a gap 
in the blue fluff. Collect the three red coins at the left side of the flower, 
and then jump up to collect the third flower. Run left and go down the pipe.

                                   - Flower 4 -

After arriving in the third area, run right to pass through the middle ring. 
Run up to the top of the slope, and drop down off the right edge of the path to 
land on the falling block. Jump across the falling blocks on the right, and 
jump right from the fifth falling block to land on the path. Jump over the two 
Bumptys, and drop down off the right side of the path to land on the thin 
falling block. Jump off the right side of the block to collect two red coins 
and the fourth flower.

                                   - Flower 5 -

Ride the falling block down to the platform, and then jump up to the path on 
the right. Pass through the paddles at the right side of the path, and drop 
down to the small falling block. Jump right to land on the big block, and hover 
jump right to collect two red coins, one from each set of three coins. After 
landing on the small blocks, jump up to the highest block at the top-left 
corner, and then jump right across the blocks to collect two red coins. On the 
far right block, jump to the big block on the left, and then jump right to the 
platform with the Bumpty to collect the fifth flower.

Eat the Bumpty and spit it off either side of the platform. Jump up to collect 
the three red coins, and drop down the gap on the right to land on a block near 
a Bullet Bill cannon. Face right, and eat the Bullet Bill when it is shot out 
of the cannon. Ride the falling block down to collect two red coins, and then 
jump up to the block on the right. Eat the Bullet Bill, and ride the block when 
it falls down. Jump to the block on the right, and run right to the goal path. 
Jump through the goal ring to complete the level.

~~ Items ~~

Flower 1
  Jump on a Goonie, and go up the pipe at the top-left corner of the first 
  area. The flower is over at the right side of the secret area.

Flower 2

  the yellow platform on the track. When the platform starts to go down the 
  track, jump right to land on a red and yellow platform, which will move up 
  the track to the flower.

Flower 3
  At the right side of the pipe that leads to the third area, shoot an egg 
  through the blue fluff on the right. Run through the gap in the fluff to find 
  the flower.

Flower 4
  Run quickly along the long, thin falling block in the third area, and jump 
  off at the right side to land near the flower.

Flower 5
  Above a platform at the top-right corner of the third area.

2 Red Coins
  There is one red coin at either side of the second flower.

4 Red Coins
  Ride the platform down past the second set of Tap-Taps in the first area to 
  find the red coins.

3 Red Coins
  At the left side of the third flower.

2 Red Coins
  At the left side of the fourth flower.

2 Red Coins
  There are two sets of coins shortly after the paddles in the third area. The 
  middle coin in each set is a red coin.

  Above the falling blocks at the top of the third area.

3 Red Coins
  At the right side of the fifth flower.

2 Red Coins
  At the left side of the lowest Bullet Bill in the third area.

5 Stars
  In the first area, shoot the winged cloud above the second platform track.

5 Stars
  Jump on a Goonie, and go up the pipe at the top-left corner of the first 
  area. Shoot the winged cloud at the bottom-right corner of the secret area.

4 Stars
  Shortly after the second set of Tap-Taps in the first area, shoot the Baron 
  Von Zeppelins holding the crate above the clouds, and stomp the crate.

5 Stars
  Shoot the winged cloud near the pipe at the end of the first area.

10 Stars
  Pass through the middle ring at the start of the third area.

===============================================================================
                      Level 5-8: Raphael The Raven's Castle
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Run right along the logs at the start of the level to the cloud at the other 
side. Jump across the five platforms, and drop down to the cloud on the right. 
Drop off the right side of the cloud to land on the red and yellow platform, 
and ride the platform up to the top of the track. When the platform gets to the 
highest point, jump to the platform up on the left. Ride the platform up the 
track and jump up to the highest red and yellow platform in the area. Ride the 
platform up to the highest point, and jump up to the platform with the doors. 
Go through the blue doors.

After arriving in the second area, jump up to the log platform up on the right, 
and then jump up to the platform near the Shy Guy pipe. Eat the Shy Guys until 
Yoshi has six eggs, and then jump to the log platform on the left. Eat the Mace 
Guy, jump up to the ledge on the left, and then jump up to the path on the 
right. Eat the second Mace Guy, and run right along the path. Eat the blue 
watermelon, and then drop down the two small steps. Jump over the gap in the 
platforms on the right, and shoot ice to defeat the first Blow Hard.

Jump right over the next two gaps, and shoot ice at the second Blow Hard. 
Ignore the third Blow Hard down on the right, and jump over the next two gaps. 
Run down the slope in the platforms, and shoot ice up at the winged cloud above 
the lowest platform to receive five stars. Drop down to the next platform on 
the right, and eat the two Shy Guys. Run right to the top of the slope in the 
platform, and jump up to the next platform. Jump on the Bouncing Bullet Bill 
and hover up to the platform above. Jump up to collect the first flower.

                                   - Flower 2 -

Jump up to the platform above after collecting the first flower, and drop down 
the small gap to the platform below. Jump on the Bouncing Bullet Bill and hover 
up the tunnel to land on the platform at the top. Collect the two red coins at 
the right side of the flower, and jump up to collect the second flower.

                                   - Flower 3 -

Run to the right side of the room and jump up to the highest platform. Collect 
the blue watermelon above the right side of the pipe, and jump to the log 
platform on the right. Run up to the top of the slope in the platform, and jump 
up to the platform above. Face left and wait for the Bullet Bill to pass, and 
then jump up to the platform at the top-right corner of the area, near the red 
arrow pointing left. Shoot ice left at the Mace Guy, and wait for a Bullet Bill 
to fire out of the cannon down on the right.

When it does, follow the Bullet Bill left along the path, and drop down off the 
left side of the path in front of the Bullet Bill. Stand under the platform 
with the red arrow under it, and jump on the Bullet Bill. Bounce up to the 
platform above, and run left to pass through the middle ring. Continue left to 
collect three red coins and the third flower, and then drop down through the 
paddles at the left side of the path. Run through the next set of paddles and 
eat the arrow platform.

Run left under the message block, and continue to the egg block at the left 
side of the path. Hit the egg block to refill the egg supply, and then run 
right to the two red arrows pointing up. Shoot an egg up in line with the red 
arrows, and then shoot eggs up to defeat the Kaboomba above the first block on 
the right. Spit the arrow platform under the red arrows, and ride it straight 
up to the top of the area. Jump off the arrow platform to the blocks on the 
right, and run right to the green pipe. Shoot the winged cloud at the left side 
of the pipe to receive five stars, and then go up the pipe.

                                   - Flower 4 -

After arriving in the third area, ride the arrow platform straight, and collect 
the three red coins in the top line of the set of eleven coins. Jump and move 
the arrow platform slightly left or right to avoid the first Raven on the 
sphere, and then collect the fourth flower between the two Ravens at the top of 
the area. Jump from the arrow platform and go up the pipe.

                                   - Flower 5 -

After arriving in the fourth area, drop down off the right side of the pipe, 
and run along the path to the log platform. Jump up to the platform, and jump 
off at the right side to land on the horizontally rotating platform. Jump off 
the left side of the platform to collect two red coins, and hover right to land 
back on the platform. Jump off the right side of the platform to collect the 
next two red coins and land on the second horizontally rotating platform. Jump 
off the right side of the platform to collect one red coin, and face left. Drop 
off the left side of the platform, and hold right to land on the path. Run down 
the steps on the right, and go through the blue doors.

After arriving in the secret area, jump left and hit the metamorphosis bubble 
to transform into a train. Go left and hold down to ride on the track. Take the 
first turning on the right, and drop off the right side of the platform. Get on 
the the next section of track, and take the first turning down. Ride left to 
hit the metamorphis bubble, and ride back on to the track on the right. Take 
the first turning right, and ride along the track to collect the seven red 
coins. Drop off the end of the track to collect the fifth flower, and after 
transforming into Yoshi, go through the blue doors on the right.

After returning to the fourth area, jump on the large spring ball and bounce up 
to the platform above. Run right along the path to pass through the middle 
ring, jump up the step on the right, and then use the large spring ball to 
bounce up to the horizontally rotating platform high above. Jump up to the 
sixth horizontally rotating platform, and jump up at left side of the platform 
to land on the log platform.

Jump up the step on the right, and wait under the sloped platform for the three 
Flightless Goonies to drop down. When they drop off the end of the slope, jump 
up to land on the platform. Run left up the slope, and jump up to the small 
platform on the left to avoid the first Bowling Goonie. Jump up to the platform 
above. When the three Flightless Goonies drop off the right side of the 
platform, jump up to the platform to avoid the second Bowling Goonie.

Jump up the next two platforms, and wait for the Bowling Goonie to roll off the 
platform on the right. Jump right to land on the platform, and then jump up to 
the ledge on the left to land near the red steps. Eat the three Flightless 
Goonies that run down the steps, and then run right up the first set of steps 
to the top. Shoot the winged cloud for five stars, and run left up the second 
set of steps. Jump to the platform on the right, and go through the red doors.

                     - Boss Fight 10: Raphael the Raven -

At the start of the boss fight, two posts will be on the sphere. When Raphael 
runs to the opposite side of the sphere from the post, quickly stomp the post. 
Raphael will then turn dark red, and will become faster. When he stomps the 
planet, jump over the flames, and stomp the post a second time. He will then 
turn bright red, and will run even faster. Stomp the post and hit Raphael a 
third time to win the boss fight.

~~ Items ~~

  In the second area, in the section with the cracked blocks, shoot the winged 
  cloud near the top-left corner of the room for the 1UP.

Flower 1

Flower 2

  ball, just after the Bouncing Bullet Bill. Jump on the Bouncing Bullet Bill 
  and bounce up the tunnel to land near the flower.

Flower 3
  At the top-right corner of the second area, wait for a Bullet Bill to be 
  fired out of the cannon. When it appears, follow the Bullet Bill left, and 
  use it to bounce up to the platform above. Run left to find the flower.

Flower 4
  Between the two Ravens at the top of the third area.

Flower 5
  At the start of the fourth area, don't jump onto the horizontally rotating 
  platform. Instead, hover jump right from below the platform, and go through 
  the blue doors in the secret tunnel. Ride the train to find the flower.

2 Red Coins

3 Red Coins
  At the right side of the third flower.

3 Red Coins
  In the third area, there are three red coins in the set of eleven coins.

7 Red Coins

  There are two red coins above each side of the first horizontally rotating 
  platform in the fourth area.

1 Red Coins
  There are five coins above the right side of the second horizontally rotating 
  platform in the fourth area. The third coin in the line is the red coin.

5 Stars
  In the second area, shoot the winged cloud after the third Blow Hard.

10 Stars

10 Stars
  Pass through the middle ring after the two horizontally rotating platforms in 
  the fourth area.

5 Stars
  Shoot the winged cloud before the red doors near the end of the fourth area.

===============================================================================
                            Extra 5: Kamek's Revenge
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Run right at the start of the level, and jump over the small logs to the 
see-saw platform on the other side. Jump up at the left side of the platform to 
collect the red coin, and then jump over to the Chomp Rock on the right. Stand 
near either side of the Chomp Rock and roll it off the edge of the log. Drop 
down to collect the key, and then hover right to the log above the first Green 
Glove to collect the red coin.

Jump right and drop down to the platform below the second Green Glove to 
collect the next red coin. Jump right over the third Green Glove, and run right 
to the red switch. Hit the egg block to refill the egg supply, and then jump on 
the red switch. Jump up the two logs on the left, and jump right to land on the 
red block platform. Shoot the winged cloud on the right to receive five stars, 
and hover jump right before the steps to collect the first flower.

                                   - Flower 2 -

Shoot the two Fly Guys above the red blocks, and collect the two red coins that 
are dropped. Shoot both winged clouds to receive ten stars, and then run right 
to the red switch. Shoot the winged cloud above the red switch for five stars, 
and jump across the four platforms on the right. Jump right from the fourth 
platform to land on the big cloud, and run right along the cloud. Jump over the 
three Flightless Goonies on the cloud, and jump right to the second cloud. Jump 
right to land on the platforms, and run right to exit the first area.

After arriving in the second area, pass through the middle ring, and jump up to 
the platform with the hut. Press up to enter the hut and put on the skis. Ride 
down the first slope and up the slope on the other side. Ride down the second 
slope, and jump over the rock to the small path on the other side of the gap. 
Ride off the end of the path to clear the gap and land on the next path. Ski 
over the Chomp Rock that rolls down the slope, and jump near the bottom of the 
slope to collect the second flower at the start of the next path.

                                   - Flower 3 -

Ski down the slope to collect the two red coins, and jump shortly after the red 
arrow on the path to clear the gap and collect the two red coins near the start 
of the next path. Ski down the steep slope, and jump over the rock at the 
bottom of the slope to clear the gap and land on the next path. Ignore Kamek on 
this section of path, as he will fly under Yoshi near the end of the path. Go 
up the slope at the end of the path, jump the gap to collect the red coin, and 
continue right to exit the second area.

After arriving in the third area, ski along the platforms and drop down the 
five steps. Jump right from the fifth step to land on the log for the red coin, 
and then jump up to the next log on the right for the next red coin. Jump right 
off the second log platform to collect the third flower, and then drop off the 
right side of the platform to land on the cloud. Jump near the right side of 
the cloud to collect the three red coins at the start of the platforms. Ski 
right along the platforms to exit the third area.

                                   - Flower 4 -

After arriving in the fourth area, ski down the steep slope and drop off the 
end to fall down to the first metamorphosis bubble. Touch the bubble to 
transform into a helicopter, and fly up to collect the red coin at the right 
side of the set of seven coins. Continue to fly up, and collect the red coin 
above the second Green Glove and the third Green Glove. Fly left after passing 
the third Green Glove, and collect the fourth flower below the small cloud.

                                   - Flower 5 -

Fly down and touch the metamorphosis bubble, and then fly left to the Green 
Gloves at the left side of the area. Collect the red coin above the second and 
third Green Glove. Continue to fly up, and touch the metamorphosis bubble above 
the fourth Green Glove. Fly up and right over the path with the six red arrows 
pointing right. Fly down after passing the path to avoid the Bumpty, and then 
fly up after the Bumpty to fly over a ledge.

Fly under the wall on the other side of the ledge, and then fly up over the 
next ledge. Fly under the next wall, and then fly up to collect the fifth 
flower. Continue right and hit the Yoshi block at the left side of the path. 
After transfroming into Yoshi, run right along the path to exit the fourth 
area. After arriving in the fifth area, run right and jump through the goal 
ring to complete the level.

~~ Items ~~

Flower 1
  Above the red blocks in the first area, shortly after the red switch.

Flower 2
  Shortly after the first Chomp Rock in the second area.

Flower 3
  After the second log platform in the third area.

Flower 4
  After transforming into a helicopter in the fourth area, fly to the middle of 
  the area to find the flower.

Flower 5
  Just before the Yoshi block at the end of the fourth area.

1 Red Coin
  Above the left side of the first see-saw platform in the first area.

2 Red Coins
  On the log platforms above the Green Gloves.

2 Red Coins
  Two Fly Guys hold red coins appear shortly after the first flower.

2 Red Coins
  At the right side of the second flower.

2 Red Coins
  On the other side of the first gap after the second flower.

1 Red Coin
  Above the final gap in the second area.

2 Red Coins
  There is one red coin above each of the two log platforms in the third area.

3 Red Coins
  At the start of the coin trail on the platforms at the end of the third area.

1 Red Coin
  Above the metamorphosis bubble at the bottom-right corner of the fourth area.

4 Red Coins
  There are two red coins above the Green Gloves at either side of the fourth 
  area.

5 Stars
  Shoot the winged cloud near the first red switch.

10 Stars
  There are two winged clouds above the red blocks, shortly after the red 
  switch.

5 Stars
  Shoot the winged cloud above the second red switch.

10 Stars
  Pass through the middle ring at the start of the second area.

Key
  In front of Chomp Rock near the start of the level.

===============================================================================
                        Level 6-1: Scary Skeleton Goonies!
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Run right at the start of the level and jump up the red steps to the path at 
the top. Stay near the start of the path and eat the two Flightless Skeleton 
Goonies that move left, and then run right down the slope. About half-way down 
the slope, hover jump right to collect the two red coins above the Spear Guys. 
On the other side of the Spear Guys, run right and drop down to the next path. 
Hover jump right from the end of the path and collect the first flower above 
the Dancing Spear Guys. Continue to hover right to land on the next path.

                                   - Flower 2 -

Jump up to the next path, and hit the two yellow egg blocks. Collect the yellow 
eggs, and then shoot an egg up at the winged cloud to receive five stars. Drop 
down to the next path on the right, and run right to the top of the slope. When 
the Spear Guy on the right walks to the right edge of the platform, shoot an 
egg to hit him off the edge of the platform. Hover right over to the platform, 
collecting the red coin in the middle of the set of three coins along the way.

Jump up to reveal a winged cloud, and then shoot the winged cloud to reveal a 
red switch. Jump on the red switch, and jump over to the path on the left. 
Press down above the red arrow to exit the first area. After arriving in the 
secret area, jump left to land on the yellow platform, and ride it along the 
track to collect the coins. Ride the platform to the end of the track to exit 
the secret area.

After returning to the first area, jump up to the path on the right, and then 
hover left to collect the red coin above the right side of the platform. Land 
on the platform, and then jump back to the path on the right. Jump up the step 
to the next path on the right, and hit the egg block to refill the egg supply. 
Shoot the winged cloud up on the right to create a bridge across the gap, and 
then jump onto the bridge.

Jump over the Dancing Spear Guy under the middle of the bridge, and then run 
across to the other side of the bridge. On the other side of the first bridge, 
jump over the Spear Guy and shoot the winged cloud up on the right to create a 
second bridge. Jump over the Dancing Spear Guy in the middle of the bridge and 
the Spear Guy at the right side of the bridge, and shoot the next winged cloud 
to create the third bridge in the area.

Jump over the Dancing Spear Guy, and jump off the right side of the bridge to 
land on the path. Jump off the right side of the path to land on the log 
platform, and walk right. Eat the Flamer Guy that bounces toward you from the 
right, and jump off the right side of the platform to land on the path with the 
two Zeus Guys. Shoot fire to defeat both Zeus Guys, and then jump up to the 
path with the red arrow at the top of the steps.

Run right down the slope in the path, and eat the Shy Guys that appear from the 
pipe until Yoshi has six eggs. Drop down off the right side of the path to land 
on the pipe, and shoot an egg off the wall above the spikes on the right to 
collect both red coins. Shoot an egg at the right winged cloud to create a 
bridge above the spikes, and then shoot the left winged cloud to receive five 
stars. Drop down off the pipe, and continue right to exit the first area.

After arriving in the second area, run right along the path and pass through 
the middle ring in the tunnel. Run right after exiting the tunnel, and use the 
platform above the right side of the path to jump up to the next path. Wait at 
the top of the slope until the Chomp creates the gap, and then run down to the 
bottom of the slope. Jump over the gap to collect the two red coins, and run up 
to the top of the slope.

Drop down to the path on the right, and run into the first tunnel. Wait for the 
Chomps to create two gaps on the right, and then jump over the first gap to 
collect two red coins. Jump over the second gap, and run up to the top of the 
slope in the path. Jump the next two gaps, and eat the Solo Toady that floats 
left near the start of the path. Run to the next gap on the right, and shoot an 
egg down to collect the second flower.

                                   - Flower 3 -

Jump to the small section of path on the right side of the gap created by the 
Chomp, and then jump over the next big gap to the path on the other side. Drop 
down off the right side of the path, and land on the Zeus Guy below. Collect 
the red coin in the middle of the set of three coins, and then jump over the 
next gap to land near a crate. Hover right over the next gap, and hold right to 
push the crate into the tunnel.

Land in the tunnel at the left side of the crate, and push the crate right to 
the wider area of the tunnel. Stomp the crate to receive six stars, and then 
run right to collect two red coins in the line of five coins. Jump up to the 
yellow platform at the right side of the tunnel, and jump over the gap to the 
path on the right. Jump over the next gap and pass through the paddles at the 
start of the path.

On the other side of the paddles, jump up to the platform on the right to 
collect the red coin, and then jump to the platform on the left. Eat the Solo 
Toady, and jump right to land on the small sloped path. When the Chomp drops 
down the gap, hover jump over the gap and land on the path at the right side of 
the Zeus Guy. Jump up to the ledge on the right, and jump right to land on the 
sloped path on the other side of the gap.

Run to the top of the slope, and shoot an egg down and right to collect the 
third flower. Jump over the next two gaps, and jump up to the ledge at the left 
side of the gap. Eat the Solo Toady, and wait for the Chomp to drop down the 
gap. Jump over the gap, drop off the right side of the path, and continue right 
to exit the second area.

                                   - Flower 4 -

After arriving in the third area, pass through the middle ring on the right, 
and jump up the small step to the next path. Run right under the three Skeleton 
Goonies, and stand near the egg plant at the top of the slope until Yoshi has 
six eggs. Drop down to the path on the right, and face left. Shoot an egg down 
and left to collect the fourth flower at the left side of the spikes, and then 
jump over the big gap on the right.

                                   - Flower 5 -

On the other side of the gap, jump up to collect the two red coins above the 
middle of the path, and jump over the next big gap to the ledge on the other 
side. Drop down off the right side of the ledge and eat the Flightless Skeleton 
Goonie running about on the path. Hit the egg block to refill the egg supply, 
and then jump up to the ledge at the right side of the path. Jump up to the 
steps above the ledge, and run right.

About half-way up the steps, face left and shoot the winged cloud to reveal a 
key. Jump to the top of the egg block on the left to collect the key, and then 
jump down to the ledge on the right. Jump over the gap to the small section of 
path, and stomp the post on the right twice. Shoot the winged cloud up on the 
right to create a bridge across the gap, and then shoot the winged cloud up on 
the left to create a beanstalk.

Climb up to the highest leaf of the beanstalk, and jump up to the platform 
above. Enter the hut and play the bonus game. After exiting the hut, pass 
through the paddles on the left and run down to the bottom of the steps. Drop 
down to the ledge at the right side of the path, and then jump over the two 
gaps on the right to land on the path under the two winged clouds.

Jump over the ledge on the right to land near the large spring ball. Bounce 
from the large spring ball, and follow the trail of coins to the red coins to 
the three red coins near the Pirahna Plant. Hover over the Pirahna Plant and 
land on the yellow platform at the left side of the tunnel. Drop off the right 
side of the ledge to collect the fifth flower. Pass through the paddles on the 
left, and drop down the yellow platforms to the path below.

Hit the egg block on the left to refill the egg supply, and then hover over the 
spikes on the right. Quickly shoot an egg up to defeat the Blow Hard, and then 
jump over the next gap. Jump over the first Tap-Tap and land on the red and 
yellow platform at the right side of the Solo Toady. Hover over the second Tap-
Tap on the right, and land on the vertically moving platform near the two 
Pirahna Plants.

Shoot an egg right to defeat the Pirahna Plant, and then hover jump through the 
gap to the path on the other side. Run right to the top of the slope in the 
path, and shoot an egg down and right to defeat the two Tap-Taps on the path. 
Jump over the gap to land on the path, and then hover jump right. Follow the 
trail of coins to collect the red coin, and pass through the goal ring to 
complete the level.

~~ Items ~~

1UP
  Bounce from the large spring ball in the third area, and hover to the tunnel 
  under the Pirahna Plant. Run right to reveal a winged cloud. Shoot the winged 
  cloud for the 1UP.

  Above the first set of Dancing Spear Guys in the first area.

Flower 2

  Above some spikes under the first egg plant in the third area.

Flower 5
  Bounce from the large spring ball in the third area, and hover over the 
  Pirahna Plant to the yellow platform. Drop down to the path on the right to 
  collect the flower.

  Above the first set of Dancing Spear Guys in the first area.

  in the first area. The middle coin in each set is a red coin.

  Guys in the first area. There is a red coin at the left side of the first 
  set, and the right side of the second set.

  the set are red coins.

  second flower. The red coins are at the top of the second set of coins.

  There are three coins above the first Zeus Guy in the second area. The middle

2 Red Coins
  In the second area, push the crate through the tunnel after the second 
  flower. In the wider area of the tunnel, run right to find the red coins.

  After passing through the paddles in the second area, jump up to the right 
  platform near the Solo Toady to find the red coin.

5 Stars
  Near the start of the first area, shoot the winged cloud between the two 
  yellow egg blocks.

5 Stars
  In the first area, shoot the left winged cloud above the spikes after the 
  first two Zeus Guys.

10 Stars
  Pass through the middle ring at the start of the second area.

6 Stars
  In the second area, push the crate through the tunnel shortly after the 
  second flower. In the wider area of the tunnel, stomp the crate.

10 Stars
  Pass through the middle ring at the start of the third area.

Key
  Go up the steps above the egg block in the third area, and shoot the winged 
  cloud on the left to reveal the key.

===============================================================================
                        Level 6-2: The Cave Of The Bandits
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Run right at the start of the level and eat the Boo Guy on top of the second 
set of mushrooms. Run right up the small slope in the path and stomp the Bandit 
at the top. Shoot the winged cloud up on the right to receive five stars, and 
then eat the Boo Guy above the set of mushrooms. Jump down to the ledge on the 
right and eat the red coin that the Coin Bandit is holding, and then jump right 
to collect the red coin in the set of five coins. Jump over the lava to the 
ledge, and jump right to collect the next red coin at the right side of the set 
of five coins.

After landing on the blue mushrooms, jump up to collect the middle red coin at 
the left side of the egg block, and hit the egg block to refill the egg supply. 
Run right to the final set of three coins above the blue mushrooms, and jump up 
to collect the middle red coin. Run down the path on the right and eat the red 
coin that the Coin Bandit holds. Stomp the Bandit that the Baron Von Zeppelin 
drops, and then shoot the winged cloud above the mushroom to reveal the flower. 
Jump up to the mushroom, and then jump up to collect the first flower.

                                   - Flower 2 -

Drop down off the right side of the mushroom, and shoot an egg up at the winged 
cloud after the bucket to receive five stars. Jump to the ledge on the right, 
and then jump over to the top of the first mushroom. Jump right to land on the 
third mushroom, and then drop down the mushroom on the right. When the three 
Lava Drops move right, quickly jump right to the next mushroom to collect the 
red coin, and then jump left to the third mushroom.

Hover right from the third mushroom, and land on the mushroom on the other side 
of the three Lava Drops. When the Lava Drop on the right moves down, jump over 
the gap to land near the egg block on the other side. Jump over to the path on 
the right, and shoot an egg up and right to collect the second flower. Walk 
near the fluff, and the top Zeus Guy will create a gap. When he drops off the 
left side of the fluff, jump into the gap and run through to the other side.

                                   - Flower 3 -

Drop down off the right side of the fluff to land on the path, and jump right 
to land on the red and yellow horizontally moving platform. Quickly shoot an 
egg up and right to hit the Fly Guy holding the 1UP, and then jump right to 
land on the pink vertically moving platform. Jump down to the path on the 
right, shoot an egg up at the winged cloud to receive five stars, and then 
continue right along the path to exit the first area.

After arriving in the second area, run right and jump through the middle ring. 
Jump up to the ledge on the right, and then hover to the ledge above the start 
point of the area. Run left along the ledge to reveal a winged cloud, and shoot 
the winged cloud to receive five stars. Jump back down to the ledge on the 
right, and then jump over the next three gaps to the highest ledge. Drop off 
the right side of the ledge, and run left to collect the red coin. Jump up to 
the path on the right and hit the egg block to refill the egg supply.

Drop down to the path on the right. Eat the Little Skull Mouser, and run left 
to collect two red coins. Jump up to the path on the right, and jump right to 
land on top of the fluff. Stomp down the right side of the fluff to reveal a 
winged cloud, and then shoot the winged cloud to receive five stars. Drop down 
the gap, eat the Little Skull Mouser, and shoot an egg through the gap on the 
left to collect the third flower.

                                   - Flower 4 -

Jump up through the gap and land on the path on the right. Jump off the right 
side of the path and stomp the Slugger at the left side of the sloped path. 
Jump over the Chomp Rock as it rolls down the slope, and then stomp the Slugger 
at the top of the slope. Drop down the three big steps on the right, and 
continue right to the five coins at the right side of the egg block. Jump up to 
collect the middle red coin, stomp the Bandit that was dropped by the Baron Von 
Zeppelin, and then jump up to the path on the right.

After landing on the path, quickly shoot an egg up and right to hit the first 
Blow Hard. Drop down to the path below, and collect the middle red coin below 
the Blow Hard. Jump up the big step to the next path on the right, and quickly 
shoot an egg right to hit the second Blow Hard. Shoot an egg up and right to 
hit the winged cloud above the Blow Hard, and then jump right to collect the 
fourth flower.

                                   - Flower 5 -

Jump down to the first platform on the right, and jump up to collect the middle 
red coin. When the Lava Drop moves down, jump over to the next platform on the 
right. Wait for the next Lava Drop to move down, and then jump right to land on 
the steps. Jump up to the top of the steps, and then jump right to land on the 
path near the egg block. When the Green Glove starts walking right, quickly run 
through the tunnel and jump up to the gap on the left to reveal a winged cloud.

Duck to avoid the Needlenose, and then shoot the winged cloud to receive five 
stars. Drop out of the gap and stomp the Green Glove below, and then quickly 
shoot an egg right to hit the Wild Ptooie Pirahna. Jump over the first Wild 
Ptooie Pirahna, and run right to the tunnel below the second Wild Ptooie 
Pirahna. Eat the Little Skull Mouser which bounces along to the left, and shoot 
the winged cloud up on the right for five stars.

Continue right and jump up to the ledge at the right side of the path. Collect 
the left red coin in the set of four coins, and then drop off the right side of 
the ledge to land on the path below. Run through the first low tunnel, and jump 
up to the middle tunnel on the right. Jump up to the high tunnel on the left to 
reveal a winged cloud, and then shoot the winged cloud for five stars. 

Drop down to the middle tunnel on the right, and then jump up to the next high 
gap on the left. Shoot the winged cloud for a 1UP, and then drop down to the 
path below. Eat the Little Skull Mouser, run through the tunnel on the right, 
and shoot an egg up to hit the Wild Ptooie Pirahna. Collect the right red coin 
in the set of six coins, and then run right to exit the second area.

After arriving in the third area, run right along the path and pass through the 
middle ring. Jump up and hit the fluff, and collect the first Super Star. Run 
right along the spikes and drop down the first small step. Continue right along 
the spikes to defeat three Little Skull Mousers, and jump to the top of the 
tall spikes. Jump right to collect the red coin in the set of four coins, and 
jump up the spikes on the right to collect the second Super Star.

Jump over to the spikes on the left, and jump up to the highest step to collect 
the red coin. Jump to the spikes on the right, and run down the three steps. At 
the bottom of the steps, run right and jump up to the small step on the other 
side of the spikes. Jump left and run left along the spikes. Collect the red 
coin at the left side of the line of coins, and then jump up to collect the 
third Super Star.

Jump up to the spikes on the right, and run down the three big steps. Run right 
at the bottom of the steps, and defeat the two Green Gloves. After the second 
Green Gloves, jump over the Chomp Rock that rolls left, and then jump over the 
top of the Slugger on the right to collect the fourth Super Star.

Continue right, and jump up after defeating the second Little Skull Mouser to 
collect the red coin at the right side of the set of four coins. Jump up to the 
third step on the right and hit the Slugger, and then jump up to the fourth 
step. Drop right down to the first step, and jump right to collect the fifth 
flower. Continue down to the goal path at the bottom of the steps. After 
transforming into Yoshi, jump through the goal ring to complete the level.

===============================================================================
                       Level 6-3: Beware The Spinning Logs
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

At the start of the level, shoot both winged clouds above for ten stars. Run 
right and jump on the log when it stops spinning. Jump right and land on the 
other side of the ledge to collect the red coin at the left side of the line. 
Jump over to the platform on the right with the three Ravens, and then jump 
right to the next platform. Collect the red coin above the right side of the 
platform, and jump down to the small spring ball on the right.

When the Lava Drop on the right moves down, bounce from the spring ball and 
hover over to the mushrooms on the right. Jump over to the second mushroom, and 
jump over the gap on the right to land near the second spinning log. When the 
log stops spinning, jump onto the log, jump up to collect the first flower, and 
then hover right to collect the red coin in the set of five coins.

                                   - Flower 2 -

After landing on the mushroom, jump right to land on the third log. Hover over 
to the log, and jump right to land on the next horizontally moving platform. 
Jump up to collect the fourth coin in the line of five coins, and land on the 
fifth log. Jump right and bounce off the Red Koopa Paratroopa to collect the 
red coin above. Hover right to collect the red coins above the next two Red 
Koopa Paratroopas, and land on the sixth log.

Jump right from the log and land on the vertically moving platform. Shoot an 
egg up to collect the red coin, and then jump over to the first mushroom on the 
right. Jump over to the fourth mushroom on the right and collect the red coin. 
Eat the Boo Guy, and jump right to the fifth mushroom. At this point, the Fuzzy 
section will begin. Try and avoid the Fuzzys as you jump over the mushrooms to 
the posts at the other side.

Jump over the posts to the platform on the right to end the Fuzzy section. Jump 
to the post on the left, and stomp it once to collect a red coin. Jump to the 
platform on the right, and then jump over the gap to the next platform. Shoot 
an egg up at the fluff and stomp the crate for six stars. Drop down to the path 
on the right, shoot an egg down and left to collect the second flower, and 
continue right along the path to exit the first area.

                                   - Flower 3 -

After arriving in the second area, shoot an egg up at the winged cloud for five 
stars, and then jump through the middle ring. Jump onto the first log, and jump 
up to collect the red coin at the right side of the set of five coins. Drop 
back down to the path on the left, and face right. Stand under the left side of 
the log, and when it starts to spin, jump up to get launched high. Hover right 
to enter a secret area.

After arriving in the secret area, go through the left blue doors. In the next 
two areas, go through the right blue doors to arrive in an area with seven Fly 
Guys holding 1UPs. Shoot eggs at the seven Fly Guys, and then go through the 
blue doors on the left to arrive in an area with three crates. Stomp the three 
crates for eighteen stars, and then go through the blue doors on the right to 
exit the secret area.

After returning to the second area, run down the slope on the left and drop off 
the end of the path. Run left along the next path, and jump left to collect the 
third flower under the log. After landing on the platform at the left side of 
the log, jump up to collect the two red coins in the line of six coins, and 
then jump back to the path on the right. Jump up to the next path on the right, 
jump over the first Chomp Rock, and run up to the top of the slope.

                                   - Flower 4 -

At the top of the slope, push the Chomp Rock down the slope on the right to 
defeat the two Boo Guys. Continue right over the gap to the next path, and push 
Chomp Rock right to defeat another Boo Guy. When the Slugger hits Chomp Rock 
left, jump over it and stomp the Slugger. Jump over the Chomp Rock when it 
rolls to the right, and then shoot an egg up and right to collect the fourth 
flower above the platform.

                                   - Flower 5 -

When the Lava Drop moves right, jump over to the platform and jump up to 
collect the right red coin. When the Lava Drop moves left, quickly hover right 
to land on the log. Jump right to land on top of the Chomp Rock, and stand at 
either side to roll it off the post. Drop down to collect the red coin, and 
then hover right to the platform. Shoot the winged cloud for five stars, 
collect the red coin above the right side of the platform, and then shoot an 
egg up to collect the fifth flower.

Jump right to the small spring ball on top of the post, and bounce up to 
collect the left red coin above. Land on the Chomp Rock, stand on either side 
to roll it off the post, and drop down to collect the red coin. Jump right and 
land on the Red Koopa Paratroopa, and then hover to the log on the right. Jump 
up to collect the middle red coin above the log, and then jump right to the 
goal path. Jump through the goal ring to complete the level.

===============================================================================
                      Level 6-4: Tap-Tap The Red Nose's Fort
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Run right at the start of the level and eat the Boo Guys on the first two 
steps. Jump up to the top of the steps, and jump across the vertically moving 
platforms to the Big Boo on the other side. Stay below the left side of the Big 
Boo, and eat the two Boo Guys. Run right and jump the gap to the vertically 
moving platform, and then jump over the next four gaps to land on a platform 
with two small spring balls.

Jump on either spring ball and bounce up to the vertically moving platform on 
the right. When the platform moves up to the highest point, jump right and eat 
the two Boo Guys on the path. Drop off the right side of the path to land on 
the vertically moving platform, and hold right when the platform moves down to 
enter the tunnel. Run to the middle of the tunnel to collect the first flower, 
duck to avoid the Lava Drop, and continue right to collect two red coins.

                                   - Flower 2 -

Run to the middle of the tunnel and duck to avoid the Lava Drop as it flies 
back to the right. Jump to the vertically moving platform on the left, ride it 
up, and then jump right to land on the path. Eat the two Boo Guys, and run down 
the four steps on the right. At the bottom of the steps, eat the Boo Guy and 
jump the gap on the right to the vertically moving platform. Jump the gap to 
the next platform, and then jump down to the pink vertically moving platform.

When the platform moves up high, jump right to the next platform, and then jump 
up to the path on the right to land near the Big Boo. Eat the two Boo Guys, run 
to the far left side of the path, and face left. When the Big Boo gets near, 
hover right to land on the other side. Continue right along the path and jump 
over the rotating flame. Jump up the four steps and eat the two Boo Guys at the 
top, shoot the winged cloud up on the right for six stars, and then drop off 
the right side of the path to land on the blue platform.

Jump up to collect the two red coins above the platform, and then ride the 
platform over to the path on the right. Run over to the right side of the path, 
and use the spring ball to bounce straight up. Hover slightly left to collect 
the first red coin, and then hover right to collect the next two red coins. 
After landing on the path, run right and jump through the vertically moving 
tunnels. On the other side of the tunnel drop down to the large spring ball on 
the right and bounce up to the second area.

After arriving in the second area, shoot an egg right to defeat the Pirahna 
Plant, and then shoot the winged cloud to receive five stars. Collect the two 
eggs on the platforms, and then drop down the tunnel on the right to exit the 
second area.

After arriving in the third area, drop down to the platform on the right, and 
jump over the next four platforms to the egg plant at the right side of the 
area. Stand near the egg plant until Yoshi has six eggs, and then shoot an egg 
up at the winged cloud on the left to receive five stars. Defeat the Salvo the 
Slime to receive a key, and then jump across the platforms to the left side of 
the area. Go through the door with the keyhole to exit the third area.

After arriving in the fourth area, jump up to the platform on the right above 
the Tap-Taps and pass through the middle ring. Collect the five stars below the 
platform, and then jump up to the platform on the right. Run right through the 
tunnel to exit the fourth area.

After arriving in the fifth area, go down the first pipe, and then go through 
the far left pipe. Shoot an egg at either of the bouncing Tap-Taps so that it 
rolls and defeats the walking Tap-Taps. Drop down off the left side of the 
platform, and shoot an egg up to the top-left corner of the room to collect the 
second flower. Jump up to tunnel on the right, and run right to exit the area.

                                   - Flower 3 -

After returning to the fifth area, go down the first pipe on the right, and go 
through the pipe on the left. Shoot an egg left to collect the third flower, 
and run right to exit the area. After returning to the fifth area, go down the 
pipe on the right, and then go down the next pipe on the right. Go through the 
pipe at the far right side of the path. Shoot eggs through the blue thorns to 
collect the four red coins on the other side, and run left to exit the area.

                                   - Flower 4 -

After returning to the fifth area, go down the first pipe on the left. Jump 
left over the three rotating flames, jump the gap, and land on the right side 
of the path with the next rotating flame. Quickly jump left over to the other 
side of the path, and jump the gap on the left to land on the next section of 
path. Jump over the two gaps on the left, and go through the far left pipe. In 
this area, shoot eggs to defeat Salvo the Slime.

Collect the key, and then run through the pipe on the right to exit the area.
After returning to the fifth area, jump right across the four gaps and go down 
the first pipe on the right. Go down the first pipe on the left, and then run 
right along the path to open the pipe with the keyhole. Go down the pipe, pass 
through the middle ring, and continue right to exit the fifth area.

After arriving in the sixth area, run right along the path and drop down to the 
blue rotating platform. Ride the platform right through the lava, and jump up 
to collect the two red coins at the left side of the flower. Jump up to collect 
the fourth flower, and hover right to collect the next two red coins.

                                   - Flower 5 -

After landing on the path, drop down to the log in the second section of lava, 
and stand at the right side. Ride the platform over to the other side of the 
lava to collect the fifth flower, and jump up to the path on the right. Pass 
through the middle ring, and then run through the pipe on the right to exit the 
sixth area.

                    - Boss Fight 11: Tap-Tap The Red Nose -

At the start of the boss fight, jump up to the platform with the two egg 
plants, and stand near either egg plant until Yoshi has six eggs. Drop down to 
the blocks below, and shoot eggs to destroy the blocks. When Tap-Tap the Red 
Nose gets near, shoot an egg and hit him into the lava to win the boss fight.

===============================================================================
                        Level 6-5: The Very Loooooong Cave
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Walk right along the path at the start of the level, and jump over the small 
lava gap. Continue right down the slope in the path, and wait at the end of the 
slope until the spike drops down. Drop off the end of the path and eat the Boo 
Guys coming out of the pipe, and then jump to the path on the right. Jump over 
the lava to the next path, and hover right to collect the two red coins. Drop 
down the step on the right, and jump over the lava to collect the first flower.

                                   - Flower 2 -

Jump over the next lava gap on the right to collect the red coin, and run down 
the small slope on the right. Jump over the Flamer Guy that bounces left, and 
then jump right to the other side of the lava. Continue right, and drop off the 
end of the path to land near the Boo Guy pipe. Eat the Boo Guys that appear 
from the pipe, and then run right. Drop off the right side of the yellow 
platform, and quickly run left to land on a hidden path.

Run down the slope in the path to collect two red coins, and eat the Boo Guy at 
the bottom of the slope. Drop off the right side of the path, run down the step 
on the left, and drop down to the path below. Run right to avoid the first 
horizontally moving Lava Drop, and run under the vertically moving Lava Drop 
when it moves up. On the other side of the second Lava Drop, eat the Fly Guy 
holding the red coin, and drop down to the path on the right.

Run left and eat the Fly Guy. Collect the red coin that is dropped, and then 
jump over to the right side of the Rock that rolls left. Continue left along 
the path, and jump onto the first red and yellow platform above the lava. Jump 
left to the second platform, and eat the Fly Guy that flies down and left. 
Collect the red coin, and jump over to the path at the left side of the lava. 
Jump up to the small platform on the left, and hover left to land on the path.

Run up the slope in the path and eat the Boo Guys that appear from the pipe 
until Yoshi has six eggs. Jump to the platform on the right, jump right to land 
on the ledge, and then jump up to land on the platform. Run up the small slope 
on the left, and jump up to the sloped path on the right. Run to the top of the 
slope, shoot an egg up and left to hit the Fly Guy holding the red coin, and 
then shoot an egg right to collect the second flower.

                                   - Flower 3 -

Jump up to the sloped path on the left and collect the red coin that the Fly 
Guy dropped, and shoot an egg left to collect the red coin on the platform 
above the Boo Guy. Jump up to the platform above and eat the Boo Guy on the 
left. Jump up to the next platform, and jump over the Chomp Rock when it rolls 
down from the left. Jump right to the small path, and then jump over the lava 
to the path on the other side.

When the Lava Bubble on the right goes down, quickly jump over the lava and 
land on the path. At the junction in the path, take the top path, and run top 
the top of the slope. Shoot an egg at the winged cloud for five stars, and run 
down the slope to the yellow platform. Drop off the right side of the platform 
to land on the path below, and then drop down to the next path. Run under the 
Drop Bubble when it moves high, and then run down the slope in the path.

Shoot an egg up to destroy the two spikes above the lava, and hover jump over 
the lava to the path on the other side. Run to the edge of the path but don't 
jump off. When the Chomp Rock appears and drops down to the path on the left, 
jump over to the path on the right and run to the far right side. Drop off the 
edge of the path and land on the Chomp Rock below. Ride the Chomp Rock over the 
lava, and jump up to the platform with the blue doors. Go through the doors.

After arriving in the second area, run right down the slope and jump through 
the middle ring. At the bottom of the slope, hit the egg block to refill the 
egg supply, and run right along the path to the fluff. Shoot an egg right to 
create gaps in the two fluff walls, and then continue right along the path. 
When the path slopes slightly down, shoot an egg up and right into the gap to 
reveal a winged cloud. Shoot the winged cloud to receive five stars.

Run right up the slope in the path, and shoot an egg right through the fluff. 
Run down the next slope, and shoot an egg up to the top-middle of the fluff to 
receive five stars. Shoot an egg through the bottom of the fluff, and run right 
through the gap. Continue right, and jump from the edge of the path to land on 
small ledge. Shoot an egg through the bottom of the fluff, and then shoot an 
egg up and right at the fluff on the next platform.

Jump right to the platform, and shoot an egg up at the horizontally moving 
winged cloud for 1UP. Shoot an egg right to create a gap in the middle of the 
tall fluff, and then jump righ to land in the gap. Shoot an egg up to reveal a 
winged cloud near the top of the fluff, and shoot another egg up at the winged 
cloud for the 1UP. Jump over to the path on the right, and jump up to the 
platform with the four eggs.

Collect the four eggs on the platform, and jump up to eat the green watermelon. 
Drop off the right side of the platform, and spit the watermelon seeds right 
through the fluff. Run through the tunnel, and shoot an egg up near the middle 
of the fluff to receive five stars. Shoot an egg right, and continue through 
the tunnel. After exiting the tunnel, jump up to collect the five red coins and 
the fourth flower. Jump up the two platforms and go through the blue doors.

                                   - Flower 4 -

After arriving in the third area, jump up to the platform above, and jump right 
to pass through the middle ring. Drop down to the path, and hit the expansion 
block. Jump up to the top of the expansion block, and then jump up to the path 
on the right. Run right along the path to collect the fourth flower, and run 
down the slope. At the bottom of the slope, stay left to avoid the eight 
Flightless Skeleton Goonies.

                                   - Flower 5 -

Jump up to the path on the right, and run right to the tunnel. Jump up to the 
platform on the right, and jump over to the path with the three red arrows. 
Drop down to the yellow platform at the right side of the path, and jump over 
the first Chomp Rock to land near the edge of the path. When the second Chomp 
Rock drops down, jump over to the path on the right. Jump and hover right to 
the path with the fourth Chomp Rock, and jump right to the next path.

Run to the top of the slope, and hover right to the path with the seventh Chomp 
Rock. Hover right to land on the path at the other side of the Chomp Rock 
section. Run right along the path and stomp the four posts for four red coins. 
Jump up to the ledge on the right to collect the red coin, and then jump up to 
collect the fifth flower. Drop off the right side of the ledge and jump through 
the goal ring to complete the level.

===============================================================================
                      Level 6-6: The Deep, Underground Maze
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Run right up the slope at the start of the level, and jump over the first Chomp 
Rock. Jump on top of the second Chomp Rock, and jump up to the gap on the right 
to reveal a winged cloud. Shoot the winged cloud to receive five stars, and 
then drop down to the path. Jump over to the left side of the Chomp Rock, and 
push it down the slope on the right. At the bottom of the slope, jump on top of 
the Chomp Rock, and then jump up to the platform above.

Run left up the steep slope to collect the three normal coins, and then jump 
right to collect the two red coins above the crate. Stomp the crate for six 
stars, drop off the right side of the path, and stomp down through the yellow 
fluff to land on the pink rotating platform. Drop off the right side of the 
platform to land on the path. Run right over the slope in the path, and then 
jump up to hit the small piece of yellow fluff.

When the Chomp Rock drops down, push it right under the first Lava Drop and 
along the path to defeat the Tap-Taps. When the Chomp Rock drops off the end of 
the path, quickly drop down to the left and stomp down through the yellow fluff 
to land on the path below. Jump over to the right side of the Chomp Rock, and 
push it up the slope on the left. Continue to push the Chomp Rock left to 
defeat three Pirahna Plants and eight Tap-Taps.

At the end of the path, jump on Chomp Rock and then jump up to the path on the 
left. Collect the key, and drop back down to the path below. Jump down to the 
path on the left, and run right along the tunnel. Run up the slope and eat the 
Spooky at the top, and use the large spring ball to bounce up to the yellow 
platform high above. Run left to the end of the tunnel, and drop down the gap  
below the rotating platform. Go through the blue doors.

After arriving in the second area, drop off the right side of the platform and 
run right along the path. Eat the two Boo Guys, and then stand at the left side 
of the yellow fluff. Stomp about half-way down the fluff, and then run left 
through the tunnel. Eat the Boo Guy, and then drop off the yellow platform to 
land in the room with the red tulip. Shoot an egg into the tulip for eight 
stars, and then jump up to collect the four red coins.

Jump back up to the platform on the right, and run through the tunnel to the 
fluff on the other side. Stomp down through the next two sections of fluff to 
land on the path below. Run right along the path to find three winged clouds 
floating above the fluff. Shoot the left winged cloud for five stars, the 
middle cloud to reveal the flower, and the right cloud for a 1UP. Shoot an egg 
up to collect the first flower, shoot another egg up to collect the key, and go 
through the blue doors on the right.

                                   - Flower 2 -

After arriving in the third area, shoot an egg up to collect the two red coins 
above the middle section of fluff, and then go through the blue doors. After 
returning to the second area, run left along the path, and eat the Flamer Guy 
near the blue doors. Stand under the blue doors, and face left. Shoot an egg up 
and left to collect the red coin and hit the winged cloud. Face right, and 
shoot an egg up and right to collect the next red coin and the second flower.

                                   - Flower 3 -

Jump up to the platform on the left and go through the blue doors. After 
arriving in the third area, drop down off the right side of the platform and 
shoot an egg up through the fluff to collect the third flower.

                                   - Flower 4 -

Run right along the path, and jump up the platforms after the first Snifit. On 
the fifth platform, eat the Spooky and the Shy Guy, and then jump up the two 
platfroms on the right. Jump onto the sloped path, and jump right to the 
platform near the Snifit. Jump up to the third platform to collect the fourth 
flower, and then jump up to the fourth platform. Shoot the winged cloud at the 
top of the room for five stars, and go through the blue doors.

                                   - Flower 5 -

After returning to the second area, jump on the small spring ball on the left 
and bounce up to the first platform above. Shoot an egg left through the fluff 
left to collect the two red coins, and jump up to the platform with the second 
large spring ball. Bounce up to the next platform, and run left to collect the 
two red coins. Pass through the paddles, and then stomp down through the fluff 
to the path at the bottom of the area. Run left along the path and eat the 
Flamer Guy. Jump up to the platform on the left and go through the blue doors.

After arriving in the third area, drop down off the right side of the platform 
and run right along the path. Jump up the platforms after the first Snifit. On 
the fifth platform, eat the Spooky and the Shy Guy, and jump up the two 
platforms on the right. On the fifth platform, shoot an egg up to reveal a 
large spring ball. Jump on the large spring ball and bounce up to the second 
platform to collect two red coins.

Run left to collect the fifth flower, and then drop down off the right side of 
the platform to the path below. Run left along the path, and eat the Flamer Guy 
near the fluff. Shoot fire left to defeat the two Zeus Guys, and then stomp the 
fluff to land in a tunnel. Shoot an egg right to defeat the Flamer Guy, and run 
right through the tunnel to collect four red coins. Jump out of the tunnel to 
land on the path, and go through the blue doors.

After returning to the second area, run right and stand under the red arrow. 
Shoot an egg up to hit the winged cloud, which will create a bridge. Use the 
large spring ball on the left to bounce up to the second yellow platform, and 
run right along the path to the fluff. Stomp the fluff to land on the bridge, 
and jump off the right side of the bridge to land on the path. Jump over the 
yellow platform to the path on the other side, and go through the blue doors.

After arriving in the fourth area, push the Chomp Rock right to defeat the Tap-
Taps. Jump over the gap at the end of the path, and hover over the Tap-Tap at 
the left side of the goal path. After landing on the goal path, jump through 
the goal ring to complete the level.

~~ Items ~~

  Shoot the third winged cloud above the fluff at the bottom-right corner of 
  the second area.

Flower 1
  Shoot the second winged cloud above the fluff at the bottom-right corner of 
  the second area.

Flower 2
  Shoot the winged cloud on the platform above the blue doors at the bottom-

Flower 3

  area.

Flower 4
  Above the platforms near the top-right corner of the third area.

Flower 5
  From the middle of the third area, shoot an egg up to the fluff above, and a
