  land on platform near the flower.

2 Red Coins
  Push Chomp Rock right down the slope near the start of the level, and it will 
  drop into a gap. Jump up from Chomp Rock to land on a platform near five 
  coins. The two right coins in the line are red coins.

4 Red Coins
  Stomp through the first section of fluff in the second area, and run left 
  through the first tunnel to find the red coins.

2 Red Coins
  Above the fluff at the bottom-right corner of the third area.

2 Red Coins
  On the platform above the blue doors at the bottom-left corner of the second 
  area.

2 Red Coins
  At the right side of the fifth flower.

4 Red Coins
  Defeat the two Zeus Guys at the top-left corner of the third area by shooting 
  fire at them, and then stomp through the nearby fluff to land in a room with 
  five coins. The four right coins in the line are red coins.

2 Red Coins
  Go through the blue doors at the top-right corner of the third area, and use 
  the first large spring ball to bounce up to the platform above. Shoot an egg 
  through the fluff on the left to find the coins.

2 Red Coins
  Go through the blue doors at the top-right corner of the third area, and use 
  the two large spring balls to bounce up to the five coins at the top-right 
  corner of the area. The two left coins in the line are red coins.

6 Stars
  Push Chomp Rock right down the slope near the start of the level, and it will 
  drop into a gap. Jump up from Chomp Rock to land on a platform, and stomp the 
  crate for the stars.

10 Stars
  Pass through the middle ring at the top of the first area.

8 Stars
  Stomp through the first section of fluff in the second area, and run left 
  through the first tunnel to find a tulip. Shoot an egg into the tulip.

5 Stars
  Shoot the first winged cloud above the fluff at the bottom-right corner of 
  the second area.

5 Stars
  Shoot the winged cloud at the top-right corner of the third area.

Key
  Push Chomp Rock all the way down the path in the first area. When Chomp Rock 
  stops in the small dip near the coins, jump on Chomp Rock, and then jump up 
  to the path on the left to find the key.

Key
  After collecting the second flower, shoot an egg straight up to find the key.

===============================================================================
                            Level 6-7: Keep Moving!!!!
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Run up the small slope in the path at the start of the level, and jump the 
small gap to the log platform. Jump over to the number platform on the right, 
and jump right to the third number platform. Jump to the set of four number 
platforms on the right to start the first Shark Chomp chase. Jump the gap at 
the end of the fourth platform, and quickly run right along the long set of 
number platforms. Jump to the ledge at the end of the number platforms to end 
the first Shark Chomp chase.

Jump up the big step on the right, and jump left to land on the green rotating 
platform. Ride the green rotating platform to the top-left corner, and jump 
left to land on the yellow platform. After the yellow platform moves around the 
corner in the track, the second Shark Chomp will appear. Jump to the platform 
on the right, and jump right after the slope in the track to land on the number 
platforms. Collect the two red coins above the platforms, and then jump right 
off the end of the platforms to end the second Shark Chomp Chase.

Jump up the three platforms on the right, and then jump left to the yellow 
platform. Near the end of the track, jump up to land on the second rotating 
platform in the area. Ride the platform and jump off at the top to land on the 
platform with the number '4' on it. Jump up the four number platforms above and 
eat the three Shy Guys holding the red coins. Collect the three red coins, and 
then drop down to the green rotating platform.

Ride the platform and jump off at the left side to land on the number platform 
above the spikes. Jump left to the fourth number platform, and then jump up to 
the third rotating platform in the area. Jump up to the sixth rotating platform 
at the top-left corner of the area, and shoot an egg up and left to collect the 
first flower. Ride the platform to the top-right corner, and then jump up to 
land on the number platform.

                                   - Flower 2 -

Jump to the third number platform on the right to start the third Shark Chomp 
chase. Quickly hover right over the platforms, and collect the two red coins 
above the seventh and eight platforms. Hover right from the seventh platform to 
land on the red and yellow platform, and ride the platform to the path to end 
the third Shark Chomp chase. Run up the steps on the right and jump through the 
middle ring above the bridge, and then continue right to exit the first area.

After arriving in the second area, drop down to the red bridge on the right, 
and drop off the end of the bridge to land on the green platform with the egg 
plant. Ride the platform along the track, eating the two Cloud Drops along the 
way. At the end of the third track, the platform will drop down to a track 
above the spikes. Eat the two Cloud Drops on the left, and then jump left to 
the yellow platform.

Ride the yellow platform to collect the two red coins, and then drop down to 
the red and yellow platform on the right. Stay on the platform as it launches 
off the end of the track to land on a log platform. Drop off the right side of 
the platform to land on the blue spiral platform below, and stand at the right 
side of the platform to move right. Walk slowly left as the platform moves 
right to ride the spiral platform down to the bottom of the track.

After collecting the two red coins, jump right to land on the yellow platform. 
Ride the platform down to land on the platform near the Tap-Taps, and jump left 
to land on the red and yellow platform. Stand on the middle of the platform to 
avoid the three sets of two Tap-Taps, and ride the platform to the circular 
track. When the platform moves up, jump up to collect the second flower.

                                   - Flower 3 -

Drop down to the log platform on the right, and then jump right to land on the 
green platform with the egg plant. Near the start of track, shoot an egg up and 
right to hit the Blow Hard. Eat the two Snifits on the way up the vertical 
section of track, and drop off either side of the platfrom near the start of 
the horizontal section of track. Shoot an egg up at the fluff at the right side 
of the Shy Guy to collect the third flower.

                                   - Flower 4 -

Jump over the two gaps on the left and run under the vertically moving Lava 
Drop. Shoot an egg at the two Tap-Taps, and then jump onto the green platform. 
Ride the platform left along the track and eat the four Cloud Drops. Jump up to 
collect the red coin after the fourth Cloud Drop, and ride the platform up the 
slope to the vertical section of track. Eat the two Snifits on the left, and 
stay at the left side of the platform to avoid the first Lava Drop.

When the first Lava Drop moves down, walk to the right side of the platform to 
avoid the second Lava Drop, and then move over to the left side of the platform  
to avoid the third Lava Drop. Stay at the left side of the platform to collect 
the red coin, and duck to avoid the first horizontally moving Lava Drop. Move 
over to the right side of the platform and duck to avoid the final Lava Drop on 
the track. Jump left at the top of the track to pass through the middle ring.

Jump over the gap to the path on the right, and drop off the right side of the 
path to land on the red platform near the circular track. Jump onto any of the 
four yellow platforms circling the track, and shoot the hidden winged cloud 
near the bottom-left corner of the fluff to receive five stars. Ride the 
platform to the top-right corner of the fluff, and shoot an egg at the left 
side of the right Snifit to reveal a key.

Collect the key, and continue to ride the platform. At the top of the track, 
jump up to land on the red platform, and jump over to the steps on the left. 
Run to the top of the steps, and continue left along the platform to the hut. 
Press up to enter the hut for a bonus game. After exiting the hut, run down the 
steps, jump down to the platform on the right, and jump right to the steps. Run 
up to the top of the steps and continue right to exit the second area.

After arriving in the third area, run through the paddles on the right and 
collect the first Super Star. Jump over the ledge on the right and run along 
the path to the egg plant up on the platform. Stand under the egg plant until 
Yoshi has six eggs, and then shoot an egg at the winged cloud to reveal the 
flower. Stomp any of the Bandits that drop down from the platforms, and then 
jump up to collect the fourth flower.

                                   - Flower 5 -

Jump up the small step on the right, and hover right over the blue thorns to 
the ledge on the other side. Hover right and land on the steps above the 
Bandit. Run left up to the top of the steps, and collect the red coin above the 
path. Jump over to the steps on the right and jump up to the path at the top. 
Drop down the big step, and run right down the steps to the path at the bottom. 
Run left along the path, and stand under the Paddles near the Bandit. When the 
Paddles open, shoot an egg up to collect the fifth flower.

Jump up to the steps on the right, and run left to the top. Jump over to the 
platform on the right and eat the Spiked Fun Guy, and then jump to the path on 
the right. Jump over the gap to the platform on the right, and eat the Potted 
Spiked Fun Guy. Stomp the Bandit on the right, and then jump right to land on 
the red platform above the six coins. Jump up the step on the right, and hover 
over the Potted Spiked Fun Guy and the Bandit to the steps on the other side.

Drop off the end of the steps, and run through the paddles on the left. Jump 
over the gap to the path on the left, and jump to the top of the pipe. Shoot an 
egg at the winged cloud to receive five stars, and shoot another egg to collect 
the two middle red coins in the set of six coins. Go down the pipe. After 
arriving in the fourth area, jump to the path on the right and run down the two 
steps to the goal path. Jump through the goal ring to complete the level.

===============================================================================
                         Level 6-8: King Bowser's Castle
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Run right at the start of the level and jump off the end of the path to hit the 
metamorphosis bubble. After transforming into the helicopter, fly right to 
collect the red coin, and follow the line of coins right. Fly up at the end of 
the coins to avoid Kamek, and collect the first flower after the set of five 
coins. Continue right to hit the second metamorphis bubble. Fly down slightly, 
and follow the line of coins right to collect the red coin and hit the third 
metamorphis bubble.

                                   - Flower 2 -

Quickly fly up to avoid the two Skeleton Goonies, and follow the line of coins 
right to collect the red coin. When Kamek appears on the left, fly down to the 
next line of coins, and then fly down to the right side of the Skeleton Goonie 
to collect the second flower. Hit the Yoshi block above the path to transform 
into Yoshi, jump through the middle ring, and go through the blue doors on the 
right to exit the first area.

                                   - Flower 3 -

After arriving in the second area, run right along the path and drop down the 
step to land near the egg plant. Stand near the egg plant until Yoshi has six 
eggs, and then shoot an egg up at any of the four rotating doors above. One of 
the four doors will drop. Go through the doors.

Door 1
  After arriving in the third area, run right along the tunnel and eat the Shy 
  Guy near the winged cloud. Shoot an egg up at the winged cloud to receive a 
  1UP, and then jump to the step on the right. When the second ball and chain 
  is horizontal, quickly jump over to the small platform on the right and duck.

  When the ball and chain has passed, jump up to the path on the right, and 
  drop down off the right side of the path to land on the ledge above the lava. 
  When the ball and chain on the right has raised, jump and hover to the path 
  at the right side of the lava. Jump up to collect the third flower, and then 
  run under the next two ball and chains to the first pink moving platform.

Door 2
  After arriving in the first section of the third area, jump up to the 
  platform above and collect the middle two red coins above the two Shy Guys on 
  Stilts. Jump up to the path on the right, and drop down the big step. Hover 
  right over the Shy Guys on Stilts to collect the two red coins, and run right 
  along the next path.

  Drop down off the right side of the path, and eat the Woozy Guys. When Yoshi 
  has six eggs, jump over to the other side of the Dancing Spear Guys, and 
  shoot five eggs at the Support Ghost. Jump up to the set of five coins to 
  collect the two red coins at the top, and then jump over the Support Ghost. 
  Go through the blue doors on the right.

  After arriving in the second section of the third area, jump down to the path 
  on the left, and drop down to the horizontally moving platform. Jump left to 
  the next platform, and then jump over to the vertically moving platform. Jump 
  up to collect the third flower at the top-left corner of the area, and then 
  jump back across the platforms to the start point of the section.

Door 3
  After arriving in the first section of the third area, jump up to collect the 
  six red coins, and then go down the pipe at the right side of the room. After 
  arriving in the second section of the third area, Tap-Tap the Golden will 
  appear on the right, and will follow you through the area. If he gets too 
  close, shoot an egg at him.

  Run left up the slope in the path, and stand near the egg plant at the top of 
  the slope until Yoshi has six eggs. Run down the small slope on the left, and 
  jump over the lava to the path on the other side. Run along the path, and 
  jump left over the gap at the bottom of the slope. Continue left along the 
  path, and run down the next big slope. At the bottom of the slope, shoot an 
  egg left to collect the third flower.

Door 4
  After arriving in the third area, run right along the path to collect the six 
  red coins and the third flower.

                                   - Flower 4 -

Door 1
  Jump over to the third platform on the right, and wait for the ball and chain 
  to pass. When it does, quickly shoot two eggs down and right to destroy the 
  blocks. Drop into the gap and duck to avoid the ball and chain, and then jump 
  up through the gap on the right to land near the red switch. Jump on the red 
  switch, and run right over the blocks to collect the four red coins.

  Drop down to the see-saw platform on the right, and jump up to collect the 
  six red coins. Run over to the right side of the platform to create a slope 
  leading up to the left. Run up the slope and jump left at the top to collect 
  the fourth flower. Drop back down to the see-saw platform, and stand at the 
  left side of the platform to create a slope leading up to the right. Run up 
  to the top of the slope and jump right to land on the path. Go through the 
  blue doors.

Door 2
  Run right along the path and jump up the small step to land near the Stretch. 
  Eat the Stretch, and jump up to the path on the right. Run to the far right 
  side of the path, and eat the Spear Guy when he faces right. Jump over the 
  two gaps on the right, and jump up to the top-right corner of the area to 
  collect the fourth flower. Jump over the two gaps on the left, and jump left 
  to the high bridge. Run to the left side of the bridge to collect two red 
  coins, and go up the pipe.

  After arriving in the third section of the third area, drop down off the left 
  side of the pipe and collect the two red coins under the egg plant. Jump on 
  top of the pipe, and hover right to collect the two red coins near the middle 
  of the line of ten coins. Stomp the jelly block so that it stretches over the 
  spikes on the right, and then jump right to land on the ledge. Drop down off 
  the right side of the ledge to land on the jelly block, and continue right 
  along the path to the egg plant. Jump up to the platform at the left side of 
  the egg plant, and jump up to the path on the left. Go through the doors.

  After arriving in the fourth section of the third area, jump up to the 
  platform above, and walk left to find Salvo the Slime. Shoot eggs to defeat 
  Salvo the Slime, and collect the key that is dropped. Drop off the right side 
  of the path, and go through the blue doors on the left. After returning to 
  the third section of the third area, drop down to the path on the right, and 
  stand under the egg plant until Yoshi has six eggs. Go through the blue doors 
  on the right.

Door 3
  Jump over the gap to the path on the other side, and jump up the two big 
  steps on the left. Continue left over the path, and jump left over the lava 
  to land on the next path. Run down to the bottom of the slope on the left, 
  and wait for Tap-Tap the Golden to jump into the gap. Jump over the gap to 
  the path on the left, and jump over the lava to the next path.

  Run down to the bottom of the big slope on the left, and jump over to the 
  left side of the gap. Shoot an egg down and right to collect the fourth 
  flower, and then jump up the two big steps on the left. Go up the pipe. After 
  arriving in the third section of the third area, eat both Shy Guys and 
  collect the six red coins that drop. Go through the blue doors.

Door 4
  Jump over the moving blocks, and run right along the path on the other side 
  to collect the fourth flower. Run right to collect the six red coins, and 
  jump up to eat the two Fly Guys holding the 1UPs. Continue right to exit the 
  third area.

                                   - Flower 5 -

After arriving in the fourth area, run right, and Kamek will appear on the 
highest set of blocks. Jump over the magic that he shoots, and then jump over 
the blocks to the path on the other side. Jump up to collect the single red 
coin at the right side of the high platform, and then jump up to the top of the 
blocks on the right. Hover right to collect the red coin at the left side of 
the platform, and then drop down to the path on the right.

Continue right, avoiding Kamek's magic when he appears, and jump over the tall 
ledge to the path on the other side. There will be a red coin up on the middle 
of three blocks. Shoot an egg up to collect the red coin, and jump up the small 
step on the right. Drop down to the path on the right to land near the flower. 
Jump through the middle ring on the right, and then shoot an egg up and left to 
collect the two red coins and the fifth flower. Continue right along the path, 
and go through the red doors.

                         - Boss Fight 12: King Bowser -

Part 1
  At the start of the boss fight, Bowser will jump up and stomp. Jump over 
  Bowser's wave, and stomp to send a wave toward Bowser. Hit Bowser with three 
  waves to win the first part of the boss fight.

Part 2
  Bowser will rise in the distance, and will roar, causing rocks to fly up. Run 
  anywhere on the path except where the red arrows are pointing to avoid the 
  rocks that drop. At this point, Baron Von Zeppelins will begin to float 
  across the area holding large eggs. Jump up to collect the eggs, and shoot 
  them at Bowser's head. Hit Bowser six times to win the boss fight.

===============================================================================
                        Extra 6: Castles - Masterpiece Set
===============================================================================

                                   - Flower 1 -

Run right at the start of the level and jump up the three steps to land near 
the first Support Ghost in the area. Eat Shy Guys until Yoshi has six eggs, and 
shoot four eggs at the Support Ghost. Folow the Support Ghost right along the 
tunnel, and jump up to the platform to collect the first flower. Jump up to the 
platform above, and jump right to collect the two red coins in the line of five 
coins. Jump up to the platform on the right, and jump up the three steps to 
land near the second Support Ghost. 

                                   - Flower 2 -

Shoot six eggs at the Support Ghost, and then hover right to collect the two 
red coins above the blob. Run right along the path and jump up the two 
platforms, and then run down the two steps on the right. Jump up the next step 
on the right, and continue right to the third Support Ghost. Shoot two eggs 
right, and then jump up to the platform above the left side of the Support 
Ghost. Go through the blue doors.

After arriving in the second area, run up the steep slope on the right and eat 
the Shy Guy at the top. Jump over to the rolling platform, and collect the 
right two red coins on the middle of the platform. Jump over to the slope on 
the right, and shoot an egg up at the winged cloud to receive five stars. Pass 
through the paddles on the right, and run up to the top of the slope.

Jump onto the rolling platform, and collect the second and fourth coins on the 
middle of the platform. Jump down to the path on the right, and eat the two Shy 
Guys. Pass through the paddles, and shoot an egg up at the winged cloud to 
receive five stars. Run up to the top of the steep slope, and jump onto the 
rolling platform below the blue thorns. Roll off the platform, and hover left 
to an area below the slope.

Collect the middle line of three coins, and jump up to the ledge on the right. 
Hover right over the spikes to the bottom tunnel, and run right to collect the 
second flower. Jump up to the platform above and run left to collect two red 
coins. Jump up to the next platform, and use the large spring ball to bounce up 
to the platform high above. Jump through the middle ring on the left, and then 
go through the blue doors on the right.

                                   - Flower 3 -

After arriving in the third area, jump up to the big step on the right, and 
then jump over to the first green platform. Hover right to the first yellow 
platform, and hold down as the platform moves up to avoid the blue thorns. Jump 
right to the second yellow platform to collect the two red cons, and then hover 
right to the red and yellow platform. Ride the platform up to the top of the 
track, and jump left to land on the green platform.

When the platform moves down, jump left over the blue thorns to land on the 'H' 
shaped track. Hold down as the platform moves up to duck under the blue thorns, 
and jump left to the green platform on the 'S' shaped track to collect the 
third flower. Hover left to the platform on the 'Y' shaped track, and then jump 
left over the blue thorns to the path near the egg block. Hit the egg block to 
refill the egg supply, and then jump onto the red and yellow platform.

                                   - Flower 4 -

Stand on the left side of the platform, and ride the platform to the blue 
thorns. Jump up to the green platform, and then jump over to the far left 
yellow platform. Ride the yellow platform to the top of the track, and jump up 
to land on the green platform. Jump to the green platform on the right, and 
then jump to the middle yellow platform.

Shoot an egg up to hit the Dangling Ghost, and then jump left to land on the 
green platform. Ride the green platfrom up to the top of the track, and jump 
right to pass through the middle ring. Shoot an egg up at the winged cloud on 
the left for five stars, and then jump on the green platform. Ride the green 
platform to exit the third area.

After arriving in the fourth area, stand on the middle of the platform and hold 
down to avoid being hit off the platform by the eggs. At the top of the track, 
jump left to collect the fourth flower, and then jump right over the gap to the 
red platform. Go through the pipe on the right.

                                   - Flower 5 -

After arriving in the fifth area, drop down to the pipe at the bottom of the 
area, and go down the pipe. After arriving in the sixth area, jump up and stomp 
down through the fluff to land on the red bridge at the bottom of the area. 
Stomp the four Green Gloves that land on the bridge, shoot the winged cloud up 
on the left for five stars, and shoot an egg up and right to collect the fifth 
flower. Drop off the left side of the bridge, and go through the pipe.

After arriving in the seventh area, stomp through the fluff to land on the red 
and yellow platform. Stand on the right side of the platform, and ride the 
platform to collect five red coins. After landing on the goal path, jump 
through the goal ring to complete the level.

~~ Items ~~

Flower 1
  Above the first Caged Ghost in the first area.

Flower 2
  Jump on the third rolling platform in the second area, and roll off it. Hover 
  right to the bottom tunnel to find the flower.

Flower 3
  At the bottom of the 'S' shaped platform trail in the third area.

Flower 4
  At the top-left corner of the fourth area.

Flower 5
  Near the bottom of the sixth area.

2 Red Coins
  In the first area, there are five coins after the first flower. The second 
  and fourth coins in the line are red coins.

2 Red Coins
  Above the second Caged Ghost in the first area.

2 Red Coins
  There are three coins on the middle of the first rolling platform in the 
  second area. The two right coins in the line are red coins.

2 Red Coins
  There are five coins on the middle of the second rolling platform in the 
  second area. The second and fourth coins in the line are red coins.

3 Red Coins
  Jump on the third rolling platform in the second area, and roll off it. Hover 
  left to find seven coins. The middle line in the set of coins are red coins.

2 Red Coins
  Jump on the third rolling platform in the second area, and roll off it. Hover 
  right to the top tunnel to find four coins. The second and third coins in the 
  line are red coins.

2 Red Coins
  At the right side of the third vertically moving platform in the third area.

5 Red Coins
  Ride the red and yellow platform in the seventh area to collect the red 
  coins.

5 Stars
  Shoot the winged cloud after the first rolling platform in the second area.

5 Stars
  In the second area, shoot the winged cloud on the other side of the paddles 
  after the second rolling platform.

10 Stars
  Pass through the middle ring at the end of the second area.

10 Stars
  Pass through the middle ring above the second Dangling Ghost in the third 
  area.

5 Stars
  Shoot the winged cloud in the top-left corner at the end of the third area.

5 Stars
  Shoot the winged cloud at the left side of the fifth flower.

~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~

4.                                Item List

~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~

Beanstalk
  Some winged clouds contain a seed which drops to the ground, which will then 
  transform into a beanstalk. You can climb the leaves on the beanstalk to 
  reach a higher point of the level.

Blue Watermelon
  When Yoshi collects this, he can freeze enemies by shooting ice at them. The 
  enemy will be defeated when Yoshi touches them.

Chomp Rock
  Chomp Rock is a large circular rock which can be pushed by Yoshi. Chomp Rock 
  can defeat most enemies.

Coin
  The most common item in the game. Collect 100 to get one extra life.

Crate
  A large crate. Stomp it to reveal six stars.

Donut Lift
  A circular platform which drops when you stand on it.

Egg
  Yoshi can collect eggs either by eating enemies, or by hitting special egg 
  blocks along the way. Eggs are very useful in hitting enemies or other 
  objects from a long distance.

Egg Block
  A green block which drops eggs when you hit it.

Egg Plant
  The Egg Plant is a small plant which fires out eggs. It will stop shooting 
  eggs once Yoshi has six eggs.

Expansion Block
  A block that grows in size when you hit it. Comes in useful for getting to 
  higher parts of levels.

Flower
  There are five flowers in each level. Collect all five to get 50% completion 
  of a level.

Goal Ring
  Jump through the goal ring to complete a level.

Green Watermelon
  The most common watermelon in the game. After Yoshi eats this, he will be 
  able to spit tiny seeds which defeat most enemies.

Hut
  A locked hut, which contains bonus level. You will need to find a key to open 
  the hut.

Key
  A key which opens locked doors. Keys can be found in various places, such as 
  winged clouds or vases.

Manual Rotating Platform
  A platform which you have to operate by jumping from one platform to the 
  other.

Message Block
  A white block which gives tips on playing the game.

Metamorphosis Bubble
  A floating bubble which transfers Yoshi into a form of vehicle.

Middle Ring
  Pass through this ring to save your progress in the level.

Needlenose Plant
  A variation of the egg plant which spits out Needlenoses.

Red Coin
  There are twenty red coins in each level. Collect all twenty to get 20% 
  completion of a level.

Red Watermelon
  When Yoshi collects this, he is able to shoot fire.

Pipe
  A very common object in the game. Some pipes generate enemies, some pipes 
  lead to secret areas, and some pipes do nothing at all.

Post
  Posts in the game vary in height, but all can be stomped. Some posts reveal 
  hidden objects when they are stomped to a certain height.

Red Switch
  The Red Switch can reveal invisible objects, such as platforms and coins. 
  Some red switches also reveal a red arrow, which points to a secret area.

Rotating Platform
  A platform which moves along a set path. There are automatic platforms which 
  rotate by themselves, and manual platforms which the player has to operate.

Star
  There are thirty stars in each level. Collect all thirty to get 30% 
  completion of a level.

Super Star
  When Yoshi collects this, Mario will transform into Powerful Mario, who is 
  invincible and can run up walls.

Spring Ball
  Either a small or a large ball with an arrow on it, which can launch Yoshi to 
  higher points of a level.

Tulip
  A red flower. Shoot an egg into the flower when it opens to get eight stars.

Vase
  A vase, which usually can be found on a ledge. Vases commonly contain objects 
  such as keys, but you will need to smash the vase first to reveal the object.

Winged Cloud
  A small winged cloud. Shoot an egg at the cloud for items.

Yoshi Block
  After touching a Metamorphosis Bubble, touch this block to transform back to 
  Yoshi.

~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~

5.                                Enemy List

~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~

~~ Enemies ~~

Aqua Lakitu
  Found on level 3-8, this is a version of the Lakitu that swims underwater. 
  Recognised by a snorkle poking out of the water, Aqua Lakitus shoot spiky 
  balls at you when they appear. 

Bandit
  Found on levels 1-8, 2-5, 2-8, 4-1, 4-4, 6-2 and 6-7, Bandits are extremely 
  fast enemies which will attempt to steal Mario and run away. They are also 
  difficult to beat, and the only way to sucessfully beat them with one hit is 
  with a stomp.

Barney Bubble
  Found on level 3-7, this is a strange, round purple creature. When Yoshi 
  jumps on a Barney Bubble, it shoots bubbles which can defeat other enemies.

Baron Von Zeppelin
  Found on levels 1-1, 1-6, 2-1, 2-3, 2-7, 3-3, 4-2, 4-3, 4-5, 5-1, 5-3, 5-6, 
  5-7 and 6-2, the Baron Von Zeppelin is a floating balloon with a smiley face 
  on it, which can carry either helpful or harmful items. Usually, they drop 
  harmful items when you run under them.

Beach Koopa
  Found on levels 3-1, 4-2, 4-5 and 4-8, the Beach Koopa is just a basic Koopa 
  Troopa without a shell.

Big Boo
  Found on levels 2-4 and 6-4, the Big Boo is a large ghost that flies toward 
  you when you face away from it, and turns invisible when you face toward it.

Blargg
  Found on level 1-4, the Blargg is a red monster that appears from the lava 
  and jumps toward you. There is a much bigger version of this monster called 
  the Garagantua Blargg.

Blow Hard
  Found on levels 2-2, 5-8 and 6-1, the Blow Hard is a large green cactus which 
  attempts to shoot you with Needlenoses. When the target locks on to Yoshi, 
  run in any direction to avoid being hit.

Boo
  Found on level 2-4, the Boo is a small ghost that flies toward you when you 
  face away from it, and turns invisible when you face toward it.

Boo Balloon
  Found on level 4-3, this is a ghost balloon. Unlike most other Boos in the 
  game, the Boo Balloon will not turn invisible when you face toward it. The 
  Boo Balloon also takes three hits to defeat.

Boo Blah
  Found on level 2-4, the Boo Blah is a small white blob that crawls along 
  surfaces and then occasionally stretches up to full height.

Boo Guy
  Found on levels 2-4, 2-8, 4-8, 6-2, 6-3, 6-4 and 6-5, the Boo Guy is a ghost 
  version of the Shy Guy.

Boo Man Bluff
  Found on level 2-4, this is a large orange Boo that is blindfolded. Because 
  of the blindfold, the Boo Man Bluff will not turn invisible when you face 
  toward it.

Bouncing Bullet Bill
  Found on level 5-8, this a large orange bullet which is fired out of a 
  cannon. This version of the Bullet Bill bounces off surfaces.

Bowling Goonie
  Found on levels 5-5 and 5-8, the Bowling Goonie is A fat, white bird that 
  rolls along the floor.

Bubble Dayzee
  Found on level 2-5 and 5-5, this is a more dangerous variation of the Crazee 
  Dayzee that blows bubbles.

Bullet Bill
  Found on levels E-1, 2-7, 4-1, 4-3, 4-4, 5-7 and 5-8, the Bullet Bill is a 
  large green bullet which is fired out of a cannon.

Bumpty
  Found on levels 5-1, 5-2, 5-3, 5-7 and E-5, the Bumpty is a small, blue 
  penguin that will bounce you away if you touch it. Bumptys are especially 
  dangerous on ice levels.

Burt
  Found on levels 1-4 and 2-8, this is a smaller version of Burt the Bashful, 
  the boss of level 1-4. Burts bounce quite high, and they sometimes bounce off 
  other Burts to get even higher.

Cactus Jack
  Found on levels 2-5, 2-6 and 5-1, the Cactus Jack is a large round spiky ball 
  which rolls when hit.

Caged Ghost
  Found on levels 3-8, 6-8 and E-6, the Caged Ghost is a huge ghost that grows 
  smaller when hit with an egg. When the Caged Ghost has been hit enough, it 
  will become a harmless blob for a short while. Caged Ghosts will spit out Shy 
  Guys if Yoshi has less than six eggs.

Chain Chomp
  Found on level 5-4, this is a small black ball resembling the head of a 
  shark. This Chomp is attached to a chain, and will lunge toward you when you 
  get near it.

Chomp
  Found on levels 1-2, 4-4 and 6-1, the Chomp lurks behind scenery in the 
  background and jumps out at points in the level to make holes in the path.

Clawdaddy
  Found on levels 3-3, 3-7 and 4-6, this is a large red crab which moves fast.

Cloud Drop
  Found on levels 5-8 and 6-7, the Cloud Drop is a teardrop-shaped enemy which 
  moves back and forth in a set direction. Similar to the Gusty, only smaller.

Coin Bandit
  Found on level 6-2, the Coin Bandit is an extremely fast version of the 
  Bandit that holds a red coin.

Crazee Dayzee
  Found on levels 1-1, 1-2, 1-5, 2-5 and 5-5, the Crazee Dayzee is a slow-
  moving, singing flower.

Dancing Spear Guy
  Found on levels 3-2, 6-1, 6-8 and E-6, the Dancing Spear Guy is a masked 
  creature that holds a spear and dances.

Dangling Ghost
  Found on levels 5-4 and E-6, the Dangling Ghost is a ghost that dangles from 
  the ceiling and tries to grab Mario.

Dizzy Dandy
  Found on levels 2-8, 3-4, 3-7 and 5-1, this an enemy which looks very similar 
  to the collectable flowers. The Dizzy Dandy rolls quickly toward Yoshi, but 
  it's easy enough to avoid providing you jump early.

Doctor Freezegood
  Found on levels 5-2 and 5-3, Doctor Freezegood is a skiing snowman.

Eggo-Dil
  Found on levels 1-7, 2-1, 2-6, 2-7 and 4-5, the Eggo-Dil is A flower with 
  five rotating petals that looks big and dangerous, but can be easily defeated 
  with a simple stomp.

Fang
  Found on levels 1-6, E-1, 2-3, 2-6, 4-2, 5-1, 5-4 and 6-8, the Fang is a 
  small blue flying bat.

Fat Guy
  Found on level 2-7, the Fat Guy is a large version of the Shy Guy.

Fishing Lakitu
  Found on level 4-8, this is a version of the Lakitu holds a fishing hook
  which it uses to try and catch Mario.

Flamer Guy
  Found on levels 6-1, 6-5, 6-6 and 6-8, the Flamer Guy is a fast moving Shy 
  Guy on fire.

Flightless Goonie
  Found on levels 2-3, 5-5, 5-6, 5-8 and E-5, the Flightless Goonie is a small 
  version of the Goonie bird without wings.

Flightless Skeleton Goonie
  Found on levels 6-1 and 6-5, this is a small version of the Skeleton Goonie 
  bird without wings.

Flopsy Fish
  Found on levels 3-3, 3-4, 3-7, 4-6 and 5-3, the Flopsy Fish is a small red 
  and yellow fish that jumps out of the water.

Fly Guy
  Found on levels 1-1, 1-2, 1-3, 1-5, 2-2, 2-3, 2-5, 2-6, 2-7, 2-8, 3-2, 3-3, 
  3-5, 3-7, E-3, 4-1, 4-2, 4-3, 4-5, 4-6, 4-7, 5-1, 5-2, 5-4, 5-5, 5-5, E-5, 6-
  2, 6-5, 6-7, 6-8, the Fly Guy is a flying version of the Shy Guy.

Flying Wiggler
  Found on level 4-1, the Flying Wiggler is an orange caterpillar with wings.

Frog Pirate
  Found on levels 3-3 and 3-4, the Frog Pirate is a big, smug-looking frog with 
  a long tongue.

Fuzzy
  Found on levels 1-7, 4-1 and 6-3, the Fuzzy is a large, white floating ball. 
  If one hits Yoshi, he becomes dizzy.

Gargantua Blargg
  Found on level 1-4, the Gargantua Blargg is a massive red monster with a huge 
  mouth that appears from the lava and chases toward you. There is a smaller 
  version of this enemy called the Blargg.

Georgette Jelly
  Found on level 5-4, this is a small red and yellow jelly.

Goomba
  Found on level 4-1, the Goomba is a brown, mushroom shaped creature. Commonly 
  seen in other Mario games, the Goomba is as dangerous as a normal Shy Guy.

Goonie
  Found on levels 5-3, 5-5, 5-7, 5-8 and E-5, this is a large, white bird. 
  While some Goonies are helpful, some can carry dangerous items which are 
  dropped when walked under.

Green Glove
  Found on levels 2-2, 5-6, E-5 and E-6, the Green Glove is a masked green 
  creature with a baseball glove.

Green Koopa Paratroopa
  Found on levels 2-1, 4-1, 4-5 and 4-6, this is a green turtle with wings.

Green Koopa Troopa
  Found on levels 2-1, 4-1, 4-2, 4-5, 4-6, 4-7 and 4-8, this is a green turtle. 
  When you jump on a Koopa Troopa, it's shell will come off. The shell can be 
  used to defeat other enemies.

Grim Leecher
  Found on level E-4, this is a small purple creature that wears a white mask. 
  After touching the Grim Leecher, the controls will be reversed.

Grinder
  Found on levels 3-1, 3-3, 3-4, 3-5, 3-7 and E-3, the Grinder is a monkey.

Grunt
  Found on levels 4-4 and E-6, the Grunt wears a spiked hat.

Gusty
  Found on levels 1-2, 2-3, 2-4, 2-6, 3-5, 4-7, 5-6 and 6-8, the Gusty is a 
  teardrop-shaped enemy which moves back and forth in a set direction. Gustys 
  can move either horizontally or vertically.

Harry Hedgehog
  Found on level 3-6, Harry Hedgehog is a tiny blue hedgehog which grows large 
  when Yoshi gets near it.

Hefty Goonie
  Found on level 5-5, this is a fat, white bird that struggles to fly.

Hootie the Blue Fish
  Found on level 3-8, this is a dangerous purple pirahna with white spots. This 
  enemy swims slowly around tunnels, and cannot be defeated.

Hot Lips
  Found on levels 4-4 and 4-8, this is a large, red creature that spits lava.

Huffin Puffin
  Found on levels 3-3, 4-7 and 5-6, the Huffin Puffin is a big white puffin. 
  This enemy will push you in a certain direction.

Jean de Fillet
  Found on levels E-4 and 6-4, Jean de Fillet is a skeleton fish.

Kaboomba
  Found on levels 2-6 and 5-8, the Kaboomba is a small cannon with legs. The 
  Kaboomba walks around, and occasionally fires cannonballs.

Kamek
  Found on levels E-5 and 6-8, Kamek can be seen at the start of all boss 
  fights in the game, but appears in the main levels only twice. Kamek flies 
  around on a broomstick.

Lakitu
  Found on levels 2-5, 5-2 and 5-6, Lakitu is an enemy that rides about on a 
  smiling cloud, occasionally throwing spiky balls.

Lantern Ghost
  Found on levels 1-3, 1-6, 2-3, 2-6, 4-2 and 5-1, this is a small creature 
  that carries a lantern. Lantern Ghosts have the same movements as Shy Guys.

Lava Bubble
  Found on levels 1-4, 1-8, 2-8, 4-4, 6-3 and 6-4, Lava bubbles are small 
  bubbles of lava that jump vertically from lava pits. Yoshi can spit fire 
  three times after eating a Lava Bubble.

Lava Drop
  Found on levels 4-3, 6-2, 6-4, 6-5, 6-6 and 6-7, the Lava Drops is a small 
  drop of lava with a smiling face. Unlike the Lava Bubbles, Lava Drops do not 
  appear from lava, and can move horizontally and vertically.

Lemon Drop
  Found on levels 1-8 and 3-4, this is a tiny yellow blob. Lemon Drops are 
  smaller versions of Salvo the Slime, the boss of level 1-8.

Little Mouser
  Found on levels 2-2, 3-6 and 6-4, the Little Mouser is a small blue mouse.

Little Skull Mouser
  Found on levels 2-2 and 6-2, the Little Skull Mouser is a small blue mouse 
  that wears a skull mask.

Loch Nestor
  Found on level 3-3, the Loch Nestor is a red spiky fish that grows bigger 
  when hit with an egg.

Lunge Fish
  Found on level 3-7, the Lunge Fish is a huge, ugly fish that jumps out of 
  water and tries to grab Yoshi.

Mace Guy
  Found on levels 5-4, 5-8 and E-6, the Mace Guy is a version of the Shy Guy 
  that swings a mace.

Magikoopa
  Found on level 6-8, the Magikoopa is a magician that shoots shapes. When the 
  shapes hit a block, it transforms into a Milde.

Milde
  Found on levels 1-7, 2-2, 2-3, 2-7, 3-2, 4-4, 4-5, 4-8 and 6-8, the Milde is 
  a small, pink round enemy. If Yoshi jumps on one, the Milde will explode and 
  will push away any nearby enemies.

Mock Up
  Found on levels 1-6 and 4-3, the Mock Up is a balloon with the writing '1UP' 
  on it. The balloon quickly inflates, and will explode if not eaten.

Mufti Guy
  Found on levels 1-5, 1-7, 2-6 and 5-5, the Mufti Guy is a Shy Guy which has 
  yellow flowers on top.

Needlenose
  Found on levels 3-1, 3-3, 3-5, 3-6, 3-8, 4-1, 4-3, 4-4, 4-6, 5-1, 5-5, 5-6, 
  5-8, 6-1, 6-2 and 6-7, the Needlenose is a small, spiked ball. Enemies such 
  as the Seedy Sally and Wild Ptooie Pirahna throw these.

Nep-Enut
  Found on levels 2-3 and 3-3, the Nep-Enut is a massive blue monster with a 
  huge mouth that appears from the water and chases toward you.

Nipper Plant
  Found on levels 1-3 and 3-8, the Nipper Plant is a small white clam-shaped 
  enemy which is formed when a Paranipper Plant touches the ground.

Paranipper Plant
  Found on levels 1-3 and 3-8, the Paranipper Plant is a tiny red and white 
  object that floats down with a white parachute. When the Paranipper Plants 
  touch the ground, they transform into Nipper Plants.

Pirahna Plant
  Found on levels 1-1, 1-2, 1-3, 1-4, 1-6, 1-7, 2-2, E-2, 3-1, 3-2, 3-8, 4-1, 
  4-2, 4-4, 4-7, E-4, 5-1, 5-3, 5-5, 5-6, 6-1 and 6-6, the Pirahna Plant is a 
  large red plant with teeth. They are stationary, but it is quite easy to be 
  caught by one due to their size.

Piscatory Pete
  Found on levels 3-3 and 3-7, Piscatory Pete is a small fish that is found in 
  submarine sections.

Pokey
  Found on level 2-5, Pokey is a green cactus with a Needlenose on top.

Potted Spiked Fun Guy
  Found on levels 3-5, 4-4 and 6-7, this is a version of the Spiked Fun Guy 
  that jumps about in a pot.

Preying Mantas
  Found on levels 3-3 and 3-7, the Preying Mantas is a small jellyfish that is 
  found in submarine sections.

Raven
  Found on levels 3-8, 5-7, 5-8 and 6-3, the Raven is a small black bird that 
  runs quickly along surfaces.

Red Koopa Paratroopa
  Found on levels 4-1, 4-3, 4-5, 4-6, 4-7 and 6-3, this is a red turtle with 
  wings.

Red Koopa Troopa
  Found on levels 4-1, 4-2, 4-3, 4-5, 4-6, 4-7 and 4-8, this is a red turtle. 
  When you jump on a Koopa Troopa, it's shell will come off, which can be used 
  to defeat other enemies.

Seedy Sally
  Found on levels 3-1, 3-3, 3-5, 3-6 and 3-7, Seedy Sally is a monkey which 
  drops Needlenoses from trees.

Shark Chomp
  Found on levels 4-4 and 6-7, the Shark Chomp is a huge version of the Chomp 
  which chases you though some areas.

Short Fuse
  Found on levels 3-1, 3-3, 3-4, 3-5, 3-6 and 3-7, the Short Fuse is a monkey 
  which drops bombs from trees.

Shy Guy
  Found on levels Intro, 1-1 1-2, 1-3, 1-4, 1-5, 1-6, 2-1, 2-2, 2-3, 2-5, 2-7,
  2-8, 3-3, 3-4, 3-5, 3-7, 3-8, E-3, 4-1, 4-2, 4-3, 4-5, 4-6, 5-1, 5-3, 5-4,
  5-5, 5-6, 5-7, 5-8, 6-6, 6-7, 6-8 and E-6, the Shy Guy is a small creature 
  that wears a white mask. Shy Guys are common creatures in the game, and pose 
  little threat. They have no attacking moves, but they will hurt Yoshi if he 
  walks into them.

Shy Guy on Stilts
  Found on levels 1-6, 3-7, 4-6, 6-8, this is a version of the Shy Guy that 
  walks about on stilts.

Skeleton Goonie
  Found on levels 5-3, 6-1, 6-5 and 6-8, the Skeleton Goonie is a large, flying 
  skeleton of the Goonie bird.

Slugger
  Found on levels 2-2, 5-6, 6-2 and 6-3, the Slugger is a masked yellow 
  creature with a baseball bat.

Sluggy
  Found on level 5-4, this is a smaller version of Sluggy the Unshaven, the 
  boss of level. A Sluggy is a small pink blob that resembles a slug.

Snifit
  Found on levels 4-4 and 6-7, the Snifit is a masked creature with a circular 
  mouth that shoot bullets.

Solo Toady
  Found on levels 2-5, E-3, 4-3, 6-1, 6-2 and 6-6, the Solo Toady appears in a 
  few levels of the game when Mario is seperated from Yoshi.

Spear Guy
  Found on levels 3-2, 3-4, 3-7 and 6-1, the Spear Guy is amasked creature that 
  holds a spear.

Spike
  Found on level 5-1, the Spike is a small penguin that throws a mace.

Spiked Fun Guy
  Found on levels 3-5, 4-4 and 6-7, the Spiked Fun Guy is a tiny green spiked 
  creature.

Spooky
  Found on level 6-6, the Spooky is a ghost disguise that the Bandit and Shy 
  Guy wears.

Spray Fish
  Found on levels 1-8, 2-6, 3-4 and 5-3, the Spray Fish is a fish which sprays 
  a stream of water.

Stretch
  Found on levels 3-3 and 6-8, this is a version of the Shy Guy that is twice 
  as tall as normal.

Support Ghost
  Found on levels 1-8 and 5-4, the Support Ghost is a harmless ghost that 
  carries a platform on top of its head.

Tap-Tap
  Found on levels 1-7, E-1, 2-1, 2-2, 2-3, 2-7, 3-2, E-3, 4-2, 4-5, 4-6, 5-2, 
  5-7, 6-1, 6-4, 6-6 and 6-7, Tap-Taps are small spiked creatures which make a 
  tapping noise as they walk. When shot with an egg or watermelon seed, they 
  roll quite a distance, but then stand up and continue walking.

Tap-Tap the Golden
  Found on level 6-8, this is a huge golden Tap-Tap that follows you through an 
  area in the final castle.

Thunder Lakitu
  Found on level 5-1, the Thunder Lakitu is aversion of the Lakitu that throws 
  fireballs down from his cloud.

Train Bandit
  Found on levels 2-5 and 2-8, the Train Bandit is a small white creature that 
  is found in some train sections.

Wall Lakitu
  Found on levels 2-7, 4-2 and 5-1, this is a version of the Lakitu that hides 
  behind walls, and occasionally appears to throw spiked balls.

Whirly Fly Guy
  Found on levels 3-3, 4-1, 5-1 and 5-4, the Whirly Fly Guy is a version of the 
  Fly Guy that flashes different colours.

Wild Ptooie Pirahna
  Found on levels 3-5, 3-8, 4-1, 4-3, 4-4, 4-6, 5-1, 5-5, 5-7, 6-2 and 6-7, 
  this is a version of the Pirahna Plant that spits Needlenoses and takes three 
  hits with an egg to defeat.

Woozy Guy
  Found on levels 1-1, 2-5, 3-3, 3-5, 4-6, 5-1, 5-6, 6-8 and E-6, the Woozy Guy 
  is a jumping version of the Shy Guy.

Zeus Guy
  Found on levels 6-1, 6-2 and 6-6, the Zeus Guy is a green creature that 
  fights and shoots lightning.

~~ Friends ~~

Melon Bug
  Found on levels 1-7 and 4-5, this is a small green bug that rolls into a ball 
  when you get near. Melon Bugs are harmless to Yoshi, and can be used to 
  defeat other enemies.

Muddy Buddy
  Found on level 5-4, the Muddy Buddy is a purple creature that can be used to 
  cross spikes.

~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~

7.                         Frequently Asked Questions

~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~

Q. How many coins are there in the game?
A. 9,523.

Q. How many enemies are there in the game?
A. 127: 115 basic enemies and 12 bosses.

Q. How many levels are there in the game?
A. 55: A training level, 48 normal levels and 6 bonus levels.

Q. I have returned to a previously completed level. How do I exit the level
   without completing it.
A. Press Start to pause the game, then tap Select to leave.

Q. What happens when you get 100% in every level?
A. Nothing.

~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~

  of the enemies.
